# Question 1 — Aortoiliac Occlusion (Leriche Syndrome) / 主髂动脉闭塞（Leriche 综合征）

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>57-year-old man</strong> comes to the physician because of a <strong>1-year history of low back pain that radiates to the buttocks when he walks</strong>. He has not had leg pain or pain at rest. The <strong>pain is relieved within 1 minute when he stops walking</strong>. He has a <strong>1-year history of erectile dysfunction</strong>. He has <strong>smoked one pack of cigarettes daily for 30 years</strong>. His pulse is 85/min, and blood pressure is <strong>160/100 mm Hg</strong>. Flexion of either hip with the knee extended does not cause pain. <strong>Pedal pulses are decreased</strong>. Sensation is intact. His hematocrit is 40%, erythrocyte sedimentation rate is <strong>20 mm/h</strong>, and serum glucose concentration is <strong>180 mg/dL</strong>. Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most likely diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Aortoiliac occlusion<br />
B) Dissecting aortic aneurysm<br />
C) Herniated nucleus pulposus<br />
D) Lumbar discitis<br />
E) Pyelonephritis<br />
F) Spinal stenosis</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: A</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Buttock pain with walking, relieved within 1 min of rest<br />
行走时臀部疼痛，休息 1 分钟内缓解</td>
<td>Classic vascular claudication: ischemia driven by exercise demand exceeding stenotic vessel capacity; relief is position-independent<br />
典型血管性间歇性跛行：运动需求超过狭窄血管供血能力所致缺血；缓解与体位无关</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Erectile dysfunction × 1 year<br />
勃起功能障碍 × 1 年</td>
<td>Component of Leriche triad: internal iliac hypoperfusion causes vasculogenic ED, not neurogenic<br />
Leriche 三联征组成之一：髂内动脉供血不足导致血管源性 ED，非神经源性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Decreased pedal pulses<br />
足背动脉搏动减弱</td>
<td>Third component of Leriche triad: confirms reduced distal arterial flow from aortoiliac occlusion<br />
Leriche 三联征第三要素：证实主髂动脉闭塞导致远端动脉血流减少</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No leg pain; pain only in buttocks/low back<br />
无腿部疼痛；疼痛仅在臀部/腰部</td>
<td>Occlusion at aortoiliac level (proximal) → proximal claudication; femoral disease causes calf pain<br />
闭塞位于主髂动脉水平（近端）→ 近端跛行；股动脉病变导致小腿痛</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Negative straight leg raise (hip flexion + knee extension, no pain)<br />
直腿抬高试验阴性（屈髋伸膝无疼痛）</td>
<td>Excludes nerve root compression (herniated disc, spinal stenosis) as cause<br />
排除神经根压迫（椎间盘突出、椎管狭窄）作为病因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>30 pack-year smoking, HTN (160/100), glucose 180 mg/dL<br />
30 包年吸烟、高血压（160/100）、血糖 180 mg/dL</td>
<td>Three converging atherosclerosis risk factors; explains accelerated aortoiliac plaque burden<br />
三大动脉粥样硬化危险因素汇聚；解释主髂动脉斑块负担加重</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Normal ESR (20 mm/h), intact sensation<br />
ESR 正常（20 mm/h），感觉完整</td>
<td>Against inflammatory/infectious etiology (discitis, pyelonephritis); against neuropathy<br />
反对炎症/感染性病因（椎间盘炎、肾盂肾炎）；反对神经病变</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Atherosclerotic plaque** accumulates at the **aortic bifurcation** and **common iliac arteries**, progressively reducing luminal diameter and impairing blood flow augmentation to the pelvis and lower extremities during exercise:

**动脉粥样硬化斑块**在**腹主动脉分叉**和**髂总动脉**处积累，逐渐缩小管腔，损害运动时向盆腔和下肢的血流增加能力：

- At rest, collateral vessels compensate adequately → no pain\
  静息时，侧支循环充分代偿 → 无疼痛

- With exercise, skeletal muscle O₂ demand increases; stenotic vessels cannot augment flow proportionally → ischemic metabolite accumulation → buttock/thigh claudication\
  运动时骨骼肌耗氧需求增加；狭窄血管无法相应增流 → 缺血代谢产物积累 → 臀部/大腿跛行

- Cessation of exercise drops O₂ demand rapidly; pain resolves within 1 minute without positional change\
  停止运动后耗氧需求迅速下降；无需改变体位，疼痛 1 分钟内消退

- Internal iliac artery hypoperfusion impairs cavernous artery inflow → vasculogenic erectile dysfunction\
  髂内动脉供血不足损害阴茎海绵体动脉血流 → 血管源性勃起功能障碍

- Smoking injures endothelium + foam cell formation; HTN creates intimal stress; hyperglycemia impairs eNOS → all three accelerate plaque progression\
  吸烟损伤内皮 + 促泡沫细胞形成；高血压造成内膜应力损伤；高血糖损害内皮 NO 合酶 → 三者共同加速斑块进展

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** occlusion level predicts pain location — aortoiliac → buttock/thigh; femoral → calf; tibial → foot.

**解剖小窍门:** 闭塞平面决定疼痛部位——主髂动脉 → 臀部/大腿；股动脉 → 小腿；胫动脉 → 足部。

## 3. Correct Answer (A) — Aortoiliac Occlusion / 正确答案 (A) — 主髂动脉闭塞

**Aortoiliac occlusion (Leriche syndrome)** is atherosclerotic obliterative disease at the aortic bifurcation and/or iliac arteries producing the pathognomonic triad of proximal claudication, erectile dysfunction, and diminished lower-extremity pulses:

**主髂动脉闭塞（Leriche 综合征）**是腹主动脉分叉和/或髂动脉的动脉粥样硬化性闭塞疾病，产生特征性三联征：近端跛行、勃起功能障碍和下肢动脉搏动减弱：

- Claudication is proximal: buttock \> thigh (not calf) — occlusion level maps to symptom distribution\
  跛行为近端：臀部 \> 大腿（非小腿）——闭塞平面与症状分布对应

- Vascular claudication: relieved by rest alone, not requiring positional change (key vs. neurogenic)\
  血管性跛行：仅需休息即可缓解，无需改变体位（与神经源性鉴别要点）

- Erectile dysfunction is vasculogenic: bilateral internal iliac compromise → absent nocturnal erections\
  勃起功能障碍为血管源性：双侧髂内动脉受累 → 夜间勃起消失

- Disease progression: claudication → rest pain → ischemic ulcers → gangrene (Rutherford stages 1→6)\
  疾病进展：跛行 → 静息痛 → 缺血性溃疡 → 坏疽（Rutherford 1→6 期）

**Diagnosis:** ABI \< 0.90 confirms PAD; duplex ultrasound or CT angiography localizes the aortoiliac lesion; ABI \> 1.3 in diabetics/CKD (calcified) — use toe-brachial index instead.

**诊断:** ABI \< 0.90 确认外周动脉病；双功能超声或 CT 血管造影定位主髂动脉病变；糖尿病/慢性肾病患者 ABI \> 1.3（血管钙化）——改用趾臂指数。

**Treatment:** Antiplatelet (aspirin or clopidogrel) + high-intensity statin + smoking cessation + BP/glucose control + supervised exercise; cilostazol for claudication; severe disease → aortobifemoral bypass or iliac angioplasty ± stenting.

**治疗:** 抗血小板（阿司匹林或氯吡格雷）+ 高强度他汀 + 戒烟 + 控压/控糖 + 监督性运动训练；西洛他唑改善跛行症状；严重病变 → 主动脉双股动脉旁路移植或髂动脉球囊扩张 ± 支架。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Aortoiliac occlusion ✓<br />
A — 主髂动脉闭塞 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — complete Leriche triad: proximal claudication relieved by rest, vasculogenic ED, decreased pedal pulses<br />
正确——Leriche 三联征完整：近端跛行休息缓解、血管源性 ED、足背动脉搏动减弱</td>
<td>All three components present; rest relief is position-independent<br />
三联征齐全；缓解与体位无关</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Dissecting aortic aneurysm<br />
B — 主动脉夹层</td>
<td>Acute catastrophic onset: tearing chest/back pain, BP differential between arms, hemodynamic instability; not a 1-year indolent course<br />
急性灾难性起病：撕裂样胸/背痛、双臂血压差、血流动力学不稳；非 1 年慢性病程</td>
<td>Acute vs. chronic: dissection = surgical emergency; PAD = years of progression<br />
急性 vs. 慢性：夹层 = 外科急症；外周动脉病 = 多年进展</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Herniated nucleus pulposus<br />
C — 髓核突出</td>
<td>Radicular leg pain with positive straight leg raise; this patient's SLR is negative; onset typically after straining/lifting<br />
根性腿痛伴直腿抬高阳性；本例 SLR 阴性；通常在用力/举重后起病</td>
<td>Negative SLR excludes nerve root compression; radiculopathy radiates to leg (not just buttock)<br />
SLR 阴性排除神经根压迫；根性痛放射至腿部（非单纯臀部）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Lumbar discitis<br />
D — 腰椎椎间盘炎</td>
<td>Infectious/inflammatory: fever, localized non-radiating back pain, elevated ESR/CRP, leukocytosis; ESR here is normal (20 mm/h)<br />
感染性/炎症性：发热、局限性非放射性背痛、ESR/CRP 升高、白细胞增多；本例 ESR 正常（20 mm/h）</td>
<td>Normal ESR + no fever + exertional pattern = against infection<br />
ESR 正常 + 无发热 + 劳力性规律 = 反对感染</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Pyelonephritis<br />
E — 肾盂肾炎</td>
<td>Upper UTI: fever, dysuria, hematuria, urinary frequency, CVA tenderness; no exertional component<br />
上尿路感染：发热、排尿困难、血尿、尿频、肋脊角压痛；无劳力性成分</td>
<td>No urinary symptoms; pain is reproducibly exercise-triggered, not infectious<br />
无泌尿系症状；疼痛可重复性运动触发，非感染性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>F — Spinal stenosis<br />
F — 椎管狭窄</td>
<td>Neurogenic claudication: worsens with standing/extension; requires sitting/forward-flexion for relief — NOT resolved by stopping walking alone; may have sensory deficits<br />
神经源性跛行：站立/伸展加重；需坐下/前屈才能缓解——仅停止行走不够；可有感觉缺损</td>
<td>Relief requires positional change (flexion) in neurogenic; vascular resolves with rest in any position<br />
神经源性需要体位改变（前屈）才能缓解；血管性任何体位休息均可缓解</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*Spinal stenosis (F) is the highest-yield distractor: both cause walking-induced buttock pain, but the single most important discriminator is that vascular claudication resolves with rest in any position, while neurogenic claudication requires forward flexion or sitting for relief.*

椎管狭窄（F）是最高频干扰项：两者均可引起行走诱发的臀部疼痛，但最重要的单一鉴别点在于：血管性跛行在任何体位下休息即可缓解，而神经源性跛行需要前屈或坐位才能缓解。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Vascular vs. Neurogenic Claudication / 血管性 vs. 神经源性间歇性跛行对比

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Vascular Claudication</strong><br />
<strong>血管性跛行</strong></th>
<th><strong>Neurogenic Claudication</strong><br />
<strong>神经源性跛行</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Cause<br />
病因</td>
<td>Atherosclerotic arterial stenosis (PAD)<br />
动脉粥样硬化性动脉狭窄（外周动脉病）</td>
<td>Lumbar spinal canal stenosis compressing nerve roots<br />
腰椎椎管狭窄压迫神经根</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pain location<br />
疼痛部位</td>
<td>Buttock/thigh (aortoiliac) or calf (femoral) — depends on occlusion level<br />
臀部/大腿（主髂动脉）或小腿（股动脉）——取决于闭塞平面</td>
<td>Bilateral legs, buttocks, may radiate diffusely<br />
双侧下肢、臀部，可弥漫放射</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Relief<br />
缓解方式</td>
<td>Stopping walking; any position works (rest alone)<br />
停止行走；任何体位均可（仅需休息）</td>
<td>Sitting or forward flexion (widens spinal canal)<br />
坐位或前屈（扩大椎管）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Standing still<br />
静止站立</td>
<td>Relieves pain (no muscle work → no ischemia)<br />
可缓解疼痛（肌肉不做功 → 无缺血）</td>
<td>Does NOT relieve pain (canal still narrowed)<br />
不能缓解疼痛（椎管仍狭窄）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pedal pulses<br />
足背动脉搏动</td>
<td>Diminished or absent<br />
减弱或消失</td>
<td>Normal<br />
正常</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Neurological exam<br />
神经系统检查</td>
<td>Intact sensation; negative SLR<br />
感觉完整；SLR 阴性</td>
<td>May show weakness, sensory loss, diminished reflexes<br />
可有肌力减退、感觉缺失、反射减弱</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Key workup<br />
关键检查</td>
<td>ABI &lt; 0.90; CT angiography<br />
踝臂指数 &lt; 0.90；CT 血管造影</td>
<td>MRI lumbar spine: canal narrowing, ligamentum flavum hypertrophy<br />
腰椎 MRI：椎管狭窄、黄韧带肥厚</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**When a middle-aged male smoker presents with buttock claudication relieved by rest (not position change), erectile dysfunction, and decreased pedal pulses, diagnose Leriche syndrome (aortoiliac occlusion) until proven otherwise.**

**当中年男性吸烟者出现休息（而非体位改变）即缓解的臀部跛行、勃起功能障碍和足背动脉搏动减弱时，在排除之前应首先诊断 Leriche 综合征（主髂动脉闭塞）。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — Leriche "3 P's" Triad / 记忆钩 — Leriche 三联征 "3 个 P":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>P</strong>ulselessness (decreased pedal pulses) — confirms aortoiliac outflow obstruction / 无脉（足背动脉搏动减弱）——证实主髂动脉流出道梗阻<br />
• <strong>P</strong>ain with walking (buttock claudication) — proximal location = aortoiliac level / 行走时疼痛（臀部跛行）——近端位置 = 主髂动脉水平<br />
• <strong>P</strong>otency loss (vasculogenic erectile dysfunction) — internal iliac hypoperfusion / 性功能丧失（血管源性勃起功能障碍）——髂内动脉供血不足</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Peripheral Arterial Disease & Leriche Syndrome / 高频知识表 — 外周动脉病与 Leriche 综合征

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Leriche triad<br />
Leriche 三联征</td>
<td>(1) Buttock/thigh claudication; (2) vasculogenic erectile dysfunction; (3) absent/diminished femoral &amp; distal pulses — caused by infrarenal aortoiliac atherosclerosis<br />
(1) 臀部/大腿跛行；(2) 血管源性勃起功能障碍；(3) 股动脉及远端搏动消失/减弱——由肾下主髂动脉粥样硬化引起</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ABI interpretation<br />
踝臂指数解读</td>
<td>Normal ≥ 1.0; borderline 0.91–0.99; mild PAD 0.70–0.90; moderate 0.40–0.69; severe/CLI &lt; 0.40; &gt; 1.30 = calcified (use TBI)<br />
正常 ≥ 1.0；临界 0.91–0.99；轻度 PAD 0.70–0.90；中度 0.40–0.69；重度/CLI &lt; 0.40；&gt; 1.30 = 钙化（改用趾臂指数）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>PAD risk factors<br />
外周动脉病危险因素</td>
<td>Smoking (strongest modifiable), DM, HTN, dyslipidemia, age &gt; 50, male sex, CKD, prior CVD; this patient has 3 of the top 4<br />
吸烟（最强可控因素）、糖尿病、高血压、血脂异常、年龄 &gt; 50、男性、慢性肾病、既往心血管病；本例具备前 4 中的 3 个</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Rutherford classification<br />
Rutherford 分期</td>
<td>1–3: claudication (mild→severe); 4: rest pain; 5: minor tissue loss (ulcer); 6: major tissue loss/gangrene → limb-threatening ischemia<br />
1–3 期：跛行（轻→重度）；4 期：静息痛；5 期：小面积组织缺失（溃疡）；6 期：大面积组织缺失/坏疽 → 肢体威胁性缺血</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Medical management<br />
药物治疗</td>
<td>Antiplatelet (ASA or clopidogrel) + high-intensity statin + ACE inhibitor + smoking cessation; cilostazol for claudication (contraindicated in HF); pentoxifylline: weaker alternative<br />
抗血小板（阿司匹林或氯吡格雷）+ 高强度他汀 + ACEI + 戒烟；西洛他唑改善跛行（心衰禁用）；己酮可可碱：效果较弱的替代方案</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Surgical options<br />
手术选择</td>
<td>Aortobifemoral bypass (gold standard for aortoiliac); iliac PTA ± stenting (endovascular, less invasive); indication: lifestyle-limiting claudication or CLI<br />
主动脉双股动脉旁路移植（主髂动脉病变金标准）；髂动脉球囊扩张 ± 支架（腔内，创伤更小）；适应证：影响生活质量的跛行或严重肢体缺血</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Vasculogenic vs. psychogenic ED<br />
血管源性 vs. 心理源性 ED</td>
<td>Vasculogenic: absent nocturnal erections, associated PAD/DM/HTN; psychogenic: nocturnal erections preserved, situational onset<br />
血管源性：夜间勃起消失，伴外周动脉病/糖尿病/高血压；心理源性：夜间勃起保留，情境性发作</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Variant — rest pain:** If pedal pulses were absent and he had rest pain → Rutherford stage 4 chronic limb-threatening ischemia (CLI); urgent revascularization within hours-days to prevent amputation\
  **题目变式——静息痛:** 若足背动脉搏动消失且出现静息痛 → Rutherford 4 期慢性肢体威胁性缺血；需在数小时至数天内紧急血运重建以防截肢

- **Variant — calf only:** If pain were in calf only → superficial femoral artery (SFA) disease, most common single-vessel PAD lesion; same mechanism, different occlusion level\
  **题目变式——仅小腿:** 若疼痛仅在小腿 → 股浅动脉病变，最常见的单支血管外周动脉病病变；机制相同，闭塞平面不同

- **Cause of death:** PAD patients die predominantly of MI and stroke (shared atherosclerotic risk factor burden), not limb ischemia per se; aggressive cardiovascular risk factor management is the priority\
  **真正死因:** 外周动脉病患者主要死于心肌梗死和脑卒中（共同的动脉粥样硬化危险因素负担），而非肢体缺血本身；积极控制心血管危险因素是首要任务

- **Mnemonic — 6 P's of acute limb ischemia:** Pain, Pallor, Pulselessness, Paresthesia, Paralysis, Poikilothermia — sudden onset distinguishes acute embolism/thrombosis from chronic PAD; surgical emergency\
  **记忆——急性肢体缺血 6P:** 疼痛、苍白、无脉、感觉异常、瘫痪、变温——突然起病区别于慢性外周动脉病；外科急症

# Question 2 — Postmenopausal Cardiovascular Disease Mortality Risk / 绝经后心血管疾病死亡风险

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>60-year-old female</strong> store clerk comes to the office for an annual health maintenance examination. Her medical history is unremarkable except for gastroesophageal reflux disease, for which she takes ranitidine at bedtime with good relief. <strong>Her last menstrual period was 6 years ago.</strong> Mammogram 5 years ago and Pap smear 2 years ago were normal. <strong>She does not exercise regularly.</strong> She eats a regular diet. <strong>She has smoked one pack of cigarettes daily for 40 years</strong> and drinks one to two glasses of wine weekly. Her family history is significant only for <strong>diet-controlled diabetes mellitus in her mother.</strong> The patient is 157 cm (5 ft 2 in) tall and weighs 68 kg (150 lb); <strong>BMI is 27 kg/m².</strong> <strong>Her waist-to-hip ratio is 1.05.</strong> Cardiopulmonary, abdominal, and genitourinary examinations are normal for her age and sex assigned at birth.</p>
<p><strong>Q: This patient's greatest risk of mortality at this time is from which of the following?</strong></p>
<p>A) Breast cancer<br />
B) Cardiovascular disease<br />
C) Cervical cancer<br />
D) Hip fracture<br />
E) Lung cancer</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: B</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>60-year-old female, LMP 6 years ago<br />
60 岁女性，末次月经 6 年前（绝经后）</td>
<td>Postmenopausal state = loss of estrogen's cardioprotective effects, dramatically raising CVD risk<br />
绝经后状态 = 雌激素心脏保护消失，CVD 风险显著升高</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Smokes 1 pack/day × 40 years (40 pack-years)<br />
每天 1 包香烟，持续 40 年（40 包-年）</td>
<td>Major independent risk factor for both CVD and lung cancer; synergistic with other risk factors<br />
CVD 和肺癌的主要独立危险因素，与其他危险因素协同增效</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Does not exercise regularly<br />
无规律运动</td>
<td>Sedentary lifestyle is a modifiable CVD risk factor<br />
久坐生活方式是可干预的 CVD 危险因素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>BMI 27 kg/m², waist-to-hip ratio 1.05<br />
BMI 27，腰臀比 1.05</td>
<td>Overweight + central obesity (WHR &gt;0.85 in women = abdominal fat distribution); central obesity strongly linked to metabolic syndrome and CVD<br />
超重 + 中心性肥胖（女性腰臀比 &gt;0.85 即为腹型肥胖），与代谢综合征及 CVD 强相关</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Family history of diet-controlled DM in mother<br />
母亲有饮食控制型糖尿病家族史</td>
<td>Suggests insulin resistance predisposition; DM is a major independent CVD risk factor<br />
提示胰岛素抵抗倾向；糖尿病是主要的独立 CVD 危险因素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Annual health maintenance examination (no acute complaint)<br />
年度健康维护检查（无急性主诉）</td>
<td>Question asks about population-level mortality statistics, not acute diagnosis<br />
题目问的是人群层面的死亡率统计，而非急性诊断</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Estrogen** exerts significant **cardioprotective effects** through multiple mechanisms; **menopause** marks a critical inflection point in women's cardiovascular risk trajectory:

**雌激素**通过多种机制发挥重要的**心脏保护作用**；**绝经**是女性心血管风险轨迹的关键转折点：

- Estrogen raises HDL cholesterol and lowers LDL cholesterol, maintaining a favorable lipid profile\
  雌激素升高 HDL 胆固醇、降低 LDL 胆固醇，维持有利的血脂谱

- Estrogen promotes vasodilation via nitric oxide upregulation on arterial endothelium\
  雌激素通过上调动脉内皮一氧化氮，促进血管舒张

- After menopause, these protections are lost, accelerating atherosclerosis and coronary artery disease\
  绝经后上述保护消失，加速动脉粥样硬化和冠状动脉疾病进展

- Smoking compounds CVD risk through endothelial dysfunction and procoagulant platelet activation\
  吸烟通过内皮功能障碍和促凝血小板激活叠加 CVD 风险

- Central obesity (WHR 1.05) promotes insulin resistance and dyslipidemia, further accelerating atherosclerosis\
  中心性肥胖（腰臀比 1.05）促进胰岛素抵抗和血脂异常，进一步加速动脉粥样硬化

**Epidemiologic rule of thumb:** Cardiovascular disease is the \#1 cause of death in the United States for both men and women; in postmenopausal women, CVD mortality surpasses all cancers combined.

**流行病学小窍门:** 心血管疾病是美国男女首位死亡原因；在绝经后女性中，CVD 死亡率超过所有癌症的总和。

## 3. Correct Answer (B) — Cardiovascular Disease / 正确答案 (B) — 心血管疾病

**Cardiovascular disease** is the leading cause of mortality in the United States, and postmenopausal women face disproportionately increased risk due to the loss of estrogen-mediated cardioprotection:

**心血管疾病**是美国首位死亡原因，绝经后女性因失去雌激素介导的心脏保护而面临不成比例的更高风险：

- CVD accounts for approximately 1 in every 3 deaths in the U.S. annually, exceeding all cancers combined\
  CVD 约占美国年度死亡总数的 1/3，超过所有癌症之和

- Prior to menopause, women have lower CVD rates than age-matched men; this protective gap closes after menopause\
  绝经前女性 CVD 发生率低于同龄男性；绝经后这一保护性差距消失

- This patient carries multiple stacked risk factors: postmenopausal status, 40 pack-year smoking history, sedentary lifestyle, central obesity (WHR 1.05), overweight BMI, and family history of DM\
  该患者存在多重叠加危险因素：绝经后状态、40 包年吸烟史、久坐生活方式、中心性肥胖（腰臀比 1.05）、超重 BMI 及糖尿病家族史

**Diagnosis:** No acute diagnosis required; this is a population-level statistical question about the leading cause of mortality in this demographic

**诊断:** 无需急性诊断；这是一道关于该人群首位死因的人群统计学问题

**Treatment:** Smoking cessation, regular aerobic exercise, heart-healthy diet; monitor blood pressure, fasting lipids, and HbA1c; consider low-dose CT lung cancer screening (40 pack-years qualifies)

**治疗:** 戒烟、规律有氧运动、心脏健康饮食；监测血压、空腹血脂及 HbA1c；考虑低剂量 CT 肺癌筛查（40 包年符合条件）

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Breast cancer<br />
A — 乳腺癌</td>
<td>Postmenopausal women not on HRT have lower endogenous estrogen, actually reducing breast cancer risk; mammogram 5 years ago was normal<br />
未使用 HRT 的绝经后女性内源性雌激素降低，乳腺癌风险实际下降；5 年前乳腺 X 线检查正常</td>

</tr>

<td>Pap smear 2 years ago was normal; no HPV history, multiple partners, or immunosuppression documented<br />
2 年前宫颈涂片正常；无 HPV 感染史、多性伴侣或免疫抑制记录</td>

<tr>
<td>D — Hip fracture<br />
D — 髋部骨折</td>
<td>Postmenopausal estrogen loss does increase bone resorption → osteoporosis → hip fracture risk, but hip fracture carries far lower mortality burden than CVD<br />
绝经后雌激素缺失确实增加骨吸收→骨质疏松→髋部骨折风险，但髋部骨折死亡负担远低于 CVD</td>
<td>Hip fracture causes significant morbidity and does increase mortality after age 60, but not on par with CVD's scale<br />
髋部骨折导致显著发病率，60 岁后确实增加死亡率，但与 CVD 的规模不可比</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Lung cancer<br />
E — 肺癌</td>
<td>40 pack-year smoking history is a significant lung cancer risk; lung cancer is the #1 cancer killer, but CVD remains the overall #1 cause of death<br />
40 包年吸烟史是重要肺癌风险；肺癌是癌症首位死因，但 CVD 仍为总体首位死因</td>
<td>The question asks for greatest overall mortality risk, not cancer-specific; CVD outranks lung cancer even in heavy smokers<br />
题目问总体最大死亡风险，而非癌症特异性；即使在重度吸烟者中，CVD 仍超过肺癌</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is (E) Lung cancer — a 40 pack-year history is alarming, but in this postmenopausal woman with multiple compounding cardiovascular risk factors, CVD still outranks lung cancer as the top mortality threat.*

最容易误选的干扰项是 (E) 肺癌——40 包年吸烟史令人警觉，但在这位有多重心血管危险因素叠加的绝经后女性中，CVD 仍超过肺癌成为首位死亡威胁。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**Cardiovascular disease is the \#1 cause of death in U.S. women, and postmenopausal status dramatically amplifies this risk by eliminating estrogen's cardioprotective effects — especially when compounded by smoking, central obesity, and a sedentary lifestyle.**

**心血管疾病是美国女性首位死亡原因，绝经后状态通过消除雌激素心脏保护作用大幅放大这一风险——尤其在叠加吸烟、中心性肥胖和久坐生活方式时。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — SMOKES CVD / 记忆钩 — "SMOKES" 心血管风险因素:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>S</strong>moking — #1 modifiable CVD risk factor; endothelial damage + procoagulant / 吸烟——首位可改变 CVD 危险因素；内皮损伤 + 促凝<br />
• <strong>M</strong>enopause — estrogen loss → ↑LDL, ↓HDL, ↓vasodilation / 绝经——雌激素消失→LDL↑、HDL↓、血管舒张↓<br />
• <strong>O</strong>besity (central) — WHR &gt;0.85 in women = metabolic syndrome risk / 肥胖（中心性）——女性腰臀比 &gt;0.85 = 代谢综合征风险<br />
• <strong>K</strong>inetics (sedentary) — physical inactivity independently raises CVD risk / 不动（久坐）——体力活动不足独立增加 CVD 风险<br />
• <strong>E</strong>ndocrine (DM/family history) — insulin resistance accelerates atherosclerosis / 内分泌（DM/家族史）——胰岛素抵抗加速动脉粥样硬化<br />
• <strong>S</strong>tatistics — CVD kills more U.S. women than all cancers combined / 统计数据——CVD 致死人数超过美国女性所有癌症总和</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Cardiovascular Risk in Postmenopausal Women / 高频知识表 — 绝经后女性心血管风险

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>CVD as #1 cause of U.S. mortality<br />
CVD 为美国首位死因</td>
<td>Accounts for ~1 in 3 U.S. deaths annually; kills more women than all cancers combined; women's CVD risk approaches men's after menopause<br />
约占美国年死亡总数 1/3；女性 CVD 死亡人数超过所有癌症之和；绝经后女性 CVD 风险接近男性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Estrogen's cardioprotective mechanisms<br />
雌激素心脏保护机制</td>
<td>Raises HDL, lowers LDL; promotes endothelial nitric oxide production (vasodilation); anti-inflammatory effects on vessel wall; all lost with menopause<br />
升高 HDL、降低 LDL；促进内皮一氧化氮生成（血管舒张）；对血管壁的抗炎作用；绝经后全部消失</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Waist-to-hip ratio (WHR) interpretation<br />
腰臀比（WHR）解读</td>
<td>Women: WHR &gt;0.85 = central obesity (this patient: 1.05, significantly elevated); Men: &gt;0.90; central obesity predicts CVD better than BMI alone because it reflects visceral fat<br />
女性：腰臀比 &gt;0.85 = 中心性肥胖（该患者 1.05，显著升高）；男性：&gt;0.90；中心性肥胖预测 CVD 优于单纯 BMI，因其反映内脏脂肪</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>HRT and CVD — WHI Trial key lesson<br />
HRT 与 CVD——WHI 试验关键教训</td>
<td>Combined estrogen + progestin HRT in postmenopausal women INCREASES CVD risk (coronary artery disease, stroke, VTE); do NOT use HRT for cardiovascular protection<br />
绝经后女性联合雌激素 + 孕激素 HRT 会增加 CVD 风险（冠心病、卒中、VTE）；不应以心血管保护为目的使用 HRT</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Lung cancer screening (USPSTF 2021)<br />
肺癌筛查（USPSTF 2021 年）</td>
<td>Annual low-dose CT (LDCT) for ages 50–80 with ≥20 pack-year history who currently smoke or quit within 15 years; this patient (60 y/o, 40 pack-years, current smoker) clearly qualifies<br />
50-80 岁、≥20 包年且目前吸烟或戒烟不足 15 年者，建议年度低剂量 CT；该患者（60 岁、40 包年、现吸烟者）明确符合条件</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Modifiable vs. non-modifiable CVD risk factors<br />
可改变与不可改变的 CVD 危险因素</td>
<td>Modifiable: smoking, physical inactivity, obesity, hypertension, dyslipidemia, DM control, diet; Non-modifiable: age, sex, postmenopausal status, family history<br />
可改变：吸烟、体力活动不足、肥胖、高血压、血脂异常、DM 控制、饮食；不可改变：年龄、性别、绝经后状态、家族史</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of leading causes of death in U.S. women (ranked):** CVD \> cancer (lung \#1, breast \#2, colorectal \#3) \> accidents \> COPD \> stroke — knowing this order is tested frequently in health maintenance questions\
  **美国女性主要死因鉴别（按排名）:** CVD \> 癌症（肺癌第 1、乳腺癌第 2、结直肠癌第 3）\> 意外事故 \> COPD \> 卒中——这一顺序在健康维护题型中频繁被考

- **Atypical CVD presentation in women:** Women are more likely to present with fatigue, jaw pain, nausea, and dyspnea rather than classic crushing substernal chest pain; awareness prevents missed diagnoses\
  **女性 CVD 的不典型表现:** 女性更易表现为疲劳、下颌痛、恶心和呼吸困难，而非典型的压榨性胸骨后胸痛；了解这一点可防止漏诊

- **Key complication of osteoporosis in postmenopause:** Hip fracture in patients \>60 carries 20–30% one-year mortality due to immobility, PE, and infection — but remains far less prevalent than CVD as a population-level killer\
  **绝经后骨质疏松的关键并发症:** \>60 岁患者髋部骨折后 1 年死亡率达 20-30%（因制动、PE 及感染），但作为人群层面的死亡原因仍远不及 CVD

- **Primary prevention counseling priorities for this patient:** Smoking cessation (highest yield single intervention), then initiate LDCT lung cancer screening, then cardiovascular risk stratification with lipid panel and blood pressure monitoring\
  **该患者一级预防咨询优先级:** 戒烟（单一干预效益最高），其次启动 LDCT 肺癌筛查，再次进行血脂检查和血压监测的心血管风险分层

# Question 3 — Large Spontaneous Pneumothorax / 大型自发性气胸

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>36-year-old man</strong> is brought to the emergency department after he developed <strong>chest pain and dyspnea</strong> while attempting a 10K run. He has had <strong>mild asthma</strong> for several years but he takes no medications for it. He says that he has developed a <strong>nonproductive cough</strong> recently. He has not had fever, but he has noticed a decrease in his appetite and a <strong>2.5-kg (5-lb) weight loss during the past 6 weeks</strong>. Vital signs are pulse 100/min, respirations 26/min, and blood pressure 100/72 mm Hg. Pulse oximetry on room air shows an <strong>oxygen saturation of 92%</strong>. <strong>Breath sounds are diminished on the right</strong> and there is <strong>increased resonance on percussion</strong>. Chest x-ray is shown.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate treatment at this time?</strong></p>
<p>A) Endotracheal intubation<br />
B) Nebulized albuterol<br />
C) Observation and administration of nasal oxygen<br />
D) Thoracotomy<br />
E) Tube thoracostomy</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Chest pain + dyspnea during exertion<br />
用力时胸痛+呼吸困难</td>
<td>Pleuritic chest pain with dyspnea during exertion is classic for spontaneous pneumothorax triggered by increased intrathoracic pressure<br />
劳力性胸膜炎性胸痛+呼吸困难是自发性气胸的典型表现，由胸腔内压增高诱发</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Breath sounds diminished on the right<br />
右侧呼吸音减低</td>
<td>Unilateral absent breath sounds → air or fluid in pleural space; laterality is the critical clue distinguishing pneumothorax from bilateral conditions like asthma<br />
单侧呼吸音消失→胸腔积气或积液；单侧性是区别气胸与哮喘等双侧疾病的关键线索</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Increased resonance on percussion<br />
叩诊过清音</td>
<td>Hyperresonance = air in pleural space; dullness would suggest effusion; this single finding rules out pleural effusion as the cause<br />
过清音=胸膜腔积气；浊音提示积液；此体征可直接排除胸腔积液</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Oxygen saturation 92% on room air<br />
室内空气下血氧饱和度92%</td>
<td>SpO2 &lt;95% indicates clinically significant hypoxia, classifying this as a large pneumothorax requiring intervention beyond observation<br />
SpO2&lt;95%提示临床显著低氧，将本例定性为大型气胸，需积极干预而非单纯观察</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>2.5-kg weight loss + decreased appetite over 6 weeks<br />
6周内体重减轻2.5kg+食欲减退</td>
<td>Constitutional symptoms flag secondary spontaneous pneumothorax; must consider underlying malignancy, TB, or Langerhans cell histiocytosis as inciting cause<br />
全身症状提示继发性自发性气胸；需考虑恶性肿瘤、结核或肺朗格汉斯细胞组织细胞增生症作为潜在病因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Tachycardia 100/min + tachypnea 26/min, BP 100/72<br />
心动过速100次/分+呼吸急促26次/分，血压100/72</td>
<td>Compensatory response to hypoxia and reduced lung volume; blood pressure is low-normal but not frankly hypotensive, ruling out tension pneumothorax<br />
对低氧和肺容量减少的代偿反应；血压偏低但未达休克水平，可排除张力性气胸</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Pneumothorax** occurs when air enters the **intrapleural space**, disrupting the negative pressure that keeps the lung expanded against the chest wall:

气胸发生于空气进入**胸膜腔**，破坏维持肺贴壁膨胀的负压状态：

- Bleb or bullae ruptures → air floods intrapleural space → lung parenchyma collapses away from chest wall\
  肺大疱破裂→空气涌入胸膜腔→肺实质从胸壁塌陷收缩

- Collapsed lung → severe V/Q mismatch → hypoxia → compensatory tachycardia and tachypnea\
  肺萎陷→严重通气/血流比例失调→低氧→代偿性心动过速和呼吸急促

- In large pneumothorax: air volume too great for spontaneous reabsorption → must be mechanically drained\
  大型气胸中：积气量过大无法自行吸收→必须机械引流排出

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Pneumothorax = hyperresonance (air rises); pleural effusion = dullness (fluid sinks). Both cause absent breath sounds — percussion note is the tiebreaker.

**解剖小窍门:** 气胸=过清音（气体上浮）；胸腔积液=浊音（液体下沉）。两者均致呼吸音消失——叩诊音是关键鉴别点。

---

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Tube Thoracostomy / 正确答案 (E) — 胸腔闭式引流

**Tube thoracostomy (chest tube)** is the definitive treatment for large pneumothorax — it provides continuous evacuation of pleural air and allows the lung to re-expand:

**胸腔闭式引流（胸管）** 是大型气胸的确定性治疗——持续排出胸膜腔积气，促进肺复张：

- Chest tube is placed in the 4th–5th intercostal space at the anterior midaxillary line\
  胸管置于第4–5肋间隙腋中线前方

- Continuous drainage removes air faster than passive reabsorption can occur, allowing lung re-expansion\
  持续引流排气速度远快于被动吸收，使肺得以复张

- Indicated when SpO2 is low, pneumothorax is large (≥2 cm on CXR), or patient is hemodynamically stressed\
  当SpO2低、气胸较大（胸片≥2cm）或患者存在血流动力学应激时均需置管

**Diagnosis:** Large right-sided spontaneous pneumothorax; unilateral hyperresonance, absent breath sounds, SpO2 92%, and confirmatory CXR make the diagnosis unambiguous.

**诊断:** 大型右侧自发性气胸；单侧过清音、呼吸音消失、SpO2 92%及胸片证实，诊断无歧义。

**Treatment:** Immediate tube thoracostomy; after placement monitor for persistent air leak; investigate underlying cause given 6-week constitutional symptoms.

**治疗:** 立即行胸腔闭式引流；置管后监测是否持续漏气；鉴于6周全身症状，需进一步排查潜在病因。

---

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Endotracheal intubation<br />
A — 气管插管</td>
<td>Positive pressure ventilation worsens pneumothorax and can precipitate tension pneumothorax; reserved for apneic, hypercapnic, or airway-unprotected patients unresponsive to other measures<br />
正压通气加重气胸，可诱发张力性气胸；仅用于呼吸暂停、CO2潴留或无法保护气道且其他措施无效者</td>
<td>Patient breathes spontaneously; chest tube must be placed before intubation if pneumothorax is known<br />
患者仍有自主呼吸；已知气胸时必须先置胸管再插管</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Nebulized albuterol<br />
B — 雾化沙丁胺醇</td>
<td>Albuterol treats bronchospasm (asthma/COPD); those conditions cause diffuse bilateral expiratory wheezes, not unilateral absent breath sounds<br />
沙丁胺醇用于支气管痉挛（哮喘/COPD）；该类疾病表现为弥漫性双侧呼气性哮鸣音，而非单侧呼吸音消失</td>
<td>Unilateral findings exclude asthma exacerbation regardless of prior asthma history<br />
单侧体征排除哮喘发作，无论既往哮喘病史如何</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Observation and nasal oxygen<br />
C — 观察并鼻导管吸氧</td>
<td>Appropriate only for small (&lt;2 cm), asymptomatic pneumothorax; this patient's hypoxia, tachycardia, and tachypnea indicate a large pneumothorax that will not self-resolve; nasal cannula is also inferior to nonrebreather mask<br />
仅适用于小型（&lt;2cm）无症状气胸；本例低氧、心动过速、呼吸急促提示大型气胸，不能自行消退；鼻导管氧疗效果也不及非重复呼吸面罩</td>
<td>SpO2 92% + tachycardia = large pneumothorax = drainage required, not watchful waiting<br />
SpO2 92%+心动过速=大型气胸=需引流，而非等待观察</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Thoracotomy<br />
D — 开胸手术</td>
<td>Thoracotomy addresses hemorrhagic emergencies (hemothorax, cardiac tamponade, aortic injury) or penetrating trauma with cardiac arrest; this patient is hemodynamically stable with no hemorrhage<br />
开胸术用于出血性急症（血胸、心脏压塞、主动脉损伤）或穿透伤致心脏骤停；本患者血流动力学稳定且无出血</td>
<td>No penetrating trauma, no hemorrhage, hemodynamically stable → far too invasive<br />
无穿透伤、无出血、血流动力学稳定→创伤过大，明显不当</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Tube thoracostomy ✓<br />
E — 胸腔闭式引流 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Large pneumothorax with hypoxia and hemodynamic stress requires immediate chest tube to evacuate pleural air and allow lung re-expansion<br />
正确——大型气胸伴低氧血症及血流动力学应激，需立即置胸管排出胸膜腔积气并促进肺复张</td>
<td>Unilateral hyperresonance + absent breath sounds + SpO2 92% = large pneumothorax = tube thoracostomy<br />
单侧过清音+呼吸音消失+SpO2 92% = 大型气胸 = 胸腔闭式引流</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most seductive distractor is (C) — observation with oxygen — which is genuinely correct for small pneumothorax; the pivot is recognizing that SpO2 92%, tachycardia, and tachypnea collectively signal a large pneumothorax beyond the threshold for watchful waiting.*

最容易误选的干扰项是(C)——观察+吸氧——对于小型气胸确实正确；关键转折点在于认识到SpO2 92%、心动过速和呼吸急促共同提示大型气胸，已超出等待观察的阈值。

---

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Primary vs. Secondary Spontaneous vs. Tension Pneumothorax / 原发性 vs. 继发性自发性 vs. 张力性气胸对比

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Primary Spontaneous</strong><br />
<strong>原发性自发性气胸</strong></th>
<th><strong>Secondary Spontaneous</strong><br />
<strong>继发性自发性气胸</strong></th>
<th><strong>Tension Pneumothorax</strong><br />
<strong>张力性气胸</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Typical patient<br />
典型患者</td>
<td>Tall, thin young male; no underlying lung disease<br />
高瘦年轻男性；无基础肺病</td>
<td>Known lung disease (COPD, asthma, TB, malignancy, HIV-PCP)<br />
已知肺部疾病（COPD、哮喘、结核、恶性肿瘤、HIV-PCP）</td>
<td>Any pneumothorax with one-way valve air leak; often iatrogenic or trauma<br />
任何气胸发生单向瓣膜漏气；常见于医源性或外伤</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pathophysiology<br />
病理生理</td>
<td>Rupture of subpleural bleb<br />
胸膜下肺大疱破裂</td>
<td>Rupture of diseased parenchyma, bronchus, or bronchopleural fistula<br />
病变肺实质、支气管破裂或支气管胸膜瘘</td>
<td>Air enters but cannot exit → progressive pressure buildup → mediastinal shift<br />
气体只进不出→压力持续升高→纵隔移位</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hemodynamics<br />
血流动力学</td>
<td>Stable<br />
稳定</td>
<td>May be compromised (less respiratory reserve)<br />
可能受损（呼吸储备差）</td>
<td>Obstructive shock: hypotension, tachycardia, JVD, tracheal deviation<br />
梗阻性休克：低血压、心动过速、颈静脉怒张、气管偏移</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Percussion<br />
叩诊</td>
<td>Hyperresonance affected side<br />
患侧过清音</td>
<td>Hyperresonance affected side<br />
患侧过清音</td>
<td>Hyperresonance affected side<br />
患侧过清音</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment<br />
治疗</td>
<td>Small: O2 + observation; Large: tube thoracostomy<br />
小型：吸氧+观察；大型：胸腔闭式引流</td>
<td>Lower threshold for tube thoracostomy due to reduced pulmonary reserve<br />
因肺储备减少，胸腔闭式引流阈值更低</td>
<td>Immediate needle decompression (2nd ICS MCL) → then chest tube<br />
立即锁骨中线第2肋间针刺减压→再置胸管</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Do NOT do first<br />
切勿首先进行</td>
<td>Intubation without chest tube<br />
未置胸管即插管</td>
<td>Intubation without chest tube<br />
未置胸管即插管</td>
<td>CXR before treatment — treat clinically<br />
治疗前等待胸片——应凭临床诊断立即处理</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A large pneumothorax with unilateral hyperresonance, absent breath sounds, and hypoxia mandates immediate tube thoracostomy — not albuterol (wrong diagnosis), not observation (too large), not intubation first (worsens pneumothorax).**

**大型气胸表现为单侧过清音、呼吸音消失及低氧血症，必须立即行胸腔闭式引流——不用沙丁胺醇（诊断错误）、不能单纯观察（气胸太大）、不能先插管（加重气胸）。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — DHART for Pneumothorax Recognition / 记忆钩 — 气胸识别 "DHART" 口诀:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>D</strong>iminished breath sounds (unilateral) — absent air movement over the collapsed lung / 呼吸音减低（单侧）——患侧萎陷肺无气流声<br />
• <strong>H</strong>yperresonance on percussion — air in pleural space, not fluid (fluid = dull) / 叩诊过清音——胸膜腔积气而非积液（积液=浊音）<br />
• <strong>A</strong>bsent lung markings on CXR — radiolucent pleural space with visible lung edge confirms diagnosis / 胸片肺纹理消失——胸膜腔透亮伴可见肺边缘确认诊断<br />
• <strong>R</strong>espiratory distress + hypoxia → large pneumothorax → chest tube immediately / 呼吸窘迫+低氧→大型气胸→立即置胸管<br />
• <strong>T</strong>ension signs (JVD + hypotension + tracheal shift) → needle first at 2nd ICS, then tube / 张力征（颈静脉怒张+低血压+气管偏移）→先于第2肋间针刺减压，再置胸管</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Pneumothorax: Diagnosis and Management / 高频知识表 — 气胸：诊断与处理

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Size classification and treatment threshold<br />
大小分类与治疗阈值</td>
<td>Small: &lt;2 cm apex-to-cupola or &lt;20% collapse → observation + high-flow O2; Large: ≥2 cm or ≥20%, or any size with hypoxia/symptoms → tube thoracostomy<br />
小型：肺尖到胸顶&lt;2cm或萎陷&lt;20%→观察+高流量吸氧；大型：≥2cm或≥20%，或任何程度伴低氧/症状→胸腔闭式引流</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Why 100% O2 (not nasal cannula)<br />
为何用100%纯氧（而非鼻导管）</td>
<td>High-flow O2 via nonrebreather mask flushes nitrogen from blood, creating a pressure gradient that pulls pleural nitrogen into bloodstream; reabsorption rate increases ~4-fold<br />
通过非重复呼吸面罩给予高流量纯氧可冲洗血液中的氮气，形成压力梯度使胸膜腔氮气被吸入血流；吸收速率提高约4倍</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Tension pneumothorax — do not wait for CXR<br />
张力性气胸——不等胸片</td>
<td>Clinical diagnosis: hypotension + tracheal deviation away from lesion + JVD + absent breath sounds + hyperresonance; treat immediately with needle at 2nd ICS midclavicular line<br />
临床诊断：低血压+气管向健侧偏移+颈静脉怒张+呼吸音消失+过清音；立即于锁骨中线第2肋间针刺</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pneumothorax before intubation rule<br />
插管前气胸处理原则</td>
<td>Known pneumothorax → place chest tube BEFORE initiating positive pressure ventilation; positive pressure converts simple to tension pneumothorax<br />
已知气胸→启动正压通气前必须先置胸管；正压通气可将简单气胸转为张力性气胸</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Secondary spontaneous pneumothorax causes<br />
继发性自发性气胸常见病因</td>
<td>COPD (most common), asthma, cystic fibrosis, TB, Pneumocystis jirovecii pneumonia (HIV), Langerhans cell histiocytosis (young smoker + constitutional symptoms), malignancy, Marfan syndrome<br />
COPD（最常见）、哮喘、囊性纤维化、结核、耶氏肺孢子菌肺炎（HIV）、肺朗格汉斯细胞组织细胞增生症（年轻吸烟者+全身症状）、恶性肿瘤、马凡综合征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Recurrence and surgical management<br />
复发与手术处理</td>
<td>First episode: ~30% recurrence within 2 years; second episode: ~50–80% recurrence; VATS with mechanical pleurodesis or pleurectomy recommended after second episode or persistent air leak<br />
首次发作：2年内复发率约30%；第二次发作：复发率约50–80%；第二次发作或持续漏气后推荐VATS联合机械胸膜固定术或胸膜切除术</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Chest tube placement anatomy<br />
胸管置入解剖位置</td>
<td>"Safe triangle": lateral border of pectoralis major, anterior axillary line, horizontal line of 5th ICS; insert above upper rib border to avoid neurovascular bundle<br />
"安全三角"：胸大肌外侧缘、腋前线、第5肋间水平线；于上位肋骨上缘插入以避开神经血管束</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of unilateral absent breath sounds:** pneumothorax (hyperresonant percussion), large pleural effusion (dull percussion), main-stem bronchus intubation (normal percussion, other lung inflating), massive atelectasis (dull + tracheal deviation toward affected side)\
  **单侧呼吸音消失的鉴别诊断:** 气胸（叩诊过清音）、大量胸腔积液（叩诊浊音）、主支气管插管（叩诊正常，对侧肺充气）、大片肺不张（浊音+气管向患侧偏移）

- **Constitutional symptoms clue:** The 6-week weight loss and decreased appetite in this question signal secondary spontaneous pneumothorax; USMLE may pair this scenario with Langerhans cell histiocytosis (young male smoker, bilateral cysts/nodules on CT, diabetes insipidus) or primary lung malignancy\
  **全身症状线索:** 本题6周体重减轻和食欲减退提示继发性自发性气胸；USMLE可能将此场景与肺朗格汉斯细胞组织细胞增生症（年轻男性吸烟者、CT双侧囊肿/结节、尿崩症）或原发性肺恶性肿瘤配对考查

- **Persistent air leak management:** If air bubbling continues in water-seal chamber \>5–7 days, suspect bronchopleural fistula; source investigation includes bronchoscopy; surgical repair or VATS may be required to prevent chronic pneumothorax\
  **持续漏气的处理:** 若水封瓶持续冒泡\>5–7天，怀疑支气管胸膜瘘；可行支气管镜检查定位；可能需手术修补或VATS以防止慢性气胸

- **Intubation sequence when pneumothorax coexists:** If the patient deteriorates and intubation becomes necessary despite pneumothorax, the sequence is: tube thoracostomy first → then rapid sequence intubation → confirm bilateral breath sounds post-intubation\
  **气胸合并插管时的操作顺序:** 若患者病情恶化需在气胸同时插管，顺序为：先行胸腔闭式引流→再快速序贯插管→插管后确认双侧呼吸音

# Question 4 — Immune Thrombocytopenic Purpura / 免疫性血小板减少性紫癜

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>15-year-old girl</strong> is brought to the emergency department by her mother because of a <strong>2-week history of heavy vaginal bleeding</strong>. Menarche was at the age of 14 years. Menses occur at irregular 21- to 35-day intervals and last 10 days with moderate flow. She has <strong>never been sexually active</strong>. She is not in distress. She is at the 55th percentile for height, 70th percentile for weight, and 60th percentile for BMI. Her temperature is <strong>38°C (100.4°F)</strong>, and blood pressure is <strong>90/55 mm Hg</strong>. Examination shows <strong>pallor</strong>. Laboratory studies show a hemoglobin concentration of <strong>9 g/dL</strong>, leukocyte count of 5500/mm³, and platelet count of <strong>15,000/mm³</strong>. Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Cervical ectropion<br />
B) Endometrial polyp<br />
C) Immune thrombocytopenic purpura<br />
D) Submucous myoma<br />
E) Thrombotic thrombocytopenic purpura</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: C</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>15-year-old girl, 2-week heavy vaginal bleeding<br />
15岁女孩，2周大量阴道出血</td>
<td>Menorrhagia in adolescents must trigger bleeding disorder workup, not only gynecologic evaluation<br />
青少年月经过多必须启动出血性疾病筛查，不能只进行妇科评估</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Platelet count 15,000/mm³<br />
血小板计数 15,000/mm³</td>
<td>Critically low; isolated severe thrombocytopenia is the single most important finding that points to ITP<br />
危急性降低；孤立性严重血小板减少是指向ITP最重要的单一发现</td>

<tr>
<td>Hemoglobin 9 g/dL + pallor<br />
血红蛋白9 g/dL + 苍白</td>

继发于血小板减少性黏膜出血的慢性失血导致中度贫血</td>
</tr>
<tr>

大量出血导致血流动力学失代偿；提示需要紧急处理的临床严重程度</td>

白细胞计数正常 5500/mm³</td>

排除血液系统恶性肿瘤（白血病使白细胞升高或降低）；确认孤立性血小板减少</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Temperature 38°C<br />
体温 38°C</td>
<td>Suggests preceding infection (EBV, H. pylori, HIV), which frequently triggers autoimmune ITP<br />
提示前驱感染（EBV、幽门螺杆菌、HIV），这些感染常诱发自身免疫性ITP</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Never sexually active<br />
从未有性生活</td>
<td>Excludes STI-related cervicitis (chlamydia, gonorrhea) as a cause of vaginal bleeding<br />
排除性传播感染相关宫颈炎（衣原体、淋球菌）作为阴道出血原因</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**ITP** is driven by **antiplatelet IgG antibodies** (targeting GPIIb/IIIa on platelet surface) that opsonize circulating platelets, leading to their destruction by **Fc receptor-bearing splenic macrophages**:

**ITP** 由 **抗血小板IgG抗体**（靶向血小板表面GPIIb/IIIa）驱动，这些抗体调理化循环血小板，导致其被 **携带Fc受体的脾脏巨噬细胞** 吞噬破坏：

- Autoimmune formation of IgG antibodies against platelet surface glycoproteins (trigger: preceding infection, idiopathic)\
  针对血小板表面糖蛋白的IgG自身抗体形成（触发因素：前驱感染、特发性）

- Antibody-coated platelets recognized via Fc receptors on splenic macrophages → phagocytosis and destruction\
  被抗体包被的血小板通过脾脏巨噬细胞Fc受体识别 → 吞噬和破坏

- Bone marrow compensates by upregulating megakaryocytes → platelet production increases, but peripheral destruction outpaces it\
  骨髓通过上调巨核细胞代偿 → 血小板生成增多，但外周破坏速度超过生成

- Result: isolated thrombocytopenia with normal coagulation (PT/PTT intact), normal platelet morphology on smear, prolonged bleeding time\
  结果：孤立性血小板减少，凝血功能正常（PT/PTT正常），血涂片血小板形态正常，出血时间延长

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The spleen is the primary site of both antiplatelet IgG antibody production AND platelet phagocytosis — which is why splenectomy achieves remission in 60–70% of refractory ITP cases.

**解剖小窍门:** 脾脏既是抗血小板IgG抗体产生的主要场所，也是血小板吞噬的主要场所——这就是为什么脾切除术在60–70%的难治性ITP病例中能获得缓解。

## 3. Correct Answer (C) — Immune Thrombocytopenic Purpura / 正确答案 (C) — 免疫性血小板减少性紫癜

**Immune Thrombocytopenic Purpura (ITP)** is an acquired autoimmune disorder defined by isolated immune-mediated platelet destruction causing thrombocytopenia and mucosal bleeding:

**免疫性血小板减少性紫癜 (ITP)** 是一种获得性自身免疫性疾病，以孤立性免疫介导的血小板破坏为特征，导致血小板减少和黏膜出血：

- Platelet count \< 100,000/mm³ (symptomatic bleeding typically when \< 30,000); this patient's 15,000 directly explains severe menorrhagia and hemodynamic instability\
  血小板计数 \< 100,000/mm³（有症状出血通常在 \< 30,000时）；本患者15,000直接解释严重月经过多和血流动力学不稳定

- Mucosal bleeding predominates: menorrhagia, epistaxis, gingival bleeding, petechiae, purpura on skin\
  黏膜出血为主：月经过多、鼻出血、牙龈出血、皮肤瘀点和紫癜

- Key lab pattern: thrombocytopenia + normal WBC + normal PT/PTT + prolonged bleeding time + normal platelet morphology on peripheral smear\
  关键实验室模式：血小板减少 + 白细胞正常 + PT/PTT正常 + 出血时间延长 + 外周血涂片血小板形态正常

- Preceding infection (EBV, H. pylori, HIV) is a common trigger; low-grade fever (38°C) in this case supports a post-infectious etiology\
  前驱感染（EBV、幽门螺杆菌、HIV）是常见诱因；本例低热（38°C）支持感染后病因

**Diagnosis:** Diagnosis of exclusion — rule out viral infection, hematologic malignancy, and drug-induced thrombocytopenia. Bone marrow biopsy shows increased megakaryocytes confirming adequate production with excess peripheral destruction.

**诊断:** 排除性诊断——排除病毒感染、血液系统恶性肿瘤及药物性血小板减少。骨髓活检显示巨核细胞增多，确认生成充足但外周破坏过多。

**Treatment:** Acute: IVIG ± corticosteroids (prednisone) for rapid platelet rise. Chronic first-line: corticosteroids. Refractory: rituximab, TPO-receptor agonists (eltrombopag, romiplostim), or splenectomy.

**治疗:** 急性期：IVIG ± 糖皮质激素（泼尼松）以快速升高血小板。慢性一线：糖皮质激素。难治性：利妥昔单抗、TPO受体激动剂（艾曲泊帕、罗米司亭）或脾切除术。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Cervical ectropion<br />
A — 宫颈外翻</td>
<td>Causes contact spotting/bleeding but never causes thrombocytopenia; platelet 15,000 is completely unexplained<br />
可引起接触性点滴出血，但绝不引起血小板减少；血小板15,000完全无法解释</td>
<td>Cervical ectropion: local structural finding, CBC normal; ITP: systemic immune-mediated platelet destruction<br />
宫颈外翻：局部结构性病变，全血细胞计数正常；ITP：全身性免疫介导的血小板破坏</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Endometrial polyp<br />
B — 子宫内膜息肉</td>
<td>Causes unpredictable uterine bleeding but does not cause thrombocytopenia or any hematologic abnormality<br />
引起不规则子宫出血，但不引起血小板减少或任何血液学异常</td>
<td>Endometrial polyp: structural cause, normal CBC; ITP: CBC shows isolated thrombocytopenia<br />
子宫内膜息肉：结构性原因，全血细胞计数正常；ITP：全血细胞计数显示孤立性血小板减少</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Immune thrombocytopenic purpura ✓<br />
C — 免疫性血小板减少性紫癜 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Platelet 15,000 + menorrhagia + normal WBC + low-grade fever post-infection = textbook ITP in an adolescent female<br />
正确——血小板15,000 + 月经过多 + 白细胞正常 + 感染后低热 = 青少年女性教科书式ITP</td>
<td>Classic presentation: isolated severe thrombocytopenia causing mucosal bleeding with preserved WBC and coagulation<br />
经典表现：孤立性严重血小板减少导致黏膜出血，白细胞和凝血功能保留</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Submucous myoma<br />
D — 黏膜下肌瘤</td>
<td>Causes abnormal uterine bleeding and pelvic pain but does not cause thrombocytopenia; also extremely rare in 15-year-olds<br />
引起异常子宫出血和盆腔疼痛，但不引起血小板减少；且在15岁患者中极为罕见</td>
<td>Myoma: structural bleeding with normal CBC; ITP: immune-mediated systemic platelet loss<br />
肌瘤：结构性出血，全血细胞计数正常；ITP：免疫介导的全身性血小板丢失</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Thrombotic thrombocytopenic purpura<br />
E — 血栓性血小板减少性紫癜</td>
<td>TTP requires the clinical pentad: thrombocytopenia + MAHA + renal dysfunction + neurologic abnormalities + fever; this patient has only thrombocytopenia and low-grade fever — MAHA, renal failure, and neuro signs are all absent<br />
TTP需要临床五联征：血小板减少+MAHA+肾功能障碍+神经系统异常+发热；本患者仅有血小板减少和低热——MAHA、肾衰竭和神经系统体征均缺失</td>
<td>TTP: schistocytes on smear + elevated creatinine + neurologic findings; ITP: normal smear, normal renal function, no neuro signs<br />
TTP：血涂片裂片红细胞 + 肌酐升高 + 神经系统表现；ITP：血涂片正常、肾功能正常、无神经系统体征</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most seductive distractor is E (TTP) because it also causes thrombocytopenia and fever — the critical distinction is that TTP requires microangiopathic hemolytic anemia (schistocytes) and renal/neurologic involvement, none of which are present in this case.*

最具迷惑性的干扰项是E（TTP），因为它同样引起血小板减少和发热——关键区别在于TTP需要微血管病性溶血性贫血（裂片红细胞）及肾脏/神经系统受累，而本例均无。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — ITP vs. TTP / ITP与TTP鉴别诊断

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>ITP (Immune Thrombocytopenic Purpura)</strong><br />
<strong>ITP（免疫性血小板减少性紫癜）</strong></th>
<th><strong>TTP (Thrombotic Thrombocytopenic Purpura)</strong><br />
<strong>TTP（血栓性血小板减少性紫癜）</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Mechanism<br />
机制</td>
<td>Antiplatelet IgG → splenic phagocytosis of platelets<br />
抗血小板IgG → 脾脏吞噬血小板</td>
<td>ADAMTS13 deficiency → vWF multimers → platelet microthrombi<br />
ADAMTS13缺乏 → vWF多聚体 → 血小板微血栓</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Anemia type<br />
贫血类型</td>
<td>Normocytic from blood loss (if any)<br />
失血所致正细胞性贫血（若有）</td>
<td>Microangiopathic hemolytic anemia (MAHA)<br />
微血管病性溶血性贫血（MAHA）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Peripheral smear<br />
外周血涂片</td>
<td>Normal platelet morphology, no RBC fragments<br />
血小板形态正常，无红细胞碎片</td>
<td>Schistocytes (fragmented RBCs) — hallmark finding<br />
裂片红细胞（破碎红细胞）——标志性表现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Renal involvement<br />
肾脏受累</td>
<td>Absent<br />
无</td>
<td>Common — elevated creatinine, hematuria<br />
常见——肌酐升高、血尿</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Neurologic symptoms<br />
神经系统症状</td>
<td>Absent<br />
无</td>
<td>Common — confusion, seizures, focal deficits<br />
常见——意识混乱、癫痫、局灶性神经功能缺损</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Coagulation (PT/PTT)<br />
凝血（PT/PTT）</td>
<td>Normal (coagulation cascade intact)<br />
正常（凝血级联完整）</td>
<td>Normal (platelet microthrombi, not coagulation factor consumption)<br />
正常（血小板微血栓，非凝血因子消耗）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment<br />
治疗</td>
<td>IVIG, steroids, splenectomy (refractory)<br />
IVIG、激素、脾切除术（难治性）</td>
<td>Plasma exchange (plasmapheresis) — urgent<br />
血浆置换（血浆分离置换）——紧急</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**An adolescent girl presenting with isolated severe thrombocytopenia (platelets 15,000/mm³) causing menorrhagia and hemodynamic instability most likely has ITP, an autoimmune disorder in which antiplatelet IgG antibodies drive splenic destruction of platelets.**

**出现孤立性严重血小板减少（血小板15,000/mm³）导致月经过多和血流动力学不稳定的青少年女孩最可能患有ITP——一种抗血小板IgG抗体驱动脾脏破坏血小板的自身免疫性疾病。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — ITP "SPASM" Features / 记忆钩 — ITP "SPASM" 五要素:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>S</strong>pleen — both makes antibodies AND destroys platelets (splenectomy cures refractory ITP) / 脾脏——既产生抗体又破坏血小板（脾切除治疗难治性ITP）<br />
• <strong>P</strong>latelets isolated low — WBC and coagulation (PT/PTT) are normal / 血小板孤立性降低——白细胞和凝血（PT/PTT）均正常<br />
• <strong>A</strong>ntiplatelet IgG (anti-GPIIb/IIIa) — the autoimmune mechanism / 抗血小板IgG（抗GPIIb/IIIa）——自身免疫机制<br />
• <strong>S</strong>mear normal — no schistocytes (distinguishes from TTP); megakaryocytes increased in marrow / 血涂片正常——无裂片红细胞（区别于TTP）；骨髓巨核细胞增多<br />
• <strong>M</strong>ucosal bleeding — menorrhagia, epistaxis, petechiae, purpura; triggered by prior infection / 黏膜出血——月经过多、鼻出血、瘀点、紫癜；由前驱感染触发</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Immune Thrombocytopenic Purpura / 高频知识表 — 免疫性血小板减少性紫癜

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>ITP pathophysiology<br />
ITP病理生理</td>
<td>Antiplatelet IgG (vs. GPIIb/IIIa) → Fc receptor-mediated splenic macrophage phagocytosis → thrombocytopenia; bone marrow shows compensatory megakaryocyte hyperplasia<br />
抗血小板IgG（对抗GPIIb/IIIa）→ Fc受体介导的脾脏巨噬细胞吞噬 → 血小板减少；骨髓显示代偿性巨核细胞增生</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Diagnostic approach<br />
诊断方法</td>
<td>Diagnosis of exclusion: isolated thrombocytopenia with normal WBC, normal PT/PTT, normal platelet morphology, prolonged bleeding time; bone marrow biopsy if uncertain<br />
排除性诊断：孤立性血小板减少，白细胞正常、PT/PTT正常、血小板形态正常、出血时间延长；不确定时行骨髓活检</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Common infectious triggers<br />
常见感染性诱因</td>
<td>EBV (most common viral trigger), H. pylori (treat eradication → platelet recovery), HIV; in children often follows URI → acute self-limited course<br />
EBV（最常见病毒性诱因）、幽门螺杆菌（根除治疗→血小板恢复）、HIV；儿童常在上呼吸道感染后发病→急性自限性病程</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ITP treatment ladder<br />
ITP治疗阶梯</td>
<td>Acute: IVIG ± corticosteroids (fastest platelet rise); Chronic first-line: prednisone; Refractory: rituximab (anti-CD20), TPO-receptor agonists (eltrombopag/romiplostim), splenectomy<br />
急性期：IVIG ± 糖皮质激素（血小板上升最快）；慢性一线：泼尼松；难治性：利妥昔单抗（抗CD20）、TPO受体激动剂（艾曲泊帕/罗米司亭）、脾切除术</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Splenectomy rationale and outcomes<br />
脾切除术原理与结果</td>
<td>Spleen is dual culprit: site of antiplatelet antibody production AND platelet destruction; removal eliminates both; 60–70% achieve durable remission<br />
脾脏是双重元凶：抗血小板抗体产生场所和血小板破坏场所；切除后消除两者；60–70%获得持久缓解</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ITP in adolescent females<br />
青少年女性ITP特点</td>
<td>Menorrhagia is presenting complaint in up to 30% of adolescent females with ITP; CBC mandatory before attributing heavy periods to hormonal variation or structural cause<br />
多达30%的ITP青少年女性以月经过多为首发主诉；在将月经过多归因于激素变化或结构原因前，必须检查全血细胞计数</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Bleeding time vs. coagulation studies<br />
出血时间与凝血检查</td>
<td>Bleeding time prolonged (platelet plug formation impaired); PT/PTT normal (coagulation cascade intact); distinguishes ITP from hemophilia (prolonged PTT) and DIC (prolonged PT/PTT + low fibrinogen)<br />
出血时间延长（血小板栓子形成受损）；PT/PTT正常（凝血级联完整）；将ITP与血友病（PTT延长）及DIC（PT/PTT延长+纤维蛋白原降低）区分</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Most feared complication<br />
最可怕的并发症</td>
<td>Intracranial hemorrhage when platelets &lt; 10,000/mm³ (platelet 15,000 in this case is in the danger zone requiring urgent platelet-raising therapy)<br />
血小板 &lt; 10,000/mm³时发生颅内出血（本例血小板15,000处于危险区，需紧急升血小板治疗）</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of adolescent menorrhagia:** Von Willebrand disease (most common inherited bleeding disorder causing menorrhagia — check VWF antigen, activity, and ristocetin cofactor); also ITP, hemophilia carrier, hypothyroidism, PCOS, structural causes\
  **青少年月经过多鉴别:** 血管性血友病（最常见遗传性出血性疾病导致月经过多——检查VWF抗原、活性和瑞斯托菌素辅因子）；也需考虑ITP、血友病携带者、甲状腺功能减退、PCOS、结构性原因

- **ITP vs. aplastic anemia:** Aplastic anemia causes pancytopenia (low WBC + low RBC + low platelets) with hypocellular bone marrow; ITP causes isolated thrombocytopenia with hypercellular marrow (increased megakaryocytes) — key distinction\
  **ITP与再生障碍性贫血对比:** 再生障碍性贫血引起全血细胞减少（白细胞低+红细胞低+血小板低），骨髓低细胞性；ITP引起孤立性血小板减少，骨髓高细胞性（巨核细胞增多）——关键区别

- **Variant — drug-induced immune thrombocytopenia:** Heparin-induced thrombocytopenia (HIT) involves IgG against PF4-heparin complex and paradoxically causes thrombosis; quinine, vancomycin, sulfonamides also implicated\
  **题目变式——药物性免疫性血小板减少:** 肝素诱导的血小板减少症（HIT）涉及针对PF4-肝素复合物的IgG，矛盾地引起血栓；奎宁、万古霉素、磺胺类药物也有关联

- **Key exam pearl — TTP vs. ITP on USMLE:** If the stem mentions "confusion," "seizures," "elevated creatinine," or "schistocytes" alongside thrombocytopenia → think TTP (treat with plasma exchange, NOT steroids alone). If isolated thrombocytopenia with normal smear → ITP\
  **考试关键要点——USMLE中TTP与ITP:** 若题干在血小板减少基础上提及"意识混乱"、"癫痫"、"肌酐升高"或"裂片红细胞" → 考虑TTP（血浆置换治疗，非单用激素）。若孤立性血小板减少伴血涂片正常 → ITP

# Question 5 — Pancreatic Head Adenocarcinoma with Superior Mesenteric Artery Encasement / 胰头腺癌伴肠系膜上动脉包裹

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>49-year-old man</strong> comes to the office because of a <strong>2-week history of dark urine</strong>. He has had a <strong>5-kg (11-lb) weight loss</strong> during the past month despite no change in appetite. He has no history of serious illness and takes no medications. His temperature is 37.5°C (99.5°F), pulse is 80/min, respirations are 12/min, and blood pressure is 132/86 mm Hg. Examination shows <strong>conjunctival icterus</strong>. A <strong>5-cm, nontender mass</strong> is palpated in the right upper quadrant of the abdomen. Serum studies show a <strong>total bilirubin concentration of 6 mg/dL, with a direct component of 5.2 mg/dL</strong>, and a lactate dehydrogenase activity of 480 U/L. Abdominal ultrasonography shows an <strong>enlarged gallbladder with no calculi</strong>, a <strong>2-cm-wide common bile duct with no calculi that tapers at the distal end</strong>, and a <strong>5-cm mass in the head of the pancreas</strong>. A CT scan of the abdomen shows a 5-cm mass in the head of the pancreas <strong>compressing the superior mesenteric vein and partially encasing the superior mesenteric artery</strong>. Results of a fine-needle biopsy show hyperchromatic, pleomorphic cells with a high nucleus-to-cytoplasm ratio. Further diagnostic studies show no evidence of metastatic disease. Which of the following factors is most predictive of a poor prognosis in this patient?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following factors is most predictive of a poor prognosis in this patient?</strong></p>
<p>A) Bilirubin concentration<br />
B) Patient's age<br />
C) Patient's sex assigned at birth<br />
D) Tumor encasement of the superior mesenteric vessels<br />
E) Tumor location in the head of the pancreas rather than the tail</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: D</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Dark urine + conjunctival icterus<br />
深色尿 + 结膜黄染</td>
<td>Bilirubinuria from conjugated hyperbilirubinemia → obstructive (cholestatic) jaundice<br />
结合型高胆红素血症导致胆红素尿 → 梗阻性（胆汁淤积性）黄疸</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>5-kg weight loss despite no appetite change<br />
体重下降 5 kg 但食欲无变化</td>
<td>Classic cancer cachexia — distinguishes malignancy from benign biliary disease<br />
典型肿瘤恶病质——有助于鉴别恶性与良性胆道疾病</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>5-cm nontender RUQ mass (palpable gallbladder)<br />
右上腹 5 cm 无痛性肿块（可触及胆囊）</td>
<td>Courvoisier's sign — gallbladder distended from distal biliary obstruction, NOT gallstones<br />
Courvoisier 征——远端胆道梗阻导致胆囊扩张，而非结石所致</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Direct bilirubin 5.2 / total 6 mg/dL<br />
直接胆红素 5.2 / 总胆红素 6 mg/dL</td>
<td>Direct &gt; 50% of total → conjugated (obstructive) hyperbilirubinemia, not hemolysis<br />
直接胆红素 &gt; 总量 50% → 结合型（梗阻性）高胆红素血症，排除溶血</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>CBD 2 cm, no calculi, tapers at distal end<br />
胆总管 2 cm，无结石，远端逐渐变细</td>
<td>Extrinsic compression at pancreatic head level — rules out choledocholithiasis<br />
胰头水平外压性梗阻——排除胆总管结石</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>SMA partially encased on CT<br />
CT 示肠系膜上动脉部分受包裹</td>
<td>Arterial encasement = contraindication to Whipple resection — curative option eliminated<br />
动脉包裹 = Whipple 手术禁忌——根治性切除被排除</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No metastatic disease<br />
无远处转移证据</td>
<td>Distant mets would also preclude resection; their absence makes local vascular encasement the decisive factor here<br />
远处转移同样是手术禁忌；无转移使局部血管包裹成为本例的决定性因素</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Pancreatic ductal adenocarcinoma** of the pancreatic head creates two simultaneous problems: **biliary obstruction** causing jaundice and **vascular encasement** that determines resectability:

**胰头部胰腺导管腺癌**同时造成两个问题：引起黄疸的**胆道梗阻**，以及决定可切除性的**血管包裹**：

- Pancreatic head tumor compresses the common bile duct at its intrapancreatic segment → cholestasis → conjugated hyperbilirubinemia → jaundice, dark urine, acholic stools\
  胰头肿瘤压迫胆总管胰腺内段 → 胆汁淤积 → 结合型高胆红素血症 → 黄疸、深色尿、陶土样大便

- Gallbladder distends (Courvoisier's sign) because obstruction is distal to the cystic duct insertion — the gallbladder cannot decompress via its normal route\
  胆囊扩张（Courvoisier 征），因梗阻位于胆囊管汇入点远侧——胆囊无法通过正常途径减压

- The superior mesenteric artery (SMA) runs posterior to the pancreatic neck; any encasement by tumor represents direct arterial invasion = unresectable per surgical criteria\
  肠系膜上动脉走行于胰颈后方；任何肿瘤包裹均代表动脉直接受侵 = 按外科标准为不可切除

- Without surgical resection (Whipple procedure = pancreaticoduodenectomy), 5-year survival drops from ~15–25% to \<5%\
  若无法手术切除（Whipple 手术 = 胰十二指肠切除术），5 年生存率从约 15-25% 降至 \<5%

**Surgical pearl:** SMA encasement is an absolute contraindication to resection; SMV compression alone (with a patent, reconstructable vessel) may still permit surgery with venous reconstruction.

**手术要点:** SMA 包裹是切除的绝对禁忌；单纯 SMV 受压（血管仍通畅、可重建）有时仍可手术并行静脉重建。

## 3. Correct Answer (D) — Superior Mesenteric Artery Encasement / 正确答案 (D) — 肠系膜上动脉包裹

**Vascular encasement of the SMA** eliminates the only curative treatment option — surgical resection — directly predicting a fatal prognosis:

**肠系膜上动脉（SMA）血管包裹**使唯一的根治性治疗手段——手术切除——成为禁忌，直接预测致命性预后：

- Pancreatic cancer prognosis is primarily determined by resectability, not by bilirubin level, tumor size, age, or sex\
  胰腺癌预后主要取决于可切除性，而非胆红素水平、肿瘤大小、年龄或性别

- SMA encasement = arterial invasion → Whipple procedure is contraindicated; attempting resection risks catastrophic hemorrhage\
  SMA 包裹 = 动脉受侵 → Whipple 手术禁忌；强行切除有灾难性出血风险

- SMV compression (also present here) adds surgical complexity, but SMA involvement is the decisive absolute contraindication\
  SMV 受压（本例也存在）增加手术难度，但 SMA 受累是决定性的绝对禁忌

- With unresectable local disease, median survival is 6–12 months vs 18–24 months post-Whipple\
  不可切除的局部病变中位生存期为 6-12 个月，而 Whipple 术后为 18-24 个月

**Diagnosis:** Pancreatic ductal adenocarcinoma, locally advanced, unresectable due to SMA encasement; confirmed by FNA showing hyperchromatic pleomorphic cells with high nucleus-to-cytoplasm ratio

**诊断:** 胰腺导管腺癌，局部进展期，因 SMA 包裹为不可切除；FNA 显示高染色质多形性细胞、核质比高，支持诊断

**Treatment:** Palliative-intent systemic therapy — gemcitabine + nab-paclitaxel or FOLFIRINOX; biliary decompression via ERCP with stent placement for symptomatic jaundice relief; surgical resection is contraindicated

**治疗:** 姑息性全身治疗——吉西他滨 + 白蛋白紫杉醇或 FOLFIRINOX；ERCP 胆道支架置入缓解症状性黄疸；手术切除为禁忌

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Bilirubin concentration<br />
A — 胆红素浓度</td>
<td>Bilirubin reflects degree of biliary obstruction, not vascular invasion or resectability; elevation can be reversed with biliary stenting<br />
胆红素反映胆道梗阻程度，而非血管侵犯或可切除性；支架置入可逆转升高</td>
<td>Bilirubin = obstructive marker only; does NOT predict surgical candidacy or cancer stage<br />
胆红素仅为梗阻标志物；不能预测手术适应证或癌症分期</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Patient's age<br />
B — 患者年龄</td>
<td>At 49 years old, he is young enough to tolerate major surgery; age alone is not the dominant prognostic factor<br />
49 岁足以耐受大手术；年龄本身不是主要预后决定因素</td>
<td>Age affects operative risk, not oncologic prognosis; resectability and stage dominate<br />
年龄影响手术风险，而非肿瘤学预后；可切除性和分期占主导</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Patient's sex assigned at birth<br />
C — 出生性别</td>
<td>Sex is not independently associated with pancreatic cancer prognosis or resectability<br />
性别与胰腺癌预后或可切除性无独立相关性</td>
<td>Cancer stage and vascular involvement are the dominant prognostic variables across all sexes<br />
癌症分期和血管受累是决定预后的主要变量，与性别无关</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Tumor encasement of the superior mesenteric vessels ✓<br />
D — 肿瘤包裹肠系膜上血管 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — SMA encasement eliminates the Whipple procedure (only curative option), condemning the patient to palliative therapy with median survival &lt;12 months<br />
正确——SMA 包裹使 Whipple 手术（唯一根治手段）成为禁忌，患者只能接受姑息治疗，中位生存期 &lt;12 个月</td>
<td>Vascular encasement = unresectable = direct predictor of fatal outcome<br />
血管包裹 = 不可切除 = 预后不良的直接决定因素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Tumor location in head vs tail<br />
E — 肿瘤位于胰头而非胰尾</td>
<td>Head location is actually associated with BETTER prognosis — jaundice causes earlier presentation and earlier diagnosis<br />
胰头位置实际上与更好的预后相关——黄疸使患者更早就诊、更早确诊</td>
<td>Pancreatic tail/body tumors are clinically silent, often present after metastasis → worse prognosis than head tumors<br />
胰体/尾癌临床隐匿，常在转移后才发现 → 预后比胰头癌差</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most seductive distractor is Choice E — many students assume head location worsens prognosis because it causes jaundice, but that jaundice is precisely what leads to earlier diagnosis; tail tumors carry worse prognosis due to late, often post-metastatic presentation.*

最易混淆的干扰项是 E——很多学生认为胰头位置因引起黄疸而预后差，但黄疸恰恰是早期发现的"警报"；胰体/尾癌位置隐匿，常在转移后才被诊断，预后反而更差。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Resectable vs Unresectable Pancreatic Ductal Adenocarcinoma / 可切除与不可切除胰腺导管腺癌对比

<td>No contact or &lt;180° contact without deformity<br />
无接触或 &lt;180° 且无变形</td>

包裹 / 接触 &gt;180°（本例）</td>

<td>&lt;5%<br />
&lt;5%</td>

中位生存期</td>

18-24 个月</td>

6-12 个月</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
