## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In a stable bipolar patient who is past the first trimester and euthymic on lithium, continue lithium with serum level monitoring and fetal cardiac echocardiography, because the risk of stopping (relapse, suicide) far outweighs the residual teratogenic risk.**

**对于已过第一孕期、锂盐治疗下心境平稳的稳定双相障碍患者，应继续锂盐治疗并监测血清浓度及行胎儿心脏超声，因为停药风险（复发、自杀）远超残余致畸风险。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "CAVE the Switch" / 记忆钩 — "CAVE 换药禁忌":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>C</strong>arbamazepine — Neural tube defects; do not switch to it in pregnancy / 卡马西平——神经管缺陷；孕期勿换用<br />
• <strong>A</strong>void stopping lithium — Relapse + suicide risk is worse than Ebstein anomaly risk / 避免停用锂盐——复发+自杀风险比Ebstein畸形风险更严重<br />
• <strong>V</strong>alproate — Most teratogenic mood stabilizer; absolutely contraindicated in pregnancy / 丙戊酸——致畸性最强的情绪稳定剂；孕期绝对禁忌<br />
• <strong>E</strong>bstein anomaly — Lithium's cardiac risk, relevant only in first trimester; monitor with fetal echo / Ebstein畸形——锂盐的心脏风险，仅与第一孕期相关；胎儿心脏超声监测</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Lithium in Pregnancy / 高频知识表 — 锂盐与妊娠

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Ebstein anomaly anatomy<br />
Ebstein畸形解剖</td>
<td>Apical displacement of tricuspid valve leaflets into right ventricle → "atrialization" of right ventricle → tricuspid regurgitation; associated arrhythmias: WPW syndrome, SVT<br />
三尖瓣叶向心尖部移位进入右心室→右心室"房室化"→三尖瓣反流；相关心律失常：WPW综合征、室上性心动过速</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Lithium in first trimester<br />
第一孕期锂盐使用</td>
<td>~1–2× increased relative risk for Ebstein anomaly; absolute risk remains very low (~1/1000); must discuss with patient; some guidelines support continuation with informed consent and close monitoring<br />
Ebstein畸形相对风险增加约1–2倍；绝对风险仍极低（约1/1000）；必须告知患者；部分指南支持在知情同意和密切监测下继续使用</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Lithium after first trimester<br />
第一孕期后锂盐使用</td>
<td>Organogenesis complete; cardiac teratogenic risk largely resolved; continue with frequent serum level monitoring and fetal cardiac echocardiography<br />
器官发生完成；心脏致畸风险基本消除；继续治疗并频繁监测血清浓度及行胎儿心脏超声心动图</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Lithium pharmacokinetics in pregnancy<br />
孕期锂盐药代动力学</td>
<td>GFR increases by ~50% in pregnancy → increased renal lithium clearance → lower serum levels → dose increases often needed; narrow therapeutic window (maintenance: 0.6–1.2 mEq/L)<br />
孕期GFR增加约50%→锂肾脏清除率增加→血清浓度降低→常需加大剂量；治疗窗窄（维持期：0.6–1.2 mEq/L）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Risks of untreated bipolar in pregnancy<br />
孕期未治双相障碍的风险</td>
<td>Acute mania/depression, poor prenatal self-care, substance use, suicide attempts, preterm labor, low birth weight — often exceeds medication risks in magnitude<br />
急性躁狂/抑郁、产前自我照护不足、物质滥用、自杀企图、早产、低出生体重——风险幅度通常超过药物风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Valproate contraindication in pregnancy<br />
丙戊酸的孕期禁忌</td>
<td>Neural tube defects (1–5%), craniofacial malformations, cardiac defects, autism spectrum disorder, persistent cognitive impairment; should be avoided throughout the entire pregnancy<br />
神经管缺陷（1–5%）、颅面畸形、心脏缺陷、自闭症谱系障碍、持续认知损害；整个孕期均应避免</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Clozapine distinction from mood stabilizers<br />
氯氮平与情绪稳定剂的区别</td>
<td>Clozapine is an atypical antipsychotic (not a mood stabilizer); used for treatment-refractory schizophrenia only; requires weekly CBC for first 6 months due to agranulocytosis risk<br />
氯氮平是非典型抗精神病药（不是情绪稳定剂）；仅用于难治性精神分裂症；因粒细胞缺乏症风险，前6个月需每周全血细胞计数</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Postpartum lithium toxicity risk:** Rapid fluid shifts and decreased renal clearance immediately after delivery increase lithium toxicity risk — serum levels must be monitored closely in the first 1–2 weeks postpartum\
  **产后锂中毒风险:** 分娩后体液快速转移和肾清除率下降立即增加锂中毒风险——产后1–2周必须密切监测血清浓度

- **Fetal cardiac echo timing:** Fetal echocardiography for lithium-exposed pregnancies is typically performed at 18–22 weeks gestation as part of the anomaly scan; this can reassure the patient if cardiac anatomy is normal\
  **胎儿心脏超声时机:** 锂盐暴露妊娠的胎儿超声心动图通常在妊娠18–22周作为畸形筛查的一部分进行；如心脏解剖正常可给患者提供reassurance

- **Peripartum mood episode risk:** Women with bipolar disorder have markedly elevated risk for postpartum psychosis and depression — a postpartum psychiatric management plan should be established before delivery\
  **围产期情绪发作风险:** 双相障碍女性产后精神病和抑郁的风险显著升高——应在分娩前制定产后精神科管理计划

- **High-dose folic acid for anticonvulsant mood stabilizers:** Patients on carbamazepine or valproate (folic acid antagonists) planning pregnancy should take 4 mg/day of folic acid preconceptionally and through the first trimester to reduce neural tube defect risk\
  **抗癫痫情绪稳定剂的高剂量叶酸补充:** 服用卡马西平或丙戊酸（叶酸拮抗剂）的备孕患者应在受孕前及第一孕期服用4 mg/天叶酸，以降低神经管缺陷风险

# Question 17 — Gestational Weight Gain Counseling in Obese Primigravida / 肥胖初产妇妊娠期体重增长指导

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>30-year-old primigravid woman</strong> at <strong>10 weeks' gestation</strong> comes to the physician for her <strong>first prenatal visit</strong>. She has <strong>polycystic ovarian syndrome</strong>. She conceived following <strong>clomiphene therapy</strong>, and her only current medication is a prenatal vitamin. She is 165 cm (5 ft 5 in) tall and weighs <strong>82 kg (180 lb)</strong>; <strong>BMI is 30 kg/m²</strong>. Examination shows a uterus consistent in size with a 10-week gestation. Which of the following is the most appropriate recommendation for this patient during her pregnancy?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate recommendation for this patient during her pregnancy?</strong></p>
<p>A) Amniocentesis<br />
B) Cesarean delivery<br />
C) Chorionic villus sampling<br />
D) Limiting pregnancy weight gain<br />
E) Measurement of serum fasting insulin concentration</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: D</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>BMI 30 kg/m² (obese)<br />
BMI 30（肥胖）</td>
<td>Determines gestational weight gain target: 11–20 lbs; drives all downstream complication risk<br />
决定妊娠期体重增长目标为 11–20 磅；驱动所有下游并发症风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>First prenatal visit at 10 weeks<br />
首次产检（10 周）</td>
<td>Ideal time to establish weight gain goals, baseline vitals, and screening plans<br />
是制定体重增长目标、基线生命体征及筛查计划的最佳时机</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Polycystic ovarian syndrome (PCOS)<br />
多囊卵巢综合征</td>
<td>Independently increases risk of gestational diabetes and insulin resistance beyond obesity alone<br />
在肥胖之外独立增加妊娠期糖尿病和胰岛素抵抗的风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Primigravida<br />
初产妇</td>
<td>No prior obstetric history; all baseline risks apply without mitigating factors<br />
无既往产科病史；所有基线风险均适用，无缓解因素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Conceived via clomiphene<br />
经克罗米芬促排卵受孕</td>
<td>Implies prior anovulation due to PCOS; confirms underlying metabolic dysfunction<br />
提示因 PCOS 导致的既往无排卵；证实潜在的代谢功能障碍</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No abnormal screening findings<br />
无异常筛查结果</td>
<td>No indication for invasive genetic testing (amniocentesis or CVS)<br />
无侵入性遗传检测（羊膜穿刺或绒毛取样）的指征</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Gestational weight gain** recommendations are stratified by **prepregnancy BMI** because adipose tissue and metabolic state directly influence fetal growth, placental function, and maternal vascular risk:

妊娠期体重增长建议按**孕前 BMI** 分层，因为脂肪组织和代谢状态直接影响胎儿生长、胎盘功能及母体血管风险：

- Excess adipose tissue → hyperinsulinemia and elevated glucose → fetal overgrowth and LGA infant\
  脂肪组织过多 → 高胰岛素血症和血糖升高 → 胎儿过度生长和大于胎龄儿

- Elevated maternal weight → increased systemic vascular resistance → gestational hypertension and preeclampsia\
  母体体重增加 → 体循环血管阻力升高 → 妊娠期高血压和子痫前期

- Macrosomic fetus → cephalopelvic disproportion and shoulder dystocia → cesarean delivery\
  巨大儿 → 头盆不称和肩难产 → 剖宫产风险升高

- PCOS co-morbidity → pre-existing insulin resistance compounds gestational metabolic risk beyond obesity alone\
  PCOS 合并症 → 已有的胰岛素抵抗在肥胖之外进一步加剧妊娠期代谢风险

**Clinical rule of thumb:** Obese patients (BMI ≥30) gain only 11–20 lbs total, versus 25–35 lbs for normal-weight patients — the higher the baseline BMI, the tighter the target.

**临床小窍门:** 肥胖患者（BMI ≥30）整个孕期仅增重 11–20 磅，而正常体重患者为 25–35 磅——基线 BMI 越高，增重目标越严格。

## 3. Correct Answer (D) — Gestational Weight Gain Restriction for Obesity / 正确答案 (D) — 肥胖患者妊娠期体重增长限制

**Limiting pregnancy weight gain** is the evidence-based standard-of-care recommendation at the first prenatal visit for any patient with prepregnancy obesity (BMI ≥30):

**限制妊娠期体重增长**是针对孕前肥胖（BMI ≥30）患者首次产检时的循证标准化推荐：

- BMI ≥30 → recommended total gestational weight gain: 11–20 lbs (5–9 kg) per IOM guidelines\
  BMI ≥30 → 美国医学研究所指南推荐妊娠期总增重：11–20 磅（5–9 千克）

- Restricting gain reduces risk of LGA infant, gestational diabetes, preeclampsia, and cesarean delivery\
  限制增重可降低大于胎龄儿、妊娠期糖尿病、子痫前期和剖宫产的风险

- PCOS further raises metabolic risk, making weight management even more critical in this patient\
  PCOS 进一步提高代谢风险，使本患者的体重管理尤为关键

**Counseling:** Dietary modification, regular low-impact exercise, and nutritional education are first-line tools to achieve target weight gain during pregnancy.

**咨询建议:** 饮食调整、规律低强度运动和营养教育是妊娠期实现目标增重的一线干预措施。

**Monitoring:** Standard GDM screening (1-hour 50 g oral glucose challenge) at 24–28 weeks; ACOG recommends considering earlier first-visit screening in high-risk patients with PCOS and obesity.

**监测:** 标准妊娠期糖尿病筛查（1 小时 50 g 口服葡萄糖激发试验）于 24–28 周进行；ACOG 建议对 PCOS 合并肥胖的高危患者考虑在首次产检时提前筛查。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Amniocentesis<br />
A — 羊膜穿刺术</td>
<td>Invasive fetal genetic test; no indication here — no abnormal noninvasive screen, no advanced maternal age<br />
侵入性胎儿遗传检测；本例无指征——无无创筛查异常、无高龄产妇</td>
<td>Reserved for confirmation after abnormal cfDNA or ultrasound, not routine<br />
仅用于游离DNA或超声异常后的确认，非常规操作</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Cesarean delivery<br />
B — 剖宫产</td>
<td>Route of delivery cannot be determined at 10 weeks; no current obstetric indication exists<br />
10 周时无法确定分娩方式；目前无产科手术指征</td>
<td>Indicated for breech, placenta previa, or arrested labor — none present now<br />
适用于臀位、前置胎盘或产程停滞——目前均不存在</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Chorionic villus sampling<br />
C — 绒毛取样</td>
<td>Invasive genetic test at 10–13 weeks; no evidence of fetal anomaly or abnormal aneuploidy screen<br />
10–13 周的侵入性遗传检测；无胎儿异常或染色体非整倍体筛查异常的证据</td>

需有适应证；单纯 PCOS 不增加胎儿染色体风险</td>

<tr>
<td>D — Limiting pregnancy weight gain ✓<br />
D — 限制妊娠期体重增长 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — BMI 30 (obese) → target 11–20 lbs to prevent LGA, GDM, preeclampsia, and C-section<br />
正确——BMI 30（肥胖）→ 目标增重 11–20 磅，预防大于胎龄儿、妊娠期糖尿病、子痫前期及剖宫产</td>
<td>IOM gestational weight gain guidelines are stratified by prepregnancy BMI<br />
美国医学研究所妊娠期体重增长指南按孕前 BMI 分层制定</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Measurement of serum fasting insulin concentration<br />
E — 血清空腹胰岛素浓度测定</td>
<td>Not standard obstetric practice; fasting insulin is not a validated GDM screening tool in pregnancy<br />
非产科标准操作；空腹胰岛素不是经过验证的妊娠期糖尿病筛查工具</td>
<td>GDM screening uses 1-hr oral glucose challenge test at 24–28 weeks, not fasting insulin<br />
妊娠期糖尿病筛查使用 24–28 周 1 小时口服葡萄糖激发试验，而非空腹胰岛素</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*Choice E is the most tempting distractor: this patient has PCOS and insulin resistance, making diabetes seem foremost — but fasting insulin has no validated role in obstetric screening; the oral glucose challenge test at 24–28 weeks is the correct tool.*

选项 E 是最具迷惑性的干扰项：患者有 PCOS 和胰岛素抵抗，糖尿病风险突出——但空腹胰岛素在产科筛查中无经验证的作用；24–28 周口服葡萄糖激发试验才是正确的筛查工具。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**For an obese pregnant patient (BMI ≥30), the first prenatal visit recommendation is to limit gestational weight gain to 11–20 lbs to prevent LGA infant, gestational diabetes, preeclampsia, and cesarean delivery.**

**对于肥胖孕妇（BMI ≥30），首次产检的核心建议是将妊娠期体重增长限制在 11–20 磅，以预防大于胎龄儿、妊娠期糖尿病、子痫前期和剖宫产。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "GLPC" Complications of Obesity in Pregnancy / 记忆钩 — 妊娠合并肥胖四大并发症 "GLPC":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>G</strong>estational diabetes — hyperinsulinemia from excess fat drives glucose dysregulation / 妊娠期糖尿病——多余脂肪引发的高胰岛素血症导致血糖失调<br />
• <strong>L</strong>arge for gestational age (LGA) — excess glucose crosses the placenta and fuels fetal growth / 大于胎龄儿——过多葡萄糖通过胎盘促进胎儿过度生长<br />
• <strong>P</strong>reeclampsia — obesity → endothelial dysfunction → hypertension and proteinuria / 子痫前期——肥胖→血管内皮功能障碍→高血压和蛋白尿<br />
• <strong>C</strong>esarean delivery — macrosomia + arrest of labor → surgical delivery required / 剖宫产——巨大儿＋产程停滞→需要手术分娩</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

<tr>
<td>IOM weight gain guidelines by prepregnancy BMI<br />
IOM 按孕前 BMI 的体重增长指南</td>
<td>Underweight (&lt;18.5): 28–40 lbs; Normal (18.5–24.9): 25–35 lbs; Overweight (25–29.9): 15–25 lbs; Obese (≥30): 11–20 lbs<br />
低体重（&lt;18.5）：28–40 磅；正常（18.5–24.9）：25–35 磅；超重（25–29.9）：15–25 磅；肥胖（≥30）：11–20 磅</td>

<td>GDM screening protocol<br />
妊娠期糖尿病筛查流程</td>

第一步：24–28 周 1 小时 50 g 口服葡萄糖激发试验；≥140 mg/dL → 第二步：3 小时 100 g OGTT 确诊；高危患者（PCOS、肥胖）可在首次产检时提前筛查</td>

<td>PCOS pregnancy-specific risks<br />
PCOS 妊娠特有风险</td>

妊娠期糖尿病、子痫前期、早产和流产风险增加；即使空腹血糖正常也伴有胰岛素抵抗和高雄激素血症</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>First prenatal visit key components<br />
首次产检核心内容</td>
<td>Complete H&amp;P, BP, weight/BMI, CBC, blood type/Rh, rubella/varicella immunity, STI screen, Pap (if due), urine culture, weight gain counseling, substance use screening<br />
完整病史体检、血压、体重/BMI、血常规、血型/Rh、风疹/水痘免疫、性病筛查、宫颈涂片（如需）、尿培养、体重增长咨询、物质使用筛查</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Amniocentesis indications and timing<br />
羊膜穿刺适应证与时机</td>
<td>Done at 15–20 weeks; indicated for diagnostic confirmation after abnormal cfDNA/ultrasound, advanced maternal age (≥35), or known family genetic disorder<br />
于 15–20 周进行；适用于游离DNA/超声异常后的诊断确认、高龄产妇（≥35 岁）或已知家族遗传病</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>LGA definition and sequelae<br />
大于胎龄儿的定义与后果</td>
<td>Birth weight &gt;90th percentile for gestational age; associated with shoulder dystocia, brachial plexus injury, neonatal hypoglycemia, and increased maternal C-section rate<br />
出生体重超过同胎龄第 90 百分位；与肩难产、臂丛神经损伤、新生儿低血糖和母体剖宫产率升高相关</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **PCOS and clomiphene:** Clomiphene citrate is first-line for ovulation induction in PCOS (acts as estrogen receptor antagonist at hypothalamus → increases GnRH pulsatility); successful conception does not eliminate PCOS metabolic risks during pregnancy\
  **PCOS 与克罗米芬:** 枸橼酸氯米芬是 PCOS 促排卵一线用药（拮抗下丘脑雌激素受体→增加 GnRH 脉冲频率）；成功受孕并不消除孕期 PCOS 代谢风险

- **Twin pregnancy weight gain:** IOM targets are higher for multiples — normal-weight twins: 37–54 lbs; obese twins: 25–42 lbs; a common NBME extension question pairing twin gestation with weight counseling\
  **双胎妊娠体重增长:** 多胎妊娠的 IOM 目标更高——正常体重双胎：37–54 磅；肥胖双胎：25–42 磅；是 NBME 将双胎妊娠与体重咨询配对的常见延伸考点

- **Underweight risk (opposite end):** BMI \<18.5 → recommend 28–40 lbs gain; insufficient gain → SGA infant, preterm birth, and intrauterine growth restriction; weight counseling is always individualized, not universally restrictive\
  **低体重风险（对立端）:** BMI \<18.5 → 推荐增重 28–40 磅；增重不足→小于胎龄儿、早产和宫内生长受限；体重咨询始终是个体化的，并非一律限制

- **Early GDM screening rationale:** ACOG 2021 guidance supports offering early fasting glucose or HbA1c (not fasting insulin) at first prenatal visit for high-risk patients; catches pre-existing type 2 DM that was undiagnosed before pregnancy\
  **早期妊娠期糖尿病筛查依据:** ACOG 2021 指南支持对高危患者在首次产检时进行早期空腹血糖或 HbA1c 检测（非空腹胰岛素），以发现孕前未确诊的 2 型糖尿病

# Question 18 — Subarachnoid Hemorrhage Workup (CT-Negative) / 蛛网膜下腔出血排查（CT 阴性）

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>previously healthy 57-year-old man</strong> comes to the emergency department <strong>1 hour</strong> after the <strong>sudden onset of severe occipital headache</strong>. His temperature is 37.2°C (99°F), pulse is 92/min, respirations are 18/min, and <strong>blood pressure is 180/98 mm Hg</strong>. He is <strong>mildly lethargic</strong> but oriented to person, place, and time. Neurologic examination shows no other abnormalities. A <strong>CT scan of the head shows no abnormalities</strong>.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Measurement of erythrocyte sedimentation rate<br />
B) Measurement of intraocular pressure<br />
C) Carotid duplex ultrasonography<br />
D) MRI of the brain with contrast<br />
E) Intravenous prochlorperazine therapy<br />
F) Cerebrospinal fluid analysis</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: F</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Sudden onset severe occipital headache<br />
突发严重枕部头痛</td>
<td>Classic "thunderclap headache" — hallmark of subarachnoid hemorrhage until proven otherwise<br />
典型"雷击样头痛"——在排除之前必须首先考虑蛛网膜下腔出血</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>1 hour after onset<br />
起病后 1 小时</td>
<td>CT is most sensitive within 6 hours; even so, sensitivity is not 100%<br />
CT 在 6 小时内灵敏度最高，但仍非 100%，不能完全排除 SAH</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>BP 180/98 mmHg<br />
血压 180/98 mmHg</td>
<td>Hypertension accompanies SAH due to sympathetic surge (Cushing reflex precursor)<br />
高血压是 SAH 的伴随反应，来源于交感激活，提示颅内事件</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Mildly lethargic<br />
轻度嗜睡</td>
<td>Altered consciousness points to intracranial pathology, not benign primary headache<br />
意识改变提示颅内器质性病变，而非良性原发性头痛</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>CT scan shows no abnormalities<br />
CT 扫描无异常</td>
<td>CT sensitivity for SAH declines with time and small bleeds; negative CT does NOT rule out SAH<br />
CT 对小量或较晚出血的灵敏度下降，阴性结果不能排除 SAH</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No focal neurologic deficits<br />
无局灶性神经系统缺损</td>
<td>Makes ischemic stroke less likely; clinical picture still warrants SAH workup<br />
降低缺血性卒中可能，但仍须完整排查 SAH</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

The hallmark of **subarachnoid hemorrhage (SAH)** is **sudden extravasation of blood into the subarachnoid space**, most commonly from a **ruptured intracranial aneurysm**. This produces the classic **"thunderclap headache"** — maximal at onset — via rapid elevation of intracranial pressure and meningeal irritation by blood products:

**蛛网膜下腔出血（SAH）** 的核心机制是**血液突然溢入蛛网膜下腔**，最常见原因是**颅内动脉瘤破裂**。血液快速升高颅内压并刺激脑膜，产生典型的**"雷击样头痛"**——即起病即达峰的剧烈头痛：

- Blood in subarachnoid space stimulates pain-sensitive meninges → immediate severe headache\
  血液刺激脑膜痛觉感受器→立即产生剧烈头痛

- Acute ICP elevation causes sympathetic surge → hypertension, bradycardia (early Cushing)\
  颅内压急升引发交感激活→高血压，可出现早期 Cushing 反应

- RBCs in CSF degrade over 2–4 hours into oxyhemoglobin, then bilirubin → **xanthochromia**\
  脑脊液中红细胞在 2–4 小时内降解为氧合血红蛋白，再降解为胆红素→产生**黄变色（xanthochromia）**

- Small-volume bleeds or imaging \>6 h post-ictus → CT misses up to 5–10% of SAH\
  小量出血或发病 6 小时后行 CT→漏诊率可达 5–10%

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The posterior communicating artery and anterior communicating artery are the most common aneurysm locations for SAH; occipital pain reflects meningeal irritation, not a structural posterior fossa lesion.

**解剖小窍门:** 后交通动脉和前交通动脉是 SAH 最常见的动脉瘤位置；枕部头痛反映的是脑膜刺激，而非后颅窝结构性损伤。

---

## 3. Correct Answer (F) — Lumbar Puncture / Cerebrospinal Fluid Analysis / 正确答案 (F) — 腰椎穿刺 / 脑脊液分析

**Cerebrospinal fluid (CSF) analysis via lumbar puncture** is the definitive next step when clinical suspicion for SAH is high but CT is negative, because CT sensitivity for SAH is not 100%:

**腰椎穿刺行脑脊液分析**是 CT 阴性但临床高度怀疑 SAH 时的决定性下一步，因为 CT 灵敏度并非 100%：

- CT sensitivity for SAH: ~98% within 6 h, but drops significantly thereafter\
  CT 对 SAH 灵敏度：6 小时内约 98%，之后显著下降

- LP findings diagnostic of SAH: xanthochromia (yellow-tinged CSF), elevated opening pressure, RBCs that do not clear across sequential tubes\
  LP 诊断 SAH 的关键发现：黄变色、开放压升高、各管 RBC 数不递减

- Xanthochromia develops 2–4 hours after bleeding and persists up to 2 weeks\
  黄变色在出血后 2–4 小时出现，可持续约 2 周

- A traumatic tap (needle artifact) causes RBC count to decrease from tube 1→4; true SAH does not clear\
  操作性出血（针刺外伤）时各管 RBC 依次递减；真性 SAH 则不递减

**Diagnosis:** CT negative + thunderclap headache → LP is mandatory to exclude SAH before attributing to a benign cause.

**诊断:** CT 阴性 + 雷击样头痛→必须行 LP 排除 SAH，不可直接归因为良性头痛。

**Treatment:** If LP confirms SAH, emergent neurosurgery/neurology consult, nimodipine (vasospasm prevention), and definitive aneurysm treatment (clipping or coiling).

**治疗:** LP 确认 SAH 后，紧急神经外科/神经内科会诊，给予尼莫地平（预防血管痉挛），并行动脉瘤夹闭或弹簧圈栓塞治疗。

---

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Measurement of erythrocyte sedimentation rate<br />
A — 红细胞沉降率检测</td>
<td>Wrong — ESR diagnoses temporal arteritis, which presents with subacute temporal/jaw pain in patients &gt;50 y, not sudden occipital thunderclap headache<br />
错误——ESR 用于诊断颞动脉炎，后者表现为亚急性颞部/下颌疼痛，不是突发枕部雷击样头痛</td>
<td>Temporal arteritis: subacute, temporal, jaw claudication, age &gt;50<br />
颞动脉炎：亚急性起病，颞部分布，下颌跛行，年龄 &gt;50 岁</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Measurement of intraocular pressure<br />
B — 眼压测量</td>
<td>Wrong — IOP measures diagnose glaucoma (painful or painless vision loss due to anterior chamber pressure elevation), not SAH<br />
错误——眼压测量诊断青光眼（前房压升高导致有痛或无痛性视力丧失），与 SAH 无关</td>
<td>Glaucoma: eye pain, vision loss, halos; no thunderclap headache<br />
青光眼：眼痛、视力下降、光晕；无雷击样头痛</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Carotid duplex ultrasonography<br />
C — 颈动脉双功能超声</td>
<td>Wrong — Carotid duplex assesses carotid stenosis (TIA/stroke workup) and has no role in SAH diagnosis<br />
错误——颈动脉超声评估颈动脉狭窄（TIA/卒中检查），对 SAH 诊断无用</td>
<td>Carotid stenosis: focal deficits, amaurosis fugax, no thunderclap<br />
颈动脉狭窄：局灶性神经缺损、一过性黑矇，无雷击样头痛</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — MRI of the brain with contrast<br />
D — 脑部增强 MRI</td>
<td>Wrong — MRI is highly sensitive for SAH/tumor/abscess but is time-consuming; LP is faster and immediately detects SAH; time to treatment matters critically<br />
错误——MRI 灵敏度高，但耗时长；LP 更快捷且可立即检测 SAH；治疗时机至关重要</td>
<td>Time is brain: LP gives results in minutes; MRI delays diagnosis and treatment<br />
时间就是大脑：LP 数分钟出结果；MRI 延误诊疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Intravenous prochlorperazine therapy<br />
E — 静脉丙氯拉嗪治疗</td>
<td>Wrong — Prochlorperazine treats migraine/primary headache; treating a potential SAH with an antiemetic without ruling out hemorrhage is dangerous<br />
错误——丙氯拉嗪用于偏头痛/原发性头痛治疗；在未排除出血前以止吐药处理可能致命</td>
<td>Primary headache diagnosis requires exclusion of SAH first<br />
原发性头痛诊断须先排除 SAH</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>F — Cerebrospinal fluid analysis ✓<br />
F — 脑脊液分析 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — CT-negative thunderclap headache mandates LP to detect xanthochromia, elevated RBCs, or elevated opening pressure diagnostic of SAH<br />
正确——CT 阴性的雷击样头痛必须行 LP，检测黄变色、RBC 升高或开放压升高以确诊 SAH</td>
<td>LP is the gold standard when CT is negative but SAH is clinically suspected<br />
CT 阴性但临床疑诊 SAH 时，LP 是金标准</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most dangerous distractor is Choice E (prochlorperazine): it seems "reasonable" for a severe headache but bypasses mandatory SAH exclusion — treating a ruptured aneurysm as migraine risks re-bleed and death.*

选项 E（丙氯拉嗪）是最危险的干扰项：看似对"重度头痛"合理，实则跳过了必须排除 SAH 的步骤——将破裂动脉瘤误当偏头痛处理，可因再出血致死。

---

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A CT-negative thunderclap headache requires emergent lumbar puncture to exclude subarachnoid hemorrhage via CSF xanthochromia and persistent red blood cells.**

**CT 阴性的雷击样头痛必须紧急行腰椎穿刺，通过脑脊液黄变色和持续性红细胞来排除蛛网膜下腔出血。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — LP after Negative CT: "XOR Rule" / 记忆钩 — CT 阴性后 LP："XOR 法则":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>X</strong>anthochromia — yellow CSF = old blood = SAH confirmed / 黄变色——黄色脑脊液 = 旧血 = SAH 确认<br />
• <strong>O</strong>pening pressure elevated — CSF under tension from ICP rise / 开放压升高——颅内压升高导致脑脊液张力增大<br />
• <strong>R</strong>BC count non-clearing — tubes 1→4 stay high (vs. traumatic tap which clears) / RBC 数不递减——各管持续升高（区别于操作性出血的递减规律）</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Subarachnoid Hemorrhage Diagnosis & Management / 高频知识表 — 蛛网膜下腔出血诊断与处理

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>CT sensitivity for SAH<br />
CT 对 SAH 的灵敏度</td>
<td>~98% within 6 hours of onset; drops to ~85–90% by 24 hours; misses small-volume bleeds<br />
起病 6 小时内约 98%；24 小时后降至约 85–90%；可漏检小量出血</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>LP findings in SAH<br />
腰穿诊断 SAH 的发现</td>
<td>Xanthochromia (pathognomonic), non-clearing RBCs tube 1→4, elevated opening pressure (&gt;20 cmH₂O)<br />
黄变色（特征性），第 1→4 管 RBC 不递减，开放压升高（&gt;20 cmH₂O）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Xanthochromia timing<br />
黄变色时间窗</td>
<td>Appears 2–4 h after bleeding, persists up to 2 weeks; most reliable SAH marker on LP<br />
出血后 2–4 小时出现，持续最长 2 周；是 LP 中最可靠的 SAH 标记物</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Most common cause of SAH<br />
SAH 最常见病因</td>
<td>Ruptured saccular (berry) aneurysm — anterior communicating and posterior communicating arteries most common<br />
囊状（浆果状）动脉瘤破裂——前交通动脉和后交通动脉最常见</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Nimodipine in SAH<br />
尼莫地平在 SAH 中的作用</td>
<td>Calcium channel blocker given to prevent cerebral vasospasm (a major cause of delayed ischemic deficits); does NOT reverse hemorrhage<br />
钙通道阻滞剂，用于预防脑血管痉挛（迟发性脑缺血的主要原因）；不能逆转出血</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hunt-Hess grading<br />
Hunt-Hess 分级</td>
<td>Grade I: asymptomatic/mild headache; Grade II: severe headache, no deficit; Grade III: drowsy; Grade IV: stupor; Grade V: coma — correlates with prognosis<br />
I级：无症状/轻度头痛；II级：剧烈头痛、无缺损；III级：嗜睡；IV级：昏迷；V级：深昏迷——与预后相关</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Sentinel bleed<br />
前哨出血</td>
<td>A smaller SAH ("warning leak") 2–8 weeks before major rupture; presents as sudden severe headache that resolves — often missed, leading to catastrophic re-bleed<br />
主要破裂前 2–8 周发生的小量 SAH（"警示漏"）；表现为突发剧烈头痛后自行缓解——常被漏诊，导致灾难性再出血</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Classic exam phrase:** "Worst headache of my life" is the trigger phrase for SAH on USMLE — always pursue LP if CT is negative regardless of how well the patient appears\
  **经典考试用语:** "一生中最严重的头痛"是 USMLE 中 SAH 的触发关键词——无论患者看起来多稳定，CT 阴性都必须行 LP

- **Complication to know:** Re-bleeding is the most feared early complication of aneurysmal SAH (highest risk within 24 hours); vasospasm peaks at days 4–14 causing delayed ischemic deficits\
  **关键并发症:** 动脉瘤性 SAH 最严重的早期并发症是再出血（24 小时内风险最高）；血管痉挛在第 4–14 天达峰，导致迟发性缺血损伤

- **Differential for thunderclap headache:** SAH, reversible cerebral vasoconstriction syndrome (RCVS), cerebral venous sinus thrombosis, hypertensive emergency, pituitary apoplexy — all require neuroimaging and often LP\
  **雷击样头痛鉴别:** SAH、可逆性脑血管收缩综合征（RCVS）、脑静脉窦血栓、高血压急症、垂体卒中——均需神经影像学检查，常需 LP

- **Why not MRI first?** MRI is more sensitive than CT for SAH (especially FLAIR sequence for subacute bleeds) but is time-consuming, less available emergently, and LP remains faster for immediate confirmation — LP is the standard next step after negative CT\
  **为何不先做 MRI?** MRI 对 SAH 灵敏度高于 CT（尤其 FLAIR 序列检测亚急性出血），但耗时长、急诊可及性差；LP 在 CT 阴性后仍是最快捷的确认手段，是标准下一步

# Question 19 — Diabetic Gastroparesis / 糖尿病性胃轻瘫

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>45-year-old woman</strong> comes to the clinic because of a <strong>2-month history of increasingly severe epigastric pain, bloating, and intermittent nausea and vomiting</strong>. During this time, she has had decreased appetite resulting in a <strong>3.6-kg (8-lb) weight loss</strong>. She has hypertension and <strong>type 2 diabetes mellitus</strong>. The conditions have been <strong>poorly controlled during the past 2 years</strong>, because she has <strong>not been adherent to her medication regimen</strong>. The patient has no history of operative procedures. Medications are metformin, insulin glargine, atorvastatin, lisinopril, and daily aspirin. She appears well. She is 157 cm (5 ft 2 in) tall and weighs 91 kg (200 lb); BMI is 37 kg/m². Temperature is 37.0°C (98.6°F), pulse is 78/min, respirations are 12/min, and blood pressure is 124/68 mm Hg. The abdomen is protuberant; there is no organomegaly or tenderness to palpation. <strong>Bowel sounds are decreased</strong>. Results of a complete blood count, metabolic profile, and determination of <strong>serum lipase activity are within the reference ranges</strong>. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in diagnosis?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Endoscopic retrograde cholangiopancreatography<br />
B) Esophageal manometry<br />
C) Gastric emptying study<br />
D) MRI of the abdomen<br />
E) Ultrasonography of the abdomen</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: C</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Type 2 diabetes mellitus, poorly controlled ×2 years<br />
2型糖尿病，控制不良2年</td>
<td>Chronic hyperglycemia → autonomic neuropathy → gastroparesis<br />
长期高血糖→自主神经病变→胃轻瘫</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Non-adherent to medication regimen<br />
药物依从性差</td>
<td>Explains sustained poor glycemic control, accelerating microvascular complications<br />
解释长期血糖控制不良，加速微血管并发症进展</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Epigastric pain, bloating, nausea and vomiting ×2 months<br />
上腹痛、腹胀、恶心呕吐2个月</td>
<td>Classic triad of gastroparesis; chronic subacute course rules out acute abdomen<br />
胃轻瘫经典三联征；慢性亚急性病程排除急腹症</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Bowel sounds decreased<br />
肠鸣音减弱</td>
<td>Indicates reduced GI motility — hallmark of autonomic dysfunction rather than obstruction<br />
提示胃肠动力减弱——自主神经功能障碍的标志，而非梗阻</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Serum lipase within reference range<br />
血清脂肪酶正常</td>
<td>Effectively rules out acute pancreatitis as cause of epigastric symptoms<br />
有效排除急性胰腺炎作为上腹症状的原因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No organomegaly, no tenderness to palpation<br />
无脏器肿大，无压痛</td>
<td>Lowers probability of structural obstruction, malignancy, or peritoneal inflammation<br />
降低机械性梗阻、恶性肿瘤或腹膜炎的可能性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>CBC and metabolic profile within reference ranges<br />
血常规和代谢全套正常</td>
<td>No infection, electrolyte disturbance, or organ failure — points to functional motility disorder<br />
无感染、电解质紊乱或器官衰竭——指向功能性动力障碍</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Diabetic autonomic neuropathy** results from chronic **hyperglycemia**-induced oxidative stress and **microvascular damage** to the nerves supplying the GI tract:

**糖尿病自主神经病变**由长期**高血糖**引起的氧化应激及支配胃肠道神经的**微血管损伤**所导致：

- Chronic hyperglycemia → damage to vasa nervorum → demyelination of autonomic (vagal) nerve fibers\
  长期高血糖→滋养血管损伤→自主（迷走）神经纤维脱髓鞘

- Impaired vagal tone + loss of interstitial cells of Cajal → reduced gastric peristalsis → delayed emptying\
  迷走神经张力受损+Cajal间质细胞丧失→胃蠕动减弱→排空延迟

- Retained gastric contents → distension → early satiety, bloating, nausea, vomiting of undigested food\
  胃内容物滞留→胃扩张→早饱、腹胀、恶心、呕吐未消化食物

- Decreased bowel sounds reflect global reduction in enteric nervous system activity\
  肠鸣音减弱反映肠神经系统活动的整体降低

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The vagus nerve is the master driver of gastric motility; diabetic autonomic neuropathy silences it, converting the stomach into a stagnant reservoir.

**解剖小窍门:** 迷走神经是胃动力的主控驱动器；糖尿病自主神经病变将其抑制，使胃变成一个停滞的"储液池"。

## 3. Correct Answer (C) — Gastric Emptying Study / 正确答案 (C) — 核医学胃排空显像

**Gastric emptying scintigraphy** is the gold standard for confirming gastroparesis, directly quantifying the rate at which the stomach clears its contents rather than inferring it indirectly:

**胃排空闪烁扫描** 是确诊胃轻瘫的金标准，直接定量胃排空速率，而非间接推断：

- Patient ingests a radiolabeled solid meal (commonly Tc-99m sulfur colloid–tagged eggs)\
  患者摄入放射性标记固体餐（通常为Tc-99m硫胶体标记的鸡蛋）

- Gamma camera images taken at 0, 1, 2, and 4 hours post-meal to track gastric retention\
  餐后0、1、2、4小时用伽马相机拍摄图像以追踪胃内滞留

- Gastroparesis defined as \>10% meal retention at 4 hours\
  胃轻瘫定义为4小时后滞留\>10%

- Non-invasive, quantitative, and directly tests the underlying physiologic abnormality\
  无创、定量，并直接检测根本的生理异常

**Diagnosis:** Clinical suspicion based on long-standing DM with classic symptoms; confirmed by gastric emptying study demonstrating delayed emptying without mechanical obstruction.

**诊断:** 基于长期糖尿病伴典型症状的临床怀疑；由胃排空显像证实排空延迟且无机械性梗阻而确诊。

**Treatment:** Dietary modification (small frequent low-fat low-fiber meals); prokinetics — metoclopramide (D2 antagonist, first-line; black box warning for tardive dyskinesia) and erythromycin (motilin agonist, short-term); improved glycemic control.

**治疗:** 饮食调整（少食多餐、低脂低纤维饮食）；促动力药——甲氧氯普胺（D2拮抗剂，一线；迟发性运动障碍黑框警告）和红霉素（胃动素激动剂，短期使用）；改善血糖控制。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Endoscopic retrograde cholangiopancreatography<br />
A — 内镜逆行胰胆管造影</td>
<td>Evaluates biliary and pancreatic ductal pathology (stones, strictures, tumors); no role in assessing gastric motility<br />
用于评估胆道和胰管病变（结石、狭窄、肿瘤）；对评估胃动力无作用</td>
<td>Serum lipase normal, no jaundice, no RUQ pain — biliary/pancreatic ductal disease is not the diagnosis<br />
血清脂肪酶正常，无黄疸，无右上腹痛——胆道/胰管疾病不是诊断</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Esophageal manometry<br />
B — 食管测压</td>
<td>Diagnoses esophageal motility disorders (achalasia, diffuse esophageal spasm); does not evaluate the stomach<br />
诊断食管动力障碍（贲门失弛缓症、弥漫性食管痉挛）；不评估胃</td>
<td>Dominant symptom is epigastric bloating with decreased bowel sounds, not dysphagia — pathology localizes to stomach<br />
主要症状为上腹胀伴肠鸣音减弱，非吞咽困难——病变定位于胃</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Gastric emptying study ✓<br />
C — 核医学胃排空显像 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Gold standard nuclear medicine test that quantifies delayed gastric emptying, confirming gastroparesis<br />
正确——量化胃排空延迟的核医学金标准检查，可确诊胃轻瘫</td>
<td>Long-standing poorly controlled DM + autonomic GI symptoms + no structural or biochemical cause = functional motility test required<br />
长期控制不良的糖尿病+自主神经性消化道症状+无结构或生化异常=需功能性动力检查</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — MRI of the abdomen<br />
D — 腹部MRI</td>
<td>Best for characterizing structural lesions (hepatocellular carcinoma, renal cell carcinoma, liver metastases); cannot assess motility<br />
最适合评估结构性病变（肝癌、肾细胞癌、肝转移）；无法评估动力</td>
<td>No mass, no organomegaly — structural malignancy is not the leading concern; functional testing is needed<br />
无肿块，无脏器肿大——结构性恶性肿瘤不是主要关注点；需要功能性检查</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Ultrasonography of the abdomen<br />
E — 腹部超声</td>
<td>Can visualize gastric distension anatomically but cannot quantify gastric emptying rate or assess motility function<br />
可从解剖角度显示胃扩张，但无法量化胃排空速率或评估动力功能</td>
<td>Ultrasound is anatomic, not functional — gastroparesis is a motility disorder requiring a motility test<br />
超声是解剖学检查，非功能性检查——胃轻瘫是动力障碍，需要动力学检查</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is E (abdominal ultrasound), as it is often ordered first for undifferentiated abdominal pain — but ultrasound cannot assess gastric motility and would miss the functional diagnosis entirely.*

腹部超声（E选项）是最具迷惑性的干扰项，因其常作为不明原因腹痛的一线检查，但超声无法评估胃动力，会完全遗漏该功能性诊断。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Gastroparesis vs. Gastric Outlet Obstruction vs. Achalasia / 胃轻瘫 vs. 胃出口梗阻 vs. 贲门失弛缓症

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Gastroparesis</strong><br />
<strong>胃轻瘫</strong></th>
<th><strong>Gastric Outlet Obstruction</strong><br />
<strong>胃出口梗阻</strong></th>
<th><strong>Achalasia</strong><br />
<strong>贲门失弛缓症</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Primary cause<br />
主要病因</td>
<td>Autonomic neuropathy (DM, post-vagotomy)<br />
自主神经病变（糖尿病、迷走神经切断术后）</td>
<td>Mechanical (PUD scarring, pyloric malignancy)<br />
机械性（消化性溃疡瘢痕、幽门恶性肿瘤）</td>
<td>LES failure to relax (loss of myenteric neurons)<br />
食管下括约肌不能松弛（肠肌丛神经元丧失）</td>

大量喷射性呕吐；振水音</td>

固体和液体吞咽困难，反流</td>
</tr>
<tr>

疼痛</td>
<td>Epigastric discomfort / bloating<br />
上腹不适/胀痛</td>
<td>Epigastric pain, may be severe<br />
上腹痛，可较严重</td>
<td>Chest pain / retrosternal discomfort<br />
胸痛/胸骨后不适</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Bowel sounds<br />
肠鸣音</td>
<td>Decreased<br />
减弱</td>
<td>High-pitched, then absent<br />
高调，后消失</td>
<td>Normal<br />
正常</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Key labs<br />
关键化验</td>
<td>Normal CBC, lipase, metabolic panel<br />
血常规、脂肪酶、代谢全套正常</td>
<td>Hypokalemic hypochloremic metabolic alkalosis<br />
低钾低氯性代谢性碱中毒</td>
<td>Usually normal<br />
通常正常</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Gold standard diagnosis<br />
诊断金标准</td>
<td>Gastric emptying scintigraphy (Tc-99m)<br />
胃排空闪烁扫描（Tc-99m）</td>
<td>Upper GI series / endoscopy<br />
上消化道造影/内镜</td>
<td>Esophageal manometry<br />
食管测压</td>
</tr>

<td>Treatment<br />
治疗</td>
<td>Prokinetics (metoclopramide, erythromycin)<br />
促动力药（甲氧氯普胺、红霉素）</td>
<td>Endoscopic dilation / surgery<br />
内镜扩张/手术</td>
<td>Pneumatic dilation, Heller myotomy, or peroral endoscopic myotomy (POEM)<br />
气囊扩张、Heller肌切开术或经口内镜肌切开术（POEM）</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In a diabetic patient with years of poor glycemic control presenting with bloating, nausea, vomiting of undigested food, and decreased bowel sounds, order a nuclear medicine gastric emptying study to confirm diabetic gastroparesis.**

**对于血糖长期控制不良的糖尿病患者，出现腹胀、恶心、呕吐未消化食物及肠鸣音减弱，应行核医学胃排空显像以确诊糖尿病性胃轻瘫。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — BAGS of Gastroparesis / 记忆钩 — 胃轻瘫 "BAGS" 口诀:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>B</strong>loating &amp; early satiety — cardinal symptoms of delayed gastric emptying / 腹胀和早饱——胃排空延迟的主要症状<br />
• <strong>A</strong>utonomic neuropathy (diabetic) — the root mechanism behind gastroparesis / 自主神经病变（糖尿病性）——胃轻瘫的根本发病机制<br />
• <strong>G</strong>astric emptying study — gold standard nuclear medicine test using Tc-99m / 胃排空显像——使用Tc-99m的核医学金标准检查<br />
• <strong>S</strong>uccussion splash + vomiting of undigested food — pathognomonic clinical red flags / 振水音+呕吐未消化食物——特征性临床红旗征</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Diabetic Gastroparesis / 高频知识表 — 糖尿病性胃轻瘫

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Definition<br />
定义</td>
<td>Delayed gastric emptying without mechanical obstruction; most common identifiable cause is diabetic autonomic neuropathy<br />
无机械性梗阻的胃排空延迟；最常见的可识别病因是糖尿病自主神经病变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pathophysiology<br />
病理生理</td>
<td>Chronic hyperglycemia → oxidative stress → damage to vagal fibers + interstitial cells of Cajal → impaired antral contractions and pyloric coordination<br />
慢性高血糖→氧化应激→迷走神经纤维+Cajal间质细胞损伤→胃窦收缩和幽门协调受损</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Classic presentation<br />
典型表现</td>
<td>Early satiety, postprandial bloating, nausea, vomiting of undigested food hours after eating, epigastric pain, succussion splash, decreased bowel sounds<br />
早饱、餐后腹胀、恶心、进食数小时后呕吐未消化食物、上腹痛、振水音、肠鸣音减弱</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Gold standard diagnosis<br />
诊断金标准</td>
<td>Nuclear medicine gastric emptying scintigraphy: patient ingests Tc-99m–labeled solid meal; &gt;10% retention at 4 hours = confirmed gastroparesis<br />
核医学胃排空闪烁扫描：患者摄入Tc-99m标记固体餐；4小时后滞留&gt;10%=确诊胃轻瘫</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>First-line treatment — prokinetics<br />
一线治疗——促动力药</td>
<td>Metoclopramide (D2 receptor antagonist): first-line but black box warning for tardive dyskinesia with use &gt;12 weeks; erythromycin (motilin agonist): highly effective short-term<br />
甲氧氯普胺（D2受体拮抗剂）：一线药，但使用&gt;12周有迟发性运动障碍黑框警告；红霉素（胃动素激动剂）：短期疗效显著</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Glycemic control importance<br />
血糖控制的重要性</td>
<td>Acute hyperglycemia itself worsens gastric motility; improving glycemic control can partially reverse symptoms independent of prokinetics<br />
急性高血糖本身加重胃动力障碍；改善血糖控制可部分逆转症状，独立于促动力药之外</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Complications<br />
并发症</td>
<td>Malnutrition and weight loss; bezoar formation; unpredictable glucose absorption → glycemic instability and hypoglycemia risk<br />
营养不良和体重减轻；胃结石形成；葡萄糖吸收不可预测→血糖不稳定和低血糖风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Other causes of gastroparesis<br />
其他胃轻瘫病因</td>
<td>Idiopathic (most common overall), post-surgical (post-vagotomy, post-fundoplication), medications (opioids, anticholinergics, GLP-1 agonists), connective tissue disease<br />
特发性（总体最常见）、术后（迷走神经切断术后、胃底折叠术后）、药物（阿片类、抗胆碱药、GLP-1激动剂）、结缔组织病</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **GLP-1 agonist connection:** Semaglutide and liraglutide (used for DM and obesity) delay gastric emptying as a mechanism of action — may exacerbate pre-existing gastroparesis or create diagnostic confusion in diabetic patients\
  **GLP-1激动剂关联:** 司美格鲁肽和利拉鲁肽（用于糖尿病和肥胖）通过延迟胃排空发挥药理作用——可能加重已有胃轻瘫或在糖尿病患者中造成诊断混淆

- **Succussion splash technique:** Examiner places stethoscope over epigastrium and rapidly moves the patient side to side \>3 hours after last meal; audible splashing = retained fluid in a non-emptying stomach; highly specific for gastroparesis or GOO\
  **振水音检查技术:** 检查者将听诊器置于上腹部，在末次进餐\>3小时后快速左右晃动患者；听到溅水声=胃不排空导致液体潴留；对胃轻瘫或胃出口梗阻高度特异

- **Metoclopramide tardive dyskinesia risk:** Involuntary repetitive movements (lip smacking, tongue protrusion, facial grimacing) — irreversible in many cases; FDA mandates REMS program; use lowest effective dose for shortest duration\
  **甲氧氯普胺迟发性运动障碍风险:** 不自主重复运动（咂嘴、伸舌、面部鬼脸）——许多情况下不可逆；FDA强制要求REMS项目；使用最低有效剂量和最短疗程

- **Variant presentation — "bezoar":** Undigested food accumulates into a solid mass (phytobezoar) in the stomach; may cause intermittent obstruction; visible on endoscopy or CT; managed with enzymatic dissolution or endoscopic removal\
  **变体表现——胃结石:** 未消化食物在胃内积聚形成固体块（植物性胃结石）；可导致间歇性梗阻；内镜或CT可见；通过酶解或内镜取出处理

# Question 20 — Achilles Tendinopathy / 跟腱病

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>54-year-old man</strong> comes to the office because of a <strong>3-week history of a dull ache along the back of his left ankle</strong> that is <strong>worse in the morning when he gets out of bed</strong>. The pain also <strong>worsens when he plays tennis on weekends</strong>. Acetaminophen once daily has provided moderate relief of the pain. Medical history is unremarkable, and the patient takes no other medications. He is 178 cm (5 ft 10 in) tall and weighs 99 kg (219 lb); <strong>BMI is 31 kg/m²</strong>. Vital signs are within normal limits. The patient appears well. There is <strong>mild swelling and tenderness to palpation at the proximal aspect of the Achilles tendon</strong>. The remainder of the examination discloses no abnormalities. <strong>Thompson test is negative</strong>. In addition to recommending rest, which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Add oxycodone as needed for pain<br />
B) Increase the frequency of acetaminophen to four times daily<br />
C) Inject cortisone into the calcaneal insertion site of the Achilles tendon<br />
D) Recommend physical therapy<br />
E) Schedule surgical intervention for the Achilles tendon</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: D</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Dull ache along back of left ankle × 3 weeks<br />
左踝后部钝痛 3 周</td>
<td>Posterior ankle pain localizes to Achilles tendon; duration suggests chronic overuse not acute rupture<br />
后踝疼痛提示跟腱病变；持续时间提示慢性劳损而非急性断裂</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Worse in the morning when getting out of bed<br />
晨起下床时加重</td>
<td>Classic "first-step pain" pattern of Achilles tendinopathy due to overnight contracture<br />
典型"第一步疼痛"，是跟腱病的经典表现，源于夜间跟腱缩短</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Worsens with weekend tennis<br />
周末打网球后加重</td>
<td>Activity-related pain = overuse/mechanical etiology, not inflammatory arthritis or infection<br />
活动相关疼痛 = 过度使用/机械性病因，而非炎症性关节炎或感染</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>BMI 31 kg/m²<br />
BMI 31 kg/m²</td>
<td>Obesity is a major risk factor for Achilles tendinopathy due to increased mechanical load<br />
肥胖是跟腱病的主要危险因素，因机械负荷增加</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Tenderness at proximal Achilles tendon<br />
跟腱近端压痛</td>
<td>Non-insertional tendinopathy (2–6 cm above calcaneus); distinct from insertional type<br />
非止点型跟腱病（跟骨上方 2–6 cm 处）；与止点型不同</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Thompson test negative<br />
Thompson 试验阴性</td>
<td>Rules out complete Achilles tendon rupture — confirms tendon is structurally intact<br />
排除跟腱完全断裂——证实跟腱结构完整</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Achilles tendinopathy** results from repetitive **mechanical overload** exceeding the tendon's capacity for repair, leading to **failed tendon healing** and degenerative changes rather than true inflammation:

**跟腱病**是由于反复**机械性超负荷**超过跟腱的修复能力，导致**跟腱愈合失败**和退行性改变，而非真正的炎症：

- Repetitive loading → microtrauma → disrupted collagen fiber organization\
  反复负荷 → 微创伤 → 胶原纤维排列紊乱

- Neovascularization and neural ingrowth → characteristic tendon pain\
  新生血管和神经长入 → 特征性的跟腱疼痛

- Morning stiffness: overnight shortening of tendon → increased strain on first load\
  晨僵：夜间跟腱缩短 → 第一次负重时张力骤增

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Non-insertional tendinopathy occurs 2–6 cm proximal to the calcaneal insertion (watershed zone of poor blood supply); insertional type occurs at the bone-tendon junction.

**解剖小窍门:** 非止点型跟腱病发生在跟骨止点近端 2–6 cm 处（血供差的分水岭区）；止点型发生在骨-腱连接处。

---

## 3. Correct Answer (D) — Physical Therapy / 正确答案 (D) — 物理治疗

**Physical therapy** is the cornerstone of conservative management for Achilles tendinopathy, targeting eccentric loading to remodel collagen and restore tendon function:

**物理治疗**是跟腱病保守治疗的基石，通过离心负荷训练重塑胶原并恢复跟腱功能：

- Eccentric heel-drop exercises (Alfredson protocol) are the most evidence-based intervention\
  离心跟腱下降练习（Alfredson 方案）是证据最充分的干预措施

- Stretching reduces morning stiffness and improves tendon compliance\
  拉伸减轻晨僵，改善跟腱顺应性

- Load management prevents re-injury during return to sport\
  负荷管理在重返运动过程中防止再损伤

- Adjuncts include NSAIDs (short-term), heel lifts, and orthotics\
  辅助措施包括 NSAIDs（短期）、鞋跟垫和矫形器

**Diagnosis:** Non-insertional Achilles tendinopathy — diagnosed clinically by posterior ankle pain, morning stiffness, activity-related worsening, proximal tendon tenderness, and negative Thompson test.

**诊断:** 非止点型跟腱病——临床诊断依据为后踝疼痛、晨僵、活动后加重、跟腱近端压痛及 Thompson 试验阴性。

**Treatment:** Rest + physical therapy (eccentric loading) + NSAIDs short-term ± heel lift; corticosteroid injection and surgery reserved for refractory cases.

**治疗:** 休息 + 物理治疗（离心负荷）+ 短期 NSAIDs ± 鞋跟垫；皮质类固醇注射和手术留给难治性病例。

---

</tr>
</tbody>

*The most tempting distractor is Choice C — corticosteroid injection sounds anti-inflammatory and targeted, but evidence shows increased rupture risk and PT must be trialed first.*

皮质类固醇注射（选项 C）是最具迷惑性的干扰项——听起来针对性强，但证据显示可增加断裂风险，且必须先尝试 PT。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**Achilles tendinopathy in an active, overweight middle-aged man with posterior ankle pain, morning stiffness, and negative Thompson test is treated conservatively with rest and physical therapy (eccentric loading) — not opioids, not corticosteroids, not surgery.**

**跟腱病表现为后踝疼痛、晨僵、Thompson 试验阴性的中年超重活跃患者，应保守治疗：休息 + 物理治疗（离心负荷）——而非阿片类、皮质类固醇或手术。**

<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — RICE-PT for Tendinopathy / 记忆钩 — 跟腱病 RICE-PT:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>R</strong>est — offload the tendon first / 休息——首先减轻跟腱负荷<br />
• <strong>I</strong>ce — reduce local pain and swelling / 冰敷——减轻局部疼痛和肿胀<br />
• <strong>C</strong>ompression + NSAIDs — short-term adjuncts / 加压 + NSAIDs——短期辅助<br />
• <strong>E</strong>ccentric loading (PT) — the evidence-based cure / 离心负荷（PT）——循证核心治疗<br />
• <strong>P</strong>rogress — gradual return to sport / 渐进——逐步重返运动</p></th>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Achilles Tendon Disorders / 高频知识表 — 跟腱相关疾病

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>

<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>

</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Thompson test interpretation<br />
Thompson 试验解读</td>
<td>Positive = complete Achilles rupture (no plantarflexion when calf squeezed); Negative = tendon structurally intact<br />
阳性 = 跟腱完全断裂（挤压小腿无跖屈）；阴性 = 跟腱结构完整</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Fluoroquinolone-associated tendinopathy<br />
氟喹诺酮相关跟腱病</td>
<td>Ciprofloxacin/levofloxacin → Achilles tendinitis/rupture risk, especially in elderly + corticosteroid users<br />
环丙沙星/左氧氟沙星 → 跟腱炎/断裂风险，尤其老年人 + 皮质类固醇使用者</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Eccentric vs. concentric exercise<br />
离心 vs. 向心运动</td>
<td>Eccentric (lengthening under load) &gt; concentric for tendinopathy remodeling; Alfredson heel-drop protocol is gold standard<br />
离心（负重下延长）&gt; 向心，用于跟腱重塑；Alfredson 跟腱下降方案是金标准</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Corticosteroid injection risk<br />
皮质类固醇注射风险</td>
<td>Peritendinous injection may be used for refractory cases but carries increased tendon rupture risk; avoid intratendinous injection<br />
腱周注射可用于难治性病例，但有增加断裂风险；避免腱内注射</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Complete Achilles rupture management<br />
跟腱完全断裂的处理</td>
<td>Surgical vs. non-surgical have comparable outcomes; younger active patients often prefer surgery; immobilization for 6–8 weeks either way<br />
手术与非手术效果相当；年轻活跃患者常倾向手术；两种方案均需固定 6–8 周</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Haglund deformity<br />
Haglund 畸形</td>
<td>Bony prominence at posterior superior calcaneus → insertional tendinopathy + retrocalcaneal bursitis; "pump bump"<br />
跟骨后上方骨性突起 → 止点型跟腱病 + 跟骨后滑囊炎；俗称"泵包"</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Differential for posterior heel pain<br />
后跟疼痛鉴别诊断</td>
<td>Achilles tendinopathy, retrocalcaneal bursitis, Haglund deformity, plantar fasciitis (inferior heel), calcaneal stress fracture, tarsal tunnel syndrome<br />
跟腱病、跟骨后滑囊炎、Haglund 畸形、足底筋膜炎（足底跟痛）、跟骨应力骨折、跗管综合征</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Fluoroquinolone risk:** Ciprofloxacin and levofloxacin inhibit matrix metalloproteinases and impair collagen synthesis, causing tendinopathy even weeks after stopping the drug — always ask about antibiotic history\
  **氟喹诺酮风险:** 环丙沙星和左氧氟沙星抑制基质金属蛋白酶并损害胶原合成，即使停药数周后仍可导致跟腱病——务必询问抗生素用药史

- **Obesity contribution:** BMI \>30 increases mechanical load on Achilles tendon × 2–3 during walking; weight loss is a disease-modifying intervention\
  **肥胖的影响:** BMI \> 30 使步行时跟腱机械负荷增加 2–3 倍；减重是改变疾病进程的干预措施

- **NSAIDs vs. acetaminophen:** NSAIDs (ibuprofen, naproxen) preferred over acetaminophen for tendinopathy — anti-inflammatory effect more relevant; use short-term (1–2 weeks) to avoid GI/renal effects\
  **NSAIDs vs. 对乙酰氨基酚:** 跟腱病首选 NSAIDs（布洛芬、萘普生）而非对乙酰氨基酚——抗炎作用更相关；短期使用（1–2 周）以避免胃肠道/肾脏副作用

- **Return to sport timeline:** Most patients with non-insertional tendinopathy improve in 3–6 months with eccentric PT; premature return (before pain-free) is the leading cause of recurrence\
  **重返运动时间:** 大多数非止点型跟腱病患者经离心 PT 后 3–6 个月改善；过早重返（疼痛未消）是复发的主要原因

# Question 21 — Attributable Risk from Cigarette Smoking / 吸烟归因危险度

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>10-year cohort study</strong> is conducted to investigate the effect of <strong>cigarette smoking</strong> on the incidence of <strong>head and neck cancers</strong> in adults. A total of <strong>10,000</strong> adult participants with no history of any type of cancer are enrolled in the study; <strong>2000 participants are current cigarette smokers</strong> and <strong>8000 are current nonsmokers</strong> and have never smoked cigarettes. During the 10-year study period, <strong>20 smokers</strong> and <strong>eight nonsmokers</strong> develop head and neck cancer. Based on these data, which of the following best represents the attributable risk from smoking for head and neck cancer among current cigarette smokers?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which value best represents the attributable risk from smoking for head and neck cancer among current cigarette smokers?</strong></p>
<p>A) 0.001<br />
B) 0.009<br />
C) 0.01<br />
D) 0.09<br />
E) 0.1</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: B</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>10-year cohort study<br />
10年队列研究</td>
<td>Cohort studies follow exposed vs. unexposed groups forward in time and directly measure incidence rates — the essential inputs for attributable risk<br />
队列研究前瞻性追踪暴露组与未暴露组，可直接计算发病率，是归因危险度计算的必要前提</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>2000 smokers / 8000 nonsmokers<br />
2000名吸烟者 / 8000名非吸烟者</td>
<td>Unequal group sizes mean raw case counts cannot be compared directly; separate incidence rates must be calculated using the correct denominator for each group<br />
两组人数不等，不能直接比较病例数；必须以各组总数为分母分别计算发病率</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>20 smokers developed cancer<br />
20名吸烟者发生癌症</td>
<td>Numerator for exposed group incidence: 20 ÷ 2000 = 0.010<br />
暴露组发病率的分子：20 ÷ 2000 = 0.010</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>8 nonsmokers developed cancer<br />
8名非吸烟者发生癌症</td>
<td>Numerator for unexposed group incidence: 8 ÷ 8000 = 0.001 — this is the background rate that must be subtracted<br />
未暴露组发病率的分子：8 ÷ 8000 = 0.001——这是必须被减去的背景基线率</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>"Attributable risk… among current cigarette smokers"<br />
"归因危险度……在当前吸烟者中"</td>
<td>Specifies AR (absolute excess risk), not RR (ratio) or PAR (population level) — directs to the subtraction formula Ie − Iu<br />
明确要求计算AR（绝对超额风险），而非RR（比值）或PAR（人群层面）——提示使用减法公式 Ie − Iu</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No history of cancer at enrollment<br />
入组时无癌症病史</td>
<td>Ensures all new cases are truly incident (not prevalent); incidence calculation is valid from time zero<br />
确保所有新发病例均为真实发病事件而非既往患病，保证发病率计算的有效性</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Attributable risk (AR)**, also called **excess risk** or **risk difference**, quantifies how much of the incidence in the **exposed group** exceeds the baseline rate observed in **unexposed individuals** — isolating the contribution of the exposure itself：

**归因危险度（AR）**，又称超额危险度或危险度差，量化暴露组发病率超出未暴露组基线率的部分——从而单独提取暴露本身的贡献：

- Core formula: AR = **Ie** − **Iu** (incidence in exposed minus incidence in unexposed)\
  核心公式：AR = **Ie** − **Iu**（暴露组发病率 减去 未暴露组发病率）

- Ie = 20 ÷ 2000 = **0.010** (smokers' 10-year cumulative incidence)\
  Ie = 20 ÷ 2000 = **0.010**（吸烟者10年累积发病率）

- Iu = 8 ÷ 8000 = **0.001** (nonsmokers' 10-year cumulative incidence — the background rate)\
  Iu = 8 ÷ 8000 = **0.001**（非吸烟者10年累积发病率——背景基线率）

- AR = 0.010 − 0.001 = **0.009** per person over 10 years\
  AR = 0.010 − 0.001 = **0.009**（10年内每人的超额风险）

**Conceptual rule of thumb:** AR answers "How much extra disease does this exposure cause?" — it is an absolute measure useful for quantifying intervention impact. Relative Risk (RR) answers "How many times more likely?" — it is a ratio useful for causal inference. Here RR = 0.010 ÷ 0.001 = 10, but the question asks for AR, not RR.

**概念小窍门:** AR 回答"该暴露额外导致多少疾病？"——是量化干预效果的绝对指标。相对危险度（RR）回答"发病率是多少倍？"——是评估因果关联的比值指标。本题中RR = 10，但题目要求的是AR，不是RR。

## 3. Correct Answer (B) — Attributable Risk = 0.009 / 正确答案 (B) — 归因危险度 = 0.009

**Attributable Risk (AR)** measures the absolute excess incidence in the exposed group that is directly caused by the exposure, after subtracting the background rate:

**归因危险度（AR）** 衡量暴露组中在减去背景率之后，直接由暴露导致的绝对超额发病率：

- Step 1 — incidence in exposed: 20 ÷ 2000 = 0.010\
  第一步——暴露组发病率：20 ÷ 2000 = 0.010

- Step 2 — incidence in unexposed: 8 ÷ 8000 = 0.001\
  第二步——未暴露组发病率：8 ÷ 8000 = 0.001

- Step 3 — AR = 0.010 − 0.001 = **0.009**\
  第三步——AR = 0.010 − 0.001 = **0.009**

- Interpretation: of the 10/1,000 smokers who develop head and neck cancer, 9/1,000 cases are attributable to smoking; 1/1,000 would have occurred regardless\
  解读：每1000名吸烟者中10例头颈癌，其中9例归因于吸烟；1例即使不吸烟也会发生

**Diagnosis:** The critical insight is that smoking does not account for 100% of cancer risk even in smokers — some baseline cancer risk exists in all humans. AR isolates only the smoking-specific excess above that baseline.

**诊断:** 关键认识是即使在吸烟者中，吸烟也不能解释100%的癌症风险——所有人都有一定的基线癌症风险。AR仅提取吸烟相关的超额风险，高于该基线的部分。

**Treatment:** This is a biostatistics question. Public health application: if smoking cessation eliminated all smoking-attributable risk, it would prevent 0.009 (9 per 1,000) head/neck cancer cases over 10 years in this population.

**治疗:** 此为生物统计题。公共卫生应用：若戒烟能消除所有归因于吸烟的风险，可在10年内预防每1000名吸烟者中9例头颈癌的发生。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — 0.001<br />
A — 0.001</td>
<td>Wrong — this equals only Iu (nonsmokers' incidence: 8/8000 = 0.001); it represents background risk alone, not the excess risk attributable to smoking<br />
错误——这仅等于Iu（非吸烟者发病率：8/8000 = 0.001）；代表背景基线风险，而非归因于吸烟的超额风险</td>
<td>Stops the calculation at Iu instead of computing Ie − Iu<br />
计算停在Iu处，未完成Ie − Iu的减法</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — 0.009 ✓<br />
B — 0.009 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — AR = Ie − Iu = (20/2000) − (8/8000) = 0.010 − 0.001 = 0.009<br />
正确——AR = Ie − Iu = (20/2000) − (8/8000) = 0.010 − 0.001 = 0.009</td>
<td>Applies the subtraction formula correctly with proper denominators for each group<br />
正确使用减法公式，各组分母准确</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — 0.01<br />
C — 0.01</td>
<td>Wrong — this equals only Ie (smokers' incidence: 20/2000 = 0.010); it does not subtract the background rate, overstating smoking's contribution<br />
错误——这仅等于Ie（吸烟者发病率：20/2000 = 0.010）；未减去背景率，高估了吸烟的贡献</td>
<td>Most common trap: correctly calculates exposed incidence but omits the defining subtraction step of AR<br />
最常见陷阱：正确算出暴露组发病率，却遗漏AR计算的核心减法步骤</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — 0.09<br />
D — 0.09</td>
<td>Wrong — likely from multiplying the correct AR (0.009) by 10 (the study duration in years); study duration is already incorporated into the cumulative incidence denominators<br />
错误——可能源于将正确的AR（0.009）乘以研究年限10年；研究年限已体现在累积发病率的分母中，不应再乘</td>
<td>Misapplies study duration as a multiplier to an already-cumulative incidence measure<br />
将研究年限作为乘数错误地应用于本已是累积发病率的指标</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — 0.1<br />
E — 0.1</td>
<td>Wrong — likely from multiplying exposed incidence (0.010) by 10 (years); reflects fundamental confusion between annual incidence rate and 10-year cumulative incidence<br />
错误——可能源于将暴露组发病率（0.010）乘以10（年）；反映出对年发病率与10年累积发病率的根本混淆</td>
<td>Confuses cumulative incidence (already aggregated over 10 years) with an annualized rate requiring year-multiplication<br />
将10年累积发病率（已涵盖整个研究期）与需乘以年数的年化率相混淆</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most seductive distractor is C (0.01) — it requires only one correct calculation (20/2000) and misses only the final subtraction; examinees who skip the "background rate" step land here.*

最具迷惑性的干扰项是C（0.01）——只需一步正确计算（20/2000），仅遗漏最后的减法；跳过"背景率"步骤的考生会选到这里。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Attributable Risk vs. Relative Risk vs. Population Attributable Risk / 归因危险度 vs. 相对危险度 vs. 人群归因危险度

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Attributable Risk (AR)</strong><br />
<strong>归因危险度</strong></th>
<th><strong>Relative Risk (RR)</strong><br />
<strong>相对危险度</strong></th>
<th><strong>Population AR (PAR)</strong><br />
<strong>人群归因危险度</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Definition<br />
定义</td>
<td>Absolute excess incidence due to exposure<br />
暴露导致的绝对超额发病率</td>
<td>Ratio of incidence: exposed vs. unexposed<br />
暴露组与未暴露组发病率之比</td>
<td>Excess incidence in entire population attributable to exposure<br />
整个人群中归因于暴露的超额发病率</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Formula<br />
公式</td>
<td>Ie − Iu<br />
Ie − Iu</td>
<td>Ie ÷ Iu<br />
Ie ÷ Iu</td>
<td>Ipop − Iu<br />
Ipop − Iu</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>This question<br />
本题结果</td>
<td>0.010 − 0.001 = <strong>0.009</strong><br />
0.010 − 0.001 = <strong>0.009</strong></td>
<td>0.010 ÷ 0.001 = <strong>10</strong><br />
0.010 ÷ 0.001 = <strong>10</strong></td>
<td>Requires total population incidence (not given)<br />
需要总人群发病率（题目未给出）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Question answered<br />
回答的问题</td>
<td>"How much extra disease from exposure?"<br />
"暴露额外导致多少疾病？"</td>
<td>"How many times more likely with exposure?"<br />
"有暴露时发病率是多少倍？"</td>
<td>"How much disease disappears if exposure eliminated population-wide?"<br />
"消除全人群暴露后能减少多少疾病？"</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Study design needed<br />
所需研究设计</td>
<td>Cohort or RCT (requires incidence)<br />
队列研究或RCT（需要发病率）</td>
<td>Cohort or RCT (incidence); OR approximates in case-control<br />
队列/RCT；病例对照用OR近似</td>
<td>Cohort + prevalence of exposure in population<br />
队列研究 + 人群暴露率</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Public health utility<br />
公共卫生用途</td>
<td>Quantifies intervention benefit; NNH = 1/AR<br />
量化干预获益；NNH = 1/AR</td>
<td>Strength of causal association<br />
因果关联强度</td>
<td>Identifies highest-priority exposures to target for policy<br />
确定政策优先干预的暴露因素</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**Attributable Risk = Incidence(smokers) − Incidence(nonsmokers) = 20/2000 − 8/8000 = 0.010 − 0.001 = 0.009, the absolute excess head and neck cancer risk caused by cigarette smoking.**

**归因危险度 = 吸烟者发病率 − 非吸烟者发病率 = 20/2000 − 8/8000 = 0.010 − 0.001 = 0.009，即吸烟导致的头颈癌绝对超额风险。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — AR "SUBTRACT" Formula Steps / 记忆钩 — AR "减法"五步口诀:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>S</strong>mokers' rate first — Ie = cases in exposed ÷ total exposed = 20/2000 = 0.010 / 先算吸烟者发病率——Ie = 暴露组病例 ÷ 暴露组总数 = 0.010<br />
• <strong>U</strong>nexposed rate second — Iu = cases in unexposed ÷ total unexposed = 8/8000 = 0.001 / 再算非吸烟者发病率——Iu = 未暴露组病例 ÷ 未暴露组总数 = 0.001<br />
• <strong>B</strong>ackground subtract — AR = Ie − Iu = 0.010 − 0.001 = <strong>0.009</strong> / 减去背景率——AR = Ie − Iu = <strong>0.009</strong><br />
• <strong>T</strong>rap = stopping at Ie alone (answer C = 0.01); this is incidence, not attributable risk / 陷阱 = 只算到Ie就停（选项C = 0.01）；那是发病率，不是归因危险度<br />
• <strong>R</strong>atio (RR) ≠ AR — RR = Ie/Iu = 10 answers "how many times more," AR answers "how much extra" / 相对危险度（RR）≠ AR——RR = 10回答"多少倍"，AR回答"多多少"</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Epidemiologic Risk Measures in Cohort Studies / 高频知识表 — 队列研究中的流行病学风险指标

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Attributable Risk (AR) definition and formula<br />
归因危险度定义与公式</td>
<td>AR = Ie − Iu; absolute excess risk in the exposed; also called "risk difference" or "excess risk"; requires incidence data (cohort or RCT only)<br />
AR = Ie − Iu；暴露人群的绝对超额风险；又称"危险度差"或"超额风险"；需要发病率数据（仅限队列研究或RCT）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Relative Risk (RR) formula and interpretation<br />
相对危险度公式与解读</td>
<td>RR = Ie/Iu; RR = 1 means no association; RR &gt; 1 means exposure increases risk; RR &lt; 1 means exposure is protective; used for strength of causal association<br />
RR = Ie/Iu；RR = 1表示无关联；RR &gt; 1表示暴露增加风险；RR &lt; 1表示暴露具有保护作用；用于衡量因果关联强度</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Attributable Risk Percent (AR%)<br />
归因危险度百分比</td>
<td>AR% = AR/Ie × 100% = (Ie − Iu)/Ie × 100%; here = 0.009/0.010 × 100% = 90%; means 90% of head/neck cancer in smokers is caused by smoking<br />
AR% = AR/Ie × 100% = (Ie − Iu)/Ie × 100%；本题 = 90%；意即吸烟者中90%的头颈癌由吸烟引起</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Number Needed to Harm (NNH)<br />
致害需治数</td>
<td>NNH = 1/AR = 1/0.009 ≈ 111; approximately 111 people must smoke for 10 years to cause 1 additional attributable head/neck cancer case; complements NNT in clinical communication<br />
NNH = 1/AR = 1/0.009 ≈ 111；约111人吸烟10年才会额外导致1例归因性头颈癌；与NNT互为补充用于临床沟通</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Case-control study limitation for AR<br />
病例对照研究对AR计算的局限</td>
<td>Case-control studies cannot directly calculate incidence rates, so AR cannot be directly derived; OR approximates RR when disease incidence is rare (&lt; 10%)<br />
病例对照研究无法直接计算发病率，因此不能直接计算AR；当疾病稀少时（&lt;10%），OR可近似RR</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Population Attributable Risk (PAR) vs. AR<br />
人群归因危险度 vs. 归因危险度</td>
<td>PAR = Ipop − Iu; requires knowing both unexposed incidence and total population incidence; PAR depends on prevalence of exposure in the population, not just strength of association<br />
PAR = Ipop − Iu；需要同时知道未暴露组发病率和总人群发病率；PAR取决于暴露在人群中的流行率，不仅仅取决于关联强度</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Cohort study design features<br />
队列研究设计特点</td>
<td>Prospective; exposure → outcome temporal direction; directly measures cumulative incidence; allows calculation of both AR and RR; best design for establishing temporal precedence<br />
前瞻性；暴露→结局的时间方向；直接测量累积发病率；可同时计算AR和RR；建立时间先后关系的最佳研究设计</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Attributable Risk Percent (AR%):**: AR% = AR/Ie = 0.009/0.010 = 90%; means if smoking were eliminated, 90% of head/neck cancers in current smokers could theoretically be prevented\
  **归因危险度百分比（AR%）:** AR% = AR/Ie = 0.009/0.010 = 90%；意即若消除吸烟，理论上可预防吸烟者中90%的头颈癌

- **Number Needed to Harm (NNH):**: NNH = 1/AR = 1/0.009 ≈ 111; useful for patient counseling — "approximately 111 people need to smoke for 10 years to cause one extra cancer attributable to smoking"\
  **致害需治数（NNH）:** NNH = 1/AR = 1/0.009 ≈ 111；用于患者宣教——"约111人吸烟10年才会额外导致一例归因性癌症"

- **Variant — when groups are equal in size:**: If both groups had 5,000 participants, raw case counts could be compared directly — but always recalculate rates to be safe; NBME frequently sets up unequal groups to test this instinct\
  **题目变式——两组人数相等时:** 若两组各5000人，可直接比较病例数——但为安全起见应始终计算率；NBME常设置不等组人数来测试这一直觉

- **Confounding caveat:**: Smokers in this cohort may also differ in alcohol use, HPV exposure, and dietary habits — these confounders could inflate the observed AR; randomization (RCT) eliminates confounding, but this is an observational cohort\
  **混杂因素提示:** 本队列中吸烟者在饮酒、HPV暴露和饮食习惯上也可能与非吸烟者不同——这些混杂因素可能夸大观察到的AR；随机化（RCT）可消除混杂，但本研究是观察性队列

# Question 22 — Neurofibromatosis Type 1 (Annual Ophthalmologic Screening) / 1型神经纤维瘤病（年度眼科筛查）

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>15-year-old girl</strong> is brought to the office for a well-child examination. She has no history of serious illness and takes no medications. Her temperature is 36.9°C (98.4°F), pulse is 86/min, respirations are 16/min, and blood pressure is <strong>100/60 mm Hg</strong>. A <strong>photograph of the back is shown</strong>. The remainder of the examination shows no abnormalities. In addition to routine annual growth and development assessments, which of the following is the most appropriate recommendation regarding routine screening in this patient?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate recommendation regarding routine screening in this patient?</strong></p>
<p>A) Yearly CT scan of the chest and abdomen<br />
B) Yearly MRI of the brain<br />
C) Yearly nerve conduction studies<br />
D) Yearly ophthalmologic examination<br />
E) No additional screening is indicated</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: D</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

考查AAP 2019指南：眼科检查年度推荐；影像学检查不作为常规</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Neurofibromatosis type 1** is caused by loss-of-function mutations in the **NF1 tumor suppressor gene** (chromosome 17q11.2), which encodes **neurofibromin**, a **RAS-GTPase activating protein**. Loss of neurofibromin leads to uncontrolled **RAS/MAPK pathway activation**, driving abnormal proliferation of **neural crest-derived cells**:

**1型神经纤维瘤病**由**NF1抑癌基因**（17号染色体q11.2）功能缺失突变引起，编码**神经纤维蛋白**（一种**RAS-GTP酶激活蛋白**）。神经纤维蛋白缺失导致**RAS/MAPK通路**失控激活，驱动**神经嵴来源细胞**异常增殖：

- Cutaneous neurofibromas: benign peripheral nerve sheath tumors from Schwann cells and fibroblasts\
  皮肤神经纤维瘤：来源于施万细胞和成纤维细胞的良性周围神经鞘瘤

- Café-au-lait macules: melanocyte dysfunction causing focal hyperpigmentation\
  牛奶咖啡斑：黑色素细胞功能异常导致局灶性色素沉着

- Lisch nodules: melanocytic hamartomas of the iris (pathognomonic)\
  Lisch结节：虹膜黑色素细胞错构瘤（病理性特征）

- Optic pathway gliomas (OPGs): low-grade pilocytic astrocytomas along optic nerves/chiasm, peak incidence before age 6\
  视路胶质瘤（OPGs）：沿视神经/视交叉的低度星形细胞瘤，发病高峰在6岁前

- Pheochromocytoma: catecholamine-secreting adrenal tumor from chromaffin cells (rare, ~1%)\
  嗜铬细胞瘤：嗜铬细胞来源的肾上腺儿茶酚胺分泌瘤（少见，约1%）

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** OPGs are the most vision-threatening complication of NF1 in children and are often asymptomatic until significant visual loss occurs — making annual ophthalmologic screening the critical early-detection tool.

**解剖小窍门:** 视路胶质瘤是NF1儿童中最威胁视力的并发症，常无症状直至出现明显视力损失——因此年度眼科筛查是关键的早期发现手段。

---

## 3. Correct Answer (D) — Annual Ophthalmologic Examination / 正确答案 (D) — 年度眼科检查

**Optic pathway glioma (OPG)** is a low-grade CNS neoplasm occurring in 15–20% of NF1 patients, most commonly before age 6, and is often asymptomatic in early stages:

**视路胶质瘤（OPG）**是发生于15-20%的NF1患者的低级别CNS肿瘤，多在6岁前出现，早期常无症状：

- Annual ophthalmologic exam detects visual acuity changes, color vision loss, proptosis, and optic disc pallor before symptomatic progression\
  年度眼科检查在症状进展前发现视力变化、色觉丧失、眼球突出和视盘苍白

- Visual field testing supplements examination; slit-lamp identifies Lisch nodules confirming NF1 diagnosis\
  视野检测辅助检查；裂隙灯识别Lisch结节以确认NF1诊断

- AAP 2019 guidelines mandate annual multidisciplinary screening: ophthalmologic, neurologic, dermatologic, BP monitoring, growth/bone health\
  AAP 2019指南要求年度多学科筛查：眼科、神经科、皮肤科、血压监测、生长/骨健康

**Diagnosis:** NF1 is a clinical diagnosis requiring ≥2 of: ≥6 café-au-lait macules, ≥2 neurofibromas, axillary/inguinal freckling, OPG, ≥2 Lisch nodules, distinctive osseous lesion, or first-degree relative with NF1.

**诊断:** NF1为临床诊断，需满足以下≥2条：≥6个牛奶咖啡斑、≥2个神经纤维瘤、腋窝/腹股沟雀斑、视路胶质瘤、≥2个Lisch结节、特征性骨病变，或一级亲属患NF1。

**Treatment:** No cure; management is complication-driven — surgical resection or MEK inhibitor (selumetinib) for symptomatic OPGs, anti-epileptic drugs for seizures, antihypertensives for pheochromocytoma, genetic counseling.

**治疗:** 无根治方法；以并发症为导向——有症状OPG行手术切除或MEK抑制剂（司美替尼），癫痫用抗癫痫药，嗜铬细胞瘤用降压药，辅以遗传咨询。

---

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Yearly CT scan of the chest and abdomen<br />
A — 每年胸腹部CT扫描</td>
<td>WRONG — AAP 2019 guidelines state imaging should be performed "as needed," not routinely; CT adds radiation risk without proven benefit in asymptomatic NF1<br />
错误——AAP 2019指南规定影像学检查"按需进行"，不常规推荐；对无症状NF1患者CT增加辐射风险且无已证实的获益</td>
<td>Imaging is symptom-driven, not annual protocol<br />
影像学以症状驱动，非年度常规</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Yearly MRI of the brain<br />
B — 每年脑部MRI</td>
<td>WRONG — Routine brain MRI is not recommended for asymptomatic NF1; MRI is indicated if neurologic symptoms arise or OPG is suspected after ophthalmic screening<br />
错误——无症状NF1不推荐常规脑MRI；MRI适用于出现神经症状或眼科筛查怀疑OPG时</td>
<td>Annual ophthalmic exam is the first-line OPG surveillance, not MRI<br />
年度眼科检查是OPG监测的一线手段，而非MRI</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Yearly nerve conduction studies<br />
C — 每年神经传导检查</td>
<td>WRONG — NCS is not useful for detecting new neurofibromas; neuroimaging (MRI) is preferred if a symptomatic neurofibroma is suspected<br />
错误——NCS对发现新神经纤维瘤无价值；若怀疑有症状的神经纤维瘤，首选神经影像（MRI）</td>
<td>New neurofibromas are detected clinically; NCS does not add surveillance value<br />
新发神经纤维瘤临床发现；NCS无监测价值</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Yearly ophthalmologic examination ✓<br />
D — 每年眼科检查 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Per AAP 2019, annual ophthalmologic examination is mandatory in NF1 to detect OPGs and Lisch nodules before symptomatic vision loss<br />
正确——根据AAP 2019，NF1患者须每年进行眼科检查，在有症状的视力损失前发现OPG和Lisch结节</td>
<td>Only modality with annual guideline mandate for NF1 screening<br />
唯一有年度指南强制要求的NF1筛查手段</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — No additional screening is indicated<br />
E — 无需额外筛查</td>
<td>WRONG — NF1 requires annual multidisciplinary surveillance; without ophthalmologic screening, OPGs and pheochromocytoma can cause irreversible complications<br />
错误——NF1需要年度多学科监测；无眼科筛查，OPG和嗜铬细胞瘤可导致不可逆并发症</td>
<td>NF1 is a high-surveillance condition, not an observe-and-wait diagnosis<br />
NF1是高监测需求疾病，不能观望等待</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Choice B (brain MRI) — it seems logical given OPG risk, but AAP guidelines reserve MRI for when ophthalmic screening raises concern, not as routine annual surveillance.*

选项B（脑部MRI）最具迷惑性——考虑到OPG风险看似合理，但AAP指南将MRI保留用于眼科筛查发现异常后，而非常规年度检查。

---

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**NF1 (autosomal dominant, NF1 gene on chr 17) causes café-au-lait spots, neurofibromas, Lisch nodules, and optic pathway gliomas — requiring annual ophthalmologic screening per AAP 2019 to catch asymptomatic OPGs before irreversible vision loss.**

**NF1（常染色体显性遗传，17号染色体NF1基因）表现为牛奶咖啡斑、神经纤维瘤、Lisch结节和视路胶质瘤——根据AAP 2019，须年度眼科筛查，在不可逆视力损失前发现无症状OPG。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "CAFÉ" Features of NF1 / 记忆钩 — NF1的"CAFÉ"特征:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>C</strong>afé-au-lait macules — ≥6 spots ≥5 mm (prepubertal) = diagnostic criterion / 牛奶咖啡斑——≥6个、≥5mm（青春期前）为诊断标准<br />
• <strong>A</strong>xillary/inguinal freckling — Crowe's sign, pathognomonic for NF1 / 腋窝/腹股沟雀斑——Crowe征，NF1病理特征<br />
• <strong>F</strong>ibromas (neurofibromas) — benign nerve sheath tumors, can undergo malignant transformation / 神经纤维瘤——良性神经鞘瘤，可恶变<br />
• <strong>E</strong>ye findings — Lisch nodules (iris hamartomas) + OPGs requiring annual eye exam / 眼部表现——Lisch结节（虹膜错构瘤）+需年度眼科检查的视路胶质瘤</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>
