## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Neurofibromatosis Type 1 Diagnosis & Complications / 高频知识表 — NF1诊断标准与并发症

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>NF1 diagnostic criteria (NIH)<br />
NF1诊断标准（NIH）</td>
<td>≥2 of: ≥6 café-au-lait macules, ≥2 neurofibromas or 1 plexiform, axillary/inguinal freckling, OPG, ≥2 Lisch nodules, distinctive osseous lesion (sphenoid dysplasia), 1st-degree relative with NF1<br />
≥2条：≥6个牛奶咖啡斑、≥2个神经纤维瘤或1个丛状神经纤维瘤、腋窝/腹股沟雀斑、视路胶质瘤、≥2个Lisch结节、特征性骨损害（蝶骨发育不良）、一级亲属患NF1</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Genetics<br />
遗传学</td>
<td>Autosomal dominant; NF1 gene on chromosome 17q11.2; encodes neurofibromin (RAS-GAP); 50% are de novo mutations; complete penetrance, variable expressivity<br />
常染色体显性遗传；17号染色体q11.2的NF1基因；编码神经纤维蛋白（RAS-GAP）；50%为新发突变；完全外显，表现度可变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Optic pathway gliomas<br />
视路胶质瘤</td>
<td>15–20% of NF1 patients; pilocytic astrocytoma (WHO grade 1); peak incidence &lt;6 years; often asymptomatic; can cause vision loss, proptosis, precocious puberty (if hypothalamic involvement)<br />
15-20%的NF1患者；毛细胞型星形细胞瘤（WHO I级）；发病高峰&lt;6岁；常无症状；可致视力丧失、眼球突出、性早熟（下丘脑受累）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pheochromocytoma<br />
嗜铬细胞瘤</td>
<td>~1% of NF1; catecholamine excess causes episodic hypertension, headache, diaphoresis; monitor BP annually; diagnose with 24hr urine catecholamines/metanephrines<br />
约1%的NF1；儿茶酚胺过多引起阵发性高血压、头痛、出汗；每年监测血压；通过24h尿儿茶酚胺/甲氧基肾上腺素诊断</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Malignant peripheral nerve sheath tumor<br />
恶性周围神经鞘瘤</td>
<td>Lifetime risk ~10% in NF1 (vs 0.001% general population); suspect if rapid neurofibroma growth, pain, new neurologic deficit; MRI + biopsy for diagnosis<br />
NF1终生风险约10%（普通人群0.001%）；若神经纤维瘤快速增大、疼痛、新发神经功能缺损则怀疑；MRI+活检确诊</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>NF1 vs NF2<br />
NF1与NF2鉴别</td>
<td>NF1 (chr 17): café-au-lait, neurofibromas, Lisch nodules, OPGs; NF2 (chr 22, merlin protein): bilateral acoustic neuromas (vestibular schwannomas), cataracts, meningiomas — no café-au-lait or Lisch nodules<br />
NF1（17号染色体）：牛奶咖啡斑、神经纤维瘤、Lisch结节、OPG；NF2（22号染色体，merlin蛋白）：双侧听神经瘤（前庭神经鞘瘤）、白内障、脑膜瘤——无牛奶咖啡斑或Lisch结节</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of café-au-lait spots:** McCune-Albright syndrome (large, irregular "coast of Maine" spots + polyostotic fibrous dysplasia + precocious puberty) vs. NF1 (smooth "coast of California" spots); isolated café-au-lait spots are common in the general population and not diagnostic alone\
  **牛奶咖啡斑鉴别:** McCune-Albright综合征（大片不规则"缅因海岸"斑+多骨纤维发育不良+性早熟）vs. NF1（边缘光滑"加利福尼亚海岸"斑）；孤立牛奶咖啡斑在普通人群中常见，单独不具诊断意义

- **Key complication requiring urgent workup:** Plexiform neurofibromas are pathognomonic for NF1 and have the highest risk of malignant transformation to MPNST; rapid growth or new pain demands MRI and surgical evaluation\
  **需紧急评估的关键并发症:** 丛状神经纤维瘤是NF1病理特征，恶变为恶性周围神经鞘瘤风险最高；快速增大或新发疼痛需MRI和外科评估

- **Treatment advance:** Selumetinib (MEK1/2 inhibitor) is FDA-approved (2020) for pediatric NF1 patients ≥2 years with symptomatic, inoperable plexiform neurofibromas — first drug approval specifically for NF1\
  **治疗进展:** 司美替尼（MEK1/2抑制剂）于2020年获FDA批准，用于≥2岁有症状、不可手术的丛状神经纤维瘤NF1儿童患者——NF1首个专项药物批准

- **Exam variant:** If the question describes bilateral acoustic neuromas (hearing loss, tinnitus) in a young adult — think NF2, not NF1; NF2 does NOT have the classic skin findings of NF1\
  **题目变式:** 若题目描述年轻成人双侧听神经瘤（听力丧失、耳鸣）——考虑NF2而非NF1；NF2没有NF1的经典皮肤表现

# Question 23 — Sex Cord-Stromal Ovarian Tumor with Precocious Puberty / 性索间质卵巢肿瘤伴性早熟

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>7-year-old girl</strong> is brought to the physician by her mother because she is concerned that her daughter has had <strong>two episodes of vaginal bleeding</strong> during the past 3 months. She also has had <strong>breast development</strong> during this time. Development had been appropriate for age. She is at the 48th percentile for height and 47th percentile for weight and BMI. <strong>Breast development is sexual maturity rating (SMR) stage 2</strong>, and <strong>axillary and pubic hair development is SMR stage 3</strong>. Examination shows normal-appearing external genitalia. Pelvic examination is deferred. An MRI of the pelvis shows a normal vagina and cervix. The uterus is <strong>4 cm long</strong>, and a <strong>7 × 6-cm left ovarian mass</strong> is seen.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Chromosomal analysis<br />
B) Measurement of serum CA 125 concentration<br />
C) CT scan of the pituitary gland<br />
D) Fine-needle aspiration of the mass<br />
E) Left oophorectomy</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>7-year-old girl with breast development and vaginal bleeding<br />
7岁女孩出现乳房发育和阴道出血</td>
<td>Secondary sexual characteristics before age 8 in females = precocious puberty by definition<br />
8岁前出现第二性征 = 性早熟定义</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>SMR stage 2 breast + SMR stage 3 pubic/axillary hair<br />
乳房SMR 2期 + 阴毛/腋毛SMR 3期</td>
<td>Multiple stages of sexual development simultaneously indicate significant exogenous hormonal excess<br />
多阶段性发育同时存在，提示显著的外源性激素超量</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Vaginal bleeding at age 7<br />
7岁出现阴道出血</td>
<td>Indicates estrogen stimulation sufficient to cause endometrial proliferation and shedding<br />
提示雌激素刺激足以引起子宫内膜增生和脱落</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>7 × 6-cm left ovarian mass on MRI<br />
MRI示7×6 cm左侧卵巢肿块</td>
<td>Large gonadal mass = most likely autonomous estrogen source causing peripheral precocious puberty<br />
较大的性腺肿块 = 最可能的自主雌激素来源，导致外周性性早熟</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Uterus 4 cm long<br />
子宫长4 cm</td>
<td>Prepubertal uterus is normally &lt;3 cm; enlargement confirms end-organ estrogen stimulation from tumor<br />
青春期前子宫正常&lt;3 cm；子宫增大证实来自肿瘤的靶器官雌激素刺激</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Development appropriate for age prior to this episode<br />
此前发育均正常</td>
<td>Acute onset argues against idiopathic central precocious puberty and points to a new tumor-driven etiology<br />
急性起病不支持特发性中枢性性早熟，指向新发肿瘤驱动的病因</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Sex cord-stromal tumors** of the ovary (most commonly **juvenile granulosa cell tumors** in children) autonomously produce **estradiol** independent of the hypothalamic-pituitary-gonadal (HPG) axis, causing **peripheral (GnRH-independent) precocious puberty**：

**卵巢性索间质肿瘤**（儿童最常见为**幼年型颗粒细胞瘤**）自主产生**雌二醇**，不依赖下丘脑-垂体-性腺（HPG）轴，导致**外周性（GnRH非依赖性）性早熟**：

- Tumor granulosa cells constitutively secrete estradiol → breast development, vaginal bleeding, uterine enlargement\
  肿瘤颗粒细胞持续分泌雌二醇 → 乳房发育、阴道出血、子宫增大

- High peripheral estrogen suppresses LH/FSH via negative feedback → distinguishes from central precocious puberty where LH/FSH would be elevated\
  外周高雌激素通过负反馈抑制LH/FSH → 区别于中枢性性早熟（后者LH/FSH升高）

- Adrenal androgens (not tumor-derived) explain SMR 3 pubic/axillary hair — adrenarche is an independent maturational process\
  肾上腺雄激素（非肿瘤来源）解释了SMR 3阴毛/腋毛——肾上腺机能初现是独立的成熟过程

- Ovarian mass may be malignant (juvenile granulosa cell tumor has malignant potential) → surgical removal is both diagnostic and therapeutic\
  卵巢肿块可能为恶性（幼年型颗粒细胞瘤具有恶性潜能）→ 手术切除兼具诊断和治疗作用

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** A prepubertal uterus measures ~2–3 cm; a uterus of 4 cm in a 7-year-old confirms estrogen-driven end-organ stimulation from an exogenous (tumor) source rather than normal variation.

**解剖小窍门:** 青春期前子宫约2–3 cm；7岁女孩子宫达4 cm，证实了来自外源性（肿瘤）雌激素驱动的靶器官刺激，而非正常变异。

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Left Oophorectomy for Ovarian Sex Cord-Stromal Tumor / 正确答案 (E) — 卵巢性索间质肿瘤的左侧卵巢切除术

**Left oophorectomy** is the definitive management for a large ovarian mass causing peripheral precocious puberty in a child：

**左侧卵巢切除术**是儿童大型卵巢肿块导致外周性性早熟的最终治疗手段：

- Surgical resection removes the autonomous estrogen-producing tumor → precocious puberty symptoms resolve\
  手术切除消除自主产生雌激素的肿瘤 → 性早熟症状消退

- Provides adequate tissue for histologic diagnosis, distinguishing granulosa cell tumor from teratoma, dysgerminoma, or other masses\
  提供足够组织进行组织学诊断，区分颗粒细胞瘤与畸胎瘤、无性细胞瘤或其他肿块

- Avoids the peritoneal seeding risk that fine-needle aspiration would carry if the mass is malignant\
  避免若肿块为恶性时细针穿刺活检导致的腹膜播散风险

- Delay in resection increases metastasis risk if malignant and prolongs inappropriate sex hormone exposure\
  若为恶性，延迟切除会增加转移风险并延长不适当的性激素暴露

**Diagnosis:** A 7-year-old with isosexual precocious puberty (breast development + vaginal bleeding + pubic/axillary hair) and a 7 × 6-cm ovarian mass → sex cord-stromal tumor (likely juvenile granulosa cell tumor) producing autonomous estrogen; a peripheral source has been identified, so no central (pituitary/CNS) workup is warranted before proceeding to surgery.

**诊断:** 7岁女孩出现同性性早熟（乳房发育+阴道出血+阴毛/腋毛）伴7×6 cm卵巢肿块 → 性索间质肿瘤（可能为幼年型颗粒细胞瘤）自主产生雌激素；已确定外周来源，术前无需进行中枢性（垂体/CNS）病因检查。

**Treatment:** Left oophorectomy → histopathologic analysis → if malignant, surgical staging and possible adjuvant chemotherapy; precocious puberty resolves following tumor removal.

**治疗:** 左侧卵巢切除术 → 组织病理学分析 → 若为恶性，手术分期及可能的辅助化疗；肿瘤切除后性早熟消退。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Chromosomal analysis<br />
A — 染色体分析</td>
<td>Genetic causes of precocious puberty (e.g., McCune-Albright GNAS mutation) are somatic point mutations not detectable on karyotype; the identified ovarian mass is far more likely the cause<br />
导致性早熟的遗传原因（如McCune-Albright的GNAS突变）是体细胞点突变，核型分析无法检测；已发现的卵巢肿块更可能是病因</td>
<td>Chromosomal analysis detects structural chromosome abnormalities (trisomy, deletions), not activating point mutations like GNAS<br />
染色体分析检测染色体结构异常（三体、缺失），而非GNAS等激活性点突变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Measurement of serum CA 125 concentration<br />
B — 测定血清CA 125浓度</td>
<td>CA-125 is nonspecific (elevated in many benign and malignant conditions) and would not change management — surgical resection is indicated regardless of CA-125 result<br />
CA-125无特异性（多种良恶性情况均升高），不会改变治疗方案——无论CA-125结果如何均需手术切除</td>
<td>CA-125 is most useful for monitoring adult epithelial ovarian cancer recurrence; AFP and β-hCG are more relevant for pediatric germ cell tumors<br />
CA-125最适用于成人上皮性卵巢癌复发监测；AFP和β-hCG对儿童生殖细胞肿瘤更相关</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — CT scan of the pituitary gland<br />
C — 垂体CT扫描</td>
<td>Pituitary imaging evaluates central precocious puberty caused by CNS lesions activating the HPG axis; this patient has a large ovarian mass making peripheral PP far more likely; no CNS symptoms are present<br />
垂体影像学评估CNS病变激活HPG轴导致的中枢性性早熟；本患者有大型卵巢肿块，外周性性早熟可能性更大；无CNS症状</td>
<td>Central PP: LH/FSH elevated, GnRH stimulation test positive; Peripheral PP: LH/FSH suppressed by negative feedback — pituitary imaging not indicated when a peripheral source is found<br />
中枢性性早熟：LH/FSH升高，GnRH激发试验阳性；外周性性早熟：LH/FSH被负反馈抑制——发现外周来源时不需垂体影像</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Fine-needle aspiration of the mass<br />
D — 肿块细针穿刺活检</td>
<td>FNA risks peritoneal seeding if the mass is malignant; yields less tissue than excision; delays definitive treatment and prolongs estrogen excess<br />
若肿块为恶性，FNA有腹膜播散风险；获取组织量少于切除；延迟最终治疗并延长雌激素过量</td>
<td>Principle for potentially malignant ovarian masses: excision (not biopsy) is simultaneously diagnostic, therapeutic, and avoids seeding<br />
可能为恶性的卵巢肿块处理原则：切除（非活检）同时具有诊断、治疗作用且避免播散</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Left oophorectomy ✓<br />
E — 左侧卵巢切除术 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — removes the autonomous estrogen source, provides histologic diagnosis, and eliminates malignant seeding risk in one definitive step<br />
正确——一步切除自主雌激素来源，提供组织学诊断，消除恶性播散风险</td>
<td>The mass is identified, large (7×6 cm), and fully explains the clinical picture; surgery is the only step that is simultaneously diagnostic, therapeutic, and curative<br />
肿块已明确、较大（7×6 cm），完全解释临床表现；手术是唯一同时具有诊断、治疗和根治作用的措施</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Choice C (CT pituitary) — CNS evaluation is appropriate for idiopathic central precocious puberty, but this patient has an obvious large ovarian mass that fully accounts for her symptoms, making central workup unnecessary before proceeding directly to surgical resection.*

最具迷惑性的干扰项是Choice C（垂体CT）——CNS评估适用于特发性中枢性性早熟，但本患者有明显的大型卵巢肿块，完全可以解释其症状，因此在直接进行手术切除前无需中枢检查。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Central vs. Peripheral Precocious Puberty / 中枢性与外周性性早熟的鉴别

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Central (GnRH-Dependent)</strong><br />
<strong>中枢性（GnRH依赖性）</strong></th>
<th><strong>Peripheral (GnRH-Independent)</strong><br />

<tr>
<td>Mechanism<br />
机制</td>
<td>Early activation of HPG axis → pulsatile GnRH release<br />
HPG轴提前激活 → GnRH脉冲释放</td>
<td>Autonomous sex steroid production from gonad, adrenal, or exogenous source<br />
来自性腺、肾上腺或外源性来源的自主性激素产生</td>

<td>Elevated (pubertal range)<br />

<td>Suppressed by negative feedback<br />
被负反馈抑制，偏低</td>

<td>Positive — LH surges<br />

特发性（最常见），CNS肿瘤，下丘脑错构瘤</td>
<td>Sex cord-stromal tumor, McCune-Albright, CAH, adrenal tumor, exogenous estrogen<br />
性索间质肿瘤，McCune-Albright，先天性肾上腺皮质增生，肾上腺肿瘤，外源性雌激素</td>

治疗基础病因——肿瘤手术切除</td>
</tr>
<tr>

本题患者</td>

不适用——无CNS发现；预期LH/FSH低</td>

是——7×6 cm卵巢肿块自主产生雌激素</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A 7-year-old with precocious puberty and a large ovarian mass has a sex cord-stromal tumor causing GnRH-independent estrogen excess; left oophorectomy is the most appropriate next step.**

**7岁女孩出现性早熟伴大型卵巢肿块，为性索间质肿瘤导致的GnRH非依赖性雌激素过量；左侧卵巢切除术是最恰当的下一步处理。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "SCAM" Causes of Peripheral Precocious Puberty / 记忆钩 — 外周性性早熟病因"SCAM"口诀:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>S</strong>ex cord-stromal tumors — granulosa cell tumor → autonomous estradiol → vaginal bleeding / 性索间质肿瘤 — 颗粒细胞瘤 → 自主雌二醇 → 阴道出血<br />
• <strong>C</strong>ongenital adrenal hyperplasia — androgen excess → virilization (heterosexual PP in girls) / 先天性肾上腺皮质增生 — 雄激素过量 → 男性化（女孩异性性早熟）<br />
• <strong>A</strong>drenal tumors — androgen or estrogen excess depending on tumor type / 肾上腺肿瘤 — 取决于肿瘤类型产生雄激素或雌激素过量<br />
• <strong>M</strong>cCune-Albright syndrome — GNAS mutation + café-au-lait spots + polyostotic fibrous dysplasia / McCune-Albright综合征 — GNAS突变 + 牛奶咖啡斑 + 多发性纤维性骨营养不良</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Ovarian Tumors Causing Precocious Puberty / 高频知识表 — 卵巢肿瘤致性早熟

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Definition of precocious puberty<br />
性早熟定义</td>
<td>Secondary sexual characteristics before age 8 in females, age 9 in males; vaginal bleeding before age 9 is always pathologic<br />
女性8岁前、男性9岁前出现第二性征；9岁前阴道出血均属病理性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Juvenile granulosa cell tumor<br />
幼年型颗粒细胞瘤</td>
<td>Most common sex cord-stromal tumor in children causing isosexual precocious puberty; produces estradiol and inhibin B autonomously; 90% stage I at diagnosis but carries malignant potential<br />
导致同性性早熟最常见的儿童性索间质肿瘤；自主产生雌二醇和抑制素B；诊断时90%为I期但具有恶性潜能</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>McCune-Albright syndrome<br />
McCune-Albright综合征</td>
<td>Somatic GNAS activating mutation; classic triad: polyostotic fibrous dysplasia + café-au-lait macules (irregular "coast of Maine" border) + precocious puberty; NOT detected on chromosomal analysis<br />
体细胞GNAS激活突变；经典三联征：多发性纤维性骨营养不良+牛奶咖啡斑（不规则"缅因州海岸"边界）+性早熟；染色体分析无法检测</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Tumor markers in pediatric ovarian masses<br />
儿童卵巢肿块肿瘤标志物</td>
<td>CA-125: nonspecific, not useful; AFP elevated in yolk sac tumors (endodermal sinus tumors); β-hCG elevated in choriocarcinoma/dysgerminoma; Inhibin B elevated in granulosa cell tumors<br />
CA-125：无特异性，无诊断价值；AFP升高见于卵黄囊瘤（内胚窦瘤）；β-hCG升高见于绒毛膜癌/无性细胞瘤；抑制素B升高见于颗粒细胞瘤</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Bone age in precocious puberty<br />
性早熟中的骨龄</td>
<td>Advanced bone age in both central and peripheral PP due to sex steroid exposure; if untreated, premature epiphyseal closure → shorter final adult height despite tall stature at presentation<br />
无论中枢性还是外周性性早熟，性激素暴露均导致骨龄提前；若不治疗，骨骺提前闭合 → 最终成人身高偏矮，尽管就诊时身材较高</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Surgical approach for pediatric ovarian mass<br />
儿童卵巢肿块手术方式</td>
<td>Oophorectomy (not FNA) for all large/suspicious masses; FNA risks seeding if malignant and is inadequate for histologic typing; surgical staging if malignancy confirmed on frozen section<br />
所有大型/可疑肿块行卵巢切除术（非FNA）；FNA有恶性播散风险且组织学分型不足；冰冻切片证实恶性后进行手术分期</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of ovarian masses in prepubertal girls:** Germ cell tumors (mature teratoma most common overall), sex cord-stromal tumors (most likely to cause hormonal excess), epithelial tumors (rare \<20 years), functional follicular cysts\
  **青春期前女孩卵巢肿块鉴别:** 生殖细胞肿瘤（成熟畸胎瘤最常见），性索间质肿瘤（最可能导致激素异常），上皮性肿瘤（\<20岁罕见），功能性卵泡囊肿

- **Key complication of delayed surgery:** If malignant, delay increases peritoneal metastasis risk; prolonged estrogen excess also accelerates bone age closure → shorter adult stature and psychological impact of premature puberty\
  **延迟手术的主要并发症:** 若为恶性，延迟会增加腹膜转移风险；持续雌激素过量还会加速骨龄闭合 → 最终成人身高偏矮，以及性早熟的心理影响

- **Inhibin B as specific marker:** Juvenile granulosa cell tumors produce inhibin B — more specific than CA-125 for this tumor subtype; useful postoperatively for monitoring recurrence\
  **抑制素B作为特异性标志物:** 幼年型颗粒细胞瘤产生抑制素B——比CA-125对该肿瘤亚型更具特异性；用于术后监测复发

- **Variant — heterosexual precocious puberty:** If androgens (not estrogens) are produced (e.g., CAH, adrenal tumor, Sertoli-Leydig cell tumor), girls develop virilization (clitoromegaly, deep voice) rather than feminization; estrogen-producing tumors → isosexual (feminizing) PP as in this case\
  **题目变式 — 异性性早熟:** 若产生雄激素（而非雌激素，如CAH、肾上腺肿瘤、支持-间质细胞瘤），女孩出现男性化（阴蒂肥大、声音低沉）而非女性化；产生雌激素的肿瘤 → 如本题的同性性早熟（女性化）

# Question 24 — Tinea Capitis / 头癣

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>3-year-old boy</strong> is brought to the physician because of a <strong>scaling lesion on the scalp</strong> for <strong>7 days</strong>. The family has no pets; the day-care center that the child attends has a pet turtle. The other children at the day-care center are <strong>asymptomatic</strong>. Examination of the scalp shows a <strong>thin plaque with alopecia and scaling</strong>. Which of the following is the most appropriate pharmacotherapy to prevent spread to the children in the day-care center?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate pharmacotherapy to prevent spread to the children in the day-care center?</strong></p>
<p>A) Oral griseofulvin for the patient only<br />
B) Oral griseofulvin for the patient and his classmates<br />
C) Topical hydrocortisone for the patient only<br />
D) Topical hydrocortisone for the patient and his classmates<br />
E) Topical selenium sulfide for the patient only<br />
F) Topical selenium sulfide for the patient and his classmates</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: A</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>3-year-old boy, scalp lesion<br />
3岁男孩，头皮损害</td>
<td>Tinea capitis is predominantly a pediatric condition; rarely seen in adults<br />
头癣主要发生于儿童，成人罕见</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Alopecia + scaling plaque<br />
脱发 + 鳞屑性斑块</td>
<td>Classic presentation of tinea capitis: scaling, alopecia, ± cervical lymphadenopathy<br />
头癣经典表现：鳞屑、脱发、±颈部淋巴结肿大</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Day-care center setting<br />
日托中心接触史</td>
<td>Tinea capitis spreads via direct contact and fomites in communal settings<br />
头癣可通过直接接触及污染物在集体场所传播</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pet turtle at day-care center<br />
日托中心有宠物龟</td>
<td>Turtles are not typical dermatophyte sources; classic zootic vectors are dogs/cats (<em>Microsporum canis</em>) — turtle is a red herring<br />
龟类不是典型皮肤癣菌来源；经典人兽共患来源为狗猫（<em>犬小孢子菌</em>）——龟是干扰信息</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Other children asymptomatic<br />
其他儿童无症状</td>
<td>Asymptomatic contacts do NOT require prophylactic antifungal treatment<br />
无症状接触者无需预防性抗真菌治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Question asks to "prevent spread"<br />
题目问"防止传播"</td>
<td>The correct prevention strategy is to treat the infected patient, not to administer prophylaxis to healthy contacts<br />
正确的预防策略是治疗感染者，而非对健康接触者给予预防用药</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Tinea capitis** is caused by **dermatophytes** (most commonly *Trichophyton tonsurans* in North America) that invade the **keratinized** layers of the scalp and hair shaft at a depth that renders topical antifungals insufficient:

头癣由**皮肤癣菌**（北美最常见为*须癣毛癣菌*）引起，侵犯头皮和毛干的**角化层**深部，使局部外用药物无法到达感染部位：

- Dermatophytes penetrate the hair follicle beyond the reach of topical antifungal agents\
  皮肤癣菌侵入毛囊深部，超出外用抗真菌药物的渗透范围

- *T. tonsurans* causes **endothrix** infection (arthrospores inside the hair shaft) → "black dot" pattern on scalp; does NOT fluoresce under Wood's lamp\
  *须癣毛癣菌*引起**发内型**感染（关节孢子位于毛干内部）→ 头皮"黑点征"；Wood灯下不发荧光

- *Microsporum* spp. cause **ectothrix** infection (spores outside hair shaft) → Wood's lamp shows green fluorescence\
  *小孢子菌*属引起**发外型**感染（孢子位于毛干外部）→ Wood灯下显绿色荧光

- Oral griseofulvin achieves therapeutic concentrations in the hair follicle via systemic absorption\
  口服灰黄霉素通过全身吸收在毛囊中达到有效治疗浓度

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Any tinea infection involving hair follicles or nails requires systemic (oral) antifungal therapy; superficial skin-only infections can often be managed topically.

**解剖小窍门:** 累及毛囊或指甲的癣病感染需要系统性（口服）抗真菌药；仅累及浅表皮肤的感染通常可局部用药治疗。

## 3. Correct Answer (A) — Oral Griseofulvin for Patient Only / 正确答案 (A) — 仅对患儿口服灰黄霉素

**Oral griseofulvin** is the traditional first-line treatment for tinea capitis because it penetrates the hair follicle systemically, where topical agents cannot reach:

**口服灰黄霉素**是头癣的传统一线治疗，因为它能通过全身循环渗透至毛囊深部——这是局部药物无法到达的部位：

- Griseofulvin is fungistatic and disrupts microtubule assembly in dermatophytes; taken with a fatty meal to enhance absorption\
  灰黄霉素为抑菌性药物，通过干扰皮肤癣菌微管组装起效；与高脂餐同服以增加吸收

- Oral terbinafine (inhibits squalene epoxidase; fungicidal) is now preferred by many guidelines due to shorter treatment course\
  口服特比萘芬（抑制角鲨烯环氧化酶；杀菌性）因疗程更短，现为多数指南首选

- Topical selenium sulfide or ketoconazole shampoo may be used as adjuncts to reduce spore shedding but do not replace oral therapy\
  局部硫化硒或酮康唑洗发水可作为辅助用药减少孢子脱落，但不能替代口服治疗

- Asymptomatic contacts at the day-care center do NOT require antifungal treatment\
  日托中心的无症状接触者无需抗真菌治疗

**Diagnosis:** Clinical diagnosis based on scaling scalp plaque with alopecia in a school-age child; confirmed by KOH preparation (hyphae/arthrospores) or fungal culture.

**诊断:** 根据学龄儿童头皮鳞屑性斑块伴脱发做临床诊断；通过KOH制片（见菌丝/关节孢子）或真菌培养确诊。

**Treatment:** Oral griseofulvin (microsize 20–25 mg/kg/day) for 6–12 weeks OR oral terbinafine for 2–4 weeks; adjuvant selenium sulfide 2.5% shampoo twice weekly.

**治疗:** 口服灰黄霉素（微粉化制剂20–25 mg/kg/天）6–12周，或口服特比萘芬2–4周；辅以2.5%硫化硒洗发水每周2次。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Oral griseofulvin for the patient only ✓<br />
A — 仅对患儿口服灰黄霉素 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Oral systemic antifungal treats tinea capitis; asymptomatic contacts do not require treatment<br />
正确——口服系统性抗真菌药治疗头癣；无症状接触者无需治疗</td>
<td>Only symptomatic patients require antifungal therapy<br />
仅症状性患者需要抗真菌治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Oral griseofulvin for the patient and his classmates<br />
B — 对患儿及同学口服灰黄霉素</td>
<td>Correct drug, wrong scope — classmates are asymptomatic; routine prophylaxis of contacts is not indicated and exposes healthy children to drug side effects<br />
药物正确，范围错误——同学无症状；对接触者常规预防用药无适应证，且使健康儿童暴露于药物副作用</td>
<td>Prophylactic treatment of asymptomatic contacts is not standard of care for tinea capitis<br />
对无症状接触者预防性治疗不是头癣的标准治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Topical hydrocortisone for the patient only<br />
C — 仅对患儿局部用氢化可的松</td>
<td>Wrong drug class — corticosteroid suppresses local immune response and may worsen tinea capitis; hydrocortisone is used for atopic dermatitis, not fungal infections<br />
药物类别错误——皮质类固醇抑制局部免疫，可加重头癣；氢化可的松用于特应性皮炎，不用于真菌感染</td>
<td>Topical steroids are contraindicated in active dermatophyte infections<br />
局部激素在活动性皮肤癣菌感染中禁忌</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Topical hydrocortisone for the patient and his classmates<br />
D — 对患儿及同学局部用氢化可的松</td>
<td>Doubly wrong — wrong drug class AND wrong scope; applying a steroid to asymptomatic contacts serves no purpose and could harm the patient<br />
双重错误——错误的药物类别且范围错误；对无症状接触者使用激素毫无意义且可能伤害患者</td>
<td>Never treat asymptomatic contacts with a drug that is contraindicated in the actual disease<br />
绝不用在实际疾病中禁忌的药物治疗无症状接触者</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Topical selenium sulfide for the patient only<br />
E — 仅对患儿局部用硫化硒</td>
<td>Wrong route of delivery — selenium sulfide cannot penetrate the hair follicle sufficiently; it is used for pityriasis versicolor and seborrheic dermatitis, not as monotherapy for tinea capitis<br />
给药途径错误——硫化硒无法充分渗透毛囊；适用于花斑糠疹和脂溢性皮炎，不作为头癣单药治疗</td>
<td>Tinea capitis mandates systemic oral therapy; topical agents are adjuncts only<br />
头癣必须系统性口服治疗；局部药物仅为辅助用药</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>F — Topical selenium sulfide for the patient and his classmates<br />
F — 对患儿及同学局部用硫化硒</td>
<td>Wrong drug AND wrong scope — selenium sulfide alone is ineffective for tinea capitis; classmates are asymptomatic and require no treatment<br />
错误的药物且范围错误——单用硫化硒对头癣无效；同学无症状，无需任何治疗</td>
<td>Adjuvant topical shampoos do not replace systemic therapy and should not be given prophylactically<br />
辅助性外用洗发水不能替代系统治疗，且不应预防性给药</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Choice E — selenium sulfide is a genuine antifungal used for tinea versicolor, making it seem plausible; the critical distinction is that topical agents cannot penetrate the hair follicle, which is why tinea capitis uniquely requires oral systemic therapy.*

选项E最具迷惑性，因为硫化硒确实是用于花斑糠疹的抗真菌药，看似合理；关键区别在于局部药物无法渗透毛囊，这正是头癣独特地需要口服系统治疗的原因。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**Tinea capitis in children requires oral antifungal therapy (griseofulvin or terbinafine) because the hair follicle is too deep for topical penetration; only the symptomatic patient needs treatment, not asymptomatic contacts.**

**儿童头癣因毛囊位置过深、局部药物无法渗透而必须口服抗真菌药（灰黄霉素或特比萘芬）；仅感染患儿需要治疗，无症状接触者无需治疗。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — SCALP for Tinea Capitis / 记忆钩 — "SCALP" 记头癣五要点:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>S</strong>calp + <strong>S</strong>chool-age children — who gets it / 头皮 + 学龄儿童——谁会得病<br />
• <strong>C</strong>ervical lymphadenopathy — hallmark exam finding / 颈部淋巴结肿大——标志性体格检查发现<br />
• <strong>A</strong>lopecia + scaling — classic visual presentation / 脱发 + 鳞屑——经典视觉表现<br />
• <strong>L</strong>acks topical penetration — why ORAL is required / 局部药物无法穿透——为何必须口服<br />
• <strong>P</strong>atient only — asymptomatic contacts are NOT treated / 仅患者——无症状接触者不治疗</p></th>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Tinea Capitis & Dermatophyte Pharmacology / 高频知识表 — 头癣及皮肤癣菌药理

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Most common causative organism (USA)<br />
最常见致病菌（美国）</td>
<td><em>Trichophyton tonsurans</em> — endothrix pattern; arthrospores inside hair shaft; does NOT fluoresce under Wood's lamp<br />
<em>须癣毛癣菌</em>——发内型；关节孢子位于毛干内部；Wood灯下不发荧光</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Wood's lamp findings<br />
Wood灯检查发现</td>
<td><em>Microsporum</em> spp. → bright green fluorescence; <em>T. tonsurans</em> → no fluorescence (most US cases are Wood's lamp negative)<br />
<em>小孢子菌</em>属→亮绿色荧光；<em>须癣毛癣菌</em>→无荧光（美国大多数病例Wood灯阴性）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>KOH preparation<br />
KOH制片</td>
<td>Scale scraped from scalp + 10% KOH → visualize hyphae or arthrospores under microscopy; practical point-of-care diagnostic<br />
刮取头皮鳞屑+10% KOH→显微镜下见菌丝或关节孢子；实用的即时诊断方法</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Kerion<br />
脓癣</td>
<td>Severe inflammatory form of tinea capitis → boggy, painful, purulent scalp mass; may cause permanent scarring alopecia; treat with oral antifungals ± short-course prednisone for inflammation<br />
头癣严重炎症形式→柔软、疼痛、化脓性头皮肿块；可致永久性瘢痕性脱发；口服抗真菌药±短程泼尼松抗炎</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Griseofulvin mechanism &amp; tips<br />
灰黄霉素机制与用药要点</td>
<td>Fungistatic; disrupts spindle microtubule assembly; take with fatty meal; drug interactions with warfarin and oral contraceptives<br />
抑菌性；干扰纺锤体微管组装；与高脂餐同服；与华法林及口服避孕药存在药物相互作用</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Terbinafine vs griseofulvin<br />
特比萘芬与灰黄霉素比较</td>
<td>Terbinafine: fungicidal, inhibits squalene epoxidase, 2–4 week course, preferred for <em>T. tonsurans</em>; griseofulvin: fungistatic, 6–12 week course, better for <em>Microsporum</em><br />
特比萘芬：杀菌性，抑制角鲨烯环氧化酶，2–4周疗程，首选用于<em>须癣毛癣菌</em>；灰黄霉素：抑菌性，6–12周疗程，对<em>小孢子菌</em>效果更好</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Topical adjuvant role<br />
局部辅助用药作用</td>
<td>Selenium sulfide 2.5% or ketoconazole 2% shampoo 2×/week reduces infectious spore shedding during treatment but is NOT a substitute for oral therapy<br />
2.5%硫化硒或2%酮康唑洗发水每周2次可在治疗期间减少传染性孢子脱落，但不能替代口服治疗</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Topical vs. oral antifungal rule:** Tinea pedis, corporis, and cruris respond to topical azoles or terbinafine cream; tinea capitis and onychomycosis always require systemic oral therapy due to deep follicular/nail matrix involvement\
  **局部与口服抗真菌药原则:** 足癣、体癣和股癣对局部唑类或特比萘芬乳膏有效；头癣和甲癣因涉及毛囊深部/甲母质，始终需要系统性口服治疗

- **Tinea incognito (steroid-modified tinea):** Misapplication of topical corticosteroids to tinea infections suppresses inflammation → lesion loses classic ring/scale morphology and becomes atypical, delaying diagnosis\
  **隐蔽型癣病（激素修饰癣病）:** 将局部皮质类固醇误用于癣病感染，抑制炎症反应→皮损失去经典环形/鳞屑形态，表现不典型，延误诊断

- **Zootic transmission patterns:** *Microsporum canis* from dogs and cats (ectothrix, Wood's lamp positive, rural areas); *T. tonsurans* is anthropophilic and spreads person-to-person in urban/school settings\
  **人兽共患传播模式:** *犬小孢子菌*来自狗猫（发外型，Wood灯阳性，农村地区）；*须癣毛癣菌*具亲人性，在城市/学校环境中人际传播

- **Prophylaxis not indicated:** Unlike bacterial meningitis (where rifampin prophylaxis for contacts IS indicated), tinea capitis does not warrant treatment of asymptomatic contacts — a high-yield exam contrast\
  **无需预防用药:** 与细菌性脑膜炎（接触者需利福平预防用药）不同，头癣不需对无症状接触者治疗——这是高频考试对比考点

# Question 25 — Primary Ciliary Dyskinesia / 原发性纤毛运动障碍

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>5-year-old boy</strong> is brought to the physician by his parents as a new patient because they are concerned that he may have an immunodeficiency. The family recently moved to the area. The parents say their son's previous physician had been examining him for the condition. The patient has had <strong>six episodes of pneumonia</strong> and <strong>10 episodes of sinusitis since birth</strong>. He underwent uncomplicated surgical drainage of the sinuses at the ages of 3 and 4 years. He had his <strong>first episode of otitis media at the age of 2 months</strong> and underwent uncomplicated placement of tympanostomy tubes at the age of 7 months. His <strong>umbilical stump fell off at the age of 2 weeks</strong>. The patient's previous leukocyte, lymphocyte, and platelet counts; <strong>serum immunoglobulin and CH50 concentrations</strong>; and diphtheria, tetanus, pneumococcal, and Haemophilus influenzae type b titers are <strong>within the reference ranges</strong>. Six previous chest x-rays showed <strong>lower lobe consolidations in inconsistent locations</strong>; subsequent x-rays showed clearing of the infiltrates. Today, vital signs are within normal limits. Examination shows no abnormalities. A CT scan of the chest is shown.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Common variable immunodeficiency<br />
B) Complement deficiency<br />
C) Leukocyte adhesion defect<br />
D) Primary ciliary dyskinesia<br />
E) Wiskott-Aldrich syndrome</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: D</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Recurrent pneumonia + sinusitis + otitis media since birth<br />
出生起反复肺炎+鼻窦炎+中耳炎</td>
<td>Triad of sinopulmonary and middle ear infections is the hallmark of PCD due to defective mucociliary clearance across all ciliated epithelia<br />
三联感染是 PCD 的标志，因为全身纤毛上皮的黏液纤毛清除障碍</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Normal immunoglobulins + normal CH50<br />
免疫球蛋白正常 + CH50 正常</td>
<td>Rules out humoral (CVID) and complement deficiencies; narrows diagnosis to structural/mechanical defect rather than immune deficiency<br />
排除体液免疫（CVID）和补体缺陷，缩小诊断范围至结构/机械性缺陷</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Normal vaccine titers (diphtheria, tetanus, pneumococcal, Hib)<br />
疫苗抗体滴度正常</td>
<td>Confirms intact B-cell function and antibody production; further excludes humoral immunodeficiency<br />
证实 B 细胞功能和抗体产生完整，进一步排除体液免疫缺陷</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Umbilical stump fell off at 2 weeks (normal)<br />
脐带在 2 周脱落（正常）</td>
<td>Normal umbilical separation rules out Leukocyte Adhesion Defect (LAD), which causes delayed separation &gt;4 weeks<br />
正常脐带脱落时间排除 LAD（LAD 导致脐带脱落延迟 &gt;4 周）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Normal leukocyte count<br />
白细胞计数正常</td>
<td>LAD would show persistently elevated peripheral WBC (leukocytes cannot marginate); PCD does not affect leukocyte counts<br />
LAD 会出现持续高白细胞（白细胞无法边集），PCD 不影响白细胞计数</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Lower lobe consolidations in inconsistent locations on CXR → bronchiectasis on CT<br />
胸片示不同位置下叶实变 → CT 示支气管扩张</td>
<td>Migratory/shifting infiltrates that clear suggest retained secretions, not a fixed anatomical lesion; CT bronchiectasis confirms chronic airway damage from mucus retention<br />
游走性浸润灶提示分泌物潴留而非固定病变；CT 支气管扩张证实慢性气道损伤</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Primary ciliary dyskinesia** arises from mutations affecting the **dynein arm proteins** (most commonly outer dynein arm) or other axonemal components, leading to **absent or dysfunctional cilia** throughout the body. The result is failure of **mucociliary escalator** function:

**原发性纤毛运动障碍**由影响**动力蛋白臂**（最常见为外动力蛋白臂）或其他轴丝组分的基因突变引起，导致全身**纤毛缺失或功能障碍**，进而**黏液纤毛清除系统**（mucociliary escalator）失效：

- Mucus and inhaled pathogens accumulate in airways → recurrent bacterial pneumonia and bronchiectasis\
  气道内黏液和吸入病原体积聚 → 反复细菌性肺炎和支气管扩张

- Ciliated sinus epithelium fails to clear mucus → chronic rhinosinusitis and surgical sinus drainage\
  鼻窦纤毛上皮清除黏液失败 → 慢性鼻窦炎，需手术引流

- Eustachian tube cilia dysfunctional → otitis media beginning in early infancy\
  咽鼓管纤毛功能障碍 → 婴儿早期即出现中耳炎

- Approximately 50% of PCD patients have situs inversus (Kartagener syndrome = PCD + situs inversus + bronchiectasis + sinusitis)\
  约 50% PCD 患者合并内脏转位（Kartagener 综合征 = PCD + 内脏转位 + 支气管扩张 + 鼻窦炎）

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Any ciliated epithelium is affected — airways, sinuses, middle ear, fallopian tubes, and sperm flagella (male infertility).

**解剖小窍门:** 所有纤毛上皮均受累——气道、鼻窦、中耳、输卵管和精子鞭毛（男性不育）。

---

## 3. Correct Answer (D) — Primary Ciliary Dyskinesia / 正确答案 (D) — 原发性纤毛运动障碍

**Primary ciliary dyskinesia (PCD)** is a rare autosomal recessive disorder caused by mutations in dynein arm or axonemal proteins, resulting in structurally or functionally defective cilia that cannot beat properly:

**原发性纤毛运动障碍（PCD）**是一种罕见的常染色体隐性遗传病，由动力蛋白臂或轴丝蛋白突变引起，导致纤毛结构或功能异常，无法正常摆动：

- Onset in infancy with recurrent sinopulmonary infections; predates any immunological maturation window\
  婴儿期起病，反复鼻窦肺部感染，早于任何免疫系统成熟窗口期

- All standard immune workup is normal (immunoglobulins, complement, lymphocyte counts, vaccine responses)\
  所有常规免疫检查均正常（免疫球蛋白、补体、淋巴细胞计数、疫苗应答）

- Characteristic CT findings: bronchiectasis (cylindrical or cystic airway dilation), often bilateral lower lobe predominant\
  CT 特征性表现：支气管扩张（柱状或囊状气道扩张），常双下肺为主

- Diagnostic gold standard: nasal nitric oxide (low in PCD) + electron microscopy of ciliary biopsy showing absent or malformed dynein arms\
  诊断金标准：鼻腔 NO 测定（PCD 中降低）+ 纤毛活检电镜见动力蛋白臂缺失或畸形

**Diagnosis:** Clinical triad of chronic sinusitis + recurrent pneumonia + otitis media in early childhood, combined with normal immunologic workup and CT bronchiectasis, points directly to PCD.

**诊断:** 幼儿期慢性鼻窦炎+反复肺炎+中耳炎三联征，结合免疫学检查正常和 CT 支气管扩张，直接指向 PCD。

**Treatment:** Airway clearance therapy (chest physiotherapy, mucolytics), aggressive antibiotic treatment of infections, surgical drainage of sinuses/tympanostomy tubes as needed; lung transplant for end-stage disease.

**治疗:** 气道清除治疗（胸部物理治疗、黏液溶解剂），积极抗生素治疗感染，按需鼻窦引流/鼓膜置管；终末期肺病行肺移植。

---

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Common variable immunodeficiency<br />
A — 普通变异型免疫缺陷</td>
<td>Onset typically in 2nd–4th decade (not infancy); requires LOW immunoglobulin levels as defining feature<br />
通常在 20–40 岁起病（非婴儿期）；必须有低免疫球蛋白水平作为诊断要件</td>
<td>Age of onset + immunoglobulin level — CVID requires low Ig; this child has normal Ig<br />
起病年龄+免疫球蛋白水平——CVID 需要低 Ig，该患儿 Ig 正常</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Complement deficiency<br />
B — 补体缺陷</td>
<td>Terminal complement (C5–C9) deficiency → recurrent Neisseria (meningococcus, gonococcus) infections; not sinopulmonary bacterial pneumonia; CH50 would be low/absent<br />
终末补体（C5–C9）缺陷 → 反复奈瑟菌感染；非鼻窦肺部细菌性肺炎；CH50 应低/缺失</td>
<td>Organism spectrum (Neisseria vs. encapsulated bacteria) + CH50 is normal here<br />
感染病原体谱（奈瑟菌 vs. 有荚膜细菌）+ 本题 CH50 正常</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Leukocyte adhesion defect<br />
C — 白细胞黏附缺陷</td>
<td>LAD causes delayed umbilical cord separation (&gt;4 weeks) and persistent leukocytosis; umbilical stump fell at 2 weeks here (normal); WBC is normal<br />
LAD 导致脐带脱落延迟（&gt;4 周）和持续白细胞增多；本题脐带 2 周脱落（正常）；白细胞正常</td>
<td>Umbilical cord separation timing + peripheral WBC — both normal here; rules out LAD<br />
脐带脱落时间+外周血白细胞——本题均正常，排除 LAD</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Primary ciliary dyskinesia ✓<br />
D — 原发性纤毛运动障碍 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Recurrent sinopulmonary + ear infections since birth with completely normal immune workup + CT bronchiectasis is the defining presentation of PCD<br />
正确——出生起反复鼻窦肺部+耳部感染，免疫检查完全正常，CT 支气管扩张，是 PCD 的典型表现</td>
<td>Normal Ig + CH50 + WBC + vaccine titers + bronchiectasis on CT = mechanical clearance defect, not immune defect<br />
免疫球蛋白+CH50+白细胞+疫苗滴度全部正常+CT 支气管扩张 = 机械清除障碍而非免疫缺陷</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Wiskott-Aldrich syndrome<br />
E — Wiskott-Aldrich 综合征</td>
<td>X-linked; triad of eczema + thrombocytopenia + infections with encapsulated bacteria/opportunistic organisms; no eczema or thrombocytopenia mentioned; platelet count is normal<br />
X 连锁遗传；湿疹+血小板减少+有荚膜细菌/机会感染三联征；本题无湿疹或血小板减少，血小板计数正常</td>
<td>Absence of eczema and thrombocytopenia; normal platelets explicitly stated<br />
无湿疹和血小板减少；题目明确血小板计数正常</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Leukocyte Adhesion Defect (C), given the recurrent bacterial infections from birth — the critical pivot is the normal umbilical cord separation at 2 weeks and the absence of leukocytosis, both of which definitively exclude LAD.*

LAD（选项 C）是最容易混淆的干扰项，因为同样表现为出生起反复细菌感染——关键鉴别点是脐带在 2 周正常脱落以及无白细胞增多，两者均可明确排除 LAD。

---

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Primary Ciliary Dyskinesia vs. Common Immunodeficiencies / 原发性纤毛运动障碍 vs. 常见免疫缺陷病对比

<table>
<colgroup>

---

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**Primary ciliary dyskinesia presents in infancy with recurrent sinopulmonary infections and otitis media due to defective cilia, with an entirely normal immune workup and CT bronchiectasis as the key diagnostic clues.**

**原发性纤毛运动障碍在婴儿期起病，因纤毛缺陷导致反复鼻窦肺部感染和中耳炎，免疫检查完全正常，CT 支气管扩张是关键诊断线索。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "SICK CILIA" for PCD Features / 记忆钩 — "SICK CILIA" 记 PCD 特征:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>S</strong>inusitis (chronic) — recurrent bacterial sinusitis requiring drainage / 慢性鼻窦炎——反复细菌性鼻窦炎需引流<br />
• <strong>I</strong>mmunology normal — all Ig, complement, WBC tests normal / 免疫检查正常——所有 Ig、补体、白细胞检查正常<br />
• <strong>C</strong>ilia defect — dynein arm mutation, absent/dysfunctional axonemal beating / 纤毛缺陷——动力蛋白臂突变，轴丝摆动缺失/异常<br />
• <strong>K</strong>artagener = PCD + situs inversus + bronchiectasis + sinusitis triad / Kartagener = PCD + 内脏转位 + 支气管扩张 + 鼻窦炎三联征<br />
• <strong>C</strong>hest CT bronchiectasis — cylindrical airway dilation, lower lobes / 胸部 CT 支气管扩张——下叶柱状气道扩张<br />
• <strong>I</strong>nfancy onset — pneumonia + otitis media from first months of life / 婴儿期起病——出生后数月即出现肺炎+中耳炎<br />
• <strong>L</strong>ow nasal NO — key screening test for PCD / 鼻腔 NO 降低——PCD 关键筛查检测<br />
• <strong>A</strong>utosomal recessive — biallelic DNAI1/DNAI2/DNAH5 mutations most common / 常染色体隐性——DNAI1/DNAI2/DNAH5 双等位基因突变最常见</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>
