## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Primary Ciliary Dyskinesia: Genetics, Diagnosis, and Kartagener Syndrome / 高频知识表 — PCD：遗传学、诊断与 Kartagener 综合征

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Genetics and inheritance<br />
遗传学与遗传方式</td>
<td>Autosomal recessive; &gt;40 causative genes identified; DNAI1, DNAI2, DNAH5 most common; encodes outer dynein arm components<br />
常染色体隐性遗传；已鉴定 &gt;40 个致病基因；DNAI1、DNAI2、DNAH5 最常见；编码外动力蛋白臂组分</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Ciliary ultrastructure defect<br />
纤毛超微结构缺陷</td>
<td>Classic: absent outer dynein arms on EM; also: absent inner dynein arms, transposition defects, or complete ciliary aplasia<br />
经典表现：电镜下外动力蛋白臂缺失；也可见内动力蛋白臂缺失、转位缺陷或完全性纤毛缺失</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Diagnostic workup<br />
诊断流程</td>
<td>Step 1: nasal NO (low in PCD, &lt;77 nL/min); Step 2: high-speed video microscopy of nasal brushings; Step 3: EM of ciliary biopsy; genetic panel<br />
第 1 步：鼻腔 NO（PCD 中降低，&lt;77 nL/min）；第 2 步：鼻刷取样高速视频显微镜；第 3 步：纤毛活检电镜；基因检测</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Kartagener syndrome<br />
Kartagener 综合征</td>
<td>Subset of PCD (~50%): situs inversus totalis + chronic sinusitis + bronchiectasis; situs inversus occurs because left-right determination requires functional nodal cilia in embryogenesis<br />
PCD 的亚型（约 50%）：完全性内脏转位+慢性鼻窦炎+支气管扩张；内脏转位因胚胎发育期结节纤毛功能性左右不对称决定失败</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>CT chest findings<br />
胸部 CT 表现</td>
<td>Bronchiectasis (cylindrical &gt; cystic), air trapping, mucus plugging, recurrent consolidations (lower lobe predominant); may also see situs inversus with dextrocardia on imaging<br />
支气管扩张（柱状&gt;囊状）、气体潴留、黏液栓塞、反复实变（下叶为主）；影像学可见内脏转位伴右位心</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Complications and prognosis<br />
并发症与预后</td>
<td>Progressive bronchiectasis → respiratory failure; male infertility (immotile sperm); female subfertility (ectopic pregnancy risk); chronic ear disease with conductive hearing loss<br />
进行性支气管扩张→呼吸衰竭；男性不育（精子不动）；女性生育力下降（异位妊娠风险）；慢性耳病伴传导性听力损失</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment approach<br />
治疗方法</td>
<td>Daily airway clearance (chest PT, flutter devices, hypertonic saline); inhaled antibiotics for chronic Pseudomonas; azithromycin for anti-inflammatory effect; lung transplant for end-stage disease<br />
每日气道清除（胸部物理治疗、振动排痰、高渗盐水吸入）；吸入抗生素治疗慢性铜绿假单胞菌感染；阿奇霉素抗炎；终末期肺病行肺移植</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of neonatal respiratory distress in PCD:** Neonatal respiratory distress occurs in ~80% of PCD newborns despite term birth — due to failure to clear fetal lung fluid via tracheal cilia; often misdiagnosed as transient tachypnea of the newborn\
  **PCD 新生儿呼吸窘迫的鉴别:** 约 80% PCD 新生儿足月出生后仍出现呼吸窘迫——因气管纤毛无法清除胎肺液；常被误诊为新生儿短暂性呼吸急促

- **Variant — heterotaxy vs. situs inversus totalis:** Situs inversus totalis (mirror-image) is associated with ~50% PCD; heterotaxy (situs ambiguus with complex cardiac defects) is associated with a different subset and carries worse prognosis due to congenital heart disease\
  **变式——异位症与完全性内脏转位:** 完全性内脏转位（镜像）与约 50% PCD 相关；内脏不定位（合并复杂心脏缺陷）与另一亚型相关，因先天性心脏病预后更差

- **Key complication — male infertility:** Sperm flagella share the same 9+2 axonemal structure as respiratory cilia; dynein arm mutations render flagella immotile; male PCD patients are virtually always infertile (azoospermia with normal sperm morphology)\
  **关键并发症——男性不育:** 精子鞭毛与呼吸道纤毛共享相同的 9+2 轴丝结构；动力蛋白臂突变使鞭毛不动；男性 PCD 患者几乎均不育（精子形态正常但无活动力）

- **USMLE test-taking pearl — immune workup is normal:** When a child has severe/recurrent infections but ALL of immunoglobulins, complement, WBC, and vaccine titers are explicitly stated as normal, think structural/mechanical defect (PCD) rather than immune deficiency; this complete normal workup is the "negative" clue that rules in PCD\
  **USMLE 考试技巧——免疫检查全部正常:** 当患儿有严重/反复感染但免疫球蛋白、补体、白细胞、疫苗滴度均明确正常时，应考虑结构/机械性缺陷（PCD）而非免疫缺陷；这种"全部正常"的阴性线索是指向 PCD 的关键

# Question 26 — Mitral Valve Prolapse Without Regurgitation: No IE Prophylaxis Indicated / 二尖瓣脱垂无反流：无需感染性心内膜炎预防

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A physician, who is covering for a colleague who is out of town, receives a telephone call at the office from a dentist regarding whether antibiotic prophylaxis is needed for a scaling procedure for the colleague's patient. The patient is a <strong>50-year-old woman</strong> with <strong>mitral valve prolapse</strong> diagnosed 15 years ago prior to her transferring to the colleague's care. She has <strong>never had endocarditis</strong>. Further review of the patient's medical record indicates <strong>no documentation of echocardiography</strong>. She also has hypertension, type 2 diabetes mellitus, and an <strong>allergy to penicillin</strong>. Medications are lisinopril and metformin. Cardiac examination from the patient's last office visit 6 months ago showed a <strong>normal pulse</strong> and <strong>no murmurs</strong>. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management of the colleague's patient?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Advise the dentist to proceed with the procedure without antibiotic prophylaxis<br />
B) Ask the dentist to postpone the procedure, and then schedule outpatient echocardiography<br />
C) Ask the dentist to postpone the procedure, and then schedule an examination in the office<br />
D) Prescribe amoxicillin to be taken 1 hour before the procedure<br />
E) Prescribe clindamycin to be taken 1 hour before the procedure</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: A</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Mitral valve prolapse, no murmurs<br />
二尖瓣脱垂，无杂音</td>
<td>No audible regurgitation → MVP alone without hemodynamic significance does not qualify for IE prophylaxis<br />
无可闻及反流→单纯 MVP 无血流动力学意义，不符合 IE 预防指征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Never had endocarditis<br />
从未发生过心内膜炎</td>
<td>Prior IE is a high-risk criterion; its absence removes one prophylaxis indication<br />
既往 IE 是高危标准之一；无此病史则排除该预防指征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No prosthetic valve, no congenital heart disease<br />
无人工瓣膜，无先天性心脏病</td>
<td>All AHA high-risk categories are absent → prophylaxis not indicated<br />
AHA 全部高危类别均不存在→不需要预防用药</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Dental scaling procedure<br />
洁牙（刮治）操作</td>
<td>A mucosal-disrupting dental procedure that causes transient bacteremia — the type of procedure where prophylaxis guidelines apply<br />
可导致短暂菌血症的黏膜破坏性牙科操作——是需评估预防用药的操作类型</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Allergy to penicillin<br />
青霉素过敏</td>
<td>A distractor: even if prophylaxis were needed, amoxicillin is contraindicated; clindamycin was historically the alternative — but prophylaxis is not indicated at all<br />
干扰因素：即便需要预防，阿莫西林也禁用；克林霉素曾是替代方案——但本例根本无需预防</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No echocardiography on record<br />
无超声心动图记录</td>
<td>A distractor suggesting workup is incomplete; however, physical exam showing no murmurs is sufficient to guide the prophylaxis decision<br />
似乎提示检查不完整，但体格检查（无杂音）已足以指导预防用药决策</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Infective endocarditis (IE) prophylaxis** before dental procedures is based on two premises: dental procedures cause **transient bacteremia**, and certain high-risk cardiac conditions are prone to developing **IE** with devastating consequences:

感染性心内膜炎（IE）牙科前预防用药基于两个前提：牙科操作可引发**短暂性菌血症**，而某些高危心脏病患者发生 **IE** 后后果极其严重：

- Scaling and extractions disrupt oral mucosa → *Streptococcus viridans* and other organisms enter bloodstream\
  刮治和拔牙破坏口腔黏膜 → 草绿色链球菌等微生物进入血流

- In high-risk cardiac substrates, bacteria adhere to damaged endothelium or prosthetic material and seed vegetation\
  在高危心脏基础上，细菌黏附于受损内皮或人工材料并形成赘生物

- AHA 2007 guidelines dramatically narrowed prophylaxis indications — uncomplicated MVP is explicitly no longer an indication\
  AHA 2007 年指南大幅缩窄预防适应证——单纯 MVP 已明确不再是适应证

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** the higher the turbulence or the greater the foreign material at the valve, the greater the risk of bacterial seeding — hence prosthetic valves carry the highest risk, while MVP without regurgitant murmur carries minimal risk.

**解剖小窍门:** 瓣膜处湍流越强或存在异物材料，细菌定植风险越高——因此人工瓣膜风险最大，而无反流杂音的 MVP 风险极低。

## 3. Correct Answer (A) — No Antibiotic Prophylaxis for Uncomplicated MVP / 正确答案 (A) — 单纯二尖瓣脱垂无需抗生素预防

**Mitral valve prolapse without regurgitation** does not meet any AHA high-risk criterion for IE prophylaxis:

**无反流的二尖瓣脱垂** 不符合 AHA 感染性心内膜炎预防的任何高危标准：

- AHA 2007 guidelines restrict prophylaxis to four conditions: prosthetic valve, prior IE, specific congenital heart disease, and cardiac transplant with valvulopathy\
  AHA 2007 年指南将预防适应证限制为四类：人工瓣膜、既往 IE、特定先天性心脏病、伴瓣膜病的心脏移植

- This patient's MVP shows no murmur → no documented regurgitation → definitively does not qualify for prophylaxis\
  该患者 MVP 无杂音 → 无记录在案的反流 → 明确不符合预防适应证

- Penicillin allergy is a red herring because antibiotic prophylaxis is not indicated in the first place\
  青霉素过敏是迷惑因素，因为本就不需要预防性抗生素

**Diagnosis:** MVP without audible regurgitation = low-risk cardiac lesion; the covering physician can advise the dentist to proceed.

**诊断:** 无可闻及反流的 MVP = 低危心脏病变；代班医生可建议牙医直接进行操作。

**Treatment:** No antibiotic prophylaxis; proceed with dental scaling as planned.

**治疗:** 无需抗生素预防；按计划进行洁牙操作。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Advise the dentist to proceed without antibiotic prophylaxis ✓<br />
A — 建议牙医直接操作，无需预防性抗生素 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — MVP without documented regurgitation does not meet any AHA high-risk criterion; proceeding is safe and appropriate<br />
正确——无记录反流的 MVP 不符合任何 AHA 高危标准；直接操作安全且恰当</td>
<td>Absence of murmur on exam clinches the decision; prophylaxis list does not include MVP<br />
体检无杂音是关键依据；预防适应证列表不包含 MVP</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Postpone procedure; schedule echocardiography<br />
B — 推迟操作；安排超声心动图检查</td>
<td>Echocardiography is not required to make the prophylaxis decision; physical exam showing no murmur is sufficient; unnecessarily delaying care harms the patient<br />
超声心动图并非做出预防决策的必要条件；体检无杂音已足够；不必要地推迟治疗有损患者利益</td>
<td>Prophylaxis guidelines do not require echo confirmation for MVP with no murmur<br />
预防指南对无杂音 MVP 不要求超声心动图确认</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Postpone procedure; schedule office examination<br />
C — 推迟操作；安排门诊就诊</td>
<td>The patient was examined 6 months ago with no new symptoms; a covering physician can make this decision from the existing record without another visit<br />
患者 6 个月前已接受检查且无新症状；代班医生可根据现有记录作出决策，无需再次就诊</td>
<td>No clinical indication to postpone a routine dental procedure in a recently examined, stable patient<br />
近期检查的稳定患者无推迟常规牙科操作的临床指征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Prescribe amoxicillin 1 hour before<br />
D — 术前 1 小时处方阿莫西林</td>
<td>Amoxicillin prophylaxis is reserved for AHA high-risk conditions (prosthetic valve, prior IE, specific CHD, cardiac transplant with valvulopathy); also contraindicated here due to penicillin allergy<br />
阿莫西林预防仅用于 AHA 高危情况；且本例青霉素过敏，亦为禁忌</td>
<td>Knowing the four prophylaxis indications prevents this error; penicillin allergy is a secondary distractor<br />
熟悉四类预防适应证可防止此错误；青霉素过敏为次要干扰因素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Prescribe clindamycin 1 hour before<br />
E — 术前 1 小时处方克林霉素</td>
<td>Clindamycin is no longer recommended for IE prophylaxis for any dental procedure due to high rates of <em>Clostridioides difficile</em> colitis and insufficient evidence of benefit<br />
克林霉素因艰难梭菌结肠炎发生率高且 IE 预防疗效证据不足，已不再推荐用于任何牙科操作的 IE 预防</td>
<td>AHA removed clindamycin from the alternative prophylaxis list in 2021; wrong on two levels here: no indication + wrong drug<br />
AHA 于 2021 年将克林霉素从替代预防药物列表中删除；本题双重错误：无适应证且药物选择错误</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most dangerous distractor is Option D: many students recall "penicillin allergy → use an alternative for dental prophylaxis" but fail to first ask whether prophylaxis is indicated at all for uncomplicated MVP — it is not.*

最危险的干扰项是 D 选项：许多学生记得"青霉素过敏→换用替代药物做牙科预防"，却忘记首先判断单纯 MVP 是否有预防指征——答案是没有。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Cardiac Conditions Requiring vs. Not Requiring IE Prophylaxis Before Dental Procedures / 牙科操作前需要与不需要 IE 预防的心脏病变对比

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>High-Risk: Prophylaxis Indicated</strong><br />
<strong>高危：需要预防</strong></th>
<th><strong>Low-Risk: No Prophylaxis</strong><br />
<strong>低危：无需预防</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Valve hardware<br />
瓣膜装置</td>
<td>Prosthetic cardiac valve (mechanical or bioprosthetic, any position)<br />
人工心脏瓣膜（机械瓣或生物瓣，任何位置）</td>
<td>Native valve disease without other criteria<br />
无其他标准的自身瓣膜病变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Prior IE history<br />
既往 IE 病史</td>
<td>Yes — any prior episode of infective endocarditis<br />
是——任何既往感染性心内膜炎发作史</td>
<td>No prior IE<br />
无既往 IE</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Congenital heart disease<br />
先天性心脏病</td>
<td>Unrepaired cyanotic CHD; prosthetic repair &lt;6 months; repaired CHD with residual defect<br />
未修补的发绀型先天性心脏病；人工材料修补 &lt;6 个月；修补后遗留缺损</td>
<td>Fully repaired CHD with no residual defect &gt;6 months; isolated ASD/VSD/PDA fully corrected<br />
完全修补后无残余缺损 &gt;6 个月；单纯完全纠正的 ASD/VSD/PDA</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Cardiac transplant<br />
心脏移植</td>
<td>Transplant recipient who develops valvulopathy<br />
发生瓣膜病的心脏移植受者</td>
<td>Transplant recipient without valvulopathy<br />
无瓣膜病的心脏移植受者</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Mitral valve prolapse<br />
二尖瓣脱垂</td>
<td>Not an indication per current AHA guidelines (even with regurgitation)<br />
按现行 AHA 指南不是适应证（即便伴反流）</td>
<td>All MVP patients — especially those without a regurgitant murmur<br />
所有 MVP 患者——尤其无反流杂音者</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Rheumatic heart disease / bicuspid AV<br />
风湿性心脏病 / 二叶式主动脉瓣</td>
<td>Not in current AHA high-risk list (removed in 2007)<br />
不在现行 AHA 高危列表中（2007 年删除）</td>
<td>Per 2007 AHA guidelines, no longer an indication<br />
按 2007 年 AHA 指南，已不再是适应证</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**IE prophylaxis before dental procedures is restricted to four high-risk conditions — prosthetic valve, prior endocarditis, specific congenital heart disease, and cardiac transplant with valvulopathy — and uncomplicated MVP does not qualify.**

**牙科操作前 IE 预防用药仅限于四类高危情况——人工瓣膜、既往心内膜炎、特定先天性心脏病、伴瓣膜病的心脏移植——单纯二尖瓣脱垂不符合指征。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "TECH" for the 4 IE Prophylaxis Indications / 记忆钩 — "TECH" 记住 IE 预防的 4 类适应证:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>T</strong>ransplant (cardiac) with valvulopathy — heart transplant recipients who develop valve disease qualify<br />
<strong>T</strong>ransplant（心脏移植）伴瓣膜病——心脏移植后出现瓣膜病变的受者符合适应证<br />
• <strong>E</strong>ndocarditis (prior history) — any prior IE episode automatically qualifies<br />
<strong>E</strong>ndocarditis（既往心内膜炎）——任何既往 IE 发作史均自动符合适应证<br />
• <strong>C</strong>ongenital heart disease — unrepaired cyanotic, prosthetic repair &lt;6 months, or residual defect<br />
<strong>C</strong>ongenital heart disease（先天性心脏病）——未修补发绀型、人工材料修补 &lt;6 个月或残余缺损<br />
• <strong>H</strong>ardware = prosthetic valve — mechanical or bioprosthetic, any cardiac position<br />
<strong>H</strong>ardware = 人工瓣膜——机械瓣或生物瓣，任何心脏位置</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — IE Prophylaxis: Guidelines, Drug Selection, and Dental Procedures / 高频知识表 — IE 预防：指南、药物选择与牙科操作

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>AHA 2007 guideline revision<br />
AHA 2007 年指南修订</td>
<td>Dramatically narrowed indications; explicitly removed MVP, rheumatic heart disease, bicuspid aortic valve, and calcific aortic stenosis from the high-risk list<br />
大幅缩窄适应证；明确将 MVP、风湿性心脏病、二叶式主动脉瓣和钙化性主动脉狭窄从高危列表中删除</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>First-line prophylaxis agent<br />
一线预防药物</td>
<td>Amoxicillin 2 g PO 30–60 min before procedure (only if no penicillin allergy and prophylaxis is indicated)<br />
阿莫西林 2 g 口服，术前 30–60 分钟（仅在无青霉素过敏且有预防适应证时）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Current penicillin-allergic alternatives<br />
现行青霉素过敏替代方案</td>
<td>Cephalexin 2 g, azithromycin 500 mg, or clarithromycin 500 mg; clindamycin is no longer recommended (AHA 2021 update)<br />
头孢氨苄 2 g、阿奇霉素 500 mg 或克拉霉素 500 mg；克林霉素已不再推荐（AHA 2021 年更新）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Why clindamycin was removed<br />
克林霉素被删除的原因</td>
<td>High incidence of <em>Clostridioides difficile</em> colitis and limited evidence of IE prevention benefit outweigh any theoretical advantage<br />
艰难梭菌结肠炎发生率高，且 IE 预防疗效证据有限，风险远超理论收益</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Dental procedures requiring prophylaxis evaluation<br />
需要评估预防的牙科操作</td>
<td>Those disrupting gingival tissue or the periapical region: scaling, extractions, root canal beyond apex; routine cleanings, X-rays, and orthodontic adjustments do NOT require prophylaxis<br />
破坏牙龈组织或根尖周区域的操作：刮治、拔牙、根管治疗超出根尖；常规清洁、X 线片和正畸调整不需要预防</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>MVP historical context<br />
MVP 历史背景</td>
<td>Pre-2007: MVP with regurgitation required prophylaxis; post-2007: MVP removed entirely from indications regardless of regurgitation<br />
2007 年前：MVP 伴反流需要预防；2007 年后：MVP 无论是否伴反流均从适应证中完全删除</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Covering physician authority<br />
代班医生的决策权限</td>
<td>A covering physician may use existing records to make prophylaxis decisions; no need to postpone stable, recently examined patients for new workup<br />
代班医生可使用现有病历作出预防决策；近期检查的稳定患者无需推迟以获取新检查结果</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of MVP presentations:** MVP can range from isolated midsystolic click to click + late systolic murmur; the murmur indicates mitral regurgitation, but even with MR, current AHA guidelines no longer require IE prophylaxis\
  **MVP 表现鉴别:** MVP 可从单纯收缩中期喀喇音到喀喇音+收缩晚期杂音不等；杂音提示二尖瓣反流，但即便有反流，现行 AHA 指南也不再要求 IE 预防

- **Key complication of unnecessary prophylaxis:** Antibiotic overuse drives resistance, allergic reactions, and *C. difficile* colitis; withholding prophylaxis in low-risk patients is the patient-safety–conscious choice\
  **不必要预防的主要并发症:** 抗生素过度使用导致耐药性、过敏反应和艰难梭菌结肠炎；对低危患者不给予预防用药是注重患者安全的正确选择

- **Variant — prosthetic mitral valve with penicillin allergy:** Would require cephalexin 2 g (if non-anaphylactic penicillin allergy) or azithromycin 500 mg (if anaphylactic); prosthetic valve = highest-risk TECH category\
  **题目变式——人工二尖瓣伴青霉素过敏:** 需头孢氨苄 2 g（非过敏反应型青霉素过敏）或阿奇霉素 500 mg（过敏反应型）；人工瓣膜 = TECH 最高危类别

- **Risk factor insight — IE in general:** IE risk factors include poor dentition, IV drug use, indwelling catheters, and immunosuppression — these inform who may present with IE clinically, but do NOT determine who receives prophylaxis before dental procedures\
  **IE 危险因素洞察:** IE 危险因素包括口腔卫生差、静脉吸毒、留置导管和免疫抑制——这些因素有助于临床识别 IE 发病，但不决定谁在牙科操作前接受预防用药

# Question 27 — Decisional Capacity Assessment in End-of-Life Care / 终末期医疗决策能力评估

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>52-year-old woman</strong> with <strong>amyotrophic lateral sclerosis</strong> has been receiving <strong>mechanical ventilation</strong> in the hospital for the past <strong>4 weeks</strong>. She is taking no medications. Attempts at discontinuing mechanical ventilation have been unsuccessful. Her parents visit her often and participate in her health care decisions. The physician tells her and her parents that she could require mechanical ventilation for <strong>several more years</strong> and recommends transfer to a facility for ventilator-dependent patients. Although her parents approve of this recommendation, the patient <strong>refuses placement</strong> and asks to have <strong>mechanical ventilation and all other life-sustaining treatments withheld</strong>. She says, "I would rather die now than spend the rest of my life in one of those places."</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Ask the parents privately about the patient's prior beliefs about long-term care<br />
B) Assess the patient's mental capacity to make her own health care decisions<br />
C) Continue current treatment and start additional treatment as needed<br />
D) Continue current treatment but do not start any new life-sustaining treatment<br />
E) Seek a court order to appoint a guardian to make her health care decisions</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: B</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>52-year-old woman, alert and communicative<br />
52岁女性，意识清醒、可沟通</td>
<td>Patient appears awake and verbal — capacity cannot be assumed absent without formal assessment<br />
患者表现为清醒可沟通，不能凭外观假设其无决策能力，需正式评估</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Amyotrophic lateral sclerosis (ALS)<br />
肌萎缩侧索硬化症（ALS）</td>
<td>ALS is a motor neuron disease that typically preserves cognition — diagnosis alone does not establish incapacity<br />
ALS以运动神经元受损为主，认知通常保留，不能因诊断本身认定患者无决策能力</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>4 weeks on mechanical ventilation, weaning failed<br />
机械通气4周，撤机失败</td>
<td>Establishes a poor prognosis for respiratory independence — patient faces a permanent, life-altering decision<br />
预后差、高度依赖呼吸机，患者面对的是影响终身的重大决策，提示需严格能力评估</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Parents approve transfer; patient refuses<br />
父母同意转院；患者拒绝</td>
<td>Conflict between surrogate preferences and patient's expressed wishes — patient's own capacity determines who holds legal authority<br />
代理人与患者意愿冲突，患者是否有决策能力决定谁的意见具有法律效力</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>"I would rather die now than spend the rest of my life in one of those places"<br />
"我宁愿现在死，也不愿在那种地方度过余生"</td>
<td>Articulate, value-based statement suggesting reasoning ability — but depression or other impairing factors must be excluded<br />
表达清晰且具逻辑性，体现价值取向，但需排除抑郁等损害决策质量的因素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Requests withdrawal of all life-sustaining treatment<br />
要求撤除所有维持生命治疗</td>
<td>High-stakes, irreversible decision — triggers mandatory rigorous capacity assessment before any treatment change<br />
高风险、不可逆决定，任何治疗变更前必须先进行严格的决策能力评估</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Decisional capacity** is the *clinical* determination of whether a patient can make informed, autonomous medical decisions. It is **task-specific** (not global) and is **not** equivalent to legal competence (a court determination):

**决策能力**是临床对患者能否自主做出知情医疗决定的判断。它具有**任务特异性**（非全局性），且**不等同于**法律意义上的"行为能力"（需法院裁定）：

- The **4-element UARCC framework** must all be met: Understanding the diagnosis/prognosis, Appreciation of personal significance, Reasoning through options, Communicating a Consistent Choice\
  **4要素UARCC框架**必须全部满足：理解（Understanding）诊断预后、领悟（Appreciation）对自身的意义、推理（Reasoning）各选项利弊、表达一致选择（Consistent Choice）

- Capacity can be assessed by **any physician** at the bedside; psychiatry consultation is helpful when capacity is in doubt\
  任何医生均可在床旁评估决策能力；当存疑时请精神科会诊更为审慎

- Factors that may **impair** capacity include: delirium, severe depression, psychosis, substance intoxication — none of these automatically establishes incapacity without formal assessment\
  可能**损害**决策能力的因素：谵妄、重度抑郁、精神病、药物中毒——任何一项都不自动等同于"无能力"，需正式评估

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** ALS destroys motor neurons, not cortical neurons — cognitive and emotional function remain intact until very late stages, so assume capacity is preserved unless assessment proves otherwise.

**解剖小窍门:** ALS破坏运动神经元，不破坏皮层神经元——认知与情感功能通常保留至晚期，默认患者保有决策能力，除非评估证明相反。

## 3. Correct Answer (B) — Decisional Capacity Assessment / 正确答案 (B) — 决策能力评估

**Decisional capacity assessment** is the mandatory first step whenever a patient makes a high-stakes decision — especially refusal of life-sustaining treatment — that conflicts with clinician or family preferences:

**决策能力评估**是患者做出重大决策（尤其是拒绝维持生命治疗）且与医生或家属意见相悖时的必要首步：

- The physician must confirm the patient possesses all four UARCC elements before honoring or overriding any refusal of mechanical ventilation\
  在接受或推翻拒绝机械通气的意愿之前，医生必须确认患者具备UARCC全部4个要素

- Excluding **depression** is especially critical — a patient requesting withdrawal of life-sustaining treatment must be screened for major depressive disorder, which can impair genuine autonomous decision-making\
  排除**抑郁症**尤为关键——请求撤除维持生命治疗的患者必须筛查重度抑郁，后者可损害真正自主的决策质量

- Once capacity is confirmed, the patient's **autonomous refusal must be respected**, regardless of family or physician disagreement — autonomy supersedes beneficence for capacitated adults\
  一旦确认具备能力，必须**尊重患者的自主拒绝**，无论家属或医生是否同意——对有能力的成年人，自主权优先于有利原则

**Diagnosis:** This patient is alert, communicative, and makes a logically consistent, value-based statement — she likely has capacity, but the assessment must be formally completed and depression excluded before any irreversible action is taken.

**诊断:** 该患者清醒、可沟通，做出符合逻辑、基于价值观的陈述——她很可能具备决策能力，但必须完成正式评估并排除抑郁，方可采取任何不可逆行动。

**Treatment:** Once capacity is confirmed, her refusal of mechanical ventilation is legally and ethically binding; palliative care and symptom management should be initiated.

**治疗:** 一旦确认其具备决策能力，其拒绝机械通气的意愿在法律和伦理上均具约束力；应启动姑息治疗和症状管理。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Ask the parents privately about the patient's prior beliefs about long-term care<br />
A — 私下询问父母关于患者过去对长期护理的看法</td>
<td>Parents' insight is supplementary, not decisive; it cannot override the patient's current expressed wishes if she has capacity — and this step skips the mandatory capacity assessment<br />
父母意见可作参考，但若患者有决策能力则不能凌驾于其当前意愿之上；此选项跳过了必须先做的能力评估</td>
<td>Surrogate input is only decisive when the patient lacks capacity; assess capacity first<br />
代理人意见只在患者无决策能力时才具决定性；应先评估能力</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Assess the patient's mental capacity to make her own health care decisions ✓<br />
B — 评估患者自主做出医疗决策的精神能力 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — mandatory first step before honoring or overriding a high-stakes refusal of life-sustaining treatment; also screens for depression<br />
正确——在接受或推翻拒绝维持生命治疗这一重大决策之前的必要首步；同时筛查抑郁</td>
<td>Capacity assessment precedes all other actions when a patient refuses life-sustaining treatment<br />
当患者拒绝维持生命治疗时，能力评估先于所有其他行动</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Continue current treatment and start additional treatment as needed<br />
C — 继续当前治疗并按需启动额外治疗</td>
<td>Ignores the patient's explicit refusal entirely; continuing and escalating treatment without assessing capacity is ethically impermissible<br />
完全无视患者明确拒绝；在未评估能力的情况下继续并升级治疗在伦理上不被允许</td>
<td>Patient autonomy over bodily integrity must be respected after capacity is confirmed<br />
确认能力后必须尊重患者对自身的自主权，不能在缺乏正当程序的情况下推翻</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Continue current treatment but do not start any new life-sustaining treatment<br />
D — 继续当前治疗，但不启动任何新的维持生命治疗</td>
<td>A partial compromise that still overrides the patient's clear request to withdraw <em>existing</em> mechanical ventilation — and is premature without a capacity assessment<br />
部分妥协方案，仍违背患者明确要求撤除<em>现有</em>机械通气的意愿，且在能力评估之前做此决定为时过早</td>
<td>Withholding new vs. withdrawing existing treatment are ethically equivalent — both require confirmed capacity first<br />
拒绝新治疗与撤除现有治疗在伦理上等同——两者均需先确认患者能力</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Seek a court order to appoint a guardian to make her health care decisions<br />
E — 申请法院命令指定监护人代为做出医疗决策</td>
<td>Premature and disrespectful of autonomy; guardianship is warranted only when a patient is found to lack capacity across all domains — which has not been established here<br />
过于仓促且不尊重自主权；只有当患者被正式评估为全面丧失决策能力后才适合申请监护——此前提尚未成立</td>
<td>Court guardianship is a last resort after capacity assessment confirms global incapacity<br />
法院监护是在能力评估确认全面丧失后的最终手段</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Choice D — "continue current treatment but withhold new treatment" feels like a reasonable ethical middle ground, but it still violates the patient's explicit request to withdraw existing mechanical ventilation, making it unjustifiable before a capacity assessment is completed.*

选项D最容易迷惑考生——"继续当前治疗但不新增"看似合理折中，但仍无视患者要求撤除*现有*机械通气的明确意愿，在完成能力评估前这样做在伦理上站不住脚。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Decisional Capacity vs. Legal Competence vs. Surrogate Decision-Making / 决策能力 vs. 法律行为能力 vs. 代理决策对比

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Decisional Capacity</strong><br />
<strong>决策能力（临床）</strong></th>
<th><strong>Legal Competence</strong><br />
<strong>法律行为能力</strong></th>
<th><strong>Surrogate Decision-Making</strong><br />
<strong>代理决策</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Who determines it<br />
由谁判定</td>
<td>Any physician (bedside assessment)<br />
任何医生（床旁评估）</td>
<td>Court of law<br />
法院</td>
<td>Invoked only when patient lacks capacity<br />
仅在患者丧失能力时启用</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Scope<br />
范围</td>
<td>Decision-specific (task-specific)<br />
针对特定决策（任务特异性）</td>
<td>Global — all decisions<br />
全面——涵盖所有决定</td>
<td>Covers decisions patient cannot make<br />
覆盖患者无法自主做出的决定</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Standard used<br />
使用标准</td>
<td>UARCC: Understanding, Appreciation, Reasoning, Consistent Choice<br />
UARCC四要素：理解、领悟、推理、一致选择</td>
<td>Legal criteria vary by jurisdiction<br />
法律标准因司法管辖区而异</td>
<td>Substituted judgment or best interest standard<br />
替代判断原则或最佳利益原则</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Reversibility<br />
可逆性</td>
<td>Can fluctuate (lost with delirium/depression, regained after treatment)<br />
可波动（谵妄/抑郁期间丧失，治疗后可恢复）</td>
<td>Rarely reversed once legally established<br />
一旦法律确定，极少撤销</td>
<td>Ends when patient regains capacity<br />
患者恢复能力即终止</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>When guardian is needed<br />
何时需要监护人</td>
<td>Only after capacity confirmed globally absent<br />
仅在评估确认全面丧失能力后</td>
<td>Court declares patient globally incompetent<br />
法院裁定患者全面无行为能力</td>
<td>Legal guardian appointed by court order<br />
法院指定法定监护人</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**Before honoring or overriding any patient's refusal of life-sustaining treatment, always perform a formal decisional capacity assessment — especially to exclude depression, which can impair autonomous end-of-life decision-making.**

**在接受或推翻患者拒绝维持生命治疗的任何意愿之前，必须先进行正式的决策能力评估——尤其要排除可损害自主终末期决策的抑郁症。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — UARCC Capacity Framework / 记忆钩 — UARCC 决策能力四要素框架:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>U</strong>nderstanding — patient grasps the diagnosis, prognosis, and treatment options / 理解——患者明白诊断、预后及治疗选项<br />
• <strong>A</strong>ppreciation — patient recognizes how the situation applies to <em>them</em> personally / 领悟——患者认识到情况对<em>自身</em>的具体意义<br />
• <strong>R</strong>easoning — patient can weigh pros and cons in a logically coherent way / 推理——患者能合乎逻辑地权衡利弊<br />
• <strong>C</strong>onsistent <strong>C</strong>hoice — patient expresses the same preference over time without coercion / 一致选择——患者在不同时间点自愿表达相同意愿</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Decisional Capacity & End-of-Life Ethics / 高频知识表 — 决策能力与终末期医疗伦理

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Who can assess capacity<br />
谁可以评估决策能力</td>
<td>Any licensed physician; psychiatry consultation helpful but not required; formal neuropsychological testing rarely needed<br />
任何执照医生均可；精神科会诊有帮助但非必须；正式神经心理测试极少需要</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Capacity is decision-specific<br />
能力具有决策特异性</td>
<td>A patient may have capacity to refuse a blood draw but lack capacity to consent to major surgery; always assess for the <em>specific</em> decision at hand<br />
患者可能有能力拒绝抽血但无能力同意大手术；始终针对<em>具体</em>决策进行评估</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Role of depression in capacity<br />
抑郁在能力评估中的作用</td>
<td>Depression impairs appreciation and reasoning, especially for irreversible end-of-life decisions; screen with PHQ-9 and treat before proceeding<br />
抑郁损害领悟与推理能力，对不可逆终末期决策影响尤甚；用PHQ-9筛查，治疗后再评估</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Withholding vs. withdrawing treatment<br />
拒绝启动 vs. 撤除治疗</td>
<td>Ethically and legally equivalent in U.S. law; both permissible when patient has capacity or surrogate follows patient's known wishes<br />
在美国法律上伦理和法律等同；患者有能力或代理人依据患者已知意愿同意时，两者均被允许</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Surrogate hierarchy when capacity absent<br />
患者无能力时代理人层级顺序</td>
<td>(1) Healthcare proxy/durable POA → (2) Spouse → (3) Adult children → (4) Parents → (5) Siblings; invoked only after capacity confirmed absent<br />
（1）医疗代理人/持久授权书 → （2）配偶 → （3）成年子女 → （4）父母 → （5）兄弟姐妹；仅在确认患者丧失能力后启用</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Autonomy vs. beneficence conflict<br />
自主权 vs. 有利原则冲突</td>
<td>When a capacitated patient refuses beneficial treatment, autonomy prevails; physician's role is to ensure the decision is informed and voluntary, not to override it<br />
当有决策能力的患者拒绝有益治疗时，自主权优先；医生职责是确保决策知情自愿，而非推翻它</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ALS-specific ethics<br />
ALS特异性伦理考量</td>
<td>ALS preserves cognition; patients often execute advance directives early; physical disability (ventilator dependence, paralysis) alone never establishes incapacity<br />
ALS保留认知功能；患者常早期立预嘱；仅凭身体残障（依赖呼吸机、瘫痪）不能认定无决策能力</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of capacity impairment:** Delirium (most common inpatient cause, acute and reversible), major depression (screen with PHQ-9), dementia (global and progressive), psychosis, severe undertreated pain, substance intoxication — each must be treated before concluding permanent incapacity\
  **影响决策能力的鉴别诊断:** 谵妄（住院最常见原因，急性可逆），重度抑郁（PHQ-9筛查），痴呆（全面性进行性），精神病，重度未控制疼痛，药物中毒——应先治疗，再判断是否永久丧失能力

- **Key complication — family override:** Parents or family members cannot override a capacitated patient's autonomous decision even if they disagree; persistent family-patient conflict should trigger ethics committee consultation\
  **关键并发症——家属凌驾:** 父母或家属不能推翻有决策能力患者的自主决定，即便意见相左；家属与患者持续冲突时应启动伦理委员会会诊

- **Variant — patient later loses capacity:** If this patient becomes unresponsive, her previously expressed wishes to withdraw ventilation are legally binding and should guide surrogate decisions via substituted judgment\
  **题目变式——患者日后丧失能力:** 若该患者日后变为无反应，其此前明确表达的撤除呼吸机意愿具有法律约束力，代理人应依替代判断原则遵从

- **Mnemonic — "CURVES" alternate framework:** Choosing and communicating, Understanding, Reasoning, Value consistency, Evaluation of consequences, Stability over time — an alternative to UARCC used in some ethics curricula\
  **记忆法——"CURVES"替代框架:** Choosing（选择与表达）、Understanding（理解）、Reasoning（推理）、Value consistency（价值一致性）、Evaluation of consequences（评估后果）、Stability over time（时间稳定性）——部分伦理课程使用的UARCC替代框架

# Question 28 — Basal Cell Carcinoma / 基底细胞癌

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>62-year-old man</strong> comes to the physician because of a <strong>lesion on his right temple for 3 months</strong>. He works as a <strong>farmer</strong>. Examination shows a <strong>1.5-cm ulcerated lesion</strong> over the right temple area; the lesion has a <strong>raised margin</strong> and a <strong>waxy border</strong>. If left untreated, which of the following is the most likely sequela of the lesion?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most likely sequela if left untreated?</strong></p>
<p>A) Local spread<br />
B) Lymphatic invasion<br />
C) Regression<br />
D) Systemic metastases</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: A</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>62-year-old man, farmer<br />
62岁男性，农民</td>
<td>Chronic UV exposure is the #1 risk factor for BCC; outdoor occupation increases lifetime sun exposure<br />
慢性紫外线暴露是BCC最主要危险因素；户外职业意味着终身累积日晒量高</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Lesion on right temple, 3 months<br />
右太阳穴病变，持续3个月</td>
<td>Sun-exposed area of head and neck is the classic location for BCC; slow growth over months is typical<br />
头颈部日光暴露区是BCC的经典好发部位；数月缓慢生长符合其生物学行为</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>1.5-cm ulcerated lesion<br />
1.5厘米溃疡性病变</td>
<td>Central ulceration ("rodent ulcer") is a hallmark of nodular BCC<br />
中央溃疡（"啮齿动物溃疡"）是结节型BCC的特征性表现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Raised margin<br />
隆起边缘</td>
<td>Rolled/raised border is the classic morphology distinguishing BCC from other skin malignancies<br />
卷起/隆起的边缘是BCC区别于其他皮肤恶性肿瘤的经典形态学特征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Waxy border<br />
蜡样边界</td>
<td>Pearly, waxy, translucent border reflects the basal cell origin and is pathognomonic for BCC<br />
珍珠样、蜡样、半透明边缘反映基底细胞起源，是BCC的病理特征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>"If left untreated" — asking sequela<br />
问"若不治疗"的后果</td>
<td>Tests understanding that BCC spreads locally but rarely metastasizes — the key distinguishing behavior<br />
考查BCC局部扩散但极少转移的关键生物学行为</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Basal cell carcinoma** arises from the **undifferentiated basal cells** of the epidermis (not keratinocytes or melanocytes). The **Hedgehog signaling pathway** (specifically PTCH1 mutation) is the molecular driver, activated by **chronic UV radiation**:

**基底细胞癌**起源于表皮的**未分化基底细胞**（不是角质细胞或黑色素细胞）。**Hedgehog信号通路**（特别是PTCH1突变）是分子驱动因素，由**慢性紫外线辐射**激活：

- UV damage → PTCH1 loss-of-function mutation → unopposed Smoothened (SMO) activity → Gli transcription factor activation → uncontrolled basal cell proliferation\
  紫外线损伤 → PTCH1功能缺失突变 → Smoothened（SMO）不受抑制 → Gli转录因子激活 → 基底细胞不受控制增殖

- Tumor lacks capacity for lymphovascular invasion due to absent expression of invasion-enabling matrix metalloproteinases in sufficient quantity\
  肿瘤因缺乏足量的侵袭性基质金属蛋白酶表达，不具备淋巴血管侵犯能力

- Local destruction occurs via direct extension — can erode bone, cartilage, and orbital structures if neglected\
  局部破坏通过直接蔓延发生——若忽视治疗可侵蚀骨骼、软骨和眶周结构

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** BCC favors the "H-zone" of the face (nasolabial fold, periocular, periauricular, temple) — embryonic fusion planes that allow deeper local invasion.

**解剖小窍门:** BCC好发于面部"H区"（鼻唇沟、眶周、耳周、太阳穴）——这些胚胎融合平面允许更深的局部侵犯。

---

## 3. Correct Answer (A) — Local Spread / 正确答案 (A) — 局部扩散

**Local spread** is the defining natural history of untreated BCC: the tumor relentlessly invades adjacent tissue through direct extension while maintaining near-zero metastatic potential:

**局部扩散**是未治疗BCC的决定性自然病程：肿瘤通过直接蔓延无情地侵犯邻近组织，同时保持接近零的转移潜能：

- BCC is locally destructive — "rodent ulcer" historically described progressive tissue erosion resembling a gnawing rat\
  BCC具局部破坏性——历史上"啮齿动物溃疡"描述了类似鼠咬的进行性组织侵蚀

- Metastatic rate \< 0.1% — one of the lowest of any malignancy\
  转移率 \< 0.1%——是所有恶性肿瘤中最低的之一

- Untreated lesions on face can erode into orbit, nasal passages, skull base over years\
  面部未治疗病变数年内可侵蚀眼眶、鼻道、颅底

**Diagnosis:** Classic triad: pearly/waxy papule or nodule + rolled borders + central ulceration on sun-exposed area (head/neck 80% of cases). Diagnosis confirmed by punch, shave, or excisional biopsy.

**诊断:** 经典三联征：日光暴露区（80%在头颈部）珍珠样/蜡样丘疹或结节 + 卷起边缘 + 中央溃疡。通过穿刺、刮削或切除活检确诊。

**Treatment:** Complete surgical excision or Mohs micrographic surgery (gold standard for high-risk areas like face/temple). Re-excision with negative margins if incomplete. Vismodegib (Hedgehog pathway inhibitor) for advanced/metastatic cases.

**治疗:** 完整手术切除或Mohs显微外科手术（面部/太阳穴等高风险区域的金标准）。切除不完全时需再次切除至阴性切缘。晚期/转移性病例使用Vismodegib（Hedgehog通路抑制剂）。

---

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Local spread ✓<br />
A — 局部扩散 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — BCC's hallmark behavior: local invasion without lymphatic or hematogenous spread<br />
正确——BCC的标志性行为：局部侵犯，无淋巴或血行播散</td>
<td>Waxy border + rolled margin + ulceration + sun-exposed site = BCC morphology<br />
蜡样边界 + 卷起边缘 + 溃疡 + 日光暴露部位 = BCC形态学</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Lymphatic invasion<br />
B — 淋巴侵犯</td>
<td>Lymphatic spread is characteristic of cutaneous SCC and oropharyngeal SCC, NOT BCC<br />
淋巴扩散是皮肤SCC和口咽SCC的特征，而非BCC</td>
<td>BCC lacks the invasive machinery (MMPs, E-cadherin loss) for lymphovascular invasion<br />
BCC缺乏淋巴血管侵犯所需的侵袭机制（MMPs、E-钙黏蛋白缺失）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Regression<br />
C — 自行消退</td>
<td>Spontaneous regression occurs in keratoacanthoma, not BCC; keratoacanthoma has dome-shape + keratin-filled crater<br />
自行消退发生于角化棘皮瘤，而非BCC；角化棘皮瘤有穹顶形态+角蛋白填充的火山口</td>
<td>Keratoacanthoma regresses in weeks-months; BCC grows relentlessly without treatment<br />
角化棘皮瘤数周至数月内消退；BCC在不治疗的情况下持续生长</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Systemic metastases<br />
D — 系统性转移</td>
<td>Systemic metastases (liver, lung, brain) are characteristic of melanoma, not BCC<br />
系统性转移（肝、肺、脑）是黑色素瘤的特征，而非BCC</td>
<td>BCC metastatic rate &lt; 0.1%; melanoma frequently metastasizes hematogenously<br />
BCC转移率 &lt; 0.1%；黑色素瘤频繁发生血行转移</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The highest-yield distractor is D (systemic metastases) — students confuse BCC with melanoma because both occur on sun-exposed skin, but BCC is derived from basal cells (not melanocytes) and virtually never metastasizes.*

D选项（系统性转移）是最高频干扰项——学生会混淆BCC与黑色素瘤，因为两者都发生在日光暴露皮肤，但BCC来源于基底细胞（非黑色素细胞），几乎不会转移。

---

</tr>

---

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**Basal cell carcinoma — the most common skin cancer — presents as a pearly, waxy nodule with rolled borders and central ulceration on sun-exposed areas, and its natural history is relentless local invasion without metastasis.**

**基底细胞癌——最常见的皮肤癌——表现为日光暴露区域珍珠样蜡样结节伴卷起边缘和中央溃疡，其自然病程是无休止的局部侵犯而不发生转移。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — BCC's "LOCAL" Rule / 记忆钩 — BCC的"局部"法则:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>L</strong>ocal invasion only — never lymphatics<br />
仅局部侵犯——从不侵犯淋巴管<br />
• <strong>O</strong>utdoor/UV exposure — #1 risk factor<br />
户外/紫外线暴露——第一大危险因素<br />
• <strong>C</strong>entral ulceration + rolled ("Cream") pearly border<br />
中央溃疡 + 卷起的珍珠样("奶油色")边缘<br />
• <strong>A</strong>lmost zero metastatic rate (&lt; 0.1%)<br />
转移率几乎为零（&lt; 0.1%）<br />
• <strong>L</strong>ocation: H-zone of face (temple, periocular, nasolabial)<br />
位置：面部H区（太阳穴、眶周、鼻唇沟）</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Basal Cell Carcinoma / 高频知识表 — 基底细胞癌

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Most common skin cancer<br />
最常见皮肤癌</td>
<td>BCC &gt; SCC &gt; Melanoma in incidence; BCC is most common overall malignancy in USA<br />
发病率：BCC &gt; SCC &gt; 黑色素瘤；BCC是美国最常见的恶性肿瘤</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Molecular pathogenesis<br />
分子发病机制</td>
<td>PTCH1 mutation (Hedgehog pathway) — targetable with Vismodegib (SMO inhibitor) for advanced disease<br />
PTCH1突变（Hedgehog通路）——晚期病变可用Vismodegib（SMO抑制剂）靶向治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>BCC subtypes<br />
BCC亚型</td>
<td>Nodular (most common, classic pearly papule); Superficial (least invasive); Morpheaform/Infiltrative (most aggressive, scar-like plaque, ill-defined borders)<br />
结节型（最常见，经典珍珠样丘疹）；表浅型（侵袭性最低）；硬化型/浸润型（最具侵袭性，瘢痕样斑块，边界不清）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment: Mohs surgery<br />
治疗：Mohs手术</td>
<td>Gold standard for BCC on face/high-risk areas; sequential resection with intraoperative margin assessment; maximizes tissue sparing<br />
面部/高风险区域BCC的金标准；序贯切除配合术中切缘评估；最大限度保留组织</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Gorlin syndrome<br />
Gorlin综合征</td>
<td>Autosomal dominant PTCH1 germline mutation → multiple BCCs at young age + jaw keratocysts + bifid ribs + calcified falx cerebri<br />
常染色体显性PTCH1胚系突变 → 年轻时多发BCC + 颌骨角化囊肿 + 分叉肋 + 钙化大脑镰</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Keratoacanthoma differentiation<br />
角化棘皮瘤鉴别</td>
<td>Keratoacanthoma: dome-shaped, keratin-filled crater, rapid growth then spontaneous involution (weeks-months); BCC: slow growth, waxy border, no regression<br />
角化棘皮瘤：穹顶形，角蛋白填充火山口，快速生长后自发消退（数周至数月）；BCC：缓慢生长，蜡样边界，不消退</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of ulcerated facial lesion:** SCC (indurated, hyperkeratotic), melanoma (pigmented, irregular), Merkel cell carcinoma (violaceous, rapidly growing), keratoacanthoma (dome + central keratin crater)\
  **面部溃疡性病变鉴别:** SCC（硬化、角化过度），黑色素瘤（色素沉着、不规则），Merkel细胞癌（紫罗兰色、快速生长），角化棘皮瘤（穹顶形+中央角蛋白火山口）

- **Key complication of neglected BCC:** Orbital invasion (periocular BCC), meningeal extension (scalp/temple BCC), carotid artery erosion — all from local spread, not metastasis\
  **忽视BCC的关键并发症:** 眶内侵犯（眶周BCC），脑膜蔓延（头皮/太阳穴BCC），颈动脉侵蚀——均来自局部扩散，而非转移

- **Risk factor profile beyond UV:** Arsenic exposure (historically medicinal), ionizing radiation, immunosuppression (transplant patients have 10× increased risk), xeroderma pigmentosum\
  **紫外线以外的危险因素:** 砷暴露（历史上医用），电离辐射，免疫抑制（移植患者风险增加10倍），着色性干皮病

- **Vismodegib mechanism:** SMO inhibitor — blocks aberrant Hedgehog signaling in advanced/metastatic BCC or Gorlin syndrome; resistance develops via SMO point mutations\
  **Vismodegib机制:** SMO抑制剂——阻断晚期/转移性BCC或Gorlin综合征中异常的Hedgehog信号；通过SMO点突变产生耐药

# Question 29 — Severe Hyperkalemia with Cardiac Toxicity / 重度高钾血症伴心脏毒性

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>57-year-old man</strong> comes to the emergency department because of a <strong>6-hour history of fatigue and mild shortness of breath</strong>. He has type 2 diabetes mellitus, hypertension, and <strong>anuric renal failure requiring hemodialysis</strong>. He reports having <strong>missed his regularly scheduled dialysis session 2 days ago</strong>. His current medications are enalapril, amlodipine, insulin, calcitriol, and calcium supplementation. His temperature is 37°C (98.6°F), pulse is 110/min, respirations are 24/min, and blood pressure is 160/100 mm Hg. Examination shows no jugular venous distention. Crackles are heard at both lung bases. Heart sounds are normal. Serum studies show a <strong>potassium concentration of 6.8 mEq/L</strong>, urea nitrogen concentration of 120 mg/dL, and creatinine concentration of 9.9 mg/dL. An ECG shows sinus tachycardia at 115/min, with <strong>widening of the PR and QRS intervals and peaked T waves</strong>.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Intravenous administration of which of the following is the most appropriate next step in treatment?</strong></p>
<p>A) Atenolol<br />
B) Calcium chloride<br />
C) Furosemide<br />
D) Lidocaine<br />
E) Magnesium sulfate<br />
F) 0.9% Saline</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: B</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Anuric renal failure on hemodialysis<br />
无尿性肾衰竭依赖血液透析</td>
<td>No renal potassium excretion; any missed dialysis leads to rapid K⁺ accumulation<br />
无法通过尿液排钾；漏透析即可迅速蓄积高钾</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Missed dialysis 2 days ago<br />
2天前漏做透析</td>
<td>Direct precipitant of hyperkalemia; establishes cause without guesswork<br />
高钾的直接诱因；无需猜测病因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Potassium 6.8 mEq/L<br />
血钾 6.8 mEq/L</td>
<td>Severe hyperkalemia (&gt;6.5 = critical); risk of ventricular fibrillation<br />
重度高钾（&gt;6.5 为危急）；室颤风险极高</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Widened PR and QRS intervals<br />
PR 间期及 QRS 增宽</td>
<td>ECG evidence of impaired conduction — myocardial membrane depolarization threshold dropping<br />
传导障碍的心电图证据——心肌细胞膜除极阈值下降</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Peaked T waves on ECG<br />
心电图出现帐篷样 T 波</td>
<td>Earliest and most classic ECG sign of hyperkalemia; signifies repolarization abnormality<br />
高钾最早出现且最经典的心电图表现；代表复极化异常</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Crackles at both lung bases<br />
双肺底湿啰音</td>
<td>Volume overload from missed dialysis — context for why furosemide is tempting but wrong<br />
漏透析所致容量过负荷——是迷惑项呋塞米的背景，但此时不是首选</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Hyperkalemia** causes life-threatening cardiac toxicity by altering the **resting membrane potential (RMP)** of myocardial cells:

**高钾血症**通过改变心肌细胞的**静息膜电位（RMP）**引发致命性心脏毒性：

- Elevated extracellular K⁺ reduces the electrochemical gradient across the cell membrane, making the RMP less negative (partial depolarization)\
  细胞外 K⁺ 升高，跨膜电化学梯度减小，RMP 变得不那么负（部分去极化）

- This slows Phase 0 (Na⁺ channel–dependent rapid depolarization), widening the QRS\
  这减慢了 0 相（Na⁺ 通道依赖的快速去极化），导致 QRS 增宽

- Repolarization is also altered, causing the tall, narrow "tented" T waves seen first on ECG\
  复极化也受影响，产生最早出现在心电图上的高尖帐篷样 T 波

- Progressive: peaked T → flat P → wide QRS → sine wave → VF/asystole\
  进展顺序：帐篷样 T → P 波消失 → QRS 增宽 → 正弦波形 → 室颤/心搏骤停

- IV calcium raises the threshold for action potential firing, stabilizing the membrane even without lowering K⁺\
  静脉钙剂提升动作电位触发阈值，即使不降低血钾也能立即稳定心肌膜

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** In hyperkalemia, think of the heart membrane as an overexcitable wire — calcium "insulates" the wire before you start pulling K⁺ out of the system.

**解剖小窍门:** 高钾时把心肌膜想象成一根过度敏感的导线——钙剂先"绝缘"这根导线，再去清除体内多余的 K⁺。

---

## 3. Correct Answer (B) — Calcium Chloride for Cardiac Membrane Stabilization / 正确答案 (B) — 氯化钙稳定心肌膜

**Calcium chloride** (or calcium gluconate) is the first-line emergent intervention when hyperkalemia produces ECG changes, because it directly antagonizes the cardiac membrane effects of hyperkalemia:

**氯化钙**（或葡萄糖酸钙）是高钾血症出现心电图改变时的一线急救干预，因为它直接拮抗高钾对心肌膜的影响：

- Raises the threshold potential of cardiac myocytes, restoring the margin between RMP and threshold\
  提升心肌细胞的阈电位，恢复 RMP 与阈值之间的安全差距

- Works within 1–3 minutes; duration 30–60 minutes — buys time for definitive treatment\
  起效 1–3 分钟；持续 30–60 分钟——为后续根治治疗争取时间

- Does NOT lower serum potassium — it is purely cardioprotective (membrane stabilizer, not a K⁺ shifter)\
  不降低血清钾——纯粹的心脏保护作用（膜稳定剂，不是转移钾）

- After calcium: shift K⁺ intracellularly (insulin + dextrose, sodium bicarbonate, β₂ agonists), then remove K⁺ (dialysis)\
  钙剂之后：将 K⁺ 转移至细胞内（胰岛素+葡萄糖、碳酸氢钠、β₂ 激动剂），再清除体内 K⁺（透析）

**Diagnosis:** ECG changes (peaked T waves + widened QRS/PR) with K⁺ 6.8 in an anuric ESRD patient who missed dialysis = severe hyperkalemia with cardiac toxicity.

**诊断:** 无尿 ESRD 漏透析患者血钾 6.8，ECG 示帐篷样 T 波 + QRS/PR 增宽 = 重度高钾血症伴心脏毒性。

**Treatment:** IV calcium chloride immediately → insulin + dextrose → urgent hemodialysis.

**治疗:** 立即静脉注射氯化钙 → 胰岛素 + 葡萄糖 → 紧急血液透析。

---

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Atenolol<br />
A — 阿替洛尔</td>
<td>β₁-blocker; lowers BP/HR but does nothing to stabilize cardiac membrane or lower K⁺; would worsen conduction in an already slowed system<br />
β₁ 受体阻滞剂；能降压降心率，但不能稳定心肌膜或降钾；还可能加重已受损的传导</td>
<td>Target = membrane stabilization, not BP control<br />
目标是膜稳定，不是降压</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Calcium chloride ✓<br />
B — 氯化钙 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — directly antagonizes cardiac membrane toxicity of hyperkalemia within minutes, buying time for K⁺ removal<br />
正确——数分钟内直接拮抗高钾对心肌膜的毒性，为清除钾争取时间</td>
<td>Only agent that addresses the immediate arrhythmia risk<br />
唯一直接处理即刻心律失常风险的药物</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Furosemide<br />
C — 呋塞米</td>
<td>Loop diuretic that can remove K⁺ via urine, but this patient is anuric — no urine means no effect; also does not stabilize the membrane<br />
袢利尿剂可经尿排钾，但此患者无尿——没有尿液即无效；也不能稳定心肌膜</td>
<td>Anuria makes furosemide ineffective; membrane stabilization comes first regardless<br />
无尿使呋塞米无效；无论如何膜稳定是第一步</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Lidocaine<br />
D — 利多卡因</td>
<td>Class Ib antiarrhythmic blocking Na⁺ channels; used for ventricular tachyarrhythmias, not for hyperkalemia-induced conduction slowing<br />
Ib 类抗心律失常药，阻断 Na⁺ 通道；用于室性快速型心律失常，不用于高钾引起的传导减慢</td>
<td>Lidocaine further suppresses conduction — wrong mechanism entirely<br />
利多卡因进一步抑制传导——机制完全错误</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Magnesium sulfate<br />
E — 硫酸镁</td>
<td>Indicated for torsades de pointes (prolonged QT + polymorphic VT); this ECG shows widened QRS/peaked T from hyperkalemia, not torsades<br />
适应证是尖端扭转型室速（QT 延长 + 多形性室速）；本例 ECG 改变源于高钾，不是尖端扭转</td>
<td>Torsades vs hyperkalemia ECG: QT prolongation vs peaked T + wide QRS<br />
尖端扭转 vs 高钾心电图：QT 延长 vs 帐篷样 T + QRS 增宽</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>F — 0.9% Saline<br />
F — 0.9% 生理盐水</td>
<td>Volume expansion in an anuric, volume-overloaded patient with crackles would worsen pulmonary edema; does not lower K⁺ or stabilize membrane<br />
对无尿、容量过负荷（有湿啰音）的患者扩容会加重肺水肿；不降钾也不稳定心肌膜</td>
<td>Saline worsens fluid overload here; no role in hyperkalemia management<br />
生理盐水会加重容量超负荷；对高钾管理无任何作用</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most dangerous distractor is E (magnesium sulfate) — ECG findings like peaked T waves and widened QRS are specific to hyperkalemia, not torsades; recognizing this distinction is critical.*

最危险的干扰项是 E（硫酸镁）——帐篷样 T 波和 QRS 增宽是高钾的特征性改变，而非尖端扭转型室速；识别这一区别至关重要。

---

ESRD/漏透析、ACE 抑制剂、保钾利尿剂</td>
<td>QT-prolonging drugs, hypomagnesemia, hypokalemia<br />
QT 延长药物、低镁血症、低钾血症</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In severe hyperkalemia with ECG changes, give IV calcium first to stabilize the cardiac membrane, then shift K⁺ intracellularly, then remove K⁺ from the body.**

**重度高钾血症伴心电图改变时，首先静脉钙剂稳定心肌膜，再将 K⁺ 转移至细胞内，最后清除体内 K⁺。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "C-SHIFT-OUT" for Hyperkalemia Management / 记忆钩 — 高钾三步法 "稳-移-排":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>C</strong>alcium — stabilizes the cardiac membrane (works in minutes, does NOT lower K⁺) / <strong>稳</strong>定心肌膜——静脉钙剂（数分钟起效，不降血钾）<br />
• <strong>S</strong>hift — insulin+dextrose, bicarb, β₂ agonists push K⁺ into cells (temporary) / <strong>移</strong>入细胞内——胰岛素+葡萄糖、碳酸氢钠、β₂ 激动剂（暂时性）<br />
• <strong>OUT</strong> — dialysis or kayexalate removes K⁺ from the body permanently / <strong>排</strong>出体外——透析或钾离子交换树脂永久性清除 K⁺</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Hyperkalemia: Causes, ECG Staging, and Treatment / 高频知识表 — 高钾血症：病因、心电图分级与治疗

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>ECG progression of hyperkalemia<br />
高钾心电图进展顺序</td>
<td>(1) Peaked T waves → (2) Flat P waves → (3) Prolonged PR → (4) Wide QRS → (5) Sine wave → (6) VF/Asystole<br />
（1）帐篷样 T → （2）P 波低平 → （3）PR 延长 → （4）QRS 增宽 → （5）正弦波 → （6）室颤/心搏骤停</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Calcium mechanism of action<br />
钙剂作用机制</td>
<td>Raises action potential threshold; does not affect serum K⁺; onset 1–3 min; lasts 30–60 min; calcium gluconate preferred peripherally (less tissue damage)<br />
提升动作电位阈值；不影响血清钾；起效 1–3 分钟；持续 30–60 分钟；外周静脉首选葡萄糖酸钙（组织损伤小）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Insulin + dextrose mechanism<br />
胰岛素 + 葡萄糖机制</td>
<td>Insulin activates Na⁺/K⁺-ATPase → drives K⁺ into cells; dextrose given simultaneously to prevent hypoglycemia; lowers K⁺ by ~0.5–1.0 mEq/L<br />
胰岛素激活 Na⁺/K⁺-ATP 酶→ 将 K⁺ 泵入细胞内；同时给葡萄糖防低血糖；可降低 K⁺ 约 0.5–1.0 mEq/L</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ESRD and potassium physiology<br />
ESRD 与钾代谢</td>
<td>Normally 90% of K⁺ excretion is renal; ESRD patients depend entirely on dialysis and GI excretion; anuric patients have zero renal K⁺ clearance<br />
正常情况下 90% 的 K⁺ 经肾排出；ESRD 患者完全依赖透析和胃肠道排钾；无尿患者肾脏 K⁺ 清除为零</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Medications causing hyperkalemia<br />
引起高钾的药物</td>
<td>ACE inhibitors (enalapril ← this patient!), ARBs, K⁺-sparing diuretics (spironolactone), NSAIDs, trimethoprim, heparin<br />
ACE 抑制剂（依那普利 ← 本题患者正在使用！）、ARB、保钾利尿剂（螺内酯）、NSAIDs、甲氧苄啶、肝素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Why NOT furosemide here<br />
为何此处不选呋塞米</td>
<td>Patient is anuric — loop diuretics require tubular fluid flow to work; no urine output = no effect; also does not address immediate cardiac toxicity<br />
患者无尿——袢利尿剂需要肾小管液流动才能发挥作用；无尿即无效；也不能处理即刻心脏毒性</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Calcium chloride vs. gluconate:** Calcium chloride provides ~3× more elemental calcium per mL than gluconate; chloride preferred in cardiac arrest or severe toxicity; gluconate preferred via peripheral IV (less caustic if extravasated)\
  **氯化钙 vs. 葡萄糖酸钙:** 氯化钙每 mL 提供的元素钙约为葡萄糖酸钙的 3 倍；心搏骤停或重度毒性时首选氯化钙；外周静脉输注首选葡萄糖酸钙（渗漏刺激性较小）

- **Pseudohyperkalemia:** Hemolysis during blood draw releases intracellular K⁺ and falsely elevates the result; always correlate with ECG — true hyperkalemia will show ECG changes, pseudohyperkalemia will not\
  **假性高钾血症:** 采血时溶血使细胞内 K⁺ 释放，导致血钾假性升高；始终与心电图对照——真性高钾有心电图改变，假性高钾则无

- **Dialysis as definitive treatment:** Hemodialysis removes K⁺ at ~25–50 mEq/hr and is the most effective K⁺ elimination method; indicated urgently in ESRD patients unresponsive to medical management\
  **透析作为根治手段:** 血液透析每小时清除约 25–50 mEq K⁺，是最有效的清钾方式；对内科治疗无效的 ESRD 患者需紧急透析

- **Enalapril contributing factor:** This patient takes enalapril (ACE inhibitor), which decreases aldosterone → reduces renal K⁺ excretion; in ESRD already unable to excrete K⁺, this compounds risk — consider dose review after stabilization\
  **依那普利是促因:** 本患者使用依那普利（ACE 抑制剂），降低醛固酮 → 减少肾脏排钾；ESRD 患者已无法经肾排钾，此药进一步叠加风险——稳定后应评估是否减量或停药

# Question 30 — Slipped Capital Femoral Epiphysis / 股骨头骨骺滑脱

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>13-year-old boy</strong> is brought to the physician because of <strong>intermittent pain in his right thigh</strong> during the past 6 weeks. The symptoms are <strong>exacerbated by running</strong>, and his mother reports that he <strong>limps for 30 minutes after running</strong>. He has no history of serious illness and takes no medications. He recalls no recent trauma to either leg. He has practiced with the school football team three times weekly for the past 2 months. He is at the 75th percentile for height and <strong>95th percentile for weight and BMI</strong>. Examination shows a normal gait. There is no tenderness of the right hip or thigh. <strong>Internal rotation of the right hip is difficult, especially when the knee is flexed.</strong> Genital and pubic hair development are <strong>sexual maturity rating (SMR) stage 3.</strong> An x-ray of the hips is shown. Which of the following is the most appropriate treatment?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate treatment?</strong></p>
<p>A) Physical therapy<br />
B) Nonsteroidal anti-inflammatory drug therapy<br />
C) Cast immobilization of the right hip and thigh<br />
D) Surgical stabilization of the femoral head<br />
E) No treatment is indicated</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: D</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>13-year-old boy, SMR stage 3<br />
13岁男孩，SMR 3期</td>
<td>Peak age for SCFE is 10–15 years; pubertal hormones weaken the physis, predisposing to slippage<br />
SCFE 高峰年龄 10–15 岁；青春期激素削弱骨骺板，易发生滑脱</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>95th percentile weight and BMI (obese)<br />
体重和 BMI 第 95 百分位（肥胖）</td>
<td>Obesity is the strongest risk factor — excess body weight increases shear stress across the physeal plate<br />
肥胖是最强危险因素——体重过大显著增加骨骺板的剪切应力</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Intermittent right thigh pain exacerbated by running<br />
跑步加重的间歇性右大腿疼痛</td>
<td>SCFE pain commonly refers to the thigh and knee; patients are often misdiagnosed as having isolated knee pathology<br />
SCFE 疼痛常放射至大腿和膝部，易被误诊为单纯膝关节病变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Internal rotation of right hip difficult, especially with knee flexed<br />
屈膝时右髋内旋受限（经典体征）</td>
<td>Obligate external rotation with hip flexion (Drehmann sign) is pathognomonic for SCFE — the slipped epiphysis forces the leg to rotate outward<br />
屈髋时强迫外旋（Drehmann 征）是 SCFE 的特征性体征——滑脱的骨骺迫使患肢向外旋转</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Limps for 30 minutes after running<br />
跑步后跛行 30 分钟</td>
<td>Activity-related antalgic gait points to a structural mechanical joint problem rather than inflammatory or soft-tissue disease<br />
运动后跛行提示结构性机械性关节问题，而非炎症性或软组织疾病</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>X-ray of hips shown<br />
双髋 X 线片</td>
<td>Klein's line along the superior femoral neck fails to intersect the femoral epiphysis on the affected side — the hallmark radiographic sign of SCFE<br />
沿股骨颈上缘的 Klein 线不经过患侧骨骺——SCFE 的标志性 X 线表现</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

During puberty, **hormonal changes** (↑GH relative to sex steroids) progressively weaken the **physeal plate** (growth plate) at the **proximal femur**, reducing resistance to shear forces across the zone of hypertrophic cartilage:

青春期，**激素变化**（GH 相对升高，性激素相对不足）逐渐削弱**近端股骨骨骺板**，降低肥大软骨区对剪切力的抵抗：

- The femoral head (epiphysis) displaces **posteroinferiorly** while the metaphysis (femoral neck) moves anterosuperiorly — classically described as "ice cream falling off the cone"\
  股骨头骨骺向**后下方**移位，干骺端（股骨颈）相对向前上方移动——经典描述为"冰淇淋从蛋筒滑落"

- This is classified as a **Salter-Harris type 1** fracture — the fracture plane runs entirely through the physis, with no bony fragment\
  归类为 **Salter-Harris I 型**骨折——骨折面完全经过骨骺板，无骨碎片

- **Obesity** amplifies vertical shear stress across the physis; repetitive athletic loading (football practice) accelerates the rate of slippage\
  **肥胖**放大骨骺板垂直剪切应力；重复运动负荷（足球训练）加速滑脱进程

- If untreated, disruption of the **medial circumflex femoral artery** → **avascular necrosis (AVN)** of the femoral head, the most feared complication\
  若不治疗，**旋股内侧动脉**受损→股骨头**缺血性坏死（AVN）**，为最严重并发症

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Flexing the hip in SCFE causes the leg to fall into obligate external rotation because the femoral neck is no longer co-axial with the displaced femoral head — the proximal femur "rotates around" the fixed epiphysis.

**解剖小窍门:** SCFE 屈髋时患肢强迫外旋，因为股骨颈与已移位的股骨头不再同轴——近端股骨围绕固定骨骺"旋转"。

## 3. Correct Answer (D) — Surgical Stabilization of the Femoral Head / 正确答案 (D) — 股骨头手术固定

**Surgical stabilization** is the only definitive treatment for SCFE — conservative measures cannot halt ongoing physeal slippage or prevent avascular necrosis of the femoral head:

**手术固定**是 SCFE 唯一确定性治疗——保守措施无法阻止骨骺板持续滑脱或预防股骨头缺血性坏死：

- A single cannulated screw is placed in situ through the femoral neck into the epiphysis to prevent further displacement; the screw crosses the physis intentionally\
  经股骨颈向骨骺原位置入单枚空心螺钉防止进一步移位；螺钉有意穿过骨骺板

- "In situ" fixation is critical — do NOT attempt closed or open reduction, as manipulation disrupts the precarious blood supply and dramatically increases AVN risk\
  "原位"固定至关重要——切勿尝试闭合或切开复位，手法操作会破坏脆弱血供，大幅增加 AVN 风险

- Contralateral prophylactic pinning is considered in high-risk patients: age \<10 years, severe obesity, or underlying endocrine disorder\
  高危患者（年龄\<10岁、重度肥胖、内分泌疾病）可考虑对侧预防性螺钉固定

**Diagnosis:** Obese pubertal male + right thigh pain + limited internal rotation + Drehmann sign + Klein's line disruption on X-ray → SCFE confirmed

**诊断:** 肥胖青春期男性＋右大腿疼痛＋内旋受限＋Drehmann 征＋X 线 Klein 线不过骨骺→确诊 SCFE

**Treatment:** In situ cannulated screw fixation; restricted weight-bearing until physeal closure is radiographically confirmed

**治疗:** 原位空心螺钉固定；限制负重直至 X 线确认骨骺闭合

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Physical therapy<br />
A — 物理治疗</td>
<td>Cannot mechanically stabilize a slipped epiphysis; delays definitive treatment and increases risk of AVN and chondrolysis<br />
无法机械性稳定滑脱的骨骺；延误治疗增加 AVN 和软骨溶解风险</td>
<td>PT addresses muscle/soft-tissue dysfunction, not physeal fractures requiring fixation<br />
物理治疗针对肌肉/软组织功能障碍，不适用于需固定的骨骺骨折</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — NSAID therapy<br />
B — 非甾体抗炎药</td>
<td>Manages pain only; does not halt physeal slippage or prevent structural complications<br />
仅能镇痛；不能阻止骨骺滑脱或预防结构性并发症</td>
<td>NSAIDs are appropriate for inflammatory arthropathy (JIA, gout), not mechanical slippage<br />
NSAIDs 适用于炎症性关节病（JIA、痛风），不适用于机械性滑脱</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Cast immobilization<br />
C — 石膏固定</td>
<td>External casting does not hold the epiphysis in place and is not an accepted modality for SCFE management<br />
外固定无法固定骨骺，不是 SCFE 的认可治疗方式</td>
<td>Hip spica cast is used for dysplasia or certain pelvic/hip fractures — not SCFE<br />
髋人字石膏用于髋关节发育不良或部分骨盆/髋部骨折，不用于 SCFE</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Surgical stabilization ✓<br />
D — 手术固定 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — in situ screw fixation secures the epiphysis, prevents further slippage, and preserves femoral head blood supply<br />
正确——原位螺钉固定骨骺，防止进一步滑脱，保护股骨头血供</td>
<td>Only intervention that mechanically arrests slippage while maintaining vascular integrity<br />
唯一能在保护血管完整性同时机械性阻止滑脱的干预措施</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — No treatment indicated<br />
E — 无需治疗</td>
<td>SCFE always requires surgical fixation; even stable SCFE will progress without intervention, leading to AVN, early osteoarthritis, and permanent gait impairment<br />
SCFE 必须手术固定；即使稳定型 SCFE 也会进展，导致 AVN、早发骨关节炎和永久性步态障碍</td>
<td>"Stable" means the patient can bear weight — it does not mean safe to observe without fixation<br />
"稳定型"指患者可负重——不代表可以不固定而仅观察</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most seductive distractor is A (physical therapy) — the patient has a normal resting gait and activity-related pain, which superficially resembles a musculoskeletal overuse syndrome. The discriminating clue is obligate external rotation on hip flexion (Drehmann sign), which unmasks the structural physeal disruption.*

最容易误选的干扰项是 A（物理治疗）——患者静态步态正常，运动相关疼痛表面上类似肌肉骨骼过度使用综合征。关键鉴别线索是屈髋时强迫外旋（Drehmann 征），揭示了结构性骨骺破坏。
