## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**An obese pubertal boy with thigh pain and obligate hip external rotation on flexion has SCFE — a Salter-Harris type 1 physeal fracture requiring urgent surgical in situ screw fixation.**

**肥胖青春期男孩出现大腿疼痛且屈髋时强迫外旋，诊断为 SCFE——一种需紧急手术原位螺钉固定的 Salter-Harris I 型骨骺骨折。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — SCFE "SLIP" Mnemonic / 记忆钩 — SCFE "SLIP" 记忆诀:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>S</strong>hear at the physis — the pathologic force that displaces the epiphysis posteroinferiorly / 骨骺板剪切力——将骨骺向后下方移位的病理性力量<br />
• <strong>L</strong>arge (obese) + pubertal male — the classic demographic profile / 肥胖青春期男性——经典人口学特征<br />
• <strong>I</strong>nternal rotation limited — Drehmann sign: obligate external rotation on hip flexion / 内旋受限——Drehmann 征：屈髋时强迫外旋<br />
• <strong>P</strong>in it in situ — surgical screw fixation is the only treatment; never reduce / 原位钉住——手术螺钉固定是唯一治疗；切勿复位</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Slipped Capital Femoral Epiphysis (SCFE) / 高频知识表 — 股骨头骨骺滑脱（SCFE）

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Stable vs. Unstable SCFE<br />
稳定型 vs. 不稳定型 SCFE</td>
<td>Stable: patient can bear weight (even with pain) — AVN risk &lt;10%; Unstable: cannot bear weight at all — AVN risk up to 50%; this case is stable<br />
稳定型：患者可负重（即使疼痛）——AVN 风险 &lt;10%；不稳定型：完全无法负重——AVN 风险高达 50%；本题为稳定型</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Salter-Harris Classification<br />
Salter-Harris 骨折分型</td>
<td>SCFE = type 1 (fracture through physis only); type 2 = physis + metaphyseal fragment; type 3 = physis + epiphyseal fragment; type 4 = through physis + both sides; type 5 = crush injury to physis<br />
SCFE = I 型（仅经骨骺板）；II 型 = 骨骺板＋干骺端碎片；III 型 = 骨骺板＋骨骺碎片；IV 型 = 穿过骨骺板两侧；V 型 = 骨骺板压缩伤</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Klein's Line (radiographic sign)<br />
Klein 线（X 线征象）</td>
<td>A line drawn along the superior femoral neck should intersect at least 20% of the epiphysis; in SCFE it misses or barely contacts the epiphysis — best seen on frog-leg lateral view<br />
沿股骨颈上缘画线应与骨骺至少相交 20%；SCFE 时该线不过骨骺或仅轻微接触——蛙式侧位显示最佳</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pain referral pattern<br />
疼痛放射模式</td>
<td>Hip pathology (including SCFE) characteristically refers pain via the obturator nerve to the medial thigh and knee — always examine the hip in any adolescent presenting with "knee pain"<br />
髋关节疾病（包括SCFE）特征性地经闭孔神经将疼痛放射至大腿内侧和膝部——任何青少年主诉"膝痛"时必须检查髋关节</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Endocrine predisposing conditions<br />
内分泌易感因素</td>
<td>SCFE in a non-obese child or outside peak age range → consider hypothyroidism, growth hormone deficiency, hypogonadism, renal osteodystrophy<br />
非肥胖儿童或超出高峰年龄的 SCFE→考虑甲状腺功能减退、GH 缺乏、性腺功能减退、肾性骨营养不良</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Bilateral involvement<br />
双侧受累</td>
<td>20–40% of cases are bilateral (simultaneous or sequential); contralateral prophylactic pinning indicated for age &lt;10 years, severe obesity, or endocrine disorder<br />
20–40% 病例双侧受累（同时或先后发生）；年龄&lt;10岁、重度肥胖或内分泌疾病者需对侧预防性固定</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Complications if untreated<br />
未治疗并发症</td>
<td>Avascular necrosis of femoral head (most feared), chondrolysis, premature osteoarthritis, leg-length discrepancy, permanent gait impairment<br />
股骨头缺血性坏死（最严重），软骨溶解，早发骨关节炎，肢体不等长，永久性步态障碍</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Why "in situ" fixation (not reduction):** The medial circumflex femoral artery — the primary blood supply to the femoral head — runs along the posterosuperior femoral neck and is easily torn by reduction maneuvers; in situ fixation preserves it\
  **为何"原位"固定（不复位）:** 旋股内侧动脉——股骨头主要血供——沿股骨颈后上方走行，复位操作极易撕裂；原位固定可保护该动脉

- **Drehmann sign (exam pearl):** With the patient supine, passively flex the hip to 90° — if the leg obligately externally rotates and abducts, the sign is positive; sensitivity for SCFE approaches 95%\
  **Drehmann 征（体格检查要点）:** 患者仰卧，被动屈髋至 90°——患肢强迫外旋并外展则为阳性；对 SCFE 的敏感性接近 95%

- **Differential for obese adolescent hip pain:** SCFE (mechanical, physeal fracture), septic arthritis (fever, elevated ESR/CRP, no weight-bearing), stress fracture (endurance athlete, normal rotation), slipped disc (older, back pain radiating to leg)\
  **肥胖青少年髋痛鉴别:** SCFE（机械性，骨骺骨折）、化脓性关节炎（发热，ESR/CRP升高，不能负重）、应力骨折（耐力运动员，旋转正常）、腰椎间盘突出（年龄偏大，腰痛放射腿部）

- **MRI utility:** MRI can detect early or preslip SCFE (physeal widening, bone marrow edema) before radiographic changes appear — valuable when clinical suspicion is high but X-ray is equivocal\
  **MRI 的价值:** MRI 可在 X 线改变出现前发现早期或"前滑脱"期 SCFE（骨骺板增宽、骨髓水肿）——临床高度怀疑但 X 线不明确时具有重要价值

# Question 31 — Preserved Decisional Capacity in Mild-to-Moderate Dementia / 轻中度痴呆患者保留的决策能力

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>An <strong>87-year-old woman</strong> with <strong>type 2 diabetes mellitus</strong> comes to the physician for evaluation of a <strong>nonhealing foot ulcer</strong> that has increasingly worse <strong>tissue necrosis and erythema</strong>. She has a 2-year history of <strong>mild to moderate dementia, Alzheimer type</strong>, with no recent changes in cognitive status. The patient lives alone with the help of various neighbors. Her only family is an out-of-town sister, with whom she last spoke 1 year ago. Physical examination shows a 2-cm ulcer that exposes the head of the first metatarsal. There is 1 cm of necrosis and 2 cm of erythema around the edge of the ulcer. On mental status examination, the patient is <strong>alert and oriented to person and place but thinks that the year is 1999</strong>. She <strong>recalls one of three objects after 5 minutes</strong>. A below-the-knee amputation is recommended. The risks and benefits of the operation are discussed with the patient. She <strong>understands and repeats the discussion correctly</strong>. Attempts to contact her sister are unsuccessful. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Consult with the hospital attorney<br />
B) Delay the amputation until her sister can be contacted<br />
C) Obtain a psychiatric assessment of this patient's mental capacity<br />
D) Schedule a follow-up examination after 1 month of antibiotic therapy<br />
E) Proceed with the amputation</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Mild to moderate dementia, Alzheimer type<br />
轻中度阿尔茨海默型痴呆</td>
<td>Raises concern for impaired capacity — but dementia alone does not equal lack of capacity<br />
引发对决策能力受损的担忧——但仅有痴呆不等于缺乏决策能力</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Alert and oriented to person and place, but thinks year is 1999<br />
清醒，对人和地点定向力保留，但认为年份是 1999 年</td>
<td>Partial cognitive impairment — temporal disorientation alone is insufficient to deny decisional capacity<br />
部分认知损害——仅时间定向力缺失不足以剥夺决策能力</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Recalls one of three objects after 5 minutes<br />
5 分钟后回忆 3 个物品中的 1 个</td>
<td>Short-term memory impairment consistent with dementia — but memory performance ≠ capacity to make decisions<br />
与痴呆一致的短期记忆损害——但记忆力表现≠做决定的能力</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Understands and repeats the discussion correctly<br />
正确理解并复述了讨论内容</td>
<td>Critical clue — demonstrates understanding of risks and benefits, directly satisfying a core capacity criterion<br />
关键线索——证明其理解了风险和获益，直接满足决策能力的核心标准</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No family available; sister cannot be contacted<br />
无家属在场，姐姐无法联系</td>
<td>Surrogate decision maker unavailable — relevant only if patient lacks capacity, which she does not<br />
代理决策者不可用——仅在患者缺乏能力时才相关，而本题患者有决策能力</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Progressive necrosis with exposed first metatarsal head<br />
进行性坏死伴第一跖骨头外露</td>
<td>Time-sensitive surgical emergency — delay risks life-threatening sepsis regardless of capacity question<br />
时间紧迫的外科急症——无论决策能力问题如何，延误都有败血症致死的风险</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Decisional capacity** is a clinical determination — made by any treating physician — based on four specific criteria rather than overall cognitive status or psychiatric diagnosis:

**决策能力**是临床判断——由任何主治医师做出——基于四项具体标准，而非总体认知状态或精神科诊断：

- Patient must express a **consistent choice** when asked about the decision repeatedly\
  患者在反复询问时必须表达**一致的选择**

- Patient must **understand** the relevant information including risks, benefits, and alternatives\
  患者必须**理解**相关信息，包括风险、获益和替代方案

- Patient must **appreciate** the personal significance of the decision for their own circumstances\
  患者必须**认识到**该决策对其自身情况的个人意义

- Patient must demonstrate **reasoning** — the ability to rationally manipulate and weigh information\
  患者必须展现**推理能力**——能够理性地运用和权衡信息

**Clinical pearl:** Capacity is decision-specific and time-specific — a patient with dementia may retain capacity for a simple consent decision while lacking capacity for complex financial planning; capacity may also fluctuate (especially in delirium).

**临床要点:** 决策能力具有决策特异性和时间特异性——痴呆患者可能对简单的同意决策保留能力，而对复杂的财务规划缺乏能力；决策能力也可能波动（尤其在谵妄时）。

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Proceed with the Amputation / 正确答案 (E) — 进行截肢手术

**Preserved decisional capacity** despite cognitive impairment means this patient retains full right to accept or refuse her own medical treatment:

**保留的决策能力**尽管存在认知损害，意味着该患者完全保留接受或拒绝其医疗处置的权利：

- Dementia diagnosis alone does not equal incapacity — many patients with mild-to-moderate dementia retain capacity for specific medical decisions\
  单纯痴呆诊断不等于无决策能力——许多轻中度痴呆患者对具体医疗决策仍保留决策能力

- This patient satisfies all four CARE criteria: she expressed consent (choice), correctly repeated the discussion (understanding), faces a life-threatening lesion she agreed to treat (appreciation), and agreed after hearing risks/benefits (reasoning)\
  该患者满足全部四项 CARE 标准：表达同意（选择），正确复述讨论（理解），同意治疗危及生命的病变（认识），听取风险/获益后同意（推理）

- Capacity assessment is the treating physician's responsibility — no psychiatric consult is required for straightforward cases like this one\
  决策能力评估是主治医师的职责——对于本题这样的明确案例无需精神科会诊

**Diagnosis:** Life-threatening diabetic foot infection with exposed bone requiring below-the-knee amputation; patient possesses decisional capacity to consent.

**诊断:** 危及生命的糖尿病足感染伴骨外露，需要膝下截肢；患者具备同意手术的决策能力。

**Treatment:** Proceed with below-the-knee amputation based on patient's valid informed consent.

**治疗:** 基于患者有效的知情同意，进行膝下截肢手术。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Consult with the hospital attorney<br />
A — 咨询医院律师</td>
<td>Legal consultation is unnecessary when a patient has demonstrated capacity — this conflates legal competency (court-determined) with clinical capacity (physician-determined)<br />
当患者已证明决策能力时无需法律咨询——这混淆了法律行为能力（法院决定）与临床决策能力（医生决定）</td>
<td>Capacity is a clinical determination, not a legal proceeding<br />
决策能力是临床判断，而非法律程序</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Delay the amputation until her sister can be contacted<br />
B — 推迟截肢直到联系上姐姐</td>
<td>Contacting family or a surrogate is appropriate only when the patient lacks capacity; this patient has demonstrated capacity and has already consented<br />
联系家属或代理人仅在患者缺乏能力时才适当；该患者已证明决策能力并已同意手术</td>
<td>Surrogate decision makers are invoked only in the absence of capacity, not as a routine second opinion<br />
代理决策者仅在患者缺乏能力时才介入，而非作为常规第二意见</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Obtain a psychiatric assessment of this patient's mental capacity<br />
C — 进行精神科评估</td>
<td>Any physician can perform a decisional capacity assessment; psychiatric referral is not required — and doing so would only delay urgent care<br />
任何医生均可进行决策能力评估；无需精神科转诊——这样做只会延误紧急治疗</td>
<td>Dementia diagnosis ≠ need for psychiatric capacity evaluation; capacity is assessed by discussion, not by specialty<br />
痴呆诊断≠需要精神科能力评估；决策能力通过谈话评估，而非通过专科</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Schedule follow-up after 1 month of antibiotic therapy<br />
D — 1 个月抗生素治疗后随访</td>
<td>Antibiotics alone cannot address osteomyelitis with exposed bone; delaying amputation risks ascending infection and life-threatening sepsis<br />
单独抗生素治疗无法解决骨外露性骨髓炎；延误截肢有感染上行和败血症致死的风险</td>
<td>Exposed bone in diabetic foot = surgical emergency, not a condition managed with outpatient antibiotics<br />
糖尿病足骨外露=外科急症，而非门诊抗生素可处理的情况</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Proceed with the amputation ✓<br />
E — 进行截肢手术 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Patient demonstrates all four decisional capacity criteria and has provided valid informed consent for the necessary procedure<br />
正确——患者满足全部四项决策能力标准，已对必要手术提供有效知情同意</td>
<td>Understanding + accurate repetition of risks/benefits = strong, sufficient evidence of capacity<br />
理解+准确复述风险/获益=决策能力的充分有力证据</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*Choice C is the most tempting distractor — dementia, temporal disorientation, and poor recall create a convincing illusion that formal psychiatric evaluation is required, but capacity is a clinical assessment any physician performs through direct conversation using the four CARE criteria.*

选项 C 是最具迷惑性的干扰项——痴呆、时间定向力障碍和记忆力差造成"需要正式精神科评估"的强烈错觉，但决策能力是任何医生均可通过直接对话使用四项 CARE 标准进行的临床评估。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A patient with mild-to-moderate dementia who correctly understands and repeats the risks and benefits of a proposed procedure retains decisional capacity and may give valid informed consent without surrogate or legal involvement.**

**能够正确理解并复述拟行手术风险和获益的轻中度痴呆患者保留决策能力，可在无需代理人或法律介入的情况下提供有效知情同意。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — CARE Criteria for Decisional Capacity / 记忆钩 — 决策能力 CARE 四标准:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>C</strong>hoice — patient expresses a consistent preference when asked repeatedly / 选择——患者在反复询问时表达一致的偏好<br />
• <strong>A</strong>ppreciation — patient recognizes how the decision applies to their personal circumstances / 认识——患者认识到该决策如何适用于其自身情况<br />
• <strong>R</strong>easoning — patient can rationally work through and weigh the available options / 推理——患者能够理性地权衡可选方案<br />
• <strong>E</strong>xplanation — patient can explain and demonstrate understanding of risks, benefits, and alternatives / 解释——患者能够解释并证明其理解了风险、获益和替代方案</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Decisional Capacity and Surrogate Decision Making / 高频知识表 — 决策能力与代理决策

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Four CARE criteria for decisional capacity<br />
决策能力四项 CARE 标准</td>
<td>Choice (consistent), Appreciation (personal significance), Reasoning (rational weighing), Explanation/Understanding (risks, benefits, alternatives) — all four must be present<br />
选择（一致性）、认识（个人意义）、推理（理性权衡）、解释/理解（风险、获益、替代方案）——四项均须具备</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Who performs capacity assessment<br />
谁进行决策能力评估</td>
<td>Any attending physician — no psychiatrist required; psychiatric consult appropriate only for borderline or unusually complex cases<br />
任何主治医师——无需精神科医生；仅在边界或异常复杂案例时精神科会诊才适当</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Dementia and decisional capacity<br />
痴呆与决策能力</td>
<td>Mild-to-moderate dementia does not automatically preclude capacity; each patient must be assessed individually for each specific decision being made<br />
轻中度痴呆不自动排除决策能力；每位患者必须针对每项具体决策进行个别评估</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Surrogate decision maker — when invoked<br />
代理决策者——何时介入</td>
<td>Only when patient demonstrably lacks capacity; hierarchy: (1) durable power of attorney for healthcare, (2) legal guardian, (3) next of kin per state law<br />
仅在患者明确缺乏能力时；层级：(1) 医疗持久授权书代理人，(2) 法定监护人，(3) 按州法律确定的近亲属</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Surrogate decision-making standard<br />
代理决策标准</td>
<td>Substituted judgment (what would patient have wanted) preferred over best interest standard (what is objectively best)<br />
替代判断标准（患者会希望什么）优于最佳利益标准（客观上什么最好）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Emergency exception to informed consent<br />
知情同意的紧急例外</td>
<td>If patient lacks capacity AND no surrogate available AND delay would cause serious harm → physician may proceed under implied consent doctrine<br />
若患者缺乏能力且无代理人且延误将造成严重伤害→医生可依默示同意原则进行处置</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Delirium vs. Dementia in capacity assessment:** Delirium causes acute, fluctuating incapacity — always attempt to restore capacity (treat underlying cause) before making irreversible decisions; dementia causes stable chronic impairment that may still permit capacity\
  **谵妄 vs. 痴呆在能力评估中:** 谵妄导致急性波动性能力丧失——在做出不可逆决策前务必尝试恢复能力（治疗基础病因）；痴呆导致稳定的慢性损害，仍可能保留决策能力

- **Capacity threshold scales with decision risk:** A low-stakes decision (blood draw, routine medication) requires only minimal demonstration of capacity; a high-stakes irreversible decision (amputation, stopping dialysis) requires robust demonstration of all four CARE criteria\
  **能力门槛随决策风险变化:** 低风险决策（抽血、常规用药）只需最低限度的能力展示；高风险不可逆决策（截肢、停止透析）需要充分展示全部四项 CARE 标准

- **Competency vs. capacity on USMLE:** These terms are often used interchangeably in test questions — competency is the legal term determined by courts; capacity is the clinical term determined by physicians assessing the four criteria\
  **USMLE 中行为能力 vs. 决策能力:** 这两个术语在试题中常互换使用——行为能力是由法院决定的法律术语；决策能力是由医生通过评估四项标准确定的临床术语

- **HIPAA and family notification:** Even when a patient has capacity, sharing medical information with family without the patient's explicit consent violates HIPAA — capacity status does not alter patient privacy rights\
  **HIPAA 与家属通知:** 即使患者有决策能力，未经患者明确同意向家属透露医疗信息也违反 HIPAA——决策能力状态不改变患者的隐私权

# Question 32 — Aortic Stenosis / 主动脉瓣狭窄

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>47-year-old woman</strong> comes to the physician because of a <strong>2-month history of substernal chest tightness</strong> and <strong>shortness of breath associated with exercise and relieved by rest</strong>. She previously walked 2 miles daily, but now she is limited to walking one-half block because of chest pain, dyspnea, and <strong>light-headedness</strong>. She has never smoked and drinks one to two beers daily. Her temperature is 36.8°C (98.2°F), pulse is 98/min, respirations are 20/min, and blood pressure is 110/82 mm Hg. <strong>Jugular venous pressure is 8 cm H2O</strong>. <strong>Crackles are heard at both lung bases</strong>. The point of maximal impulse is increased but not displaced; S1 is normal, but <strong>S2 is decreased</strong>. There is a <strong>grade 3/6, harsh systolic murmur at the cardiac base</strong>. Serum studies show a total cholesterol concentration of 210 mg/dL, HDL-cholesterol concentration of 95 mg/dL, and LDL-cholesterol concentration of 100 mg/dL.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most likely cause of this patient's heart failure?</strong></p>
<p>A) Alcohol use disorder<br />
B) Amyloidosis<br />
C) Anemia<br />
D) Aortic stenosis<br />
E) Atrial fibrillation<br />
F) Cor pulmonale<br />
G) Hemochromatosis<br />
H) Ischemic heart disease<br />
I) Mitral regurgitation</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: D</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Harsh systolic murmur at cardiac base<br />
心底部粗糙收缩期杂音</td>
<td>Classic auscultatory signature of aortic stenosis — turbulent flow through a narrowed, calcified valve<br />
主动脉瓣狭窄的经典听诊标志——血流通过狭窄钙化瓣口产生湍流</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Decreased S2<br />
第二心音减弱</td>
<td>Reflects reduced aortic valve leaflet mobility; calcified valve closes weakly, diminishing A2<br />
反映主动脉瓣瓣叶活动度下降；钙化瓣膜关闭力弱，A2减弱</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Exertional chest pain + dyspnea + light-headedness (near-syncope)<br />
劳力性胸痛+呼吸困难+头晕（晕厥前兆）</td>
<td>Classic SAD triad of severe aortic stenosis: Syncope, Angina, Dyspnea<br />
重度主动脉瓣狭窄的经典SAD三联征：晕厥、心绞痛、呼吸困难</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>PMI increased but NOT displaced<br />
心尖搏动增强但未移位</td>
<td>Indicates concentric LV hypertrophy (pressure overload pattern), not dilated cardiomyopathy<br />
提示同心性左室肥厚（压力超负荷模式），而非扩张型心肌病</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>JVP 8 cm H2O + bilateral lung crackles<br />
颈静脉压升高 + 双肺底湿啰音</td>
<td>Signs of established heart failure — backward failure causing pulmonary congestion and systemic venous hypertension<br />
已确立心力衰竭的体征——向后衰竭导致肺淤血和体静脉高压</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>HDL 95 mg/dL, LDL 100 mg/dL<br />
HDL 95，LDL 100</td>
<td>Highly favorable lipid profile makes ischemic heart disease an extremely unlikely primary etiology<br />
极佳血脂状况使冠心病作为主要病因的可能性极低</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Age 47, early-onset presentation<br />
47岁，早发病例</td>
<td>Raises suspicion for congenital bicuspid aortic valve or prior rheumatic heart disease rather than senile calcification<br />
提示先天性二叶式主动脉瓣或既往风湿性心脏病，而非老年性钙化</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Aortic stenosis** imposes **pressure overload** on the left ventricle by obstructing flow through a narrowed, calcified, or fibrotic aortic valve:

**主动脉瓣狭窄**通过狭窄、钙化或纤维化的主动脉瓣阻塞血流，对左心室造成**压力超负荷**：

- Valve obstruction → increased afterload → LV must generate higher systolic pressure to maintain forward cardiac output\
  瓣膜梗阻 → 后负荷增加 → 左室须产生更高收缩压以维持正向心输出量

- Compensatory **concentric LV hypertrophy** (wall thickens, cavity does not dilate) → PMI increased but NOT displaced\
  代偿性**同心性左室肥厚**（室壁增厚，心腔不扩大）→ 心尖搏动增强但不移位

- Fixed obstruction limits cardiac output augmentation → exertional symptoms emerge as demand exceeds fixed supply (angina, syncope, dyspnea)\
  固定性梗阻限制心输出量增加 → 需求超过固定供给时出现劳力性症状（心绞痛、晕厥、呼吸困难）

- Sustained pressure overload → LV failure → pulmonary venous congestion (crackles) and elevated JVP\
  持续压力超负荷 → 左心衰 → 肺静脉淤血（湿啰音）和颈静脉压升高

- Calcified, immobile valve leaflets → **diminished A2** (aortic component of S2 becomes soft or absent)\
  钙化、活动受限的瓣叶 → **A2减弱**（第二心音主动脉瓣成分变软或消失）

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The aortic valve is best auscultated at the right 2nd intercostal space (upper sternal border); its murmur classically radiates to the carotid arteries bilaterally.

**解剖小窍门:** 主动脉瓣最佳听诊位置在右侧第2肋间（胸骨上缘）；其杂音经典地向双侧颈动脉传导。

## 3. Correct Answer (D) — Aortic Stenosis / 正确答案 (D) — 主动脉瓣狭窄

**Aortic stenosis** is valvular obstruction of the left ventricular outflow tract caused by calcification, fibrosis, or congenital malformation of the aortic valve:

**主动脉瓣狭窄**是由主动脉瓣钙化、纤维化或先天畸形引起的左室流出道梗阻：

- Crescendo-decrescendo (diamond-shaped) harsh systolic murmur, best heard at the upper right sternal border (cardiac base), radiates to carotids\
  渐强-渐弱（菱形）粗糙收缩期杂音，右侧胸骨上缘（心底）最响，向颈动脉传导

- Pulsus parvus et tardus: weak and delayed carotid upstroke — hallmark of severe AS due to reduced stroke volume\
  Pulsus parvus et tardus：颈动脉搏动弱且迟缓——重度AS的标志，因每搏输出量降低所致

- Decreased or absent S2 (A2) due to restricted mobility of calcified or fused valve leaflets\
  第二心音（A2）减弱或消失，因钙化或融合瓣叶活动受限

- Prognosis correlates with symptom onset: angina (5-year survival) → syncope (3-year) → dyspnea/HF (1–2-year)\
  预后与症状出现相关：心绞痛（5年生存期）→ 晕厥（3年）→ 呼吸困难/心衰（1-2年）

**Diagnosis:** Echocardiography is the gold standard — confirms valve area (\<1.0 cm² = severe), mean gradient (\>40 mmHg = severe), and LV systolic function

**诊断:** 超声心动图为金标准——确认瓣口面积（\<1.0 cm²=重度）、平均跨瓣压差（\>40 mmHg=重度）及左室收缩功能

**Treatment:** Aortic valve replacement is definitive — surgical SAVR for younger/lower-risk patients; transcatheter TAVR for elderly or high surgical risk; vasodilators are contraindicated

**治疗:** 主动脉瓣置换术为根治方法——年轻/低风险患者行外科SAVR；老年或高手术风险患者行经导管TAVR；血管扩张剂为禁忌

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Alcohol use disorder<br />
A — 酒精使用障碍</td>
<td>Alcoholic cardiomyopathy requires heavy chronic use (typically &gt;10 drinks/day for years); 1–2 beers/day is insufficient; produces dilated cardiomyopathy, not a valvular murmur<br />
酒精性心肌病需长期大量饮酒（通常每天&gt;10杯，持续多年）；1-2杯/天不足以致病；引起扩张型心肌病，而非瓣膜性杂音</td>
<td>Dilated CMP: displaced PMI + soft or no murmur; this patient has non-displaced PMI + harsh basal murmur<br />
扩张型心肌病：PMI移位+杂音轻或无；本例PMI不移位+心底粗糙杂音</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Amyloidosis<br />
B — 淀粉样变性</td>
<td>Causes restrictive cardiomyopathy with stiff walls; uncommon without associated plasma cell dyscrasia or chronic inflammatory disease; no murmur<br />
引起心壁僵硬的限制型心肌病；无相关浆细胞病或慢性炎症则罕见；无杂音</td>
<td>Restrictive pattern: low ECG voltage, thick walls without murmur; no systemic features here<br />
限制型模式：心电图低电压，心壁增厚但无杂音；本例无全身性表现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Anemia<br />
C — 贫血</td>
<td>Severe anemia produces a soft flow murmur at the apex, not a harsh basal murmur; would also cause significant tachycardia (&gt;100/min); no pallor or bleeding history<br />
重度贫血产生心尖部轻柔血流性杂音，而非心底粗糙杂音；同时伴明显心动过速（&gt;100/min）；无苍白或出血史</td>
<td>Anemia murmur: soft, apical, no S2 change; this patient has harsh basal murmur + decreased S2<br />
贫血杂音：轻柔、心尖部、S2不变；本例为心底粗糙杂音+S2减弱</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Aortic stenosis ✓<br />
D — 主动脉瓣狭窄 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Harsh crescendo-decrescendo systolic murmur at the cardiac base + decreased S2 + exertional SAD triad + concentric LVH (increased non-displaced PMI) + heart failure signs = classic aortic stenosis<br />
正确——心底粗糙渐强-渐弱收缩期杂音+S2减弱+劳力性SAD三联征+同心性左室肥厚（PMI增强不移位）+心衰体征=经典主动脉瓣狭窄</td>
<td>All findings converge on fixed LV outflow obstruction; no other single diagnosis accounts for this complete picture<br />
所有体征均指向固定性左室流出道梗阻；无任何其他单一诊断能解释此完整表现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Atrial fibrillation<br />
E — 心房颤动</td>
<td>Produces an irregularly irregular pulse and palpitations; no characteristic murmur; can cause heart failure but cannot produce a harsh systolic murmur with decreased S2<br />
产生心律绝对不齐和心悸；无特征性杂音；可引起心衰但不产生伴S2减弱的粗糙收缩期杂音</td>
<td>Pulse here is regular at 98/min; no irregular rhythm documented<br />
本例脉搏规整98/min；无不规则心律记录</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>F — Cor pulmonale<br />
F — 肺源性心脏病</td>
<td>Right heart failure secondary to chronic lung pathology; patient has no pulmonary disease history; presents with RV heave and signs of RHF, not a basal systolic murmur<br />
继发于慢性肺病的右心衰；患者无肺部疾病史；表现为右室抬举和右心衰体征，而非心底收缩期杂音</td>
<td>Dominant findings here are LV-sided; no COPD, pulmonary HTN, or hypoxic lung disease<br />
本例主要为左室体征；无慢阻肺、肺动脉高压或低氧性肺病</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>G — Hemochromatosis<br />
G — 血色病</td>
<td>Iron overload causes restrictive or dilated cardiomyopathy; classically presents in men &gt;40 with liver cirrhosis, diabetes, bronze skin, and gonadal failure; no murmur<br />
铁过载引起限制型或扩张型心肌病；经典表现为40岁以上男性伴肝硬化、糖尿病、皮肤铜色和性腺功能衰竭；无杂音</td>
<td>No systemic iron overload features; patient is a woman without hepatic, endocrine, or dermatologic findings<br />
无全身铁过载表现；患者为女性，无肝脏、内分泌或皮肤异常</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>H — Ischemic heart disease<br />
H — 缺血性心脏病</td>
<td>Exertional chest pain raises concern for CAD, but the highly favorable lipid profile (HDL 95, LDL 100), absence of smoking history, and lack of other CAD risk factors make this very unlikely<br />
劳力性胸痛引起冠心病考虑，但极佳血脂（HDL 95，LDL 100）、无吸烟史及缺乏其他冠心病危险因素使之可能性极低</td>
<td>CAD does not explain harsh basal murmur + decreased S2; ischemia alone cannot produce these findings<br />
冠心病无法解释心底粗糙杂音+S2减弱；单独缺血不能产生这些体征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>I — Mitral regurgitation<br />
I — 二尖瓣反流</td>
<td>Produces a holosystolic murmur loudest at the apex, radiating to the left axilla; associated with MVP, endocarditis, and prior MI; does not decrease S2<br />
产生全收缩期杂音，心尖部最响，向左腋下传导；与MVP、心内膜炎和既往心梗相关；不引起S2减弱</td>
<td>MR murmur is holosystolic at apex, not crescendo-decrescendo at the cardiac base<br />
MR杂音为心尖部全收缩期，而非心底部渐强-渐弱型</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is H (Ischemic heart disease) given classic exertional chest pain, but the favorable lipid profile and — most critically — the harsh basal murmur with decreased S2 are not explained by ischemia and unmistakably point to aortic stenosis.*

最容易误选H（缺血性心脏病），因为有经典劳力性胸痛，但极佳血脂——最关键的是——心底粗糙杂音伴S2减弱无法用缺血解释，这些体征毫无疑问地指向主动脉瓣狭窄。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Aortic Stenosis vs. Mitral Regurgitation vs. Hypertrophic Cardiomyopathy / 主动脉瓣狭窄 vs. 二尖瓣反流 vs. 肥厚型心肌病

<table>
<colgroup>

Valsalva动作</td>

杂音减弱</td>

增强，不移位（同心性肥厚）</td>

向左移位（离心性肥厚/扩张）</td>
<td>Increased, not displaced<br />
增强，不移位</td>

典型病因</td>

老年钙化、二叶式主动脉瓣、风湿性心脏病</td>

MVP、心内膜炎、风湿、心梗</td>
<td>Autosomal dominant sarcomere mutation<br />
常染色体显性遗传肌节蛋白突变</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A harsh crescendo-decrescendo systolic murmur at the cardiac base with decreased S2, concentric LV hypertrophy, and the exertional triad of angina, syncope, and dyspnea is the hallmark presentation of aortic stenosis progressing to heart failure.**

**心底部粗糙渐强-渐弱收缩期杂音伴第二心音减弱、同心性左室肥厚，以及劳力性心绞痛、晕厥、呼吸困难三联征，是主动脉瓣狭窄进展为心力衰竭的标志性表现。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — AS Symptom Triad "SAD" (in order of worsening prognosis) / 记忆钩 — 主动脉瓣狭窄症状三联征 "SAD"（按预后恶化顺序）:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>S</strong>yncope — exertional loss of consciousness; average survival ~3 years without valve replacement / 晕厥——劳力性意识丧失；未行瓣膜置换平均存活约3年<br />
• <strong>A</strong>ngina — ischemia despite normal coronaries (supply-demand mismatch from fixed outflow obstruction); ~5-year survival / 心绞痛——冠脉正常仍发生缺血（固定性流出道梗阻导致供需失衡）；约5年生存期<br />
• <strong>D</strong>yspnea/Heart failure — LV decompensation and pulmonary congestion; worst prognosis, ~1–2 years / 呼吸困难/心力衰竭——左室失代偿和肺淤血；预后最差，约1-2年生存期</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Aortic Stenosis / 高频知识表 — 主动脉瓣狭窄

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Etiology by age<br />
不同年龄病因</td>
<td>&lt;65 years: congenital bicuspid aortic valve (most common congenital cardiac defect, 1–2% of population); 65–75 years: rheumatic heart disease; &gt;75 years: senile calcific degeneration<br />
&lt;65岁：先天性二叶式主动脉瓣（最常见先天性心脏畸形，占人群1-2%）；65-75岁：风湿性心脏病；&gt;75岁：老年退行性钙化</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Murmur characteristics<br />
杂音特征</td>
<td>Crescendo-decrescendo (diamond-shaped) harsh systolic murmur, loudest at right 2nd ICS; radiates to bilateral carotids; may radiate to apex (Gallavardin phenomenon — high-frequency components)<br />
渐强-渐弱（菱形）粗糙收缩期杂音，右侧第2肋间最响；向双侧颈动脉传导；可向心尖传导（Gallavardin现象——高频成分）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Peripheral pulse finding<br />
外周脉搏特征</td>
<td>Pulsus parvus et tardus: weak (parvus = small) and delayed (tardus = slow) carotid upstroke; hallmark of severe AS; palpated at carotid<br />
Pulsus parvus et tardus：颈动脉搏动弱（parvus=小）且迟缓（tardus=慢）；重度AS的标志；于颈动脉处扪及</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Echo criteria for severity<br />
超声心动图严重程度标准</td>
<td>Severe AS: valve area &lt;1.0 cm² (normal 3–4 cm²), mean gradient &gt;40 mmHg, peak velocity &gt;4 m/s; moderate: 1.0–1.5 cm²; mild: &gt;1.5 cm²<br />
重度AS：瓣口面积&lt;1.0 cm²（正常3-4 cm²），平均压差&gt;40 mmHg，峰值流速&gt;4 m/s；中度：1.0-1.5 cm²；轻度：&gt;1.5 cm²</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment<br />
治疗</td>
<td>Definitive: aortic valve replacement — SAVR for younger/lower-risk; TAVR for elderly/high surgical risk; vasodilators (nitrates, ACE inhibitors) are CONTRAINDICATED — reduce preload, cause critical hypotension<br />
根治：主动脉瓣置换——年轻/低风险行SAVR；老年/高手术风险行TAVR；血管扩张剂（硝酸盐、ACEI）为禁忌——降低前负荷，引起严重低血压</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Bicuspid aortic valve<br />
二叶式主动脉瓣</td>
<td>Most common congenital cardiac malformation (1–2%); causes early-onset AS (40s–60s); associated with aortic root dilation → risk of aortic dissection independent of stenosis severity<br />
最常见先天性心脏畸形（1-2%）；引起早发性AS（40-60岁）；伴主动脉根部扩张→主动脉夹层风险与狭窄程度无关</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Heyde syndrome<br />
Heyde综合征</td>
<td>Triad of AS + acquired von Willebrand disease (turbulent flow degrades high-molecular-weight vWF multimers) + GI angiodysplasia → GI bleeding; resolves after valve replacement<br />
AS+获得性血管性血友病（湍流降解高分子量vWF多聚体）+消化道血管发育不良三联征→消化道出血；瓣膜置换后缓解</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of harsh systolic murmur at the cardiac base:** Aortic stenosis (crescendo-decrescendo, decreased S2, carotid radiation), aortic sclerosis (similar murmur character but no gradient or symptoms, S2 preserved), pulmonary stenosis (best at left 2nd ICS, wide split S2, no carotid radiation)\
  **心底部粗糙收缩期杂音鉴别:** 主动脉瓣狭窄（渐强-渐弱，S2减弱，向颈动脉传导），主动脉瓣硬化（杂音性质相似但无压差或症状，S2保留），肺动脉瓣狭窄（左侧第2肋间最响，S2宽分裂，无颈动脉传导）

- **Contraindicated medications in AS:** Vasodilators (nitroglycerin, ACE inhibitors, ARBs) and aggressive diuresis are dangerous — fixed outflow obstruction means the heart cannot compensate for a drop in preload or afterload, causing severe hypotension\
  **AS禁忌药物:** 血管扩张剂（硝酸甘油、ACEI、ARB）和过度利尿危险——固定性流出道梗阻意味着心脏无法代偿前负荷或后负荷下降，导致严重低血压

- **Variant — low-flow, low-gradient AS:** Some patients with severe AS and reduced EF have paradoxically low gradients despite severe stenosis; dobutamine stress echo used to confirm true severity vs. pseudo-severe AS\
  **题目变式——低流量低压差AS:** 部分重度AS合并射血分数降低的患者可出现压差矛盾性低值；行多巴酚丁胺负荷超声以确认真性重度AS vs. 假性重度AS

- **Key complication — sudden cardiac death:** Can occur in severe symptomatic AS, particularly with exertion; strenuous exercise and competitive sports are contraindicated until valve replacement is performed\
  **关键并发症——猝死:** 可发生于重度症状性AS，尤其在运动时；在行瓣膜置换术前禁止剧烈运动和竞技体育

# Question 33 — Disseminated Intravascular Coagulation / 弥散性血管内凝血

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>30-year-old man</strong> who is in the US Army is brought to the emergency department of a military hospital 40 minutes after being <strong>hit by a motor vehicle</strong> traveling 25 mph while he was walking. On arrival, he is <strong>unconscious</strong>. Temperature is 36.0°C (96.8°F), pulse is 113/min, respirations are 22/min, and <strong>blood pressure is 80/55 mm Hg</strong>. Pulse oximetry on room air shows an oxygen saturation of 90%. On examination, the <strong>abdomen is rigid</strong>. He is resuscitated with <strong>8 units of packed red blood cells, 6 units of fresh frozen plasma, and 2 units of platelets</strong>. Emergency laparotomy shows transection of the small bowel 5 cm proximal to the cecum. Laboratory studies done 45 minutes after arriving in the surgical intensive care unit show an <strong>activated partial thromboplastin time of 42 seconds</strong> and a <strong>prothrombin time of 25 seconds (INR=3.2)</strong>. Which of the following is the most likely cause of the coagulation abnormalities in this patient?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most likely cause of the coagulation abnormalities?</strong></p>
<p>A) Cirrhosis<br />
B) Disseminated intravascular coagulation<br />
C) Factor VII deficiency<br />
D) Hyperfibrinogenemia<br />
E) Thrombocytopenia</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: B</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Major trauma (hit by motor vehicle)<br />
重大创伤（被机动车撞击）</td>
<td>Massive tissue injury releases tissue factor systemically → triggers extrinsic coagulation cascade throughout the vasculature<br />
大量组织损伤全身性释放组织因子 → 激活全身血管系统外源性凝血级联</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>BP 80/55 mmHg (hemorrhagic shock)<br />
血压 80/55 mmHg（失血性休克）</td>
<td>Hypoperfusion + acidosis impair clotting factor enzyme function; hemorrhagic shock is a classic DIC precipitant<br />
低灌注+酸中毒损害凝血因子酶功能；失血性休克是DIC的经典诱因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Abdomen rigid → emergency laparotomy<br />
腹部板状强直 → 急诊剖腹探查</td>
<td>Bowel transection releases additional intracellular tissue factor; intraabdominal hemorrhage worsens coagulation cascade activation<br />
小肠横断释放额外细胞内组织因子；腹腔积血加重凝血级联激活</td>
</tr>
<tr>

大量输血（8单位红细胞+6单位FFP+2单位血小板）</td>
<td>Reflects severity of hemorrhage; dilutional coagulopathy from crystalloid/packed RBCs; clinician already suspected coagulopathy (hence FFP + platelets)<br />
反映出血严重程度；晶体/红细胞稀释性凝血病；临床医师已预判凝血病（故给予FFP+血小板）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>aPTT 42 seconds (elevated; normal &lt;35s)<br />
aPTT 42秒（升高；正常 &lt;35秒）</td>
<td>Intrinsic + common pathway factor depletion (XII, XI, IX, VIII, X, V, II, I)<br />
内源性+共同途径凝血因子耗竭（XII、XI、IX、VIII、X、V、II、I因子）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>PT 25s / INR 3.2 (elevated)<br />
PT 25秒 / INR 3.2（升高）</td>
<td>Extrinsic + common pathway factor depletion (VII, X, V, II, I); both PT and aPTT elevated together = DIC or severe liver disease<br />
外源性+共同途径凝血因子耗竭（VII、X、V、II、I因子）；PT和aPTT均升高 = DIC或重度肝病</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No prior liver disease, acute onset post-trauma<br />
无既往肝病史，创伤后急性起病</td>
<td>Excludes chronic hepatic etiology (cirrhosis); temporal correlation with trauma strongly favors DIC over structural cause<br />
排除慢性肝脏病因（肝硬化）；与创伤的时间相关性强烈支持DIC而非结构性病因</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Massive trauma** triggers **disseminated intravascular coagulation (DIC)** through systemic release of **tissue factor (TF)** from injured endothelium and parenchymal cells, causing simultaneous **widespread microthrombus formation** and **consumption coagulopathy**:

**大量创伤**通过受损内皮细胞和实质细胞系统性释放**组织因子（TF）**触发**弥散性血管内凝血（DIC）**，导致**广泛微血栓形成**和**消耗性凝血病**同时发生：

- Tissue injury → massive TF release → TF + Factor VIIa complex → activates extrinsic coagulation cascade throughout microcirculation\
  组织损伤 → 大量TF释放 → TF+VIIa因子复合物 → 激活微循环全程外源性凝血级联

- Widespread thrombin generation → fibrin microthrombi form in capillaries and arterioles → downstream organ ischemia\
  弥漫性凝血酶生成 → 毛细血管和小动脉形成纤维蛋白微血栓 → 下游器官缺血

- Consumption of clotting factors (I, II, V, VII, VIII, X) and platelets → elevated PT + aPTT + INR + thrombocytopenia\
  凝血因子（I、II、V、VII、VIII、X）和血小板被消耗 → PT+aPTT+INR升高+血小板减少

- Compensatory fibrinolysis activated → plasmin degrades fibrin → elevated D-dimer + decreased fibrinogen\
  代偿性纤溶激活 → 纤溶酶降解纤维蛋白 → D-dimer升高+纤维蛋白原降低

- Fibrin strands in microcirculation mechanically shear erythrocytes → microangiopathic hemolytic anemia (MAHA) + schistocytes on smear\
  微循环纤维蛋白链机械切割红细胞 → 微血管病性溶血性贫血（MAHA）+血涂片裂体细胞

**Pathophysiologic rule of thumb:** DIC is the only condition with BOTH bleeding AND thrombosis simultaneously — patients clot in the microcirculation while bleeding macroscopically at surgical sites.

**病理生理小窍门:** DIC是唯一同时发生出血和血栓的疾病——患者微循环内凝血，同时宏观手术部位大量出血。

## 3. Correct Answer (B) — Disseminated Intravascular Coagulation / 正确答案 (B) — 弥散性血管内凝血

**Disseminated intravascular coagulation (DIC)** is a systemic consumptive coagulopathy in which uncontrolled thrombin generation depletes coagulation factors and platelets, producing paradoxical simultaneous thrombosis and hemorrhage:

**弥散性血管内凝血（DIC）** 是一种系统性消耗性凝血病，失控的凝血酶生成耗竭凝血因子和血小板，产生血栓与出血并存的矛盾状态：

- Both PT and aPTT elevated: extrinsic pathway factors (VII) and intrinsic pathway factors (VIII, IX, XI) plus common pathway (X, V, II, fibrinogen) are all consumed\
  PT和aPTT均升高：外源性途径（VII因子）、内源性途径（VIII、IX、XI因子）和共同途径（X、V、II因子、纤维蛋白原）均被消耗

- Thrombocytopenia: platelets are consumed forming widespread fibrin-platelet microthrombi throughout the microcirculation\
  血小板减少：血小板在微循环中形成广泛纤维蛋白-血小板微血栓时被消耗

- Decreased fibrinogen: consumed in clot formation; this is the OPPOSITE of hyperfibrinogenemia and distinguishes DIC from option D\
  纤维蛋白原降低：在凝血过程中被消耗；这与高纤维蛋白原血症相反，可与D选项鉴别

- Elevated D-dimer: secondary fibrinolysis breaks down fibrin microthrombi, releasing fibrin split products\
  D-dimer升高：继发性纤溶降解纤维蛋白微血栓，释放纤维蛋白裂解产物

**Diagnosis:** Acute major trauma + hemorrhagic shock + elevated PT/aPTT/INR = DIC until proven otherwise; confirm with low fibrinogen, elevated D-dimer, thrombocytopenia, and schistocytes

**诊断:** 急性重大创伤+失血性休克+PT/aPTT/INR升高 = 排除其他前提下考虑DIC；通过低纤维蛋白原、D-dimer升高、血小板减少及裂体细胞进一步确认

**Treatment:** (1) Treat underlying cause — hemorrhage control, source control; (2) Replace consumed products — FFP for all clotting factors, cryoprecipitate for fibrinogen, platelets; (3) Correct the lethal triad — hypothermia, acidosis, coagulopathy

**治疗:** （1）治疗根本原因——控制出血、清除病灶；（2）补充被消耗产品——FFP补充所有凝血因子，冷沉淀补充纤维蛋白原，输注血小板；（3）纠正死亡三联征——低体温、酸中毒、凝血病

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Cirrhosis<br />
A — 肝硬化</td>
<td>Wrong — cirrhosis requires years of chronic liver injury; this patient has acute onset with no prior hepatic history, no ascites, no jaundice, no portal hypertension signs<br />
错误——肝硬化需要多年慢性肝损伤；此患者急性起病，无既往肝病史，无腹水、黄疸或门脉高压体征</td>
<td>Cirrhosis: chronic history + stigmata of liver failure; DIC: acute trauma temporal correlation<br />
肝硬化：慢性病史+肝衰竭体征；DIC：与急性创伤时间相关</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Disseminated intravascular coagulation ✓<br />
B — 弥散性血管内凝血 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — massive trauma releases tissue factor, triggering systemic coagulation cascade with consumption of all clotting factors and platelets, explaining both elevated PT and aPTT<br />
正确——大量创伤释放组织因子，触发全身凝血级联，消耗所有凝血因子和血小板，解释PT和aPTT均升高</td>
<td>Both PT and aPTT elevated in acute trauma setting = DIC until proven otherwise<br />
急性创伤背景下PT和aPTT均升高 = 排除其他前提下首先考虑DIC</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Factor VII deficiency<br />
C — VII因子缺乏症</td>
<td>Wrong — congenital, rare bleeding disorder; Factor VII is extrinsic pathway only, so isolated deficiency prolongs PT only; aPTT would be normal (intrinsic pathway intact)<br />
错误——先天性、罕见出血疾病；VII因子仅参与外源性途径，单独缺乏只延长PT；aPTT应正常（内源性途径完整）</td>
<td>Factor VII deficiency: isolated PT prolongation, normal aPTT; DIC: both PT and aPTT elevated<br />
VII因子缺乏：仅PT延长，aPTT正常；DIC：PT和aPTT均延长</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Hyperfibrinogenemia<br />
D — 高纤维蛋白原血症</td>
<td>Wrong — hyperfibrinogenemia promotes thrombosis (not bleeding) via enhanced fibrin formation; fibrinogen levels are ELEVATED; DIC causes DECREASED fibrinogen from consumption — directly opposite<br />
错误——高纤维蛋白原血症通过增强纤维蛋白形成促进血栓（非出血）；纤维蛋白原水平升高；DIC导致纤维蛋白原因消耗而降低——完全相反</td>
<td>Hyperfibrinogenemia: elevated fibrinogen, prothrombotic; DIC: decreased fibrinogen, bleeding<br />
高纤维蛋白原血症：纤维蛋白原升高，促血栓；DIC：纤维蛋白原降低，出血</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Thrombocytopenia<br />
E — 血小板减少症</td>
<td>Wrong — isolated thrombocytopenia does NOT prolong PT or aPTT (coagulation cascade is platelet-independent); PT and aPTT would be normal; bleeding is purely mucocutaneous (petechiae, purpura)<br />
错误——单纯血小板减少症不延长PT或aPTT（凝血级联与血小板无关）；PT和aPTT应正常；出血仅为皮肤黏膜出血（瘀点、紫癜）</td>
<td>Thrombocytopenia: normal PT/aPTT; DIC: both PT and aPTT elevated with thrombocytopenia<br />
血小板减少症：PT/aPTT正常；DIC：PT和aPTT均延长同时伴血小板减少</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most dangerous distractor is Choice E — DIC does cause thrombocytopenia, making it tempting, but isolated thrombocytopenia cannot explain the elevated PT and aPTT; only DIC (or liver failure) produces the combined picture of elevated PT + aPTT, and the acute trauma context clinches DIC over chronic liver disease.*

E选项是最危险的干扰项——DIC确实会导致血小板减少，但单纯血小板减少无法解释PT和aPTT同时延长；在急性创伤背景下，PT和aPTT均升高的组合首先考虑DIC，慢性肝病可被急性起病及无肝病史排除。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**Massive traumatic injury triggered systemic tissue factor release in this soldier, consuming all coagulation factors and platelets (DIC), which explains the combined elevation of PT, aPTT, and INR in the acute post-operative setting.**

**这名士兵的重大创伤触发全身性组织因子释放，消耗所有凝血因子和血小板（DIC），这解释了急性术后PT、aPTT及INR同时升高的原因。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "CLOT" for DIC Lab Findings / 记忆钩 — "CLOT" 记忆DIC实验室特征:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>C</strong>onsumption coagulopathy — PT↑, aPTT↑, INR↑ from depletion of all clotting factors / 消耗性凝血病 — 所有凝血因子耗竭致PT↑、aPTT↑、INR↑<br />
• <strong>L</strong>ysis (fibrinolysis) active — D-dimer↑ from fibrin degradation products released by plasmin / 纤溶亢进 — 纤溶酶释放纤维蛋白降解产物致D-dimer↑<br />
• <strong>O</strong>ut goes fibrinogen — fibrinogen↓ consumed in clot formation (opposite of hyperfibrinogenemia) / 纤维蛋白原减少 — 纤维蛋白原↓在凝血中被消耗（与高纤维蛋白原血症相反）<br />
• <strong>T</strong>hrombocytopenia — platelets↓ consumed forming microvascular fibrin-platelet thrombi / 血小板减少症 — 血小板↓在形成微血管纤维蛋白-血小板血栓时被消耗</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — DIC: Causes, Labs, and Management / 高频知识表 — DIC：病因、检验与处理

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Classic DIC triggers (STOMP)<br />
DIC经典触发因素（STOMP）</td>
<td><strong>S</strong>epsis (most common overall), <strong>T</strong>rauma (most common surgical), <strong>O</strong>bstetric (abruption, amniotic fluid embolism, HELLP), <strong>M</strong>alignancy (especially AML-M3/APL via Auer rod procoagulants), <strong>P</strong>ancreatitis (acute severe)<br />
<strong>S</strong>epsis脓毒症（最常见）、<strong>T</strong>rauma创伤（外科最常见）、<strong>O</strong>bstetric产科（胎盘早剥、羊水栓塞、HELLP）、<strong>M</strong>alignancy恶性肿瘤（尤AML-M3/APL经Auer小体促凝物质）、<strong>P</strong>ancreatitis急性重症胰腺炎</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Full DIC lab panel (6 key values)<br />
DIC完整实验室检查（6个关键指标）</td>
<td>PT↑, aPTT↑, INR↑ (factor consumption); Platelets↓; Fibrinogen↓; D-dimer↑; Peripheral smear: schistocytes (helmet cells) from MAHA; Factor VIII↓ (distinguishes from liver failure where VIII is normal)<br />
PT↑、aPTT↑、INR↑（因子消耗）；血小板↓；纤维蛋白原↓；D-dimer↑；外周血涂片：MAHA裂体细胞（头盔细胞）；VIII因子↓（与肝衰竭鉴别，肝衰竭VIII因子正常）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>DIC vs. liver failure key differentiator<br />
DIC与肝衰竭关键鉴别点</td>
<td>Factor VIII is synthesized by endothelium (not hepatocytes) — it is NORMAL or ELEVATED in liver failure but DECREASED in DIC (consumed); if Factor VIII is low → DIC, not liver disease<br />
VIII因子由内皮细胞合成（非肝细胞）——肝衰竭时正常或升高，DIC时降低（被消耗）；若VIII因子低→DIC，非肝病</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Lethal triad in trauma DIC<br />
创伤DIC"死亡三联征"</td>
<td>Hypothermia + Acidosis + Coagulopathy — mutually reinforcing vicious cycle: hypothermia impairs factor enzyme activity, acidosis worsens it, coagulopathy causes ongoing blood loss → more acidosis<br />
低体温+酸中毒+凝血病——相互强化的恶性循环：低体温损害因子酶活性，酸中毒加重，凝血病致持续失血→更多酸中毒</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Damage control resuscitation (DCR)<br />
损伤控制性复苏（DCR）</td>
<td>Balanced transfusion ratio 1:1:1 (pRBC:FFP:platelets) prevents dilutional coagulopathy; permissive hypotension (MAP ~50 mmHg) until hemorrhage controlled; avoid large-volume crystalloid<br />
平衡输血比例1:1:1（红细胞:FFP:血小板）防止稀释性凝血病；允许性低血压（MAP约50 mmHg）直至出血控制；避免大量晶体液</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Acute DIC vs. chronic DIC (Trousseau)<br />
急性DIC与慢性DIC（Trousseau综合征）</td>
<td>Acute (trauma, sepsis): rapid, life-threatening, bleeding predominates, PT/aPTT markedly elevated; Chronic (occult malignancy): compensated, thrombosis may predominate (migratory thrombophlebitis), labs may be near-normal<br />
急性（创伤、脓毒症）：急速、危及生命、出血为主，PT/aPTT显著升高；慢性（隐匿性恶性肿瘤）：代偿性，血栓可能为主（游走性血栓性静脉炎），实验室检查可接近正常</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of elevated PT + elevated aPTT:** DIC, severe liver disease (distinguish by Factor VIII level), massive transfusion/dilutional coagulopathy, supratherapeutic heparin (anticoagulant effect on aPTT \> PT), late vitamin K deficiency; Factor VIII is the single most useful discriminator between DIC and liver failure\
  **PT和aPTT均升高的鉴别诊断:** DIC、重度肝病（通过VIII因子水平鉴别）、大量输血/稀释性凝血病、超治疗剂量肝素（aPTT\>PT）、晚期维生素K缺乏；VIII因子是鉴别DIC与肝衰竭最有用的单一指标

- **Obstetric DIC variant:** Amniotic fluid embolism, placental abruption, and retained dead fetus are high-yield obstetric DIC triggers; fetal tissue is rich in tissue factor and phospholipids that directly activate the coagulation cascade\
  **产科DIC变式:** 羊水栓塞、胎盘早剥和死胎滞留是高频产科DIC触发因素；胎儿组织富含直接激活凝血级联的组织因子和磷脂

- **AML-M3 (APL) and DIC:** Acute promyelocytic leukemia causes DIC via procoagulant release from Auer rods in granules of promyelocytes; initiating ATRA (all-trans retinoic acid) can transiently worsen DIC before differentiation occurs — monitor labs closely\
  **AML-M3（APL）与DIC:** 急性早幼粒细胞白血病通过早幼粒细胞颗粒Auer小体释放促凝物质引发DIC；启动ATRA（全反式维甲酸）治疗后分化前DIC可短暂加重——需密切监测实验室指标

- **Key complication — MAHA:** Microangiopathic hemolytic anemia from fibrin strand shearing of RBCs presents with schistocytes (helmet/triangle cells) on peripheral blood smear, elevated LDH, decreased haptoglobin, and indirect hyperbilirubinemia — the same peripheral smear findings seen in TTP/HUS\
  **关键并发症——MAHA:** 纤维蛋白链切割红细胞所致微血管病性溶血性贫血表现为外周血涂片裂体细胞（头盔/三角形细胞）、LDH升高、触珠蛋白降低及间接胆红素升高——与TTP/HUS外周血涂片表现相同

# Question 34 — Chronic Anal Fissure Requiring Surgical Repair / 慢性肛裂需手术修复

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>25-year-old woman</strong>, gravida 1, para 1, comes to the office because of a <strong>3-month history</strong> of chronic moderate <strong>perianal pain and bleeding</strong> that began <strong>3 days after she gave birth via cesarean delivery</strong>. Before the onset of her symptoms, she had <strong>constipation</strong> associated with the use of postdelivery oxycodone therapy. The constipation resolved after she discontinued the medication, but her bowel movements have been painful and she has noticed blood on the toilet tissue. One week ago, the patient's obstetrician prescribed <strong>topical hydrocortisone and diltiazem</strong>, which provide temporary relief but do not resolve her symptoms. The patient's medical history otherwise is unremarkable and she takes no other medications. Family history is unremarkable. Vital signs are temperature 37.2°C (99.0°F), pulse 80/min, respirations 20/min, and blood pressure 130/80 mm Hg. Examination of the anus shows a <strong>deep wound in the posterior midline</strong> with <strong>exposure of the internal sphincter muscle</strong> and an associated <strong>1.5-cm skin tag</strong>.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Biopsy of the wound<br />
B) Colonoscopy<br />
C) Metronidazole therapy<br />
D) Surgical repair</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: D</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>3-month history of perianal pain and bleeding<br />
3个月慢性肛周疼痛伴出血</td>
<td>Duration &gt;8 weeks defines CHRONIC fissure — conservative management alone is insufficient<br />
病程超8周即为慢性肛裂——单纯保守治疗效果不佳</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Constipation from postdelivery oxycodone<br />
产后阿片类药物导致的便秘</td>
<td>Hard stool passage raises intraluminal pressure and initiates the anal tear<br />
硬便通过使肛管内压升高，是肛裂形成的初始诱因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Topical hydrocortisone and diltiazem — temporary relief only<br />
局部氢化可的松和地尔硫䓬——仅暂时缓解</td>
<td>Failed conservative therapy is the direct indication for surgical repair<br />
保守治疗失败是手术修复的直接指征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Deep wound in the posterior midline<br />

<td>&gt;90% of anal fissures occur at the posterior midline due to its relatively poor vascular supply<br />
超90%肛裂位于后正中线，因该处血供相对不足</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Exposure of the internal sphincter muscle<br />
内括约肌暴露</td>
<td>Hallmark of chronic fissure — persistent IAS spasm → ischemia → non-healing wound cycle<br />
慢性肛裂的标志性特征——内括约肌持续痉挛→缺血→伤口不愈合恶性循环</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Associated 1.5-cm skin tag (sentinel pile)<br />
伴1.5cm皮赘（前哨痔）</td>
<td>Pathognomonic of a chronic fissure; indicates a longstanding, indolent process<br />
慢性肛裂的特征性伴随体征，提示病程迁延</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Anal fissures** arise from a **tear in the anoderm** at the anal verge, most commonly triggered by **hard stool passage**. The posterior midline is preferentially affected due to its relatively poor submucosal arterial supply:

肛裂由肛缘**皮肤裂伤（anoderm tear）**引起，最常见诱因是**硬便通过**。后正中线因黏膜下动脉供血相对不足而最易受累：

- Tear exposes the underlying **internal anal sphincter (IAS)** → reflexive IAS spasm → elevated resting anal pressure → tissue ischemia\
  裂伤暴露深层**内括约肌（IAS）** → 反射性内括约肌痉挛 → 肛管静息压升高 → 组织缺血

- Ischemia impairs epithelialization → fissure fails to heal → becomes **chronic** (\>8 weeks)\
  缺血妨碍上皮化 → 伤口愈合失败 → 肛裂进展为**慢性**（\>8周）

- Chronic fissure triad: **exposed IAS at wound base**, **sentinel skin tag** distally, **hypertrophied anal papilla** proximally\
  慢性肛裂三联征：**创底内括约肌暴露**、远端**前哨皮赘**、近端**肛乳头肥大**

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The posterior midline has fewer submucosal arterial branches than the lateral walls — this relative ischemia explains why ~90% of fissures preferentially occur there.

**解剖小窍门:** 后正中线黏膜下动脉分支少于侧壁，相对缺血解释了约90%的肛裂为何好发于此处。

## 3. Correct Answer (D) — Lateral Internal Sphincterotomy / 正确答案 (D) — 侧方内括约肌切开术

**Surgical repair** (lateral internal sphincterotomy, LIS) is the definitive treatment for chronic anal fissures or those that fail conservative management:

**手术修复**（侧方内括约肌切开术，LIS）是慢性肛裂或保守治疗无效者的根治性治疗方式：

- LIS partially divides the **hypertonic IAS** → reduces anal resting pressure → restores mucosal blood flow → promotes healing\
  LIS部分切断**高张力内括约肌** → 降低肛管静息压 → 恢复黏膜血流 → 促进伤口愈合

- Cure rate \>90% with a single procedure; superior to all conservative modalities for chronic fissures\
  单次手术治愈率\>90%；对慢性肛裂疗效优于所有保守治疗措施

- Conservative therapy (topical vasodilators, stool softeners, sitz baths) is adequate for **acute** fissures (\<8 weeks) but insufficient for **chronic** ones\
  保守治疗（局部扩血管药、大便软化剂、坐浴）对**急性**肛裂（\<8周）有效，对**慢性**肛裂则不够充分

**Diagnosis:** Chronic anal fissure — 3 months of recurrent perianal pain and bleeding, posterior midline deep wound with exposed IAS and sentinel skin tag, failed topical diltiazem and hydrocortisone therapy.

**诊断:** 慢性肛裂——3个月反复肛周疼痛出血，后正中线深部创面伴内括约肌暴露及前哨皮赘，局部地尔硫䓬和氢化可的松治疗无效。

**Treatment:** Lateral internal sphincterotomy (LIS) — partial IAS division to interrupt the pain-spasm-ischemia cycle and allow wound healing.

**治疗:** 侧方内括约肌切开术（LIS）——部分切断内括约肌，打断疼痛-痉挛-缺血恶性循环，促进伤口愈合。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Biopsy of the wound<br />
A — 伤口活检</td>
<td>Wrong — unnecessary and will worsen pain; the classic triad (posterior midline, exposed IAS, sentinel skin tag) is diagnostic of anal fissure without biopsy<br />
错误——操作不必要且会加重疼痛；典型三联征（后正中线、内括约肌暴露、前哨皮赘）已可临床诊断肛裂，无需活检</td>
<td>Biopsy warranted only for atypical fissures (lateral location, multiple, suspicion for Crohn's or malignancy)<br />
仅非典型肛裂（侧方位置、多发、疑似克罗恩病或恶性肿瘤）才需活检</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Colonoscopy<br />
B — 结肠镜</td>
<td>Wrong — colonoscopy evaluates intraluminal colorectal pathology; this patient's pathology is at the external anal verge with no systemic red flags for IBD or malignancy<br />
错误——结肠镜用于评估肠腔内结直肠病变；该患者病变位于外部肛缘，无提示IBD或恶性肿瘤的全身性红旗征</td>
<td>Colonoscopy warranted if atypical fissure accompanied by systemic symptoms (weight loss, diarrhea) suggesting IBD<br />
若非典型肛裂伴全身症状（体重下降、腹泻）提示IBD时才需结肠镜</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Metronidazole therapy<br />
C — 甲硝唑治疗</td>
<td>Wrong — metronidazole targets anaerobic/parasitic infections; this patient has no evidence of infection (no fever, no purulent discharge, no fluctuant mass)<br />
错误——甲硝唑针对厌氧菌/寄生虫感染；该患者无感染证据（无发热、无脓性分泌物、无波动性肿块）</td>
<td>Metronidazole used for perianal Crohn's disease or perianal abscess — not for mechanical anal fissure<br />
甲硝唑适用于肛周克罗恩病或肛周脓肿，不适用于机械性肛裂</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Surgical repair ✓<br />
D — 手术修复 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — chronic fissure (3 months, &gt;8 weeks) with failed topical vasodilator therapy → lateral internal sphincterotomy is the definitive next step<br />
正确——慢性肛裂（3个月，&gt;8周）且局部扩血管药治疗失败→侧方内括约肌切开术是确定性下一步处理</td>
<td>Chronic duration + failed conservative therapy = surgical indication regardless of other findings<br />
慢性病程+保守治疗失败=手术指征，与其他伴随发现无关</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most seductive distractor is Choice A (biopsy) — students anxious about ruling out malignancy may reach for it, but the posterior midline location combined with exposed IAS and sentinel skin tag is pathognomonic for chronic anal fissure; biopsy would inflict unnecessary pain with zero diagnostic gain.*

最大干扰项是活检（选项A）——担心排除恶性肿瘤的学生容易被误导，但后正中线位置+内括约肌暴露+前哨皮赘三联征已是慢性肛裂的特征性诊断；活检仅增加不必要的疼痛，无任何诊断收益。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A chronic anal fissure (\>8 weeks) presenting with a posterior midline wound, exposed internal anal sphincter, and sentinel skin tag requires surgical repair (lateral internal sphincterotomy) after failure of conservative vasodilator therapy.**

**慢性肛裂（\>8周）表现为后正中线创面、内括约肌暴露及前哨皮赘，保守扩血管治疗失败后需行手术修复（侧方内括约肌切开术）。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — SCAR Signs of Chronic Fissure / 记忆钩 — 慢性肛裂"SCAR"四要素:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>S</strong>phincter (internal) exposed at wound base — the hallmark that separates chronic from acute / <strong>S</strong>——内括约肌（Sphincter）创底暴露——区分急慢性的标志<br />
• <strong>C</strong>hronic means &gt;8 weeks — conservative therapy is no longer enough / <strong>C</strong>——慢性（Chronic）即&gt;8周——保守治疗已不够充分<br />
• <strong>A</strong>t the posterior midline — site of relative ischemia, explains predilection / <strong>A</strong>——位于（At）后正中线——相对缺血的好发解剖部位<br />
• <strong>R</strong>epair surgically (LIS) — cuts the IAS spasm-ischemia cycle for good / <strong>R</strong>——手术修复（Repair/LIS）——永久打断内括约肌痉挛-缺血恶性循环</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Anal Fissure / 高频知识表 — 肛裂

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Classic presentation<br />
典型表现</td>
<td>Sharp tearing anal pain during and after defecation + bright red blood on toilet tissue; pain may persist for hours post-bowel movement<br />
排便时及排便后撕裂样肛门疼痛+便纸鲜红血迹；疼痛可持续数小时</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Location rule<br />
好发部位规律</td>
<td>Posterior midline ~90%; anterior midline ~10% (especially women); lateral location = atypical → workup for Crohn's, HIV, syphilis, anal carcinoma<br />
后正中线约90%；前正中线约10%（女性多见）；侧方=非典型→排查克罗恩病、HIV、梅毒、肛管癌</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Conservative management<br />
保守治疗</td>
<td>Sitz baths, stool softeners, increased fiber, topical anesthetics, topical vasodilators (0.2% nitroglycerin or 2% diltiazem); effective for acute fissures (&lt;8 weeks)<br />
坐浴、大便软化剂、膳食纤维增加、局部麻醉药、局部扩血管药（0.2%硝酸甘油或2%地尔硫䓬）；对急性肛裂（&lt;8周）有效</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Lateral internal sphincterotomy (LIS)<br />
侧方内括约肌切开术</td>
<td>Gold standard for chronic/refractory fissures; &gt;90% cure rate; main risk is minor fecal incontinence (~5%)<br />
慢性/难治性肛裂的金标准；治愈率&gt;90%；主要风险为轻度大便失禁（约5%）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Botulinum toxin injection<br />
肉毒素注射</td>
<td>Second-line alternative to LIS; temporarily paralyzes IAS to allow healing; lower incontinence risk but higher recurrence rate (~50% at 2 years)<br />
LIS的二线替代方案；暂时麻痹内括约肌促进愈合；大便失禁风险较低但复发率较高（2年约50%）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Risk factors<br />
危险因素</td>
<td>Constipation (most common), diarrhea, vaginal delivery (perineal trauma), low-fiber diet, Crohn's disease<br />
便秘（最常见）、腹泻、阴道分娩（会阴创伤）、低纤维饮食、克罗恩病</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Distinguishing hemorrhoids<br />
与痔疮鉴别</td>
<td>Hemorrhoids cause painless bleeding or prolapse-related discomfort; fissures cause severe pain WITH defecation; locations and physical exam differ<br />
痔疮表现为无痛出血或脱垂不适；肛裂表现为排便时剧痛；二者部位和体检表现不同</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of perianal pain with bleeding:** anal fissure (pain during defecation, posterior midline tear), hemorrhoids (painless bright red bleeding or prolapse pain), perianal abscess (constant throbbing pain with fever and fluctuance), anal fistula (chronic purulent drainage from perianal opening)\
  **肛周疼痛出血的鉴别诊断:** 肛裂（排便时疼痛，后正中线裂伤）、痔疮（无痛鲜红色出血或脱垂痛）、肛周脓肿（持续跳痛伴发热及波动感）、肛瘘（肛周开口慢性脓性分泌物）

- **LIS complication — fecal incontinence:** partial IAS division risks minor gas/stool leakage (~5%); risk is higher in multiparous women and elderly patients with baseline sphincter weakness; informed consent must address this tradeoff\
  **LIS并发症——大便失禁:** 部分内括约肌切断有轻度气/便漏风险（约5%）；多次分娩女性及存在基础括约肌薄弱的老年患者风险更高；知情同意须告知此权衡

- **Atypical fissure workup:** lateral, multiple, or treatment-refractory fissures should prompt biopsy plus evaluation for Crohn's disease (colonoscopy, CRP, fecal calprotectin), HIV, syphilis, and anal squamous cell carcinoma\
  **非典型肛裂的诊断评估:** 侧方、多发或治疗难治性肛裂应行活检，并评估克罗恩病（结肠镜、CRP、粪便钙卫蛋白）、HIV、梅毒及肛管鳞癌

- **Obstetric context:** vaginal delivery (not cesarean) is the classic obstetric risk factor for anal fissures due to direct perineal trauma; this patient's fissure was instead triggered by opioid-induced constipation after C-section — a pharmacologic etiology\
  **产科相关背景:** 阴道分娩（而非剖宫产）因直接会阴创伤是肛裂经典产科危险因素；本题患者的肛裂由剖宫产后阿片类药物所致便秘诱发——属于药理性病因

# Question 35 — Acute Cocaine Intoxication / 急性可卡因中毒

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>42-year-old man</strong> is brought to the emergency department by paramedics 1 hour after his girlfriend found him <strong>confused and agitated</strong> in his home. The girlfriend says that when she spoke with him on the telephone last night, she noted no problems, but she became worried when he did not answer his telephone 3 hours ago. He has a 3-year history of chronic back pain for which he takes oxycodone. He also has major depressive disorder and seasonal allergies treated with citalopram and diphenhydramine, respectively. On arrival, he is confused, screaming loudly, and actively pulling against wrist restraints. His <strong>temperature is 38°C (100.4°F)</strong>, <strong>pulse is 163/min</strong>, respirations are 24/min, and <strong>blood pressure is 215/105 mm Hg</strong>. Physical examination shows <strong>diaphoresis</strong> and tremulousness. The <strong>pupils are dilated</strong>. Which of the following is the most likely cause of this patient's confusion?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most likely cause of this patient's confusion?</strong></p>
<p>A) Acetaminophen overdose<br />
B) Cannabis withdrawal<br />
C) Cocaine intoxication<br />
D) Diphenhydramine toxicity<br />
E) Opioid withdrawal</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: C</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Confused, agitated, screaming, pulling against restraints<br />
意识混乱、激越、尖叫、抵抗约束</td>
<td>Severe CNS stimulation — rules out sedative/opioid intoxication (which causes CNS depression)<br />
严重中枢神经系统兴奋——排除镇静药/阿片类中毒（后者引起CNS抑制）</td>

心率163次/分</td>

极度心动过速→大量交感神经激增；严重程度倾向中毒而非戒断</td>

</tr>
<tr>

体温38°C</td>
<td>Hyperthermia from increased sympathetic tone, psychomotor agitation, and impaired heat dissipation<br />
交感神经张力增高、运动性激越及散热障碍共同导致体温升高</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Takes oxycodone + citalopram + diphenhydramine<br />
正在使用羟考酮+西酞普兰+苯海拉明</td>
<td>Three classic distractors built into the vignette: opioid withdrawal, serotonin syndrome, and anticholinergic toxicity must each be systematically excluded<br />
题目中植入的三个经典干扰项：必须系统排除阿片戒断、5-羟色胺综合征和抗胆碱毒性</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Cocaine** is a **triple monoamine reuptake inhibitor** that blocks presynaptic transporters for **dopamine (DAT)**, **norepinephrine (NET)**, and **serotonin (SERT)**, flooding all three synaptic clefts simultaneously:

**可卡因**是一种**三重单胺再摄取抑制剂**，同时阻断突触前**多巴胺转运体（DAT）**、**去甲肾上腺素转运体（NET）**和**5-羟色胺转运体（SERT）**，使三种突触间隙浓度骤升：

- **Norepinephrine** excess → α1-receptor activation → peripheral vasoconstriction → hypertension; β1-activation → tachycardia; direct sympathetic sweat gland stimulation → diaphoresis\
  **去甲肾上腺素**过量→α1受体激活→外周血管收缩→高血压；β1激活→心动过速；直接刺激交感性汗腺→大汗

- **Dopamine** excess → mesolimbic reward pathway → euphoria; in high doses → paranoia, hallucinations, psychomotor agitation\
  **多巴胺**过量→中脑边缘奖赏通路→欣快感；大剂量时→偏执妄想、幻觉、精神运动性激越

- **Serotonin** excess → mood elevation and contributes to CNS stimulation; at high doses may contribute to hyperthermia\
  **5-羟色胺**过量→情绪高涨和中枢兴奋；大剂量时可能参与体温升高

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Cocaine also blocks voltage-gated Na⁺ channels — this is the mechanism behind its historical use as a nasal surgical anesthetic and explains why cocaine toxicity can cause wide-complex dysrhythmias.

**解剖小窍门:** 可卡因同时阻断电压门控Na⁺通道——这是其历史上用于鼻腔手术麻醉的机制，也解释了可卡因毒性为何可引起宽QRS心律失常。

## 3. Correct Answer (C) — Cocaine Intoxication / 正确答案 (C) — 可卡因中毒

**Cocaine intoxication** produces the full **sympathomimetic toxidrome** through simultaneous catecholamine flooding at peripheral and central synapses:

**可卡因中毒**通过外周和中枢突触同时发生儿茶酚胺洪泛，产生完整的**拟交感神经毒综合征**：

- Tachycardia (HR 163) + hypertension (BP 215/105) + hyperthermia (T 38°C) = the autonomic triad of sympathomimetic excess\
  心动过速（HR 163）+高血压（BP 215/105）+体温升高（T 38°C）=拟交感神经过量的自主神经三联征

- Mydriasis from α1 and β-adrenergic stimulation of the iris dilator muscle\
  瞳孔散大：虹膜扩大肌受α1及β肾上腺素能刺激所致

- Diaphoresis from thermoregulatory activation and direct sympathetic cholinergic sweat gland stimulation — the key feature distinguishing this from anticholinergic toxidrome\
  大汗：体温调节激活及交感胆碱能汗腺直接刺激所致——鉴别抗胆碱毒综合征的关键特征

- Severe agitation and confusion from dopaminergic and noradrenergic CNS overstimulation\
  严重激越和意识混乱：多巴胺能和去甲肾上腺素能中枢神经系统过度兴奋所致

**Diagnosis:** Acute sympathomimetic toxidrome with abrupt onset and no prodrome, occurring in a patient without prior documented cocaine use — most consistent with cocaine (or amphetamine-class) intoxication.

**诊断:** 急性起病、无前驱期的拟交感神经毒综合征，发生于无可卡因使用记录的患者——最符合可卡因（或苯丙胺类）中毒。

**Treatment:** Benzodiazepines first-line (lorazepam/diazepam) for agitation, seizures, and cardiovascular stabilization; phentolamine for refractory hypertension; avoid β-blockers (risk of unopposed α-adrenergic vasoconstriction worsening hypertension); active cooling for hyperthermia.

**治疗:** 苯二氮䓬类一线治疗（劳拉西泮/地西泮）用于激越、癫痫发作及心血管稳定；酚妥拉明用于难治性高血压；避免β受体阻滞剂（未拮抗α肾上腺素能血管收缩会加重高血压）；积极物理降温处理高热。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Acetaminophen overdose<br />
A — 对乙酰氨基酚过量</td>
<td>Presents with nausea, vomiting, RUQ pain, then jaundice and fulminant liver failure — zero sympathomimetic features; no agitation or autonomic instability<br />
表现为恶心、呕吐、右上腹痛，继而黄疸和暴发性肝衰竭——完全无拟交感特征；无激越或自主神经不稳定</td>
<td>No hepatotoxicity signs (jaundice, coagulopathy); no elevated LFTs mentioned<br />
无肝毒性表现（黄疸、凝血功能障碍）；未提及转氨酶升高</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Cannabis withdrawal<br />
B — 大麻戒断</td>
<td>Mild syndrome: irritability, anxiety, insomnia, decreased appetite — does NOT produce severe autonomic instability, hypertensive emergency, or extreme tachycardia<br />
轻度综合征：易激惹、焦虑、失眠、食欲下降——不会引起严重自主神经不稳定、高血压急症或极度心动过速</td>
<td>Degree of HR 163 and BP 215/105 is incompatible with cannabis withdrawal<br />
HR 163和BP 215/105的程度与大麻戒断不相符</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Cocaine intoxication ✓<br />
C — 可卡因中毒 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Classic sympathomimetic toxidrome: tachycardia, hypertension, hyperthermia, diaphoresis (WET), mydriasis, agitation, all present<br />
正确——经典拟交感神经毒综合征：心动过速、高血压、体温升高、大汗（皮肤湿润）、瞳孔散大、激越，全部具备</td>
<td>Diaphoresis (wet) + full sympathomimetic triad + no withdrawal stigmata<br />
大汗（皮肤湿润）+完整拟交感三联征+无戒断标志性体征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Diphenhydramine toxicity<br />
D — 苯海拉明毒性</td>
<td>Anticholinergic toxidrome: DRY, flushed, hot skin; urinary retention; decreased bowel sounds; sedation/delirium — patient here has DIAPHORESIS which definitively excludes this<br />
抗胆碱毒综合征：皮肤干燥、潮红、发热；尿潴留；肠鸣音减弱；镇静/谵妄——本患者存在大汗，明确排除此诊断</td>
<td>Diaphoresis vs. dry flushed skin is the single definitive discriminator<br />
大汗 vs. 皮肤干燥潮红是唯一决定性鉴别点</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Opioid withdrawal<br />
E — 阿片类戒断</td>
<td>Also causes tachycardia, hypertension, mydriasis, tremors, and diaphoresis — but hallmark features are lacrimation, rhinorrhea, piloerection, and yawning, none of which are described here; severity of autonomic instability also more consistent with cocaine<br />
也可引起心动过速、高血压、瞳孔散大、震颤和大汗——但标志性体征为流泪、流涕、鸡皮疙瘩和哈欠，本例均未描述；自主神经不稳定程度亦更符合可卡因中毒</td>
<td>Absent CROW signs (Cramping, Rhinorrhea, Obsessive craving, Watery eyes)<br />
缺乏CROW体征（腹痛/腹泻、流涕、强烈觅药欲、流泪）</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The toughest distractor is opioid withdrawal (E) — the patient chronically uses oxycodone, and withdrawal does produce tachycardia, hypertension, mydriasis, and diaphoresis. The discriminating pivot is the complete absence of CROW signs (Cramping/diarrhea, Rhinorrhea, Obsessive drug-craving, Watery eyes/lacrimation) and the extraordinary degree of cardiovascular instability (HR 163, BP 215/105), which far exceeds typical opioid withdrawal.*

最难排除的干扰项是阿片戒断（E）——患者长期使用羟考酮，且阿片戒断确实可引起心动过速、高血压、瞳孔散大和大汗。鉴别关键在于完全缺乏CROW体征（腹痛/腹泻、流涕、强烈觅药欲、流泪），以及极度的心血管不稳定（HR 163、BP 215/105）远超典型阿片戒断程度。
