## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**Cocaine blocks presynaptic reuptake of norepinephrine, dopamine, and serotonin, producing the sympathomimetic toxidrome of tachycardia, hypertension, hyperthermia, diaphoresis (WET skin), mydriasis, and agitation — distinguished from anticholinergic toxidrome by the presence of sweating.**

**可卡因阻断突触前去甲肾上腺素、多巴胺和5-羟色胺的再摄取，产生拟交感神经毒综合征——心动过速、高血压、体温升高、大汗（皮肤湿润）、瞳孔散大和激越——以皮肤出汗有别于抗胆碱毒综合征。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "MAD HT" Sympathomimetic Toxidrome / 记忆钩 — "MAD HT" 拟交感毒综合征:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>M</strong>ydriasis — dilated pupils from α1/β-adrenergic iris dilator stimulation / 瞳孔散大——α1/β肾上腺素能刺激虹膜扩大肌<br />
• <strong>A</strong>gitation — dopamine + norepinephrine CNS excess → psychomotor restlessness / 激越——多巴胺+去甲肾上腺素中枢过量→精神运动性不安<br />
• <strong>D</strong>iaphoresis — WET skin; the single feature that excludes anticholinergic toxidrome / 大汗——皮肤湿润；排除抗胆碱毒综合征的唯一特征<br />
• <strong>H</strong>ypertension + <strong>H</strong>yperthermia — norepinephrine vasoconstriction + heat generation from agitation / 高血压+体温升高——去甲肾上腺素血管收缩+激越产热<br />
• <strong>T</strong>achycardia — β1-adrenergic cardiac stimulation driving HR &gt; 150 / 心动过速——β1肾上腺素能心脏刺激使HR &gt; 150次/分</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Cocaine Pharmacology and Toxicology / 高频知识表 — 可卡因药理及毒理学

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Mechanism of action<br />
作用机制</td>
<td>Triple reuptake blocker: dopamine (DAT) + norepinephrine (NET) + serotonin (SERT); also voltage-gated Na⁺ channel blocker (local anesthetic effect)<br />
三重再摄取阻断：多巴胺（DAT）+去甲肾上腺素（NET）+5-羟色胺（SERT）；同时阻断电压门控Na⁺通道（局部麻醉效应）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment of intoxication<br />
急性中毒治疗</td>
<td>Benzodiazepines first-line (lorazepam/diazepam) for agitation + cardiovascular effects; AVOID β-blockers (unopposed α-vasoconstriction); phentolamine (α-blocker) for refractory HTN; active cooling for hyperthermia<br />
苯二氮䓬类一线治疗（劳拉西泮/地西泮）用于激越+心血管效应；禁用β受体阻滞剂（α血管收缩失拮抗）；酚妥拉明（α阻滞剂）用于难治性高血压；积极物理降温</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Cardiovascular complications<br />
心血管并发症</td>
<td>Coronary vasospasm → MI even in young patients without atherosclerosis; Na⁺ channel blockade → wide-complex tachycardia/VF; chronic cardiomyopathy from catecholamine toxicity<br />
冠状动脉痉挛→年轻无动脉粥样硬化患者也可发生心肌梗死；Na⁺通道阻断→宽QRS心动过速/室颤；儿茶酚胺毒性致慢性心肌病</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Cocaethylene<br />
可卡乙烯</td>
<td>Cocaine + ethanol co-ingestion → liver produces cocaethylene via transesterification; same pharmacological effects as cocaine but ~5× longer half-life and greater cardiotoxicity; dramatically increases sudden cardiac death risk<br />
可卡因+乙醇同时摄入→肝脏经转酯反应产生可卡乙烯；药理效应与可卡因相同，但半衰期约长5倍、心脏毒性更强；显著增加心源性猝死风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Wet vs. dry in toxidromes<br />
毒综合征中的湿 vs. 干</td>
<td>Sympathomimetic (cocaine, amphetamines): DIAPHORESIS (wet); Anticholinergic (diphenhydramine, TCA, atropine): DRY, flushed, hot — "mad as a hatter, red as a beet, dry as a bone"<br />
拟交感（可卡因、苯丙胺）：大汗（湿）；抗胆碱（苯海拉明、三环类、阿托品）：干燥、潮红、发热——"疯如疯帽匠，红如甜菜根，干如骨头"</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Opioid withdrawal vs. sympathomimetic<br />
阿片戒断 vs. 拟交感中毒</td>
<td>Both: tachycardia, hypertension, mydriasis, diaphoresis. KEY difference: opioid withdrawal → rhinorrhea, lacrimation, piloerection, yawning, GI cramping/diarrhea (CROW signs); cocaine → none of these<br />
共同：心动过速、高血压、瞳孔散大、大汗。关键区别：阿片戒断→流涕、流泪、鸡皮疙瘩、哈欠、腹绞痛/腹泻（CROW体征）；可卡因中毒→以上均无</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Chronic cocaine complications<br />
慢性可卡因并发症</td>
<td>Nasal septum perforation (intranasal use); stroke (hemorrhagic &gt; ischemic); "crack lung" (pulmonary hemorrhage + diffuse alveolar damage); paranoid psychosis; fetal growth restriction<br />
鼻中隔穿孔（鼻吸）；卒中（出血性&gt;缺血性）；"快克肺"（肺出血+弥漫性肺泡损伤）；偏执型精神病；胎儿生长受限</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of sympathomimetic toxidrome:** Cocaine, amphetamines/methamphetamine, MDMA (ecstasy), PCP, synthetic cathinones ("bath salts"), and thyroid storm can all produce similar presentations; urine toxicology and clinical context help differentiate\
  **拟交感神经毒综合征鉴别:** 可卡因、苯丙胺/甲基苯丙胺、MDMA（摇头丸）、PCP、合成卡西酮（"浴盐"）及甲状腺危象均可呈现相似表现；尿液毒理学和临床背景有助于鉴别

- **Cocaine chest pain workup:** Young patient + chest pain + cocaine → ECG + troponin to rule out MI; coronary spasm can cause ST elevation without thrombosis; nitrates and CCBs preferred over β-blockers for spasm management\
  **可卡因胸痛评估:** 年轻患者+胸痛+可卡因→心电图+肌钙蛋白排除心肌梗死；冠状动脉痉挛可在无血栓的情况下引起ST段抬高；痉挛管理优先选择硝酸酯类和CCB而非β受体阻滞剂

- **Serotonin syndrome consideration:** This patient also takes citalopram (SSRI); if cocaine were combined with an SSRI, serotonin syndrome could be in the differential — both share agitation and hyperthermia, but serotonin syndrome adds clonus, hyperreflexia, and tremor\
  **5-羟色胺综合征考量:** 该患者同时服用西酞普兰（SSRI）；若可卡因与SSRI联用，5-羟色胺综合征可进入鉴别诊断——两者共有激越和体温升高，但5-羟色胺综合征还伴有阵挛、反射亢进和震颤

- **Key pharmacokinetics:** Cocaine has a very short half-life (~1 hour); primary metabolite is benzoylecgonine (detectable in urine for 2–4 days); cocaine + ethanol → cocaethylene (longer-acting, more cardiotoxic metabolite)\
  **关键药代动力学:** 可卡因半衰期极短（约1小时）；主要代谢产物为苯甲酰爱冈宁（尿液中可检出2–4天）；可卡因+乙醇→可卡乙烯（作用时间更长、心脏毒性更强的代谢产物）

# Question 36 — Rh Isoimmunization with Fetal Hemolytic Anemia / Rh同种异体免疫致胎儿溶血性贫血

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>21-year-old woman</strong>, <strong>gravida 2, para 1</strong>, at <strong>36 weeks' gestation</strong> is admitted to the hospital in labor. She received <strong>no prenatal care</strong>. She has no history of operative procedures. She reports that she occasionally used cocaine before she knew she was pregnant but has abstained from illicit drug use during the past 8 months. On admission, the cervix is 5 cm dilated and 100% effaced; the vertex is at 0 station. There is a moderate amount of blood-tinged mucus. The membranes are artificially ruptured, yielding clear fluid. Her <strong>blood group is A, Rh-negative</strong>; a <strong>serum anti-D antibody titer is positive</strong>. During the next 30 minutes, fetal heart monitoring shows regular, <strong>sinusoidal wave forms</strong>. Which of the following is the most likely cause of this fetal heart rate pattern?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most likely cause of this fetal heart rate pattern?</strong></p>
<p>A) Abruptio placentae<br />
B) Fetal heart defect<br />
C) Maternal cocaine use<br />
D) Placenta previa<br />
E) Rh isoimmunization</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Blood group A, Rh-negative<br />
血型A，Rh阴性</td>
<td>At risk for Rh isoimmunization if exposed to Rh(D)-positive fetal blood during any fetomaternal hemorrhage<br />
若接触Rh(D)阳性胎儿血液（任何胎母出血事件），均有发生Rh同种异体免疫的风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Serum anti-D antibody titer positive<br />
血清抗D抗体滴度阳性</td>
<td>Confirms prior sensitization; IgG subclass antibodies can cross the placenta and hemolyze fetal RBCs<br />
确认既往已致敏；IgG亚类抗体可穿越胎盘溶解胎儿红细胞</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Gravida 2, para 1<br />
第2次妊娠，有1次分娩史</td>
<td>Prior delivery likely caused fetomaternal hemorrhage and initial sensitization to the Rh(D) antigen<br />
既往分娩可能引起胎母输血，导致对Rh(D)抗原的初次致敏</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No prenatal care<br />
未行产前检查</td>
<td>Missed RhoGAM prophylaxis at 28 weeks; antibody titer never monitored or treated<br />
错过28周RhoGAM预防注射；抗体滴度从未被监测或处理</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Sinusoidal fetal heart rate pattern<br />
正弦型胎心率模式</td>
<td>Pathognomonic for severe fetal anemia (Hgb &lt; 7 g/dL); caused by decreased oxygen delivery from hemolysis<br />
严重胎儿贫血（Hgb&lt;7 g/dL）的特征性表现；由溶血引起氧输送减少所致</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Clear amniotic fluid after AROM<br />
人工破膜后羊水清亮</td>
<td>Rules out active fetomaternal hemorrhage from abruption or previa as the immediate cause<br />
排除胎盘早剥或前置胎盘所致的急性胎母出血作为即时病因</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Rh isoimmunization** develops when an **Rh(D)-negative** mother is exposed to **Rh(D)-positive** fetal red blood cells, triggering a maternal immune response that generates **anti-D IgG antibodies**:

**Rh同种异体免疫**发生于**Rh(D)阴性**母亲接触**Rh(D)阳性**胎儿红细胞，触发母体免疫应答，产生**抗D IgG抗体**：

- Prior delivery (G1) caused fetomaternal hemorrhage → primary **sensitization** to Rh(D) antigen → IgM memory response\
  既往G1分娩引起胎母出血 → 对Rh(D)抗原的初次**致敏** → IgM记忆应答

- Current (G2) pregnancy: re-exposure to Rh(D) antigen → rapid high-titer **anti-D IgG** production\
  本次（G2）妊娠：再次接触Rh(D)抗原 → 迅速产生高滴度**抗D IgG**

- Anti-D IgG crosses placenta → opsonizes fetal Rh(D)-positive RBCs → **extravascular hemolysis** in fetal spleen\
  抗D IgG穿越胎盘 → 调理素化胎儿Rh(D)阳性红细胞 → 在胎儿脾脏发生**血管外溶血**

- Progressive **hemolytic anemia** → decreased oxygen-carrying capacity → fetal hypoxia → compensatory tachycardia with fixed oscillation\
  进行性**溶血性贫血** → 携氧能力下降 → 胎儿缺氧 → 代偿性心动过速伴固定振荡

- Result: **sinusoidal FHR pattern** — regular sine-wave oscillation 2–5 cycles/min, amplitude 5–15 bpm, absent accelerations\
  结果：**正弦型胎心率模式** — 规律正弦波振荡，2–5次/分，幅度5–15 bpm，无加速

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** IgG (NOT IgM) crosses the placenta — only the secondary IgG-mediated response causes fetal hemolytic disease.

**解剖小窍门:** IgG（而非IgM）穿越胎盘——只有继发性IgG介导的应答才会引起胎儿溶血病。

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Rh Isoimmunization / 正确答案 (E) — Rh同种异体免疫

**Rh isoimmunization** is the sensitization of an Rh(D)-negative mother to fetal Rh(D) antigen, causing hemolytic disease of the fetus and newborn (HDFN):

**Rh同种异体免疫**是Rh(D)阴性母亲对胎儿Rh(D)抗原的致敏过程，导致胎儿及新生儿溶血病（HDFN）：

- Anti-D antibodies are IgG subclass → cross the placenta freely by active transport\
  抗D抗体为IgG亚类 → 经主动转运自由穿越胎盘

- Fetal Rh(D)-positive RBCs coated with IgG → destroyed by macrophages → anemia\
  胎儿Rh(D)阳性红细胞被IgG包被 → 被巨噬细胞破坏 → 贫血

- **Sinusoidal FHR pattern** is the hallmark of severe fetal anemia, with no fetal well-being accelerations\
  **正弦型胎心率**是严重胎儿贫血的标志性表现，无胎儿健康加速

- No prenatal care → no RhoGAM prophylaxis at 28 weeks → sensitization progressed undetected\
  无产前检查 → 28周未注射RhoGAM → 致敏进程未被发现

**Diagnosis:** Rh-negative mother + positive anti-D titer + G2P1 + sinusoidal FHR = fetal hemolytic anemia from Rh isoimmunization

**诊断:** Rh阴性母亲 + 抗D滴度阳性 + G2P1 + 正弦型胎心率 = Rh同种异体免疫致胎儿溶血性贫血

**Treatment:** Expedite delivery given 36 weeks; assess neonatal cord blood Hgb and bilirubin; phototherapy or exchange transfusion postnatally; intrauterine transfusion reserved for preterm hydrops

**治疗:** 36周考虑加速分娩；评估新生儿脐血Hgb和胆红素；产后光疗或换血治疗；宫内输血保留给早产胎儿水肿

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Abruptio placentae<br />
A — 胎盘早剥</td>
<td>Classic triad: severe uterine pain, board-like abdomen, heavy vaginal bleeding — all absent here; cocaine stopped 8 months ago<br />
经典三联征：剧烈子宫疼痛、板状腹、大量阴道出血——本例均无；可卡因已戒8个月</td>
<td>Only blood-tinged mucus (bloody show) present; no pain; clear amniotic fluid — inconsistent with abruption<br />
仅有血性黏液（见红）；无疼痛；羊水清亮——与胎盘早剥不符</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Fetal heart defect<br />
B — 胎儿心脏缺陷</td>
<td>Structural defects (VSD, ToF) cause arrhythmias but NOT a sinusoidal pattern; typically detected on prenatal ultrasound<br />
结构性缺陷（室间隔缺损、法洛四联症）引起心律失常但不引起正弦型；通常产前超声可发现</td>
<td>Sinusoidal pattern = anemia marker; structural cardiac disease would show irregular rhythm, not sine-wave oscillation<br />
正弦型 = 贫血标志；结构性心脏病表现为不规则节律，而非正弦波振荡</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Maternal cocaine use<br />
C — 母体可卡因使用</td>
<td>Patient abstained for 8 months; cocaine-induced vasospasm causes acute abruption during or shortly after use, not months later<br />
患者已戒8个月；可卡因致血管痉挛引起使用期间或使用后不久的急性胎盘早剥，而非数月后</td>
<td>No pain, no heavy bleeding, clear fluid — cocaine-related sinusoidal pattern requires concurrent hemorrhage<br />
无疼痛、无大量出血、羊水清亮——可卡因相关正弦型需同时存在出血</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Placenta previa<br />
D — 前置胎盘</td>
<td>Presents with painless bright-red vaginal bleeding; digital cervical exam is contraindicated — yet exam here was safely performed<br />
表现为无痛性鲜红色阴道出血；禁忌阴道检查——然而本例宫颈检查安全完成无异常</td>
<td>Cervix fully examined (5 cm, 100% effaced) without incident; only scant blood-tinged mucus, not hemorrhage<br />
宫颈完整检查（5 cm，100%消失）无异常；仅少量血性黏液，并非出血</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Rh isoimmunization ✓<br />
E — Rh同种异体免疫 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Rh-negative + positive anti-D titer + prior delivery + sinusoidal FHR = fetal hemolytic anemia<br />
正确——Rh阴性 + 抗D阳性 + 有分娩史 + 正弦型胎心 = 胎儿溶血性贫血</td>
<td>Only option with a direct biochemical mechanism linking the labs (anti-D titer) to the FHR finding (anemia → sinusoidal)<br />
唯一具有直接生化机制将实验室指标（抗D滴度）与胎心发现（贫血→正弦型）联系起来的选项</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The strongest distractor is (A) Abruptio placentae, since cocaine use is a classic risk factor — but the 8-month abstinence, absence of pain, clear amniotic fluid, and positive anti-D titer all redirect unambiguously to Rh isoimmunization.*

最强干扰项是(A)胎盘早剥，因为可卡因是其经典危险因素——但8个月戒断史、无腹痛、羊水清亮以及抗D阳性均明确指向Rh同种异体免疫。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Sinusoidal vs. Other Abnormal FHR Patterns / 正弦型与其他异常胎心率模式对比

<th><strong>Late Decelerations</strong><br />

子痫前期、宫内生长受限、过期妊娠</td>

羊水过少、脐带脱垂、胎头受压</td>

侧卧位、吸氧、停催产素；加快分娩</td>
<td>Position change; amnioinfusion if appropriate<br />
改变体位；适当羊水灌注</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**An Rh-negative mother sensitized by a prior delivery generates anti-D IgG antibodies that cross the placenta and cause fetal hemolytic anemia, manifesting as a sinusoidal fetal heart rate pattern.**

**Rh阴性母亲因既往分娩而致敏，产生抗D IgG抗体穿越胎盘导致胎儿溶血性贫血，表现为正弦型胎心率模式。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "SINE = Severity" Mnemonic / 记忆钩 — "SINE = 严重性"助记:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>S</strong>inusoidal FHR — first think fetal anemia, not arrhythmia / 正弦型胎心——首先想到胎儿贫血，而不是心律失常<br />
• <strong>I</strong>gG crosses the placenta (IgM does NOT) — only IgG-mediated sensitization causes HDFN / IgG穿越胎盘（IgM不能）——只有IgG介导的致敏引起HDFN<br />
• <strong>N</strong>o RhoGAM → no protection → sensitization → hemolysis each subsequent pregnancy / 未用RhoGAM→无保护→致敏→每次后续妊娠加重溶血<br />
• <strong>E</strong>rythroblastosis fetalis = fetal RBC destruction by maternal anti-D antibodies / 胎儿成红细胞增多症 = 母体抗D抗体破坏胎儿红细胞</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Rh Isoimmunization & Fetal Hemolytic Disease / 高频知识表 — Rh同种异体免疫与胎儿溶血病

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Sensitizing events<br />
致敏事件</td>
<td>Delivery, spontaneous/therapeutic abortion, amniocentesis, ectopic pregnancy, abdominal trauma, antepartum hemorrhage — any fetomaternal hemorrhage<br />
分娩、自然/人工流产、羊膜穿刺、异位妊娠、腹部创伤、产前出血——任何胎母输血均可致敏</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>RhoGAM indications &amp; timing<br />
RhoGAM适应证与时机</td>
<td>Given at 28 weeks gestation AND within 72 hours of delivery to all Rh-negative mothers; repeat after any sensitizing event<br />
所有Rh阴性母亲于妊娠28周及分娩后72小时内注射；任何致敏事件后重复注射</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Sinusoidal FHR definition<br />
正弦型胎心率定义</td>
<td>Uniform sine-wave oscillation 2–5 cycles/min, amplitude 5–15 bpm, absent accelerations — indicates Hgb typically &lt; 7 g/dL<br />
均匀正弦波振荡，2–5次/分，幅度5–15 bpm，无加速——提示Hgb通常&lt;7 g/dL</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Why G2 worse than G1<br />
为何第2胎比第1胎更重</td>
<td>G1 delivery → primary IgM response (weak, doesn't cross placenta); G2 → rapid secondary high-titer IgG response → crosses placenta → hemolysis<br />
G1分娩→初级IgM应答（弱，不穿胎盘）；G2→迅速继发性高滴度IgG应答→穿越胎盘→溶血</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>MCA Doppler surveillance<br />
大脑中动脉多普勒监测</td>
<td>MCA peak systolic velocity &gt; 1.5 MoM = fetal anemia; non-invasive method preferred over serial amniocenteses for monitoring<br />
大脑中动脉峰值收缩期流速&gt;1.5 MoM = 胎儿贫血；无创方法优于连续羊膜穿刺监测</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hydrops fetalis<br />
胎儿水肿</td>
<td>End-stage: generalized edema, ascites, pleural and pericardial effusions from high-output cardiac failure; universally fatal without intervention<br />
终末期：全身水肿、腹水、胸腔和心包积液，因高输出量心衰所致；不干预则预后极差</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Postnatal management of HDFN<br />
HDFN产后处理</td>
<td>Cord blood Hgb + bilirubin; phototherapy for hyperbilirubinemia; IVIG to reduce hemolysis; exchange transfusion for severe anemia or bilirubin toxicity<br />
脐血Hgb+胆红素；高胆红素血症行光疗；IVIG减少溶血；严重贫血或胆红素毒性行换血治疗</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Other causes of sinusoidal FHR:** parvovirus B19 (fetal aplastic crisis), fetomaternal hemorrhage, twin-to-twin transfusion syndrome (recipient twin); rarely, opioid administration creates a pseudo-sinusoidal pattern\
  **正弦型胎心率其他原因:** 细小病毒B19（胎儿再生障碍危象）、胎母出血、双胎输血综合征（受血儿）；偶见阿片类药物使用造成假性正弦型

- **ABO incompatibility vs. Rh incompatibility:** ABO (O-type mother + A or B baby) is milder because anti-A/B IgM does not cross the placenta; Rh disease worsens with each sensitized pregnancy\
  **ABO不相容与Rh不相容对比:** ABO（O型母亲+A或B型胎儿）较轻，因抗A/B IgM不穿越胎盘；Rh溶血病随每次致敏妊娠加重

- **Kleihauer-Betke test:** detects fetal hemoglobin-containing RBCs in maternal blood to quantify fetomaternal hemorrhage volume; determines whether additional RhoGAM vials are needed beyond the standard 300 mcg dose\
  **Kleihauer-Betke试验:** 检测母体血液中含胎儿血红蛋白的红细胞以量化胎母出血量；确定是否需要超出标准300 mcg剂量的额外RhoGAM

- **Variant — anti-Kell and other alloantibodies:** Kell antigen (anti-K) causes fetal anemia by suppressing erythropoiesis (not just hemolysis); MCA Doppler essential because bilirubin-based amniocentesis underestimates severity\
  **题目变式——抗Kell及其他同种异体抗体:** Kell抗原（抗K）通过抑制红系造血（而非仅溶血）引起胎儿贫血；大脑中动脉多普勒至关重要，因胆红素羊水检查会低估严重程度

# Question 37 — Narcolepsy / 发作性睡病

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>22-year-old college student</strong> comes to the physician because of a <strong>3-year history of falling asleep during her classes</strong>; she worries that she will not be able to continue with her education because of this. She says that she <strong>always has had difficulty staying awake during class, even in high school</strong>. She also occasionally has trouble staying awake during movies. She says she has no problems getting to sleep or waking up. She goes to bed between midnight and 1 AM and gets up at 8 AM. She has <strong>tried sleeping for longer durations, even up to 8½ hours, but she still has been unable to stay awake during the day</strong>. She has the greatest difficulty staying awake during her classes after lunch. She thinks that she sleeps very soundly and moves little during sleep because <strong>her bedsheets are neat when she awakens</strong> in the morning. She <strong>does not remember having dreams</strong>. She reports that <strong>no one has ever told her that she snores</strong>. She is 170 cm (5 ft 5 in) tall and weighs 62 kg (136 lb); <strong>BMI is 21 kg/m²</strong>. Physical examination shows no abnormalities. On mental status examination, she has a concerned mood and a reactive affect. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in diagnosis?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Minnesota Multiphasic Personality Inventory<br />
B) Overnight pulse oximetry<br />
C) Pulmonary function tests<br />
D) MRI of the brain<br />
E) Multiple sleep latency tests</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>3-year history of falling asleep in class, since high school<br />
从高中起持续3年的课堂睡眠史</td>
<td>Chronic onset in adolescence points to an intrinsic sleep disorder, not acute illness or lifestyle change<br />
青春期起病的慢性病程提示内源性睡眠障碍，而非急性疾病或生活方式改变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Adequate sleep (7–8.5 hrs), still excessively sleepy<br />
睡眠充足（7–8.5小时），仍过度嗜睡</td>
<td>Rules out simple sleep deprivation; EDS despite sufficient sleep is the hallmark of narcolepsy<br />
排除单纯睡眠剥夺；充足睡眠后仍有EDS是发作性睡病的标志性特征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No snoring, normal BMI (21 kg/m²)<br />
无鼾声，BMI正常（21 kg/m²）</td>
<td>Strongly argues against OSA, which classically presents with snoring and obesity<br />
强烈反对OSA，OSA典型表现为打鼾加肥胖</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Neat bedsheets on waking<br />
醒来床单整洁</td>
<td>Minimal movement during sleep argues against REM sleep behavior disorder or periodic limb movements<br />
睡眠中移动极少，不支持REM睡眠行为障碍或周期性肢体运动障碍</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Does not remember having dreams<br />
不记得做梦</td>
<td>Paradoxically common in narcolepsy due to abnormal REM processing and sleep fragmentation<br />
由于REM处理异常和睡眠碎片化，在发作性睡病中矛盾性地常见</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Greatest difficulty staying awake after lunch<br />
午饭后最难保持清醒</td>
<td>Post-prandial dip exacerbates narcoleptic episodes; classic USMLE clue for daytime somnolence<br />
餐后困倦加剧发作性睡病发作；白天嗜睡的经典USMLE线索</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Narcolepsy** results from the selective loss of **orexin (hypocretin)**-producing neurons in the **lateral hypothalamus**, destabilizing the brain's sleep-wake "flip-flop switch":

**发作性睡病**源于**侧下丘脑**中产生**orexin（下丘脑分泌素）**的神经元选择性丧失，破坏了大脑睡眠-觉醒"触发器"的稳定性：

- Orexin-A and Orexin-B normally activate monoaminergic wake-promoting nuclei (locus coeruleus, raphe, tuberomammillary nucleus) to maintain stable wakefulness\
  Orexin-A和Orexin-B正常情况下激活单胺能觉醒核团（蓝斑、中缝核、结节乳头核）以维持稳定觉醒

- Without orexin, the mutual inhibition between wake and REM circuits breaks down, allowing sudden, unwanted transitions from wakefulness directly into REM sleep\
  缺乏orexin，觉醒与REM回路之间的相互抑制崩溃，导致从觉醒状态突然、非预期地直接过渡到REM睡眠

- These abnormal wakefulness→REM transitions manifest as cataplexy, sleep paralysis, hypnagogic hallucinations, and sleep-onset REM periods (SOREMPs) on MSLT\
  这些异常的觉醒→REM转换表现为猝倒、睡眠麻痹、入睡幻觉，以及MSLT上的睡眠起始REM期（SOREMPs）

- The condition is strongly associated with **HLA-DQB1\\06:02** (\>90% of type 1 cases), implicating autoimmune destruction of orexinergic neurons\
  该病与**HLA-DQB1\\06:02**强烈相关（\>90%的1型病例），涉及orexin能神经元的自身免疫性破坏

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Orexin neurons reside exclusively in the lateral hypothalamus — damage here removes the stabilizer from the entire sleep-wake cycle.

**解剖小窍门:** Orexin神经元仅位于侧下丘脑——此处受损相当于移除了整个睡眠-觉醒周期的稳定器。

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Multiple Sleep Latency Test / 正确答案 (E) — 多次睡眠潜伏期测试

**Multiple Sleep Latency Test (MSLT)** is the gold-standard diagnostic test for narcolepsy when cataplexy is absent, as in this patient:

**多次睡眠潜伏期测试（MSLT）**是无猝倒症状时发作性睡病的金标准诊断检查，如本例患者：

- Consists of 4–5 scheduled 20-minute nap opportunities spaced 2 hours apart during the day\
  由白天每隔2小时安排的4–5次20分钟小睡机会组成

- Narcolepsy is confirmed by mean sleep latency (MSL) ≤8 minutes AND ≥2 sleep-onset REM periods (SOREMPs)\
  发作性睡病通过平均睡眠潜伏期（MSL）≤8分钟且≥2次睡眠起始REM期（SOREMPs）确诊

- Must be preceded by overnight polysomnography (PSG) to rule out other sleep disorders and ensure adequate prior sleep\
  必须先行夜间多导睡眠图（PSG）以排除其他睡眠障碍并确认前夜睡眠充足

- If cataplexy is present, diagnosis can be made clinically without MSLT; if absent, MSLT is required\
  若存在猝倒，可无需MSLT临床诊断；若缺失，则需要MSLT

**Diagnosis:** Suspected narcolepsy type 2 (without cataplexy) — chronic EDS despite adequate sleep, normal BMI, absent snoring, and neat bedsheets all point here; MSLT is required to confirm.

**诊断:** 怀疑2型发作性睡病（无猝倒）——充足睡眠后仍有慢性EDS、BMI正常、无鼾声、床单整洁均指向此诊断；需MSLT确认。

**Treatment:** Modafinil or armodafinil for EDS (first-line, Schedule IV); sodium oxybate for EDS + cataplexy; scheduled daytime naps as adjunct lifestyle measure.

**治疗:** 莫达非尼或阿莫达非尼治疗EDS（一线，IV类管制药）；羟丁酸钠用于EDS+猝倒；计划性白天小睡作为辅助生活方式措施。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Minnesota Multiphasic Personality Inventory<br />
A — 明尼苏达多相人格量表</td>
<td>Screens for psychopathology; no psychiatric red flags here — affect is reactive and mood is appropriate concern; organic workup must precede psychiatric screening<br />
筛查精神病理；此处无精神科危险信号——情感是反应性的，情绪是适当的担忧；器质性检查必须先于精神科筛查</td>
<td>Psychiatric assessment is premature before ruling out a primary sleep disorder<br />
在排除原发性睡眠障碍之前进行精神科评估为时过早</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Overnight pulse oximetry<br />
B — 夜间脉搏血氧监测</td>
<td>Screens for OSA via nocturnal hypoxemia; absent snoring + normal BMI make OSA very unlikely; also misses narcolepsy entirely<br />
通过夜间低氧血症筛查OSA；无鼾声+BMI正常使OSA可能性极小；而且完全遗漏发作性睡病</td>
<td>MSLT (preceded by PSG) covers both OSA assessment and narcolepsy; oximetry alone is insufficient<br />
MSLT（先行PSG）同时涵盖OSA评估和发作性睡病；单独血氧监测不够</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Pulmonary function tests<br />
C — 肺功能检查</td>
<td>Evaluates airflow obstruction and lung volumes; no respiratory symptoms, no dyspnea, no wheeze — entirely irrelevant<br />
评估气流阻塞和肺容量；无呼吸道症状、无呼吸困难、无喘息——完全无关</td>
<td>Somnolence without any respiratory symptoms has no pulmonary basis to investigate<br />
无任何呼吸道症状的嗜睡没有肺部检查依据</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — MRI of the brain<br />
D — 脑部MRI</td>
<td>Appropriate later if MSLT/PSG are unrevealing, to look for hypothalamic or CNS lesions causing secondary narcolepsy; not the first step without focal neurological signs<br />
若MSLT/PSG无阳性发现，之后适合用于寻找继发性发作性睡病的下丘脑或CNS病变；无局灶性神经体征时不作为第一步</td>
<td>No focal deficits, no headache, no signs of mass effect — structural imaging is a step-2 workup here<br />
无局灶性缺损、无头痛、无占位效应迹象——结构影像学是此处的第二步检查</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Multiple sleep latency tests ✓<br />
E — 多次睡眠潜伏期测试 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — gold-standard for narcolepsy without cataplexy; demonstrates short sleep latency and SOREMPs confirming diagnosis<br />
正确——无猝倒发作性睡病的金标准；证实短睡眠潜伏期和SOREMPs以确诊</td>
<td>Directly targets the most likely diagnosis given EDS + adequate sleep + no snoring/obesity<br />
直接针对EDS+充足睡眠+无鼾声/肥胖情况下的最可能诊断</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is (B) overnight pulse oximetry — OSA can cause EDS, but the combination of absent snoring, normal BMI, and neat bedsheets makes OSA very unlikely; moreover, oximetry would miss narcolepsy entirely.*

最具迷惑性的干扰项是（B）夜间脉搏血氧监测——OSA确实可引起EDS，但无鼾声、BMI正常和床单整洁的组合使OSA可能性极小；而且血氧监测完全无法诊断发作性睡病。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Narcolepsy vs. Obstructive Sleep Apnea vs. Idiopathic Hypersomnia / 发作性睡病 vs. 阻塞性睡眠呼吸暂停 vs. 特发性嗜睡症

<th><strong>Narcolepsy</strong><br />
<strong>发作性睡病</strong></th>
<th><strong>Obstructive Sleep Apnea</strong><br />
<strong>阻塞性睡眠呼吸暂停</strong></th>

典型体型</td>

肥胖，颈粗（Mallampati升高）</td>

鼾声/呼吸暂停发作</td>

<tr>

MSLT结果</td>
<td>MSL ≤8 min + ≥2 SOREMPs<br />
MSL≤8分钟+≥2个SOREMPs</td>

MSL可能降低；0–1个SOREMP</td>

MSL≤8分钟；0–1个SOREMP；总睡眠延长</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>First-line treatment<br />
一线治疗</td>
<td>Modafinil; sodium oxybate (type 1)<br />
莫达非尼；羟丁酸钠（1型）</td>
<td>CPAP<br />
持续气道正压通气</td>

莫达非尼；克拉霉素（实验性）</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A young patient with chronic EDS despite adequate sleep, normal BMI, absent snoring, and neat bedsheets most likely has narcolepsy — confirmed by MSLT showing MSL ≤8 minutes and ≥2 SOREMPs.**

**一名年轻患者在充足睡眠后仍有慢性白天过度嗜睡、BMI正常、无鼾声、床单整洁，最可能患发作性睡病——由MSLT（MSL≤8分钟且≥2个SOREMPs）确诊。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — CHESS of Narcolepsy / 记忆钩 — 发作性睡病"CHESS"五联征:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>C</strong>ataplexy — sudden bilateral muscle atonia triggered by strong emotion; consciousness preserved / 猝倒——强烈情绪触发的突然双侧肌张力消失；意识保留<br />
• <strong>H</strong>ypnagogic/hypnopompic hallucinations — vivid dream-like perceptions at sleep onset or awakening / 入睡/觉醒幻觉——入睡或觉醒时生动的梦样感知<br />
• <strong>E</strong>xcessive daytime sleepiness — cardinal symptom present in ALL narcolepsy types despite adequate night sleep / 白天过度嗜睡——所有发作性睡病类型均存在的主要症状，即使夜间睡眠充足<br />
• <strong>S</strong>leep paralysis — brief inability to move or speak at sleep-wake transitions / 睡眠麻痹——睡眠-觉醒转换时短暂无法移动或说话<br />
• <strong>S</strong>OREMPs — ≥2 sleep-onset REM periods on MSLT = diagnostic criterion for narcolepsy type 2 / SOREMPs——MSLT上≥2次睡眠起始REM期 = 2型发作性睡病诊断标准</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Narcolepsy Diagnosis & Management / 高频知识表 — 发作性睡病的诊断与治疗

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Narcolepsy Type 1 vs. Type 2<br />
发作性睡病1型vs.2型</td>
<td>Type 1: EDS + cataplexy OR CSF orexin-A &lt;110 pg/mL; Type 2: EDS without cataplexy, normal orexin, diagnosed by MSLT<br />
1型：EDS+猝倒，或CSF orexin-A&lt;110 pg/mL；2型：无猝倒的EDS，orexin正常，由MSLT诊断</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>MSLT Protocol<br />
MSLT操作规程</td>
<td>4–5 naps × 20 min, 2 hrs apart; must be preceded by overnight PSG; positive: MSL ≤8 min AND ≥2 SOREMPs<br />
4–5次小睡×20分钟，间隔2小时；必须先行夜间PSG；阳性：MSL≤8分钟且≥2个SOREMPs</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Orexin Pathophysiology<br />
Orexin病理生理</td>
<td>Lateral hypothalamus neurons produce orexin-A and -B; stabilize wakefulness via locus coeruleus and raphe; lost in narcolepsy type 1 (autoimmune)<br />
侧下丘脑神经元产生orexin-A和-B；通过蓝斑和中缝核稳定觉醒；在1型发作性睡病中（自身免疫性）丧失</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>HLA Association<br />
HLA关联</td>
<td>&gt;90% of narcolepsy type 1 carries HLA-DQB1<em>06:02; strongest HLA–disease link in all of neurology/psychiatry&lt;br&gt;&gt;90%的1型发作性睡病携带HLA-DQB1</em>06:02；神经病学/精神病学中最强的HLA-疾病关联</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Cataplexy vs. Syncope vs. Seizure<br />
猝倒vs.晕厥vs.癫痫</td>
<td>Cataplexy: triggered by emotion, consciousness fully preserved, resolves in seconds-minutes, no postictal state; syncope: triggered by orthostasis/Valsalva; seizure: postictal confusion<br />
猝倒：由情绪触发，意识完全保留，数秒至数分钟内恢复，无发作后状态；晕厥：由体位性低血压/Valsalva触发；癫痫：有发作后意识混乱</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pharmacotherapy<br />
药物治疗</td>
<td>Modafinil/armodafinil: first-line EDS (Schedule IV); Sodium oxybate: EDS + cataplexy (Schedule I dispensed under REMS); Venlafaxine/SSRIs: cataplexy only; Amphetamines: second-line EDS<br />
莫达非尼/阿莫达非尼：EDS一线（IV类）；羟丁酸钠：EDS+猝倒（I类，REMS下配发）；文拉法辛/SSRI：仅用于猝倒；苯丙胺类：EDS二线</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>CSF Orexin-A Measurement<br />
CSF Orexin-A测量</td>
<td>Via lumbar puncture; level &lt;110 pg/mL or &lt;1/3 of mean normal is diagnostic for type 1; useful when MSLT is inconclusive or cannot be performed<br />
经腰椎穿刺；水平&lt;110 pg/mL或&lt;正常均值的1/3诊断1型；当MSLT不确定或无法进行时有用</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of chronic EDS in young adults:** Narcolepsy, idiopathic hypersomnia, delayed sleep phase syndrome, OSA (if obese/snoring), depression, hypothyroidism, and medication side effects (antihistamines, benzodiazepines)\
  **年轻成人慢性EDS鉴别诊断:** 发作性睡病、特发性嗜睡症、睡眠时相延迟综合征、OSA（若肥胖/打鼾）、抑郁症、甲状腺功能减退和药物副作用（抗组胺药、苯二氮䓬类）

- **Secondary narcolepsy:** Hypothalamic lesions (craniopharyngioma, MS plaques, Niemann-Pick type C, anti-Ma2 paraneoplastic) can destroy orexin neurons; MRI is appropriate if primary sleep workup is negative\
  **继发性发作性睡病:** 下丘脑病变（颅咽管瘤、MS斑块、C型尼曼-皮克病、抗Ma2副肿瘤综合征）可破坏orexin神经元；若原发性睡眠检查阴性，MRI是适当的后续检查

- **Pediatric/post-infectious narcolepsy:** Cases increased after 2009 H1N1 pandemic and Pandemrix vaccination in Europe, suggesting molecular mimicry targeting orexin neurons; onset commonly in adolescence\
  **儿童/感染后发作性睡病:** 2009年H1N1大流行和欧洲Pandemrix疫苗接种后病例增加，提示靶向orexin神经元的分子模拟；通常在青春期发病

- **Kleine-Levin Syndrome (KLS) vs. narcolepsy:** KLS presents with episodic hypersomnia (16–20 hrs/day) in adolescent males plus megaphagia and hypersexuality during attacks, with full normality between episodes — contrasts with narcolepsy's chronic, daily EDS\
  **Kleine-Levin综合征（KLS）vs.发作性睡病:** KLS表现为青春期男性发作性嗜睡（每天16–20小时）加发作期暴食和性欲亢进，发作间期完全正常——与发作性睡病的慢性每日EDS形成对比

# Question 38 — Lithium-Induced Hypothyroidism / 锂剂诱发的甲状腺功能减退症

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>38-year-old woman</strong> comes to the office because of a <strong>6-month history of progressive fatigue and muscle weakness</strong>. During this time, she has not been able to concentrate at work and has noticed that her <strong>voice has become hoarse</strong>. During the past 3 months, she has had a <strong>5.4-kg (12-lb) weight gain</strong> despite limiting her food intake. She has bipolar disorder, type 2 diabetes mellitus, and hypercholesterolemia. Her medications are metformin, lisinopril, <strong>lithium</strong>, and pravastatin. She does not smoke cigarettes, drink alcohol, or use illicit drugs. Her temperature is 37°C (98.6°F), <strong>pulse is 50/min</strong>, respirations are 14/min, and blood pressure is 130/90 mm Hg. Examination shows <strong>cold skin and coarse hair</strong> over the scalp. There is a <strong>firm, nontender, symmetrically enlarged thyroid gland</strong>. <strong>Deep tendon reflexes are 1+</strong>. Her serum thyroid-stimulating hormone concentration is <strong>25 μU/mL</strong>. Results of serum electrolyte concentrations and renal function tests are within the reference ranges. <strong>Antithyroid peroxidase antibody testing is negative</strong>.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most likely cause of these findings?</strong></p>
<p>A) Autoimmune thyroiditis<br />
B) Granulomatous infiltration<br />
C) Iodine deficiency<br />
D) Medication adverse effect<br />
E) Pituitary dysfunction</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: D</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Lithium in medication list<br />
药物列表中有锂剂</td>
<td>Lithium causes hypothyroidism and goiter in up to 50% of patients within 1–2 years of treatment<br />
锂剂在治疗1–2年内可导致高达50%的患者出现甲减和甲状腺肿</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>TSH 25 μU/mL (markedly elevated)<br />
TSH 25 μU/mL（显著升高）</td>
<td>Confirms primary hypothyroidism; elevated TSH indicates the thyroid gland is failing to respond to stimulation<br />
确认原发性甲减；TSH升高说明甲状腺无法对刺激做出应答</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Anti-TPO antibodies NEGATIVE<br />
抗甲状腺过氧化物酶抗体阴性</td>
<td>Rules out Hashimoto's thyroiditis (the most tempting distractor); points to a non-autoimmune etiology<br />
排除桥本甲状腺炎（最诱人的干扰选项）；指向非自身免疫性病因</td>

</tr>
<tr>

脉搏50次/分（心动过缓）</td>
<td>Hallmark of hypothyroidism; reduced metabolic rate slows cardiac conduction and heart rate<br />
甲减的标志性体征；代谢率降低导致心脏传导和心率减慢</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>5.4-kg weight gain despite limiting food intake<br />
限制饮食仍体重增加5.4千克</td>
<td>Pathognomonic of hypothyroidism: decreased basal metabolic rate leads to weight gain independent of caloric intake<br />
甲减的特征性表现：基础代谢率降低导致与热量摄入无关的体重增加</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Cold skin, coarse hair, DTR 1+ (hyporeflexia)<br />
皮肤发冷、头发粗糙、腱反射1+（反射减弱）</td>
<td>Triad of hypothyroid signs: peripheral vasoconstriction, myxedematous skin/hair changes, and delayed tendon reflex relaxation<br />
甲减三联体征：外周血管收缩、粘液性水肿皮肤/毛发改变、腱反射延迟松弛</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Lithium** interferes with thyroid function through multiple direct mechanisms, ultimately reducing **T3/T4 production and release** and triggering a compensatory rise in **TSH** that drives goiter formation:

**锂剂**通过多种直接机制干扰甲状腺功能，最终减少**T3/T4的合成和释放**，并触发**TSH**代偿性升高，驱动甲状腺肿形成：

- Lithium blocks iodine organification → tyrosine residues on thyroglobulin cannot be iodinated → less T3/T4 synthesized\
  锂剂阻断碘的有机化 → 甲状腺球蛋白上的酪氨酸残基无法碘化 → T3/T4 合成减少

- Lithium inhibits thyroglobulin proteolysis → stored thyroid hormone cannot be cleaved and released into circulation\
  锂剂抑制甲状腺球蛋白水解 → 储存的甲状腺激素无法被裂解释放入血

- Low circulating T4 → pituitary senses reduced negative feedback → TSH rises compensatorily\
  循环T4降低 → 垂体感知到负反馈减弱 → TSH代偿性升高

- Chronically elevated TSH drives thyroid cell proliferation → diffuse, symmetric, nonnodular goiter\
  长期TSH升高驱动甲状腺细胞增殖 → 弥漫性、对称性、无结节甲状腺肿

- Occurs in up to 50% of patients on lithium, typically within 1–2 years of initiation; does NOT require stopping lithium\
  发生于高达50%的锂剂治疗患者，通常在开始治疗后1–2年内出现；无需停用锂剂

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Lithium-induced goiter is always diffuse and nonnodular — a nodular or asymmetric thyroid in a lithium-treated patient should prompt ultrasound evaluation for alternative pathology.

**解剖小窍门:** 锂剂诱发的甲状腺肿始终是弥漫性无结节的——锂剂治疗患者出现结节性或不对称甲状腺时应行超声评估其他病理。

## 3. Correct Answer (D) — Medication Adverse Effect (Lithium) / 正确答案 (D) — 药物不良反应（锂剂）

**Lithium-induced hypothyroidism** is a direct pharmacologic effect of lithium on thyroid hormone synthesis and release, producing a primary hypothyroid state with elevated TSH, diffuse goiter, and absent autoimmune markers:

**锂剂诱发甲减**是锂剂对甲状腺激素合成和释放的直接药理学效应，产生原发性甲减状态，表现为TSH升高、弥漫性甲状腺肿和自身免疫标志物阴性：

- Classic hypothyroid symptoms: fatigue, weight gain, bradycardia, hoarseness, cold intolerance, hyporeflexia, coarse hair, cold skin\
  典型甲减症状：乏力、体重增加、心动过缓、声音嘶哑、怕冷、腱反射减弱、头发粗糙、皮肤发冷

- TSH elevated (primary hypothyroidism pattern); anti-TPO antibodies NEGATIVE (no autoimmune component — key differentiator from Hashimoto's)\
  TSH升高（原发性甲减模式）；抗TPO抗体阴性（无自身免疫成分——与桥本甲状腺炎的关键鉴别点）

- Lithium does NOT need to be discontinued; thyroid dysfunction is treated independently with levothyroxine\
  锂剂无需停用；甲状腺功能障碍用左甲状腺素单独治疗

**Diagnosis:** Primary hypothyroidism (TSH 25 μU/mL, diffuse goiter, classic symptoms) with negative anti-TPO antibodies in a patient on chronic lithium therapy — medication adverse effect is the most parsimonious explanation.

**诊断:** 长期锂剂治疗患者出现原发性甲减（TSH 25 μU/mL、弥漫性甲状腺肿、典型症状）且抗TPO抗体阴性——药物不良反应是最简洁的解释。

**Treatment:** Levothyroxine (T4 replacement) titrated to normalize TSH; lithium can be continued with appropriate thyroid hormone supplementation and monitoring.

**治疗:** 左甲状腺素（T4替代）滴定至TSH正常；在适当的甲状腺激素补充和监测下可继续使用锂剂。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Autoimmune thyroiditis<br />
A — 自身免疫性甲状腺炎</td>
<td>Identical clinical picture BUT anti-TPO (and anti-thyroglobulin) antibodies would be POSITIVE in Hashimoto's<br />
临床表现完全相同，但桥本甲状腺炎的抗TPO（和抗甲状腺球蛋白）抗体应为阳性</td>
<td>Anti-TPO NEGATIVE → autoimmune thyroiditis ruled out; lithium provides the alternative mechanism<br />
抗TPO阴性 → 排除自身免疫性甲状腺炎；锂剂提供了替代机制</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Granulomatous infiltration<br />
B — 肉芽肿性浸润</td>
<td>Subacute (de Quervain) thyroiditis presents with TENDER thyroid, preceding viral illness, and initial hyperthyroidism — opposite profile<br />
亚急性（德奎尔万）甲状腺炎表现为甲状腺压痛、前驱病毒感染史和初期甲亢——与本题相反</td>
<td>Thyroid is nontender; no viral prodrome; patient has hypothyroidism not hyperthyroidism<br />
甲状腺无压痛；无病毒前驱症状；患者为甲减而非甲亢</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Iodine deficiency<br />
C — 碘缺乏</td>
<td>Endemic goiter from iodine deficiency is rare in developed countries with iodized salt; no geographic context or dietary deficiency suggested<br />
碘盐普及的发达国家中碘缺乏引起的地方性甲状腺肿罕见；题目无相关地理背景或饮食缺乏提示</td>
<td>Lithium use is a far more specific and proximal cause given the clinical context<br />
结合临床背景，锂剂使用是更具特异性和直接性的病因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Medication adverse effect ✓<br />
D — 药物不良反应 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Lithium directly impairs thyroid hormone synthesis and release, causing hypothyroidism + goiter in up to 50% of patients; negative anti-TPO confirms non-autoimmune mechanism<br />
正确——锂剂直接损害甲状腺激素合成和释放，导致高达50%的患者出现甲减+甲状腺肿；抗TPO阴性确认为非自身免疫机制</td>
<td>Lithium on medication list + TSH ↑ + anti-TPO negative + diffuse nontender goiter = textbook lithium-induced hypothyroidism<br />
药物列表中有锂剂 + TSH升高 + 抗TPO阴性 + 弥漫性无压痛甲状腺肿 = 教科书式锂剂诱发甲减</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Pituitary dysfunction<br />
E — 垂体功能障碍</td>
<td>Pituitary failure causes secondary hypothyroidism with DECREASED or inappropriately normal TSH; this patient's TSH is 25 — the opposite<br />
垂体功能衰竭导致继发性甲减，TSH降低或不适当正常；该患者TSH为25，恰恰相反</td>
<td>TSH 25 μU/mL = primary (thyroid-level) failure; secondary hypothyroidism would show low TSH with low T4<br />
TSH 25 μU/mL = 原发性（甲状腺水平）衰竭；继发性甲减表现为TSH低且T4低</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most dangerous distractor is Choice A (Hashimoto's thyroiditis) — the hypothyroid clinical picture is identical, but the NEGATIVE anti-TPO antibody is the single decisive pivot that shifts the diagnosis from autoimmune to drug-induced thyroid dysfunction.*

最危险的干扰选项是A（桥本甲状腺炎）——甲减的临床表现完全相同，但抗TPO抗体阴性是唯一决定性转折点，将诊断从自身免疫性转向药物诱发性甲状腺功能障碍。

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A patient on lithium with classic hypothyroid features (high TSH, diffuse goiter, bradycardia, weight gain) and NEGATIVE anti-TPO antibodies has lithium-induced hypothyroidism, NOT Hashimoto's — lithium does not need to be stopped.**

**使用锂剂的患者出现典型甲减特征（TSH升高、弥漫性甲状腺肿、心动过缓、体重增加）且抗TPO抗体阴性，诊断为锂剂诱发甲减而非桥本甲状腺炎——无需停用锂剂。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — LITH for Lithium's Thyroid Effects / 记忆钩 — "LITH"记锂剂甲状腺效应:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>L</strong>ithium blocks iodine organification → less T3/T4 synthesized / 锂剂阻断碘有机化 → T3/T4 合成减少<br />
• <strong>I</strong>nhibits thyroglobulin proteolysis → stored hormone cannot be released / 抑制甲状腺球蛋白水解 → 储存激素无法释放<br />
• <strong>T</strong>SH rises compensatorily → diffuse, nontender, symmetric goiter forms / TSH代偿性升高 → 形成弥漫性、无压痛、对称性甲状腺肿<br />
• <strong>H</strong>ashimoto's ruled out by NEGATIVE anti-TPO — the single decisive clue! / 抗TPO阴性排除桥本甲状腺炎——唯一决定性线索！</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Lithium Adverse Effects and Thyroid Dysfunction / 高频知识表 — 锂剂不良反应与甲状腺功能障碍

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Prevalence of lithium thyroid dysfunction<br />
锂剂甲状腺功能障碍发生率</td>
<td>Up to 50% of lithium-treated patients develop thyroid dysfunction; hypothyroidism and goiter are most common; hyperthyroidism and autoimmune thyroiditis can also occur<br />
高达50%的锂剂治疗患者出现甲状腺功能障碍；甲减和甲状腺肿最常见；也可发生甲亢和自身免疫性甲状腺炎</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Mechanism of lithium-induced hypothyroidism<br />
锂剂诱发甲减的机制</td>
<td>Blocks iodine organification; inhibits thyroglobulin proteolysis (preventing hormone release); may impair TSH receptor signaling; net effect = ↓T3/T4, ↑TSH, goiter<br />
阻断碘有机化；抑制甲状腺球蛋白水解（阻止激素释放）；可能损害TSH受体信号；净效应 = T3/T4降低、TSH升高、甲状腺肿</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Other high-yield lithium adverse effects<br />
其他高频锂剂不良反应</td>
<td>Fine resting tremor; nephrogenic diabetes insipidus (NDI); nystagmus; leukocytosis; cardiac T-wave flattening/inversion; weight gain; teratogenicity (Ebstein anomaly)<br />
细颤；肾源性尿崩症（NDI）；眼球震颤；白细胞增多；心脏T波平坦/倒置；体重增加；致畸性（Ebstein畸形）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Baseline monitoring before lithium initiation<br />
开始锂剂治疗前的基线监测</td>
<td>Thyroid function tests (TFTs), renal function (BMP/CMP — lithium is renally cleared; renal failure → toxicity), ECG, electrolytes, CBC, pregnancy test<br />
甲状腺功能检查（TFT）、肾功能（锂经肾清除；肾衰竭→中毒）、心电图、电解质、全血细胞计数、妊娠试验</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Management of lithium-induced hypothyroidism<br />
锂剂诱发甲减的处理</td>
<td>Add levothyroxine — do NOT discontinue lithium; if lithium is stopped, hypothyroidism is reversible; monitor TSH every 6–12 months in all lithium-treated patients<br />
加用左甲状腺素——不要停用锂剂；若停用锂剂，甲减可逆；对所有锂剂治疗患者每6–12个月监测TSH</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Primary vs secondary hypothyroidism distinction<br />
原发性与继发性甲减的区别</td>
<td>Primary (thyroid fails): TSH HIGH + T4 low; Secondary (pituitary fails): TSH LOW or inappropriately normal + T4 low; this patient's TSH 25 = primary<br />
原发性（甲状腺衰竭）：TSH升高+T4降低；继发性（垂体衰竭）：TSH降低或不适当正常+T4降低；该患者TSH 25 = 原发性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Lithium toxicity vs therapeutic side effects<br />
锂剂中毒与治疗剂量不良反应</td>
<td>Toxicity (level &gt;1.5 mEq/L): coarse tremor, ataxia, confusion, seizures, cardiac arrhythmia; Therapeutic side effects (normal levels): fine tremor, NDI, thyroid dysfunction, weight gain<br />
中毒（血药浓度&gt;1.5 mEq/L）：粗大震颤、共济失调、意识混乱、癫痫发作、心律失常；治疗剂量不良反应（正常血药浓度）：细颤、NDI、甲状腺功能障碍、体重增加</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Drug interactions that raise lithium levels<br />
升高锂剂血药浓度的药物相互作用</td>
<td>NSAIDs, thiazide diuretics, and ACE inhibitors (like lisinopril in this patient) all reduce renal lithium clearance → lithium accumulation → toxicity risk<br />
NSAIDs、噻嗪类利尿剂和ACEI（如本患者服用的赖诺普利）均降低肾脏锂清除率→锂蓄积→中毒风险</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Lithium and NDI (nephrogenic diabetes insipidus):** Lithium blocks aquaporin-2 (AQP2) channels in the collecting duct, rendering the kidney unable to concentrate urine despite ADH → polyuria and polydipsia; treated with amiloride (potassium-sparing diuretic that reduces lithium uptake in collecting duct) — NOT thiazides\
  **锂剂与肾源性尿崩症:** 锂剂阻断集合管中的水通道蛋白2（AQP2），使肾脏尽管有ADH仍无法浓缩尿液 → 多尿和多饮；用阿米洛利（减少锂在集合管摄取的保钾利尿剂）治疗——不用噻嗪类

- **Ebstein anomaly and lithium teratogenicity:** First-trimester lithium exposure is associated with Ebstein anomaly (apical displacement of tricuspid valve); the risk is lower than historically reported but remains a counseling point for women of childbearing age on lithium\
  **Ebstein畸形与锂剂致畸性:** 妊娠早期锂剂暴露与Ebstein畸形（三尖瓣心尖移位）相关；风险低于历史报道但仍是育龄期女性使用锂剂的咨询要点

- **Drug interactions in this case:** This patient is on lisinopril (ACE inhibitor), which reduces renal lithium clearance and can raise lithium levels toward toxicity — a clinically important co-prescription to flag and monitor\
  **本题药物相互作用:** 该患者服用赖诺普利（ACEI），可降低肾脏锂清除率并使锂浓度升至中毒水平——是需要标注和监测的临床重要联合用药

- **Variant — lithium triggering autoimmune thyroiditis:** In predisposed patients, lithium can precipitate true autoimmune (Hashimoto's) thyroiditis, in which case anti-TPO antibodies WOULD be positive; the negative anti-TPO in this question specifically points to pure drug-effect, not autoimmune triggering\
  **题目变式——锂剂触发自身免疫性甲状腺炎:** 在易感患者中，锂剂可诱发真正的自身免疫性（桥本）甲状腺炎，此时抗TPO抗体会为阳性；本题抗TPO阴性特别指向纯药物效应，而非自身免疫触发

# Question 39 — Anaphylactic Reaction / 过敏性休克（速发型超敏反应）

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>27-year-old man</strong> comes to the emergency department because of a <strong>progressive rash and wheezing</strong>. Yesterday, the patient received the diagnosis of cellulitis of his right leg, and <strong>cephalexin therapy was begun</strong>. He has a history of <strong>mild, intermittent asthma and eczema</strong>. His only other medication is inhaled albuterol as needed. He had a <strong>mild allergic reaction to ampicillin as a child</strong>. He is in moderate distress. His temperature is 37°C (98.6°F), <strong>pulse is 118/min</strong>, respirations are 22/min, and <strong>blood pressure is 90/60 mm Hg</strong>. Examination shows a 3 x 3-cm, erythematous, warm, tender rash on the right leg that is unchanged from yesterday. There are <strong>new, raised, 1 x 2-cm pruritic lesions on the upper and lower extremities and trunk</strong>. <strong>Diffuse, scattered inspiratory and expiratory wheezes are heard bilaterally</strong>. Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most likely diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Anaphylactic reaction<br />
B) Rocky Mountain spotted fever<br />
C) Staphylococcal scalded skin syndrome<br />
D) Toxic shock syndrome<br />
E) Urticarial vasculitis</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: A</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Cephalexin started yesterday<br />
昨日开始使用头孢氨苄</td>
<td>New drug exposure is the most common trigger for anaphylaxis; temporal link is critical<br />
新药暴露是过敏性休克最常见诱因；时间相关性是确诊关键</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Prior allergic reaction to ampicillin<br />
童年时对氨苄西林有轻度过敏反应</td>
<td>Both ampicillin and cephalexin are beta-lactams; cross-reactivity raises anaphylaxis risk significantly<br />
氨苄西林与头孢氨苄同属 β-内酰胺类；交叉反应性显著增加过敏风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>History of asthma and eczema (atopy)<br />
哮喘与湿疹病史（特应性体质）</td>
<td>Atopic individuals have heightened IgE-mediated responses; atopy is a major risk factor for anaphylaxis<br />
特应性体质患者 IgE 介导反应增强；是过敏性休克的重要危险因素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>New urticarial lesions on extremities and trunk<br />
四肢及躯干出现新发荨麻疹样皮损</td>
<td>Urticaria is the hallmark cutaneous manifestation of IgE-mediated mast cell degranulation<br />
荨麻疹是 IgE 介导的肥大细胞脱颗粒的典型皮肤表现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Diffuse bilateral inspiratory and expiratory wheezes<br />
双侧弥漫性吸气和呼气期哮鸣音</td>
<td>Bronchospasm from histamine release indicates respiratory system involvement, a hallmark of anaphylaxis<br />
组胺释放引起的支气管痉挛提示呼吸系统受累，是过敏性休克的标志性表现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Tachycardia (118/min) + hypotension (90/60 mmHg)<br />
心动过速（118/min）+ 低血压（90/60 mmHg）</td>
<td>Cardiovascular collapse from profound vasodilation defines severe anaphylaxis; distinguishes it from mild allergic reaction<br />
严重血管扩张导致心血管虚脱，是重度过敏性休克的定义性特征，区别于轻度过敏反应</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Anaphylaxis** is a systemic, **IgE-mediated** type I hypersensitivity reaction triggered by **re-exposure to a sensitizing antigen** (here, a beta-lactam antibiotic):

**过敏性休克**是一种全身性、**IgE 介导**的 I 型超敏反应，由**再次接触致敏抗原**（本例为 β-内酰胺类抗生素）触发：

- Prior ampicillin exposure sensitized the immune system → IgE antibodies were produced and bound to mast cells and basophils\
  既往氨苄西林暴露使免疫系统致敏 → 产生 IgE 抗体并结合于肥大细胞和嗜碱性粒细胞表面

- Cephalexin (cross-reactive beta-lactam) re-exposure → antigen cross-links IgE on mast cells → massive degranulation → release of histamine, tryptase, leukotrienes, prostaglandins\
  头孢氨苄（交叉反应性 β-内酰胺类）再次暴露 → 抗原交联肥大细胞表面 IgE → 大规模脱颗粒 → 释放组胺、类胰蛋白酶、白三烯、前列腺素

- Histamine H1 activation → vasodilation + increased vascular permeability → urticaria, angioedema, hypotension; bronchoconstriction → wheezing\
  组胺 H1 激活 → 血管扩张 + 血管通透性增加 → 荨麻疹、血管性水肿、低血压；支气管收缩 → 哮鸣

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Anaphylaxis affects at least 2 organ systems simultaneously — skin (urticaria), respiratory (bronchospasm), and/or cardiovascular (hypotension/tachycardia).

**解剖小窍门:** 过敏性休克同时累及至少 2 个器官系统——皮肤（荨麻疹）、呼吸（支气管痉挛）和/或心血管（低血压/心动过速）。

## 3. Correct Answer (A) — Anaphylactic Reaction / 正确答案 (A) — 过敏性休克

**Anaphylaxis** is a rapidly progressive, life-threatening systemic hypersensitivity reaction requiring immediate recognition and treatment:

**过敏性休克**是一种快速进展、危及生命的全身性超敏反应，需要立即识别和处理：

- Multisystem involvement: skin (urticaria/angioedema), respiratory (bronchospasm/stridor), cardiovascular (hypotension/tachycardia), GI (nausea/vomiting)\
  多系统受累：皮肤（荨麻疹/血管性水肿）、呼吸（支气管痉挛/喘鸣）、心血管（低血压/心动过速）、消化（恶心/呕吐）

- Onset typically within 30–60 minutes of allergen exposure; IgE-mediated reactions are faster than non-IgE\
  通常在接触变应原后 30–60 分钟内发病；IgE 介导反应比非 IgE 介导反应更迅速

- Risk factors: atopy (asthma, eczema, allergic rhinitis), prior drug allergies, repeated allergen exposures\
  危险因素：特应性体质（哮喘、湿疹、过敏性鼻炎）、既往药物过敏史、反复接触变应原

- Beta-lactam cross-reactivity: penicillins and cephalosporins share the beta-lactam ring; cross-reactivity is ~1–2% but higher with shared R1 side chains\
  β-内酰胺类交叉反应：青霉素类与头孢菌素类共享 β-内酰胺环；交叉反应率约 1–2%，共享 R1 侧链时更高

**Diagnosis:** Clinical diagnosis based on acute onset of multisystem involvement after allergen exposure; serum tryptase can confirm mast cell degranulation retrospectively.

**诊断:** 基于变应原暴露后急性多系统受累的临床诊断；血清类胰蛋白酶可在事后确认肥大细胞脱颗粒。

**Treatment:** IM epinephrine (1:1000, 0.3–0.5 mg in lateral thigh) is first-line; adjuncts include antihistamines (H1 + H2 blockers), systemic corticosteroids, bronchodilators, and IV fluids for hypotension.

**治疗:** 肌注肾上腺素（1:1000，大腿外侧 0.3–0.5 mg）为首选；辅助治疗包括抗组胺药（H1 + H2 阻断剂）、全身性糖皮质激素、支气管扩张剂，以及低血压时补充静脉液体。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Anaphylactic reaction ✓<br />
A — 过敏性休克 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — drug-triggered IgE-mediated multisystem reaction with urticaria, bronchospasm, hypotension, tachycardia<br />
正确——药物触发的 IgE 介导多系统反应，伴荨麻疹、支气管痉挛、低血压、心动过速</td>
<td>New beta-lactam + prior penicillin allergy + atopy + acute multisystem collapse<br />
新用 β-内酰胺类 + 既往青霉素过敏 + 特应性体质 + 急性多系统虚脱</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Rocky Mountain spotted fever<br />
B — 落基山斑疹热</td>
<td>Caused by Rickettsia rickettsii via tick bite; rash is petechial/maculopapular (not urticarial), no wheezing; onset 2–14 days post-bite with fever and headache<br />
由立克次体经蜱叮咬传播；皮疹为淤点/斑丘疹（非荨麻疹），无哮鸣音；叮咬后 2–14 天发病，伴发热和头痛</td>
<td>No tick exposure; urticaria + bronchospasm do not fit RMSF<br />
无蜱叮咬史；荨麻疹 + 支气管痉挛不符合落基山斑疹热</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Staphylococcal scalded skin syndrome<br />
C — 葡萄球菌烫伤样皮肤综合征</td>
<td>Caused by S. aureus exotoxin (exfoliatin); presents with diffuse erythema → desquamation (not urticaria), fever, and Nikolsky sign; primarily in children and immunosuppressed adults; no wheezing<br />
由金黄色葡萄球菌外毒素（表皮剥脱素）引起；表现为弥漫性红斑 → 脱皮（非荨麻疹），伴发热和尼科尔斯基征；主要见于儿童和免疫抑制成人；无哮鸣音</td>
<td>Desquamation vs. urticaria; no bronchospasm; Nikolsky sign absent here<br />
脱皮 vs. 荨麻疹；无支气管痉挛；此患者无尼科尔斯基征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Toxic shock syndrome<br />
D — 中毒性休克综合征</td>
<td>Also S. aureus exotoxin (TSST-1); classic triad is fever + diffuse macular erythroderma (not urticaria) + desquamation + multiorgan failure; does not cause bronchospasm or urticaria; associated with tampon use/wound infection<br />
同为金黄色葡萄球菌外毒素（TSST-1）；经典三联征为发热 + 弥漫性斑状红皮症（非荨麻疹）+ 脱皮 + 多器官衰竭；不引起支气管痉挛或荨麻疹；与卫生棉条使用/伤口感染相关</td>
<td>No fever; urticaria + wheezing not part of TSS; no tampon/wound source identified<br />
无发热；荨麻疹 + 哮鸣不属于 TSS；无卫生棉条/伤口来源</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Urticarial vasculitis<br />
E — 荨麻疹性血管炎</td>
<td>Rare small-vessel vasculitis with chronic, recurrent urticaria (lesions last &gt;24h, leave bruising), arthralgias, hematuria, and proteinuria; more common in middle-aged women; does NOT cause acute hemodynamic instability<br />
罕见小血管血管炎，伴慢性复发性荨麻疹（皮损持续 &gt;24 小时、留有瘀斑）、关节痛、血尿、蛋白尿；更常见于中年女性；不引起急性血流动力学不稳定</td>
<td>Acute onset + hemodynamic instability + drug exposure points to anaphylaxis, not vasculitis<br />
急性起病 + 血流动力学不稳定 + 药物暴露指向过敏性休克而非血管炎</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Choice E (urticarial vasculitis) because it shares urticaria; the key distinguisher is the acute hemodynamic collapse and bronchospasm within 24 hours of a new drug — features exclusive to anaphylaxis.*

选项 E（荨麻疹性血管炎）是最具迷惑性的干扰项，因为两者均有荨麻疹；关键鉴别点在于新用药物后 24 小时内急性血流动力学虚脱和支气管痉挛——这是过敏性休克的专有特征。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Anaphylaxis vs. Other Acute Drug/Infectious Reactions / 过敏性休克 vs. 其他急性药物/感染性反应
