<strong>中毒性休克综合征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Urticarial Vasculitis</strong><br />
<strong>荨麻疹性血管炎</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Mechanism<br />
机制</td>
<td>IgE-mediated mast cell degranulation<br />
IgE 介导的肥大细胞脱颗粒</td>
<td>Bacterial superantigen (TSST-1)<br />
细菌超抗原（TSST-1）</td>
<td>Small-vessel immune complex deposition<br />
小血管免疫复合物沉积</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Onset<br />
起病</td>
<td>Minutes to hours after allergen<br />
接触变应原后数分钟至数小时</td>
<td>Days (after infection)<br />
数天（感染后）</td>
<td>Days to weeks (chronic/recurrent)<br />
数天至数周（慢性/复发）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Skin lesion<br />
皮肤病变</td>
<td>Urticaria + angioedema<br />
荨麻疹 + 血管性水肿</td>
<td>Diffuse erythroderma → desquamation<br />
弥漫性红皮症 → 脱皮</td>
<td>Urticaria lasting &gt;24h, leaves bruising<br />
荨麻疹持续 &gt;24 小时，留有瘀斑</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Respiratory<br />
呼吸系统</td>
<td>Bronchospasm (wheezing, stridor)<br />
支气管痉挛（哮鸣、喘鸣）</td>
<td>Absent<br />
无</td>
<td>Cough, hemoptysis (rare)<br />
咳嗽、咯血（罕见）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hemodynamics<br />
血流动力学</td>
<td>Hypotension + tachycardia (vasodilation)<br />
低血压 + 心动过速（血管扩张）</td>
<td>Hypotension + tachycardia (cytokine storm)<br />
低血压 + 心动过速（细胞因子风暴）</td>
<td>Typically stable<br />
通常稳定</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Fever<br />
发热</td>
<td>Absent (afebrile)<br />
无（体温正常）</td>
<td>High fever (&gt;38.9°C)<br />
高热（&gt;38.9°C）</td>
<td>Variable, low-grade<br />
可变，低热</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment<br />
治疗</td>
<td>IM epinephrine (first-line)<br />
肌注肾上腺素（一线）</td>
<td>Antibiotics + supportive care<br />
抗生素 + 支持治疗</td>
<td>NSAIDs, hydroxychloroquine<br />
NSAIDs、羟氯喹</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A patient with atopy and prior beta-lactam allergy who develops urticaria, bronchospasm, tachycardia, and hypotension shortly after starting a new cephalosporin has anaphylaxis — treat immediately with IM epinephrine.**

**有特应性体质和既往 β-内酰胺类过敏史的患者，开始使用新头孢菌素后不久出现荨麻疹、支气管痉挛、心动过速和低血压，诊断为过敏性休克——立即肌注肾上腺素治疗。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — URTICA for Anaphylaxis Features / 记忆钩 — "URTICA" 记忆过敏性休克特征:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>U</strong>rticaria — hives, the cardinal skin sign / 荨麻疹——皮肤的主要表现<br />
• <strong>R</strong>espiratory bronchospasm — wheezing/stridor / 呼吸性支气管痉挛——哮鸣/喘鸣<br />
• <strong>T</strong>achycardia — compensatory response to vasodilation / 心动过速——血管扩张的代偿反应<br />
• <strong>I</strong>gE-mediated — must have prior sensitization / IgE 介导——必须有既往致敏<br />
• <strong>C</strong>ollapse (hypotension) — profound vasodilation / 循环虚脱（低血压）——严重血管扩张<br />
• <strong>A</strong>drenaline (epinephrine) — first-line treatment, no exceptions / 肾上腺素——一线治疗，无例外</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Anaphylaxis Recognition and Management / 高频知识表 — 过敏性休克的识别与处理

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Diagnostic criteria<br />
诊断标准</td>
<td>Anaphylaxis is likely when: (1) acute skin/mucosal symptoms + respiratory/cardiovascular compromise; OR (2) ≥2 systems involved after allergen exposure; OR (3) hypotension alone after known allergen<br />
满足以下任一：(1) 急性皮肤/黏膜症状 + 呼吸/心血管受损；(2) 变应原暴露后 ≥2 系统受累；(3) 已知变应原暴露后单独出现低血压</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>First-line treatment<br />
一线治疗</td>
<td>Epinephrine 0.3–0.5 mg IM (1:1000) into the anterolateral thigh — do NOT delay for antihistamines or steroids first<br />
肾上腺素 0.3–0.5 mg 肌注（1:1000）于大腿前外侧——不要先用抗组胺药或激素而延误治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Beta-lactam cross-reactivity<br />
β-内酰胺类交叉反应</td>
<td>True cross-reactivity between penicillins and cephalosporins is ~1–2%; risk is higher with shared R1 side chains (e.g., amoxicillin/cefadroxil); history of severe penicillin reaction warrants avoidance of cephalosporins<br />
青霉素类与头孢菌素类真实交叉反应率约 1–2%；共享 R1 侧链时（如阿莫西林/头孢羟氨苄）风险更高；严重青霉素反应史建议避免使用头孢菌素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Atopy as risk factor<br />
特应性体质作为危险因素</td>
<td>Asthma, eczema, allergic rhinitis increase risk of anaphylaxis AND increase risk of fatal anaphylaxis (especially asthma → bronchospasm is harder to reverse)<br />
哮喘、湿疹、过敏性鼻炎增加过敏性休克风险，也增加致死性过敏性休克风险（尤其哮喘→支气管痉挛更难逆转）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Biphasic anaphylaxis<br />
双相过敏性休克</td>
<td>Recurrence of symptoms 1–72 hours after apparent resolution (without re-exposure); occurs in ~20% of cases; reason to observe patients ≥4–6 hours after epinephrine<br />
明显缓解后 1–72 小时症状复发（无再次暴露）；发生率约 20%；这是肾上腺素治疗后需观察 ≥4–6 小时的原因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Serum tryptase<br />
血清类胰蛋白酶</td>
<td>Peaks 1–2 hours after anaphylaxis onset, returns to baseline by 24 hours; useful for confirming mast cell activation retrospectively; useful when diagnosis is uncertain<br />
过敏性休克发作后 1–2 小时达峰，24 小时内恢复基线；可用于事后确认肥大细胞激活；诊断不确定时有用</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of drug hypersensitivity reactions:** Anaphylaxis (IgE, immediate) vs. serum sickness (immune complex, 7–21 days: fever, urticaria, arthralgias) vs. DRESS syndrome (T-cell, 2–8 weeks: rash, eosinophilia, organ involvement)\
  **药物超敏反应鉴别:** 过敏性休克（IgE，即刻型）vs. 血清病（免疫复合物，7–21 天：发热、荨麻疹、关节痛）vs. DRESS 综合征（T 细胞介导，2–8 周：皮疹、嗜酸性粒细胞增多、器官受累）

- **Variant — anaphylactoid reaction:** Clinically identical to anaphylaxis but NOT IgE-mediated (e.g., radiocontrast media, NSAIDs, opioids cause direct mast cell degranulation); treatment is identical — epinephrine first\
  **题目变式——类过敏反应:** 临床表现与过敏性休克相同，但非 IgE 介导（如造影剂、NSAIDs、阿片类药物直接引起肥大细胞脱颗粒）；治疗相同——首选肾上腺素

- **Key complication — refractory anaphylaxis in beta-blocker users:** Beta-blockers blunt epinephrine response; use glucagon IV (bypasses beta-receptor) as rescue therapy; always note beta-blocker use in anaphylaxis patients\
  **重要并发症——β 受体阻断剂使用者的难治性过敏性休克:** β 受体阻断剂削弱肾上腺素的反应；静脉使用胰高血糖素（绕过 β 受体）作为救援治疗；过敏性休克患者中务必关注 β 受体阻断剂使用情况

- **Risk factor — epinephrine auto-injector discharge planning:** Patients with anaphylaxis should be discharged with an epinephrine auto-injector (EpiPen), allergy referral, and education on avoiding the offending agent\
  **危险因素——肾上腺素自动注射器的出院计划:** 过敏性休克患者出院时应配备肾上腺素自动注射器（EpiPen）、转介过敏科，并教育患者避免接触致敏物质

# Question 40 — Enterohemorrhagic E. coli O157:H7 Infection / 肠出血性大肠杆菌 O157:H7 感染

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>37-year-old man</strong> comes to the physician because he has had <strong>two bowel movements containing bright red blood</strong> during the past 6 hours. He has a <strong>3-day history of intermittent severe abdominal cramps</strong> and <strong>diarrhea</strong>. He has had <strong>five loose stools daily</strong> during this period. He has no history of serious illness and <strong>takes no medications</strong>. His last visit to a physician was 5 years ago. His most recent travel experience was a trip to Canada 6 months ago. His temperature is 37°C (98.6°F), pulse is 98/min, and blood pressure is 126/78 mm Hg. Abdominal examination shows <strong>diffuse severe tenderness</strong> with no peritoneal signs. Bowel sounds are increased. Rectal examination shows no abnormalities. There is no stool in the rectal vault. His hemoglobin concentration is 13 g/dL, <strong>leukocyte count is 12,300/mm³</strong>, and platelet count is 302,000/mm³.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most likely causal organism?</strong></p>
<p>A) Clostridium difficile<br />
B) Clostridium perfringens<br />
C) Cryptosporidium parvum<br />
D) Enterotoxigenic Escherichia coli<br />
E) Escherichia coli O157:H7</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Bright red blood in stool<br />
鲜血便</td>
<td>Indicates hemorrhagic colitis, not watery diarrhea — points away from enterotoxigenic organisms<br />
提示出血性结肠炎而非水样泻——排除产肠毒素菌株</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Severe abdominal cramps + 5 loose stools/day for 3 days<br />
重度腹绞痛 + 每日 5 次稀便持续 3 天</td>
<td>Acute infectious colitis timeline; severity suggests invasive or toxin-producing organism<br />
急性感染性结肠炎时间线；严重程度提示侵袭性或产毒素病原体</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No medications (no prior antibiotics)<br />
未服用任何药物（无抗生素使用史）</td>
<td>Rules out C. difficile — requires prior antibiotic disruption of normal flora<br />
排除艰难梭菌——其发病需要抗生素破坏正常菌群</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Leukocytosis (WBC 12,300/mm³)<br />
白细胞增多（12,300/mm³）</td>
<td>Suggests bacterial etiology rather than viral or parasitic infection<br />
提示细菌性病原，而非病毒或寄生虫感染</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Afebrile (temperature 37°C)<br />
无发热（体温 37°C）</td>
<td>EHEC classically presents without high fever despite bloody diarrhea — distinguishes it from Shigella/Salmonella<br />
EHEC 经典表现为无高热，尽管有血便——与志贺菌/沙门菌相区别</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Diffuse severe tenderness, no peritoneal signs<br />
弥漫性重度压痛，无腹膜刺激征</td>
<td>Colitis without perforation — consistent with EHEC hemorrhagic colitis<br />
结肠炎未穿孔——符合 EHEC 出血性结肠炎表现</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Escherichia coli O157:H7** is an **enterohemorrhagic E. coli (EHEC)** strain that produces **Shiga toxin (Stx)**, which binds to **Gb3 receptors** on intestinal epithelial and endothelial cells, triggering massive cytotoxicity:

**大肠杆菌 O157:H7** 是一种**肠出血性大肠杆菌（EHEC）**菌株，产生 **Shiga 毒素（Stx）**，与肠道上皮细胞和内皮细胞上的 **Gb3 受体**结合，引发大规模细胞毒性反应：

- Shiga toxin cleaves the 28S rRNA of the 60S ribosomal subunit → inhibits protein synthesis → cell death\
  Shiga 毒素切割 60S 核糖体亚基的 28S rRNA→抑制蛋白质合成→细胞死亡

- Intestinal wall destruction → loss of mucosal integrity → bloody diarrhea (hemorrhagic colitis)\
  肠壁破坏→黏膜完整性丧失→血便（出血性结肠炎）

- Toxin absorbed into bloodstream → systemic endothelial damage → risk of Hemolytic Uremic Syndrome (HUS)\
  毒素吸收入血→全身内皮损伤→溶血性尿毒症综合征（HUS）风险

**Pathogen rule of thumb:** EHEC causes bloody diarrhea WITHOUT high fever — afebrile bloody stool in a healthy patient with no antibiotic history is the classic EHEC fingerprint.

**病原体小窍门:** EHEC 引起血便但**无高热**——健康患者出现无发热 + 血便 + 无抗生素使用史是 EHEC 的经典指纹特征。

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Escherichia coli O157:H7 / 正确答案 (E) — 大肠杆菌 O157:H7

**Enterohemorrhagic E. coli O157:H7 (EHEC)** is the leading cause of hemorrhagic colitis in developed countries, most commonly transmitted via undercooked beef, unpasteurized dairy, or contaminated produce:

**肠出血性大肠杆菌 O157:H7（EHEC）** 是发达国家出血性结肠炎的主要病原体，最常通过未熟透的牛肉、未经巴氏消毒的乳制品或受污染农产品传播：

- Produces Shiga toxin (Stx1 and/or Stx2) → hemorrhagic colitis with bright red bloody diarrhea\
  产生 Shiga 毒素（Stx1 和/或 Stx2）→出血性结肠炎伴鲜红色血便

- Classically afebrile or low-grade fever despite severe bloody diarrhea\
  典型表现为无发热或低热，尽管有严重血便

- Incubation period 3–4 days; illness lasts 5–10 days; HUS develops ~1 week after diarrhea onset\
  潜伏期 3–4 天；病程 5–10 天；HUS 约在腹泻发病后 1 周出现

**Diagnosis:** Stool culture on sorbitol-MacConkey agar (EHEC does NOT ferment sorbitol → colorless colonies); confirmed by Shiga toxin ELISA or PCR

**诊断:** 山梨醇 MacConkey 培养基粪便培养（EHEC 不发酵山梨醇→无色菌落）；Shiga 毒素 ELISA 或 PCR 确认

**Treatment:** Supportive care (oral/IV hydration); AVOID antibiotics — lysis releases more Shiga toxin and substantially increases HUS risk; avoid antiperistaltics (loperamide)

**治疗:** 支持治疗（口服/静脉补液）；**禁用抗生素**——细菌溶解会释放更多 Shiga 毒素，显著增加 HUS 风险；禁用止蠕动药物（洛哌丁胺）

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Clostridium difficile<br />
A — 艰难梭菌</td>
<td>Requires prior antibiotic use or hospitalization to disrupt flora; causes watery (not bloody) diarrhea in most cases<br />
需要既往抗生素使用或住院史破坏菌群；通常引起水样泻而非血便</td>
<td>No antibiotic history; bloody stool not typical for C. diff<br />
无抗生素使用史；血便非艰难梭菌典型表现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Clostridium perfringens<br />
B — 产气荚膜梭菌</td>
<td>Enterotoxin from contaminated food causes watery diarrhea (8–24 hr self-limited); does NOT cause bloody diarrhea; separately causes gas gangrene after trauma<br />
受污染食物中的肠毒素引起水样泻（8–24 小时自限性）；不引起血便；外伤后可引起气性坏疽</td>
<td>Short, self-limited watery diarrhea; no bloody component<br />
短暂、自限性水样泻；无血便成分</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Cryptosporidium parvum<br />
C — 微小隐孢子虫</td>
<td>Parasitic infection causing profuse watery diarrhea; primarily affects immunocompromised patients (HIV/AIDS); does NOT cause bloody diarrhea<br />
寄生虫感染引起大量水样泻；主要影响免疫功能低下患者（HIV/AIDS）；不引起血便</td>
<td>Immunocompromised host; watery not bloody; no leukocytosis<br />
免疫低下宿主；水样泻而非血便；通常无白细胞增多</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Enterotoxigenic Escherichia coli<br />
D — 产肠毒素大肠杆菌</td>
<td>ETEC produces heat-labile (LT) and heat-stable (ST) enterotoxins → watery "traveler's diarrhea"; does NOT produce Shiga toxin; does NOT cause bloody diarrhea<br />
ETEC 产热敏感（LT）和热稳定（ST）肠毒素→水样"旅行者腹泻"；不产 Shiga 毒素；不引起血便</td>
<td>Watery secretory diarrhea; traveler's diarrhea context; no blood<br />
水样分泌性腹泻；旅行者腹泻背景；无血便</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Escherichia coli O157:H7 ✓<br />
E — 大肠杆菌 O157:H7 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — EHEC produces Shiga toxin → hemorrhagic colitis with bloody diarrhea, leukocytosis, and afebrile presentation in a patient with no antibiotic history<br />
正确——EHEC 产 Shiga 毒素→出血性结肠炎，表现为血便、白细胞增多、无发热，且患者无抗生素使用史</td>
<td>Bloody diarrhea + afebrile + leukocytosis + no antibiotic history<br />
血便 + 无发热 + 白细胞增多 + 无抗生素使用史</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The trickiest distractor is Choice D (ETEC) — both are E. coli strains and both cause diarrhea, but ETEC produces LT/ST enterotoxins causing watery secretory diarrhea, while EHEC uses Shiga toxin to destroy the mucosal wall, causing bloody diarrhea — the presence of blood is the pivotal differentiator.*

最常见的干扰项是选项 D（ETEC）——两者同为大肠杆菌且均引起腹泻，但 ETEC 通过 LT/ST 肠毒素引起水样分泌性腹泻，而 EHEC 通过 Shiga 毒素破坏黏膜壁引起血便——是否出血是关键鉴别点。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Bloody vs. Watery Infectious Diarrhea Pathogens / 感染性血便与水样泻病原体对比

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Bloody Diarrhea Pathogens</strong><br />
<strong>血便病原体</strong></th>
<th><strong>Watery Diarrhea Pathogens</strong><br />
<strong>水样泻病原体</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Key organisms<br />
主要病原体</td>
<td>E. coli O157:H7, Shigella, Salmonella, Campylobacter, Entamoeba histolytica<br />
大肠杆菌 O157:H7、志贺菌、沙门菌、弯曲杆菌、溶组织阿米巴</td>
<td>ETEC, Vibrio cholerae, C. difficile, Cryptosporidium, Giardia, Norovirus<br />
ETEC、霍乱弧菌、艰难梭菌、隐孢子虫、贾第鞭毛虫、诺如病毒</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Mechanism<br />
机制</td>
<td>Mucosal invasion or cytotoxin (Shiga toxin) → wall destruction → bleeding<br />
黏膜侵袭或细胞毒素（Shiga 毒素）→肠壁破坏→出血</td>
<td>Enterotoxin → hypersecretion of fluid without mucosal damage<br />
肠毒素→体液过度分泌但黏膜无损伤</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Fever<br />
发热</td>
<td>Often present (except EHEC — classically afebrile despite bloody stool)<br />
通常存在（EHEC 除外——经典表现无热，尽管有血便）</td>
<td>Usually absent or low-grade<br />
通常无或低热</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Fecal leukocytes<br />
粪便白细胞</td>
<td>Present (inflammatory colitis)<br />
存在（炎症性结肠炎）</td>
<td>Absent (non-inflammatory, secretory)<br />
缺乏（非炎症性，分泌性）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Antibiotic approach<br />
抗生素策略</td>
<td>AVOID in EHEC (↑HUS risk); treat Shigella and Salmonella typhi<br />
EHEC 禁用（↑HUS 风险）；志贺菌和伤寒沙门菌需治疗</td>
<td>Indicated for ETEC (traveler's diarrhea); supportive for viral<br />
适用于 ETEC（旅行者腹泻）；病毒性给予支持治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Major complication<br />
主要并发症</td>
<td>EHEC → HUS (hemolytic anemia + thrombocytopenia + AKI)<br />
EHEC → HUS（溶血性贫血 + 血小板减少 + 急性肾损伤）</td>
<td>Cholera → severe dehydration and electrolyte imbalance<br />
霍乱→严重脱水和电解质紊乱</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**E. coli O157:H7 (EHEC) produces Shiga toxin causing hemorrhagic colitis with afebrile bloody diarrhea — avoid antibiotics to prevent HUS.**

**大肠杆菌 O157:H7（EHEC）产 Shiga 毒素引起出血性结肠炎，表现为无热血便——禁用抗生素以预防 HUS。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "SHEBA" for EHEC / 记忆钩 — "SHEBA" 记忆 EHEC:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>S</strong>higa toxin — cleaves 28S rRNA → cell death / Shiga 毒素——切割 28S rRNA→细胞死亡<br />
• <strong>H</strong>emorrhagic colitis — bloody diarrhea, afebrile / 出血性结肠炎——血便，无热<br />
• <strong>E</strong>-coli O157:H7 — undercooked beef, unpasteurized dairy / 大肠杆菌 O157:H7——未熟牛肉、未巴氏杀菌乳制品<br />
• <strong>B</strong>an antibiotics — lysis releases more toxin → ↑HUS / 禁抗生素——溶菌释放更多毒素→↑HUS<br />
• <strong>A</strong>void loperamide — antiperistaltics increase toxin absorption / 禁止泻药——止蠕动药增加毒素吸收</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — E. coli O157:H7 and HUS / 高频知识表 — 大肠杆菌 O157:H7 与 HUS

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Transmission routes<br />
传播途径</td>
<td>Undercooked ground beef, unpasteurized milk/juice, contaminated produce (spinach, sprouts), person-to-person fecal-oral contact<br />
未熟碎牛肉、未经巴氏杀菌乳制品/果汁、受污染农产品（菠菜、豆芽）、人际粪口接触</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Shiga toxin mechanism<br />
Shiga 毒素机制</td>
<td>Cleaves 28S rRNA of 60S ribosomal subunit → halts protein synthesis → apoptosis; binds Gb3 (globotriaosylceramide) receptor on endothelium<br />
切割 60S 核糖体亚基的 28S rRNA→终止蛋白质合成→细胞凋亡；与内皮细胞上 Gb3（球三糖酰基神经酰胺）受体结合</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>HUS triad<br />
HUS 三联征</td>
<td>Microangiopathic hemolytic anemia + thrombocytopenia + acute kidney injury; most common in children aged &lt;5; occurs ~5–10 days after diarrhea onset<br />
微血管病性溶血性贫血 + 血小板减少 + 急性肾损伤；最常见于 &lt;5 岁儿童；腹泻发病后约 5–10 天出现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>EHEC vs. ETEC distinction<br />
EHEC 与 ETEC 鉴别</td>
<td>EHEC: Shiga toxin → bloody diarrhea, afebrile, HUS risk; ETEC: LT/ST enterotoxins → watery traveler's diarrhea, no HUS risk<br />
EHEC：Shiga 毒素→血便、无热、HUS 风险；ETEC：LT/ST 肠毒素→水样旅行者腹泻、无 HUS 风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Why antibiotics are contraindicated<br />
抗生素禁忌原因</td>
<td>Antibiotics lyse bacteria → massive release of preformed Shiga toxin → systemic absorption → increased HUS incidence by 17-fold in some studies<br />
抗生素溶菌→大量预先合成的 Shiga 毒素释放→全身吸收→某些研究显示 HUS 发生率增加 17 倍</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Diagnosis method<br />
诊断方法</td>
<td>Sorbitol-MacConkey agar: EHEC does not ferment sorbitol → colorless (vs. pink for normal E. coli); confirm with Shiga toxin ELISA or PCR<br />
山梨醇 MacConkey 培养基：EHEC 不发酵山梨醇→无色菌落（普通大肠杆菌为粉红色）；Shiga 毒素 ELISA 或 PCR 确认</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>HUS management<br />
HUS 处理</td>
<td>Supportive: dialysis for AKI, transfusion for severe anemia; NO antibiotics, NO antiperistaltics; plasma exchange for TTP (not HUS)<br />
支持治疗：透析治疗 AKI，输血治疗严重贫血；禁用抗生素和止蠕动药；血浆置换用于 TTP（不用于 HUS）</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of afebrile bloody diarrhea:** EHEC is the classic afebrile bloody diarrhea; high fever + bloody diarrhea with tenesmus suggests Shigella; gradual onset with fever suggests Salmonella; poultry exposure + bloody diarrhea suggests Campylobacter\
  **无发热血便鉴别:** EHEC 是经典无热血便；高热 + 血便伴里急后重提示志贺菌；逐渐起病伴发热提示沙门菌；禽肉接触史 + 血便提示弯曲杆菌

- **HUS vs. TTP distinction:** HUS = triad (anemia + thrombocytopenia + AKI), triggered by EHEC, common in children; TTP = pentad (adds neurologic symptoms + fever), caused by ADAMTS13 deficiency, common in adults\
  **HUS 与 TTP 鉴别:** HUS = 三联征（贫血 + 血小板减少 + AKI），由 EHEC 触发，儿童多见；TTP = 五联征（加神经系统症状 + 发热），由 ADAMTS13 缺乏引起，成人多见

- **Key complication watch:** Even after diarrhea resolves, monitor CBC and creatinine for 1–2 weeks in EHEC patients — HUS can develop after apparent clinical improvement\
  **关键并发症监测:** 即使腹泻消退，EHEC 患者仍需在 1–2 周内监测 CBC 和肌酐——HUS 可在表面临床好转后发生

- **Variant — non-O157 EHEC:** Other Shiga toxin-producing E. coli (STEC) strains (e.g., O104:H4) cause similar hemorrhagic colitis and HUS — same management principles apply\
  **题目变式——非 O157 EHEC:** 其他产 Shiga 毒素大肠杆菌（STEC）菌株（如 O104:H4）引起类似出血性结肠炎和 HUS——适用相同处理原则

# Question 41 — Long-Acting Injectable Antipsychotic for Schizophrenia Nonadherence / 长效注射型抗精神病药用于精神分裂症不依从性管理

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>50-year-old man</strong> with a <strong>30-year history of paranoid schizophrenia</strong> is admitted to a psychiatric facility because of an <strong>exacerbation of his condition</strong>. His history includes <strong>multiple admissions to the hospital</strong> for his condition. The physician prescribes oral antipsychotic therapy and the patient agrees to take the medication while in the facility, but <strong>he says that he does not need it and he will stop taking the medication as soon as he is discharged</strong>. He states, "I don't trust any of you. You're all out to get me. But I'll play along until my time here is done." Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Administer the antipsychotic therapy until the patient's paranoia completely resolves<br />
B) Change the oral antipsychotic therapy to a long-acting injectable formulation<br />
C) Commit the patient to the facility against his will<br />
D) Discharge the patient with support from the local community mental health center, telling him that he can always return to the facility if he needs help in the future<br />
E) Maximize the dose of the antipsychotic therapy until the patient gains insight into his illness</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: B</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>30-year history of paranoid schizophrenia<br />
30年偏执型精神分裂症病史</td>
<td>Chronic, severe mental illness requiring lifelong treatment; spontaneous sustained remission is not expected<br />
需终身治疗的慢性重度精神疾病；不期待自发持续缓解</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Multiple prior hospitalizations<br />
多次住院史</td>
<td>Indicates a revolving-door hospitalization pattern driven by nonadherence and relapse cycles<br />
提示由不依从性和复发循环驱动的"旋转门"住院模式</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Will stop medication as soon as discharged<br />
出院后将立即停药</td>
<td>Overt declaration of planned nonadherence — the single strongest indicator for switching to LAI<br />
明确宣告计划性停药——改用长效注射剂的最强单一指征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>"I don't need it" — lacks insight<br />
"我不需要它"——缺乏病识感</td>
<td>Anosognosia (lack of illness insight) is present in ~50% of schizophrenia patients; oral adherence cannot be self-motivated<br />
病觉缺失存在于约 50% 的精神分裂症患者中；口服依从性无法自我驱动</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Currently consents to treatment<br />
目前同意接受治疗</td>
<td>Patient has capacity and is agreeable now — the window to switch to LAI before discharge is open<br />
患者目前有决定能力且同意配合——在出院前转换为 LAI 的窗口期已开放</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Nonadherence** is the leading cause of relapse in **schizophrenia**: when oral antipsychotics are **self-discontinued**, dopamine D2 receptor blockade is lost and positive symptoms (hallucinations, delusions, paranoia) rapidly re-emerge:

**不依从性**是**精神分裂症**复发的首要原因：当口服抗精神病药被**自行停用**时，多巴胺 D2 受体阻断作用消失，阳性症状（幻觉、妄想、偏执）迅速再现：

- **Long-acting injectable (LAI)** antipsychotics use a **depot formulation** (esterified drug in oil or microspheres) that releases drug slowly over 2–12 weeks after IM injection\
  **长效注射型（LAI）**抗精神病药采用**储库剂型**（酯化药物溶于油剂或微球中），肌肉注射后缓慢释放药物，持续 2–12 周

- This bypasses daily oral adherence entirely — the patient cannot simply "forget" or "choose not to" take the medication\
  这完全绕过每日口服依从性问题——患者无法简单地"忘记"或"选择不服"药物

- LAI maintains steady plasma drug levels, reducing peak-trough fluctuations and associated adverse effects\
  LAI 维持稳定血药浓度，减少峰谷波动及相关不良反应

- Evidence shows LAI reduces rehospitalization rates by 30–50% in high-risk nonadherent patients\
  证据表明，LAI 在高风险不依从性患者中可降低再住院率 30–50%

**Clinical rule of thumb:** When a patient explicitly states intent to stop medication after discharge, switch to LAI — not dose escalation, not forced commitment.

**临床小窍门:** 当患者明确表示出院后打算停药时，改用 LAI——而不是增加剂量，也不是强制住院。

## 3. Correct Answer (B) — Long-Acting Injectable Antipsychotic / 正确答案 (B) — 长效注射型抗精神病药

**Long-acting injectable (LAI) antipsychotics** are depot formulations that maintain therapeutic drug levels for weeks to months after a single injection, directly solving the nonadherence problem in this patient:

**长效注射型（LAI）抗精神病药**是储库剂型，单次注射后可维持数周至数月的治疗药物浓度，直接解决该患者的不依从性问题：

- LAIs are available as both first-generation (haloperidol decanoate, fluphenazine decanoate) and second-generation (aripiprazole, olanzapine pamoate, paliperidone palmitate, risperidone microspheres) formulations\
  LAI 分为第一代（癸酸氟哌啶醇、癸酸氟奋乃静）和第二代（阿立哌唑、帕莫酸奥氮平、帕利哌酮棕榈酸酯、利培酮微球）两类

- Dosing intervals range from every 2 weeks (haloperidol decanoate) to every 3 months (aripiprazole lauroxil)\
  给药间隔从每 2 周（癸酸氟哌啶醇）到每 3 个月（月桂酸阿立哌唑）不等

- Adverse effect profiles are similar to oral equivalents; agent selection is guided by prior treatment response\
  不良反应谱与口服等效药物相似；药物选择依据既往治疗反应

- This patient's explicit intent to stop oral medication makes LAI not merely preferred but clinically necessary\
  该患者明确表示要停止口服药物，使 LAI 不仅仅是优选方案，而是临床必要措施

**Diagnosis:** Paranoid schizophrenia with explicit anticipatory nonadherence and a revolving-door hospitalization pattern.

**诊断:** 偏执型精神分裂症，伴明确预期不依从性及反复住院模式。

**Treatment:** Switch current oral antipsychotic to an equivalent LAI formulation; overlap oral and LAI therapy for initial weeks if needed to maintain therapeutic levels during the loading phase.

**治疗:** 将当前口服抗精神病药转换为等效 LAI 剂型；如需在负荷阶段维持治疗水平，初始数周可口服与 LAI 重叠使用。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Administer until paranoia completely resolves<br />
A — 持续给药直至偏执完全消解</td>
<td>Even full symptom remission does not prevent relapse after discharge; complete resolution is an unrealistic endpoint for 30-year chronic schizophrenia<br />
即使症状完全缓解也不能防止出院后复发；对于 30 年慢性精神分裂症，完全消解不是现实终点</td>
<td>Symptom control ≠ prevention of future relapse; the nonadherence problem remains unsolved regardless of inpatient response<br />
症状控制≠预防未来复发；无论住院反应如何，不依从性问题仍未解决</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Change to long-acting injectable ✓<br />
B — 改为长效注射剂型 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Directly addresses explicit nonadherence by eliminating the need for daily self-administered oral dosing<br />
正确——通过消除每日自行口服给药的需求，直接解决明确的不依从性问题</td>
<td>Patient's stated intent to stop meds = strongest indication for LAI<br />
患者表示打算停药 = LAI 最强适应证</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Commit against his will<br />
C — 违背意愿强制住院</td>
<td>Patient currently consents to treatment; he presents no imminent danger to self or others; indefinite commitment is neither ethically justified nor an effective solution to nonadherence<br />
患者目前同意治疗；他对自己或他人没有即时危险；无限期强制住院在伦理上既无依据，也不能有效解决不依从性</td>
<td>Involuntary commitment requires imminent danger to self/others or grave disability — not merely planned future nonadherence<br />
非自愿承诺需要对自己/他人构成即时危险或严重残疾——而非仅仅是计划中的未来不依从</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Discharge with community mental health support<br />
D — 出院并给予社区心理健康支持</td>
<td>Community support does not override deliberate nonadherence; this patient will self-discontinue oral medication regardless of follow-up availability<br />
社区支持无法凌驾于故意不依从之上；无论有无随访机会，该患者都会自行停止口服药物</td>
<td>LAI is the superior strategy to break the hospitalization-relapse-rehospitalization cycle; community support is an adjunct, not a substitute<br />
LAI 是打破住院-复发-再住院循环的更优策略；社区支持是辅助手段，而非替代</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Maximize dose until insight is gained<br />
E — 加大剂量直至获得病识感</td>
<td>Dose escalation increases adverse effects (EPS, tardive dyskinesia, metabolic effects) and paradoxically contributes to oral nonadherence; insight rarely improves from dose alone<br />
剂量升级增加不良反应（锥体外系反应、迟发性运动障碍、代谢影响），反而助长口服不依从性；病识感极少单凭增加剂量而改善</td>
<td>Higher oral doses = more side effects = more reason for patient to self-discontinue — the exact opposite of the goal<br />
更高口服剂量 = 更多副作用 = 患者自行停药的更多理由——与目标恰恰相反</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Choice D — community mental health support sounds compassionate and patient-centered, but it does not pharmacologically guarantee medication delivery; only LAI removes the patient's ability to simply choose not to take the drug.*

Choice D 是最具迷惑性的干扰项——社区心理健康支持听起来富有同情心且以患者为中心，但无法在药理学层面保证药物递送；只有 LAI 才能消除患者简单地选择不服药的可能性。

可用第二代药物</td>

阿立哌唑、奥氮平、利培酮、喹硫平、氯氮平</td>
<td>Aripiprazole, olanzapine pamoate, paliperidone palmitate, risperidone microspheres<br />
阿立哌唑、帕莫酸奥氮平、帕利哌酮棕榈酸酯、利培酮微球</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In a schizophrenia patient who explicitly declares intent to stop oral medication after discharge, switch to a long-acting injectable (LAI) antipsychotic — the only intervention that pharmacologically guarantees ongoing treatment delivery.**

**对于明确表示出院后将停止口服药物的精神分裂症患者，改用长效注射型（LAI）抗精神病药——这是唯一能在药理学层面保证持续给药的干预措施。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "STAY on LAI" / 记忆钩 — "STAY 留在 LAI":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>S</strong>chizophrenia with no insight — patient doesn't believe he needs medication / 无病识感的精神分裂症——患者不相信自己需要药物<br />
• <strong>T</strong>old you he will stop — explicit anticipatory nonadherence declared before discharge / 告诉你他会停药——出院前明确声明预期不依从<br />
• <strong>A</strong>ll those prior hospitalizations — revolving-door pattern = proven relapse risk / 所有那些既往住院史——"旋转门"模式 = 已证实的复发风险<br />
• <strong>Y</strong>ield oral to depot injection — LAI removes the patient's choice to skip doses / 将口服改为储库注射——LAI 消除了患者跳过剂量的选择权</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Long-Acting Injectable Antipsychotics in Schizophrenia / 高频知识表 — 精神分裂症中的长效注射型抗精神病药

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>LAI depot mechanism<br />
LAI 储库机制</td>
<td>Esterified antipsychotic suspended in oil or microspheres; slow hydrolysis releases active drug over weeks–months after deep IM injection<br />
酯化抗精神病药悬浮于油剂或微球中；深部肌肉注射后缓慢水解，在数周至数月内释放活性药物</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Indications for LAI<br />
LAI 适应证</td>
<td>Known nonadherence; anticipated nonadherence; revolving-door hospitalizations; patient preference for less frequent dosing; anosognosia<br />
已知不依从；预期不依从；反复住院；患者偏好减少给药频率；病觉缺失</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>First-generation LAI agents<br />
第一代 LAI 药物</td>
<td>Haloperidol decanoate (every 4 weeks); fluphenazine decanoate (every 2–4 weeks)<br />
癸酸氟哌啶醇（每 4 周）；癸酸氟奋乃静（每 2–4 周）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Second-generation LAI agents<br />
第二代 LAI 药物</td>
<td>Paliperidone palmitate (monthly or every 3 months); aripiprazole monohydrate/lauroxil (monthly/every 6 weeks/3 months); risperidone microspheres (every 2 weeks); olanzapine pamoate (every 2–4 weeks)<br />
帕利哌酮棕榈酸酯（每月或每 3 个月）；阿立哌唑（每月/每 6 周/3 个月）；利培酮微球（每 2 周）；帕莫酸奥氮平（每 2–4 周）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>LAI adverse effects vs. oral<br />
LAI vs 口服不良反应</td>
<td>Similar profiles — LAI does not eliminate EPS, tardive dyskinesia, or metabolic effects; it solves adherence only<br />
不良反应谱相似——LAI 不能消除锥体外系反应、迟发性运动障碍或代谢影响；它仅解决依从性问题</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Olanzapine pamoate special warning<br />
帕莫酸奥氮平特殊警告</td>
<td>Post-injection delirium/sedation syndrome (PDSS) occurs in ~0.07% of injections; requires 3-hour supervised observation post-injection at a registered facility<br />
注射后谵妄/镇静综合征（PDSS）发生于约 0.07% 的注射；需在注册机构进行 3 小时监督观察</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Involuntary commitment criteria<br />
非自愿承诺标准</td>
<td>Requires imminent danger to self/others OR grave disability/inability to care for self — planned nonadherence alone does not meet threshold<br />
需要对自己/他人构成即时危险，或严重残疾/无法照料自己——单独计划性不依从不满足门槛</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Key complication of LAI:** Olanzapine pamoate carries a unique post-injection delirium/sedation syndrome (PDSS) risk; mandatory 3-hour observation at a certified healthcare facility is required after every injection\
  **LAI 关键并发症:** 帕莫酸奥氮平具有独特的注射后谵妄/镇静综合征（PDSS）风险；每次注射后必须在认证医疗机构进行强制 3 小时观察

- **Differential — when LAI is refused:** If the patient also refuses LAI injection, consider Assisted Outpatient Treatment (AOT) / court-ordered outpatient treatment, available in most US states for nonadherent patients with prior hospitalizations\
  **鉴别——患者拒绝 LAI 时:** 如果患者也拒绝 LAI 注射，考虑在大多数美国州适用于有住院史不依从患者的辅助门诊治疗（AOT）/法院命令门诊治疗

- **Risk factor for nonadherence:** Anosognosia (lack of insight into illness) is present in ~50% of schizophrenia patients and is the single strongest predictor of medication nonadherence, relapse, and rehospitalization\
  **不依从性风险因素:** 病觉缺失（缺乏对疾病的病识感）存在于约 50% 的精神分裂症患者中，是药物不依从、复发和再住院的单一最强预测因素

- **Variant — clozapine exception:** Clozapine (reserved for treatment-resistant schizophrenia) has no LAI formulation; for clozapine patients with nonadherence, mandatory weekly/biweekly monitoring visits serve as adherence checkpoints\
  **题目变式——氯氮平例外:** 氯氮平（保留用于治疗耐药精神分裂症）无 LAI 剂型；对于不依从的氯氮平患者，强制性每周/双周监测访视作为依从性检查点

# Question 42 — Ureterolithiasis (Small Stone) / 输尿管结石（小结石）

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>An <strong>8-year-old boy</strong> is brought to the emergency department because of a <strong>2-day history of urinary urgency and frequency</strong> and <strong>right-sided abdominal cramps</strong>. The cramps are intermittent, and he <strong>cannot get comfortable in any position</strong> when they occur. He has not had fever, diarrhea, or constipation, but he has vomited twice. He has no history of similar episodes or serious illness. He takes no medications. His <strong>paternal uncle has a history of renal calculi</strong>, and his cousin has Crohn disease. The patient has no dietary restrictions. His temperature is 37.5°C (99.5°F). The <strong>right flank is tender to palpation</strong>. An abdominal x-ray shows a <strong>3-mm ovoid, opaque mass in the right pelvis</strong>. Laboratory studies show: Serum Urea nitrogen 20 mg/dL, Creatinine 0.1 mg/dL; Urine pH 6.5, <strong>RBC 30–50/hpf</strong>, WBC 3–5/hpf. In addition to administration of morphine, which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in management (after morphine)?</strong></p>
<p>A) Oral administration of allopurinol<br />
B) Oral administration of fluids<br />
C) Oral administration of hydrochlorothiazide<br />
D) Oral administration of potassium citrate<br />
E) Oral administration of pyridoxine<br />
F) Lithotripsy</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: B</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Intermittent right flank pain, cannot get comfortable in any position<br />
间歇性右侧腹痛，无法通过任何体位缓解</td>
<td>Classic renal colic; restlessness distinguishes it from peritonitis (peritonitis: patient lies still)<br />
典型肾绞痛；辗转难安与腹膜炎鉴别（腹膜炎患者静卧）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>3-mm ovoid, radiopaque mass in right pelvis<br />
右侧骨盆3mm卵圆形不透X线肿块</td>
<td>Radiopaque = calcium-based or struvite stone (NOT uric acid); 3 mm is far below 6 mm intervention threshold<br />
不透X线 = 含钙或鸟粪石（非尿酸石）；3mm远低于6mm干预阈值</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>RBC 30–50/hpf in urine<br />
尿液红细胞30–50/高倍视野</td>
<td>Microscopic hematuria is a hallmark of nephrolithiasis caused by urothelial abrasion<br />
显微镜下血尿是结石擦伤尿路上皮的标志性表现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No fever, WBC 3–5/hpf (not pyuria), Creatinine 0.1<br />
无发热，尿WBC不高（无脓尿），肌酐0.1</td>
<td>No UTI, no obstructive nephropathy → clinically stable → conservative management is appropriate<br />
无UTI、无梗阻性肾病 → 临床稳定 → 保守治疗合适</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Paternal uncle with renal calculi<br />
父方叔叔有肾结石史</td>
<td>Genetic predisposition to stone formation; family history is a major risk factor in pediatric nephrolithiasis<br />
结石形成的遗传易感性；家族史是儿科肾结石的主要危险因素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Cousin with Crohn disease<br />
表亲患克罗恩病</td>
<td>Crohn disease causes fat malabsorption → increased intestinal oxalate absorption → calcium oxalate stones; likely a deliberate distractor<br />
克罗恩病导致脂肪吸收障碍→肠道草酸吸收增加→草酸钙结石；此处很可能是干扰信息</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Ureterolithiasis** occurs when a **calculus** becomes lodged in the ureter, triggering **ureteral smooth muscle spasm** and partial **obstruction**:

**输尿管结石**是指结石嵌顿于输尿管，引发**输尿管平滑肌痉挛**和不完全**梗阻**：

- A stone migrating down the ureter causes intense peristaltic spasm → severe, colicky, intermittent pain radiating from flank to groin to scrotum/labia\
  结石沿输尿管下行引发强烈蠕动性痉挛 → 剧烈阵发性疼痛，从腰部放射至腹股沟及阴囊/大阴唇

- The moving stone abrades the urothelium → hematuria (microscopic or gross)\
  移动的结石擦伤尿路上皮 → 血尿（镜下或肉眼）

- Radiopaque stones (calcium oxalate, calcium phosphate, struvite) are visible on plain x-ray; radiolucent stones (uric acid, cystine) are not\
  不透X线结石（草酸钙、磷酸钙、鸟粪石）在X线平片可见；透X线结石（尿酸、胱氨酸）不可见

- Stone passage rate: ≤ 5 mm → ~80% spontaneous; 5–10 mm → ~50%; \> 10 mm → unlikely without intervention\
  结石自行排出率：≤5mm约80%；5–10mm约50%；\>10mm无干预难以排出

**Size rule of thumb:** stones \< 6 mm in a clinically stable patient → oral hydration + analgesia; stones ≥ 6 mm or complicated → urologic intervention

**尺寸小窍门:** 临床稳定患者结石 \<6mm → 口服水化 + 镇痛；结石 ≥6mm 或有并发症 → 泌尿外科干预

---

## 3. Correct Answer (B) — Oral Hydration for Spontaneous Stone Passage / 正确答案 (B) — 口服水化促自发排石

**Oral fluid administration** increases urine flow to facilitate spontaneous passage of a small stone in a clinically stable patient:

**口服补液**通过增加尿流量，在临床稳定患者中促进小结石自发排出：

- This 3-mm stone is far below the 6-mm intervention threshold → high probability of spontaneous passage (~80%)\
  3mm结石远低于6mm干预阈值 → 自发排出概率高（约80%）

- Increased fluid intake dilutes urine, reduces stone-forming solute concentration, and augments ureteral peristalsis\
  增加液体摄入稀释尿液、降低结石形成溶质浓度，并增强输尿管蠕动

- Morphine addresses acute pain; hydration addresses the underlying mechanism of moving the stone through\
  吗啡处理急性疼痛；水化解决排石的根本机制

- Patient is stable: afebrile, normal renal function (Cr 0.1), no pyuria → no urgent intervention needed\
  患者稳定：无发热、肾功能正常（肌酐0.1）、无脓尿 → 无需紧急干预

**Diagnosis:** Small (3-mm) radiopaque ureterolithiasis in a clinically stable pediatric patient with family history of nephrolithiasis

**诊断:** 有肾结石家族史的儿科患者，3mm不透X线输尿管结石，临床稳定

**Treatment:** Oral hydration + analgesia (morphine already given); strain urine to capture stone for composition analysis; urology referral if no passage in 4–6 weeks or worsening symptoms

**治疗:** 口服水化 + 镇痛（吗啡已给予）；过滤尿液收集结石做成分分析；若4–6周内未排出或症状加重则转诊泌尿科

---

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Oral administration of allopurinol<br />
A — 口服别嘌醇</td>
<td>For uric acid stones (radiolucent); this stone is radiopaque → rules out uric acid; allopurinol is also preventive, not acute<br />
用于尿酸结石（透X线）；本题结石不透X线 → 排除尿酸石；别嘌醇也是预防药，非急性期用药</td>
<td>Radiopaque on x-ray → not uric acid stone<br />
X线不透X线 → 非尿酸结石</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Oral administration of fluids ✓<br />
B — 口服补液 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — 3-mm stone in clinically stable patient; oral hydration facilitates spontaneous passage<br />
正确——临床稳定患者的3mm小结石；口服水化促进自发排出</td>
<td>Stone &lt; 6 mm + stable = conservative management<br />
结石&lt;6mm + 临床稳定 = 保守治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Oral administration of hydrochlorothiazide<br />
C — 口服氢氯噻嗪</td>
<td>Reduces renal calcium excretion → prevents recurrent calcium stones; not for acute management; reserved after dietary modification fails<br />
减少肾钙排泄 → 预防钙结石复发；非急性期治疗；在饮食调整失败后方用</td>
<td>Thiazides = secondary prevention, not acute treatment<br />
噻嗪类 = 二级预防，非急性期处理</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Oral administration of potassium citrate<br />
D — 口服枸橼酸钾</td>
<td>Alkalinizes urine to prevent/dissolve uric acid stones; this radiopaque stone is calcium-based, not uric acid<br />
碱化尿液预防/溶解尿酸结石；本题不透X线结石为含钙结石，非尿酸石</td>
<td>Potassium citrate targets uric acid (radiolucent); wrong stone type<br />
枸橼酸钾针对尿酸结石（透X线）；结石类型不符</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Oral administration of pyridoxine<br />
E — 口服吡哆醇（维生素B6）</td>
<td>Proposed to reduce urinary oxalate excretion, but large randomized trials show no significant benefit for stone prevention<br />
理论上减少尿草酸排泄，但大型随机试验显示预防结石无显著获益</td>
<td>No evidence base for acute or preventive stone management<br />
急性期或预防性处理均无循证依据</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>F — Lithotripsy<br />
F — 体外冲击波碎石术</td>
<td>Reserved for stones ≥ 6 mm or those failing conservative management; this 3-mm stone has ~80% spontaneous passage rate<br />
用于≥6mm或保守治疗失败的结石；3mm结石自行排出率约80%，无需碎石</td>
<td>Stone size &lt; 6 mm → conservative first; lithotripsy is overtreatment here<br />
结石&lt;6mm → 先保守治疗；此处碎石为过度治疗</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is F (lithotripsy) — examinees may feel active intervention is warranted, but the 3-mm size firmly places this patient in the spontaneous passage category where conservative management prevails.*

最容易错选的干扰项是F（碎石术）——考生可能倾向于主动干预，但3mm的结石尺寸明确属于可自行排出的范畴，保守治疗才是首选策略。

---

预防治疗</td>

</tr>
<tr>
<td>Acute management (&lt; 6 mm, stable)<br />
急性期处理（&lt;6mm，稳定）</td>
<td>Oral hydration + analgesia<br />
口服水化 + 镇痛</td>
<td>Oral hydration + analgesia<br />
口服水化 + 镇痛</td>
<td>Oral hydration + analgesia + antibiotics<br />
口服水化 + 镇痛 + 抗生素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Intervention threshold<br />
干预阈值</td>
<td>≥ 6 mm or failing to pass<br />
≥6mm或保守治疗失败</td>
<td>≥ 6 mm or failing to pass<br />
≥6mm或保守治疗失败</td>
<td>Often large → percutaneous nephrolithotomy<br />
常体积较大→经皮肾镜取石术</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A small (\< 6 mm), radiopaque ureteral stone in a clinically stable patient (no fever, no renal dysfunction) is managed conservatively with oral hydration and analgesia — lithotripsy and preventive medications are not indicated acutely.**

**临床稳定患者（无发热、无肾功能损害）的小结石（\<6mm）不透X线输尿管结石，保守处理：口服水化 + 镇痛——急性期不需要碎石术或预防性药物。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — PASS the Stone / 记忆钩 — "PASS" 排石四要素:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>P</strong>ain control first (morphine or NSAIDs) — always start here / 疼痛控制优先（吗啡或NSAIDs）——始终从此开始<br />
• <strong>A</strong>bundant oral fluids — flush the stone through the ureter / 大量口服补液——冲刷结石通过输尿管<br />
• <strong>S</strong>ize &lt; 6 mm → spontaneous passage expected; ≥ 6 mm → consider intervention / 尺寸&lt;6mm → 预期自行排出；≥6mm → 考虑干预<br />
• <strong>S</strong>train the urine — catch the stone for composition analysis to guide prevention / 过滤尿液——收集结石做成分分析以指导预防</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Nephrolithiasis / 高频知识表 — 肾结石

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Stone size and spontaneous passage rate<br />
结石尺寸与自行排出率</td>
<td>&lt; 5 mm: ~80% pass spontaneously; 5–10 mm: ~50%; &gt; 10 mm: unlikely without intervention; clinical decision threshold is 6 mm<br />
&lt;5mm约80%自行排出；5–10mm约50%；&gt;10mm无干预难以排出；临床决策阈值为6mm</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Indications for urgent urologic intervention<br />
紧急泌尿科干预指征</td>
<td>Fever + obstruction (urosepsis risk), solitary kidney with obstruction, bilateral obstruction, intractable pain/vomiting, stone &gt; 6 mm failing to pass, renal function deterioration<br />
发热+梗阻（尿脓毒症风险）、孤立肾梗阻、双侧梗阻、顽固性疼痛/呕吐、&gt;6mm结石未排出、肾功能恶化</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Preferred imaging in pediatrics<br />
儿科首选影像</td>
<td>Ultrasound first (no radiation); plain x-ray second; non-contrast CT is gold standard but last resort in children to minimize radiation exposure<br />
首选超声（无辐射）；X线平片次之；非增强CT是金标准但儿科最后考虑以减少辐射</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Medical expulsive therapy<br />
药物促排治疗</td>
<td>Alpha-1 blockers (tamsulosin) relax ureteral smooth muscle → increase spontaneous passage rate for distal ureteral stones ≤ 10 mm<br />
α1受体阻滞剂（坦索罗辛）松弛输尿管平滑肌 → 提高≤10mm远端输尿管结石自行排出率</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Metabolic workup after first pediatric stone<br />
儿科首次结石后代谢筛查</td>
<td>24-hour urine: calcium, oxalate, citrate, uric acid, phosphate, creatinine; serum: calcium, PTH, uric acid, bicarbonate; stone composition analysis<br />
24小时尿：钙、草酸、枸橼酸、尿酸、磷酸、肌酐；血清：钙、PTH、尿酸、碳酸氢盐；结石成分分析</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Crohn disease and calcium oxalate stones<br />
克罗恩病与草酸钙结石</td>
<td>Fat malabsorption → fatty acids bind calcium in gut → free oxalate absorbed → hyperoxaluria → calcium oxalate stones; treated with low-fat diet + calcium supplementation with meals<br />
脂肪吸收不良→脂肪酸在肠道结合钙→游离草酸被吸收→高草酸尿→草酸钙结石；治疗：低脂饮食+随餐补钙</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of renal colic:** appendicitis has fever, RLQ tenderness, no hematuria; pyelonephritis has fever and pyuria; musculoskeletal pain is constant and relieved by rest; peritonitis patient lies still rather than writhing\
  **肾绞痛鉴别:** 阑尾炎有发热、右下腹压痛、无血尿；肾盂肾炎有发热和脓尿；肌肉骨骼疼痛持续且休息可缓解；腹膜炎患者静卧而非辗转

- **Allopurinol mechanism:** inhibits xanthine oxidase → reduces conversion of hypoxanthine/xanthine to uric acid → lowers serum and urine uric acid; used for gout and prevention of uric acid nephrolithiasis, not for acute passage\
  **别嘌醇机制:** 抑制黄嘌呤氧化酶→减少次黄嘌呤/黄嘌呤转化为尿酸→降低血清和尿液尿酸；用于痛风及尿酸性肾结石预防，不用于急性排石

- **Thiazide diuretics for calcium stones:** thiazides increase distal tubular calcium reabsorption → reduce urinary calcium → prevent recurrent calcium stone formation; not for acute management\
  **噻嗪类利尿剂用于钙结石:** 噻嗪类增加远曲小管钙重吸收→减少尿钙→预防钙结石复发；不用于急性期处理

- **Imaging caveat — uric acid stones:** uric acid stones are radiolucent and invisible on plain x-ray; a "normal" x-ray in a patient with classic renal colic symptoms should prompt CT or ultrasound, not reassurance\
  **影像学注意——尿酸结石:** 尿酸结石透X线，X线平片不可见；典型肾绞痛症状患者X线"正常"应行CT或超声检查，而非仅凭X线阴性结果排除

# Question 43 — Myasthenia Gravis (Thymoma-Associated) / 重症肌无力（胸腺瘤相关）

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>previously healthy 57-year-old woman</strong> comes to the physician because of a <strong>6-month history of muscle weakness and fatigue</strong>. The weakness <strong>began in the muscles of her face</strong> and has progressed to all of the muscles in her body. Examination shows <strong>bilateral ptosis</strong> and <strong>weakness of the left abducens muscle</strong>. An x-ray of the chest shows a <strong>mediastinal mass</strong>. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in diagnosis of this patient's neurologic findings?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Nerve conduction studies with repetitive stimulation<br />
B) MRI of the cervical spine<br />
C) Somatosensory evoked potentials<br />
D) Biopsy of a peripheral nerve<br />
E) Biopsy of a skeletal muscle</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: A</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>57-year-old woman<br />
57岁女性</td>
<td>MG has bimodal onset: young women (teens–20s) and older adults (50s–60s); this patient fits the second peak<br />
重症肌无力双峰发病：青年女性及老年人（50-60岁）；此患者符合第二高峰</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Weakness began in facial muscles<br />
肌无力始于面部肌肉</td>
<td>Cranial/bulbar muscle involvement is the hallmark of MG; ocular and facial muscles are most commonly affected first<br />
颅神经/延髓肌受累是重症肌无力的特征；眼肌和面肌最常首先受累</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Bilateral ptosis<br />
双侧上睑下垂</td>
<td>Ptosis from levator palpebrae weakness is the most common presenting sign of ocular MG<br />
提上睑肌无力导致的上睑下垂是眼肌型重症肌无力最常见的首发体征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Weakness of left abducens muscle<br />
左侧外展肌无力</td>
<td>CN VI palsy causing impaired lateral gaze points to neuromuscular junction failure at extraocular muscles, not a structural lesion<br />
第六颅神经麻痹导致眼球外展障碍，提示眼外肌神经肌肉接头功能障碍而非结构性病变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Mediastinal mass on chest x-ray<br />
胸部X线显示纵隔肿块</td>
<td>Thymoma is present in ~15% of MG patients; thymoma/thymic hyperplasia drives autoimmune anti-nAChR antibody production<br />
约15%的重症肌无力患者合并胸腺瘤；胸腺瘤/胸腺增生驱动抗乙酰胆碱受体自身抗体产生</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Progressive spread to all muscles<br />
无力逐渐累及全身肌肉</td>
<td>Generalized MG with fatigability on use is the classic progression from focal ocular/bulbar to generalized disease<br />
广泛型重症肌无力伴使用后疲劳性是从局限性眼/延髓型向广泛型发展的经典过程</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Myasthenia gravis** is an autoimmune disorder in which **anti-nicotinic acetylcholine receptor (nAChR) antibodies** bind to and destroy the **postsynaptic neuromuscular junction (NMJ)**, reducing the number of functional receptors and causing **fatigable muscle weakness**:

**重症肌无力**是一种自身免疫性疾病，**抗烟碱型乙酰胆碱受体（nAChR）抗体**与**突触后神经肌肉接头（NMJ）**结合并破坏受体，减少功能性受体数量，导致**疲劳性肌无力**：

- ACh is released normally from motor nerve terminals, but fewer postsynaptic nAChRs are available for binding\
  运动神经末梢正常释放乙酰胆碱，但突触后可供结合的烟碱型受体数量减少

- With repetitive nerve stimulation, the available ACh pool depletes faster than receptor recovery → decremental CMAP response on EMG\
  反复神经电刺激时，可用ACh库耗竭速度超过受体恢复速度→肌电图复合肌肉动作电位（CMAP）递减反应

- Thymoma creates aberrant T-cell education: autoreactive T-helper cells escape tolerance and stimulate B-cells to produce anti-nAChR IgG\
  胸腺瘤导致T细胞教育异常：自身反应性辅助T细胞逃脱免疫耐受，刺激B细胞产生抗nAChR IgG抗体

- Weakness worsens with sustained activity ("fatigability") and improves with rest — rest allows partial ACh replenishment\
  持续活动后无力加重（"疲劳性"），休息后改善——休息允许ACh部分补充

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Eyes first, then bulbar (speech/swallow), then limbs, then respiratory — follow this gradient when staging MG severity.

**解剖小窍门:** 眼肌先受累，再延髓肌（语言/吞咽），再肢体肌，最后呼吸肌——按此梯度评估重症肌无力严重程度。

## 3. Correct Answer (A) — Nerve Conduction Studies with Repetitive Stimulation / 正确答案 (A) — 重复电刺激神经传导检查

**Repetitive nerve stimulation (RNS)** is the electrophysiologic test of choice for confirming NMJ transmission defects in suspected myasthenia gravis:

**重复神经电刺激（RNS）**是确认疑似重症肌无力神经肌肉接头传导障碍的首选电生理检查：

- Low-frequency stimulation (2–5 Hz) produces a \>10% decrement in compound muscle action potential (CMAP) amplitude — the diagnostic hallmark of MG\
  低频刺激（2-5 Hz）产生复合肌肉动作电位（CMAP）幅度\>10%递减——这是重症肌无力的标志性诊断发现

- High-frequency stimulation does NOT produce an incremental response in MG (unlike LEMS, where high-frequency stimulation shows facilitation)\
  高频刺激在重症肌无力中不产生递增反应（与Lambert-Eaton综合征相反，后者高频刺激显示易化）

- Single-fiber EMG (SFEMG) measuring jitter is even more sensitive (\>95%) but technically demanding; RNS is the standard first-line electrodiagnostic test\
  测量抖动值的单纤维肌电图（SFEMG）更灵敏（\>95%）但技术要求高；重复电刺激是标准一线电诊断检查

**Diagnosis:** RNS showing decremental response → confirm with anti-AChR antibody titers (positive in ~85% generalized MG) → CT chest to characterize the mediastinal mass (thymoma vs. hyperplasia)

**诊断:** RNS显示递减反应→抗乙酰胆碱受体抗体滴度证实（约85%广泛型重症肌无力阳性）→胸部CT评估纵隔肿块（胸腺瘤vs增生）

**Treatment:** Pyridostigmine (AChEI) for symptomatic control; immunosuppression (prednisone, azathioprine); thymectomy (especially with thymoma); IVIG or plasmapheresis for myasthenic crisis

**治疗:** 溴吡斯的明（乙酰胆碱酯酶抑制剂）控制症状；免疫抑制治疗（泼尼松、硫唑嘌呤）；胸腺切除术（尤其合并胸腺瘤时）；危象时给予IVIG或血浆置换

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Nerve conduction studies with repetitive stimulation ✓<br />
A — 重复电刺激神经传导检查 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Decremental CMAP response on low-frequency RNS is the hallmark electrophysiologic finding confirming NMJ dysfunction in MG<br />
正确——低频重复电刺激的CMAP递减反应是确认重症肌无力NMJ功能障碍的标志性电生理发现</td>
<td>Decremental response (&gt;10% CMAP drop at 2–5 Hz) + fatigable bulbar/ocular weakness = MG<br />
递减反应（2-5 Hz时CMAP下降&gt;10%）+疲劳性延髓/眼肌无力=重症肌无力</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — MRI of the cervical spine<br />
B — 颈椎MRI</td>
<td>Evaluates central cord syndrome or myelopathy, presenting with motor/sensory deficits and upper motor neuron signs — not bilateral ptosis or abducens palsy<br />
评估中央脊髓综合征或脊髓病，表现为运动/感觉缺损及上运动神经元体征——不会出现双侧上睑下垂或外展肌麻痹</td>
<td>No UMN signs, no sensory loss, no neck pain; bilateral ptosis and CN VI palsy point to NMJ disorder, not spinal cord pathology<br />
无上运动神经元体征、无感觉缺失、无颈痛；双侧上睑下垂和第六颅神经麻痹指向NMJ疾病而非脊髓病变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Somatosensory evoked potentials<br />
C — 躯体感觉诱发电位</td>
<td>Assesses integrity of somatosensory pathways (peripheral nerve → spinal cord → cortex); MG is a pure motor NMJ disorder with no somatosensory involvement<br />
评估躯体感觉通路（周围神经→脊髓→皮质）完整性；重症肌无力是纯运动性NMJ疾病，无躯体感觉受累</td>
<td>No sensory complaints in this patient; weakness is purely motor, fatigable, and ocular/bulbar in distribution<br />
患者无感觉主诉；无力纯粹是运动性、疲劳性，分布于眼肌/延髓肌</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Biopsy of a peripheral nerve<br />
D — 周围神经活检</td>
<td>Diagnoses peripheral neuropathy (e.g., mononeuritis multiplex, vasculitic neuropathy); this patient has NMJ dysfunction, not axonal or demyelinating neuropathy<br />
诊断周围神经病变（如多灶性单神经炎、血管炎性神经病）；此患者为NMJ功能障碍，非轴索或脱髓鞘性神经病</td>
<td>MG has normal nerve conduction except at NMJ; nerve biopsy would show no abnormality and misses the correct pathologic site<br />
重症肌无力除NMJ外神经传导正常；神经活检无异常发现且遗漏了正确的病理部位</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Biopsy of a skeletal muscle<br />
E — 骨骼肌活检</td>
<td>Diagnoses inflammatory myopathies (dermatomyositis, polymyositis, IBM) with lymphocyte infiltration and muscle fiber necrosis; these never cause ptosis or abducens palsy<br />
诊断炎性肌病（皮肌炎、多发性肌炎、包涵体肌炎），表现为淋巴细胞浸润和肌纤维坏死；这些疾病从不引起上睑下垂或外展肌麻痹</td>
<td>Inflammatory myopathy: proximal limb weakness + elevated CK + no ocular involvement; MG: ocular + bulbar + fatigability + normal CK<br />
炎性肌病：近端肢体无力+CK升高+无眼部受累；重症肌无力：眼部+延髓+疲劳性+CK正常</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is E (muscle biopsy) — both myositis and MG cause generalized weakness, but myositis never produces ptosis or extraocular muscle palsy, and MG has normal CK with fatigable rather than resting weakness.*

肌肉活检（E选项）是最容易混淆的干扰项——肌炎和重症肌无力均可导致广泛无力，但肌炎从不引起上睑下垂或眼外肌麻痹，而重症肌无力CK正常且表现为疲劳性无力而非静息性无力。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Myasthenia Gravis vs. Lambert-Eaton Myasthenic Syndrome vs. Botulism / 重症肌无力 vs. Lambert-Eaton肌无力综合征 vs. 肉毒中毒

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
<col style="width: 25%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Myasthenia Gravis</strong><br />
<strong>重症肌无力</strong></th>
<th><strong>Lambert-Eaton (LEMS)</strong><br />
<strong>Lambert-Eaton综合征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Botulism</strong><br />
<strong>肉毒中毒</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Mechanism<br />
机制</td>
<td>Anti-nAChR Ab → postsynaptic receptor destruction<br />
抗nAChR抗体→突触后受体破坏</td>
<td>Anti-VGCC Ab → presynaptic; reduced ACh vesicle release<br />
抗VGCC抗体→突触前；ACh囊泡释放减少</td>
<td>C. botulinum toxin blocks presynaptic ACh vesicle fusion<br />
肉毒梭菌毒素阻断突触前ACh囊泡融合</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Ocular involvement<br />
眼部受累</td>
<td>Prominent — ptosis and diplopia are the hallmark<br />
显著——上睑下垂和复视是特征</td>
<td>Mild or absent<br />
轻微或缺如</td>
<td>Yes — descending cranial nerve palsies<br />
是——自上向下的颅神经麻痹</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Deep tendon reflexes<br />
深腱反射</td>
<td>Normal<br />
正常</td>
<td>Diminished at rest, transiently improved post-exercise<br />
静息时减弱，运动后短暂改善</td>
<td>Diminished or absent<br />
减弱或消失</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Repetitive stimulation<br />
重复电刺激</td>
<td>Decremental (&gt;10% drop) at low frequency 2–5 Hz<br />
低频2-5 Hz递减（&gt;10%下降）</td>
<td>Incremental (&gt;100% facilitation) at high frequency ≥50 Hz<br />
高频≥50 Hz递增（&gt;100%易化）</td>
<td>Decremental at low Hz, similar to MG<br />
低频递减，类似重症肌无力</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Associated malignancy<br />
相关肿瘤</td>
<td>Thymoma in 15%<br />
15%合并胸腺瘤</td>
<td>Small cell lung cancer in ~60%<br />
约60%合并小细胞肺癌</td>
<td>None — exogenous or wound toxin<br />
无——外源性或创伤毒素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Treatment<br />
治疗</td>
<td>Pyridostigmine + immunosuppression + thymectomy<br />
溴吡斯的明+免疫抑制+胸腺切除</td>
<td>3,4-Diaminopyridine; treat underlying SCLC<br />
3,4-二氨基吡啶；治疗基础小细胞肺癌</td>
<td>Antitoxin; supportive ventilatory care<br />
抗毒素；呼吸支持治疗</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In a patient with fatigable weakness starting in the ocular and bulbar muscles plus a mediastinal mass (thymoma), MG is the diagnosis — confirmed by repetitive nerve stimulation showing a decremental CMAP response.**

**对于出现疲劳性无力（始于眼肌和延髓肌）合并纵隔肿块（胸腺瘤）的患者，重症肌无力是诊断——通过重复电刺激显示CMAP递减反应来确诊。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — TIRED for MG / 记忆钩 — "TIRED" 助记重症肌无力:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>T</strong>hymoma — associated in 15%; always order chest imaging when MG is suspected / 胸腺瘤——15%合并；疑诊重症肌无力时必须行胸部影像检查<br />
• <strong>I</strong>mmunologic — anti-nAChR IgG destroys postsynaptic receptors at the NMJ / 免疫机制——抗nAChR IgG破坏NMJ突触后受体<br />
• <strong>R</strong>epetitive stimulation — decremental CMAP at 2–5 Hz is the key diagnostic test / 重复电刺激——2-5 Hz时CMAP递减是关键诊断检查<br />
• <strong>E</strong>yes first — ptosis and diplopia are the most common initial presentation / 眼部首发——上睑下垂和复视是最常见的首发表现<br />
• <strong>D</strong>ecrement vs. Increment — MG decrements (low Hz); LEMS increments (high Hz) / 递减vs递增——重症肌无力低频递减；Lambert-Eaton高频递增</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Myasthenia Gravis Diagnosis & Management / 高频知识表 — 重症肌无力的诊断与治疗

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Electrodiagnosis<br />
电诊断</td>
<td>RNS at 2–5 Hz: &gt;10% CMAP decrement = MG; single-fiber EMG (increased jitter) is most sensitive (&gt;95%) but reserved for seronegative or diagnostically uncertain cases<br />
2-5 Hz重复电刺激：CMAP递减&gt;10%=重症肌无力；单纤维肌电图（抖动值增加）最灵敏（&gt;95%）但保留用于血清阴性或诊断不确定病例</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Antibody profile<br />
抗体谱</td>
<td>Anti-AChR Ab: ~85% sensitivity for generalized MG, ~50% for ocular MG; anti-MuSK Ab: positive in ~40% of seronegative generalized MG; anti-LRP4 Ab: rarest subtype<br />
抗AChR抗体：广泛型重症肌无力灵敏度约85%，眼肌型约50%；抗MuSK抗体：约40%血清阴性广泛型重症肌无力阳性；抗LRP4抗体：最罕见亚型</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Ice pack test<br />
冰袋试验</td>
<td>Apply ice to closed eyelid for 2 min → transient ptosis improvement in MG (cold inhibits AChE → more ACh available); fast, safe bedside test requiring no equipment<br />
冰袋敷于闭合眼睑2分钟→重症肌无力上睑下垂短暂改善（低温抑制乙酰胆碱酯酶→更多ACh可用）；快速、安全的床旁检查，无需设备</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Myasthenic crisis<br />
重症肌无力危象</td>
<td>Life-threatening respiratory failure; triggered by infection, surgery, or medication; monitor FVC and NIF; intubate when FVC &lt;15 mL/kg or NIF &lt; −20 cmH₂O; treat with IVIG or plasmapheresis<br />
危及生命的呼吸衰竭；感染、手术或药物诱发；监测FVC和NIF；FVC&lt;15 mL/kg或NIF&lt; −20 cmH₂O时插管；用IVIG或血浆置换治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Drugs to avoid<br />
禁用药物</td>
<td>Aminoglycosides, fluoroquinolones, beta-blockers, magnesium, calcium channel blockers, neuromuscular blocking agents — all impair NMJ transmission and can precipitate crisis<br />
氨基糖苷类、氟喹诺酮类、β受体阻断剂、镁剂、钙通道阻断剂、神经肌肉阻滞剂——均损害NMJ传导，可诱发危象</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Thymectomy indications<br />
胸腺切除适应证</td>
<td>Mandatory for all MG patients with thymoma; also recommended for AChR-Ab–positive generalized MG in patients aged 18–65 even without thymoma (improves long-term remission rates)<br />
所有合并胸腺瘤的重症肌无力患者必须行胸腺切除；18-65岁AChR抗体阳性广泛型重症肌无力患者即使无胸腺瘤也推荐胸腺切除（改善长期缓解率）</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of fatigable ocular weakness:** MG (NMJ postsynaptic — normal reflexes), LEMS (NMJ presynaptic — hyporeflexia improved by exercise), Graves' ophthalmopathy (restrictive — proptosis, lid retraction), mitochondrial myopathy (progressive external ophthalmoplegia — no fatigability)\
  **眼肌疲劳性无力的鉴别:** 重症肌无力（NMJ突触后——反射正常）、Lambert-Eaton综合征（NMJ突触前——反射减弱但运动后改善）、Graves眼病（限制性——眼球突出、眼睑退缩）、线粒体肌病（进行性眼外肌麻痹——无疲劳性）

- **Key complication:** Respiratory failure in myasthenic crisis — do NOT rely on O₂ sat alone (hypercapnia precedes hypoxia); bedside spirometry (FVC, NIF) is essential for monitoring\
  **关键并发症:** 重症肌无力危象中的呼吸衰竭——不要仅依靠血氧饱和度监测（高碳酸血症先于低氧血症出现）；床旁肺活量测定（FVC、NIF）对监测至关重要

- **Variant — ocular MG:** Restricted to ptosis and diplopia for ≥2 years without generalization; AChR-Ab often negative (~50%); ice pack test and SFEMG are preferred diagnostics; lower thymoma risk\
  **题目变式——眼肌型重症肌无力:** 上睑下垂和复视局限≥2年而不泛化；AChR抗体常阴性（约50%）；冰袋试验和单纤维肌电图为首选诊断方法；胸腺瘤风险较低

- **Cause of death in untreated crisis:** Respiratory muscle failure → hypercapnic respiratory failure → arrest; early recognition of bulbar involvement (dysphagia, dysarthria) predicts impending respiratory compromise\
  **未治疗危象的死因:** 呼吸肌衰竭→高碳酸血症性呼吸衰竭→心跳骤停；早期识别延髓受累（吞咽困难、构音障碍）可预测即将发生的呼吸功能失代偿

# Question 44 — Galactocele / 乳汁潴留囊肿

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>29-year-old woman</strong>, gravida 1, para 1, comes to the physician <strong>1 week after noticing a mildly tender lump in her left breast</strong>. <strong>Five months ago</strong>, she delivered a healthy newborn at term following an uncomplicated pregnancy and spontaneous vaginal delivery. She is <strong>breast-feeding</strong> and says her infant feeds equally from both breasts. The patient has no history of serious illness, and her only medication is a prenatal vitamin. Her mother was diagnosed with breast cancer at the age of 61 years. The patient's vital signs are within normal limits. Examination shows <strong>no axillary or supraclavicular lymphadenopathy</strong>. There is a <strong>3-cm, smooth, mobile, cystic, tender mass in the upper outer quadrant of the left breast</strong>.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Bromocriptine therapy<br />
B) Dicloxacillin therapy<br />
C) Discontinuing breast-feeding<br />
D) Fine-needle aspiration of the mass<br />
E) Increasing breast-feeding on the left breast</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: D</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>29-year-old, 5 months postpartum<br />
29岁，产后5个月</td>
<td>Classic demographic for galactocele — occurs in actively lactating or recently lactating women<br />
乳汁潴留囊肿的经典人群——发生在哺乳期或近期刚停止哺乳的女性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Currently breast-feeding, infant feeds from both breasts<br />
目前哺乳，婴儿双侧均喂</td>
<td>Active lactation creates ductal pressure; uneven obstruction can lead to localized milk accumulation<br />
哺乳期乳管内压力高，局部导管阻塞可导致乳汁积聚成囊</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Smooth, mobile, cystic, mildly tender mass<br />
光滑、可移动、囊性、轻压痛包块</td>
<td>Cystic quality points away from solid malignancy or abscess; favors benign fluid-filled cyst<br />
囊性特征有别于实性肿瘤或脓肿，提示良性含液囊肿</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No fever, vital signs normal<br />
无发热，生命体征正常</td>
<td>Rules out mastitis and breast abscess, which present with systemic inflammatory signs<br />
排除乳腺炎和乳腺脓肿，后两者伴全身炎症表现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No axillary or supraclavicular lymphadenopathy<br />
无腋窝或锁骨上淋巴结肿大</td>
<td>Low suspicion for malignancy despite family history; benign process more likely<br />
尽管有家族史，淋巴结阴性降低恶性可能，提示良性病变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Mother diagnosed with breast cancer at age 61<br />
母亲61岁诊断乳腺癌</td>
<td>Raises index of suspicion but late-onset family history is lower-risk than early-onset (&lt;50)<br />
提高警觉，但晚发型家族史（&gt;50岁）风险低于早发型（&lt;50岁）</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Galactocele** arises from **obstruction of a lactiferous duct**, causing **milk** to accumulate within a cystic cavity instead of flowing outward:

**乳汁潴留囊肿**由**输乳管阻塞**引起，导致**乳汁**积聚于囊腔而无法正常排出：

- Inspissated secretions or external compression of the duct → proximal milk stasis → cyst formation\
  导管内分泌物黏稠或外部压迫 → 近端乳汁淤积 → 囊肿形成

- Contents are milk (triglycerides, proteins, water), not serous fluid — distinguishing it from a simple cyst\
  囊内容物为乳汁（甘油三酯、蛋白质、水），而非浆液，有别于单纯囊肿

- The cyst wall is formed by dilated ductal epithelium and may become mildly inflamed but not infected\
  囊壁由扩张的导管上皮构成，可有轻度炎症但不伴感染

- Unlike mastitis, there is no bacterial invasion → no fever, no induration, no erythema\
  与乳腺炎不同，无细菌侵入 → 无发热、无硬结、无皮肤红斑

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Galactoceles most commonly occur in the subareolar or upper outer quadrant where major lactiferous ducts converge; obstruction at any point creates downstream milk pooling.

**解剖小窍门:** 乳汁潴留囊肿最常见于乳晕下区或外上象限，此处主要输乳管汇聚；任意一点阻塞均可导致远端乳汁积聚。

---

## 3. Correct Answer (D) — Fine-Needle Aspiration / 正确答案 (D) — 细针穿刺抽吸

**Fine-needle aspiration (FNA)** serves dual purposes — **diagnostic confirmation** and **therapeutic relief** — making it the ideal first step for a cystic breast mass in a lactating woman:

**细针穿刺抽吸（FNA）**同时具备**诊断确认**和**治疗缓解**双重作用，是哺乳期女性囊性乳腺包块的理想首选步骤：

- FNA of a galactocele yields milky white fluid, confirming milk-filled cyst and ruling out abscess (purulent) or malignancy (bloody/cellular)\
  穿刺乳汁潴留囊肿可抽出乳白色液体，确认乳汁性囊肿，排除脓肿（脓性）或恶性肿瘤（血性/细胞丰富）

- Aspiration itself often resolves the cyst and relieves tenderness — thus therapeutic and diagnostic simultaneously\
  抽吸操作本身常可使囊肿消退并缓解压痛——兼具治疗与诊断双效

- If fluid is non-milky, atypical cells are present, or mass recurs, further workup (ultrasound, biopsy) is warranted\
  若液体非乳白色、含异型细胞或包块复发，需进一步检查（超声、活检）

**Diagnosis:** Clinical diagnosis based on postpartum status, breast-feeding, and cystic mobile mass; confirmed by milky aspirate on FNA.

**诊断:** 基于产后哺乳状态和囊性可移动包块的临床诊断；FNA抽出乳白色液体即可确诊。

**Treatment:** FNA aspiration is first-line; galactoceles often resolve spontaneously or with aspiration; surgical excision reserved for refractory or recurrent cases.

**治疗:** FNA抽吸为一线处理；乳汁潴留囊肿多可自行消退或经抽吸后消退；反复发作或难治性病例才需手术切除。

---

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Bromocriptine therapy<br />
A — 溴隐亭治疗</td>
<td>Treats hyperprolactinemia/prolactinoma causing galactorrhea; not indicated for a focal cystic mass from ductal obstruction<br />
用于治疗高泌乳素血症/垂体催乳素瘤导致的溢乳；不适用于导管阻塞引起的局部囊性包块</td>
<td>Galactorrhea (diffuse) vs. galactocele (focal cyst) — dopamine agonist addresses hormonal excess, not mechanical obstruction<br />
乳汁溢出（弥漫性）vs. 乳汁潴留囊肿（局灶囊肿）——多巴胺激动剂解决激素过剩，而非机械性阻塞</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Dicloxacillin therapy<br />
B — 双氯西林治疗</td>
<td>Anti-staphylococcal antibiotic for mastitis/abscess; this patient lacks fever, erythema, induration, or systemic signs of infection<br />
抗葡萄球菌抗生素用于乳腺炎/脓肿；本患者无发热、红斑、硬结或全身感染表现</td>
<td>Mastitis/abscess requires erythema + tenderness + fever vs. galactocele has cystic mass + normal vitals<br />
乳腺炎/脓肿需要红斑+触痛+发热；乳汁潴留囊肿表现为囊性包块+生命体征正常</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Discontinuing breast-feeding<br />
C — 停止哺乳</td>
<td>Has not been shown to consistently improve galactocele; may worsen engorgement and increase ductal pressure<br />
未被证实能持续改善乳汁潴留囊肿；可能加重乳房充血并增加导管压力</td>
<td>Galactocele is from local ductal obstruction, not from breast-feeding itself; stopping feeding does not clear the obstruction<br />
乳汁潴留囊肿源于局部导管阻塞，而非哺乳行为本身；停止哺乳不能清除阻塞</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Fine-needle aspiration of the mass ✓<br />
D — 细针穿刺抽吸包块 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — confirms diagnosis with milky aspirate and provides immediate therapeutic relief of the cystic mass<br />
正确——乳白色抽吸物确认诊断，同时立即治疗缓解囊性包块</td>
<td>Dual diagnostic + therapeutic value in one step; the standard of care for a cystic breast mass in a lactating woman<br />
一步同时兼具诊断和治疗价值；哺乳期女性囊性乳腺包块的标准处理</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Increasing breast-feeding on the left breast<br />
E — 增加左侧哺乳频率</td>
<td>May temporarily relieve mild ductal congestion but does not address an established cystic obstruction<br />
可暂时缓解轻度导管充血，但不能处理已形成的囊性阻塞</td>
<td>Frequent feeding helps prevent galactocele formation but cannot aspirate or resolve an existing 3-cm cyst<br />
频繁哺乳有助于预防乳汁潴留囊肿形成，但无法抽吸或消解已存在的3cm囊肿</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is (B) Dicloxacillin, because breast masses in postpartum women prompt reflex concern for mastitis — but the absence of fever, erythema, and skin changes, plus the cystic fluctuant quality, clearly distinguishes galactocele from infectious pathology.*

最容易误选的干扰项是(B)双氯西林，因为产后女性乳腺包块容易条件反射联想到乳腺炎——但无发热、无红斑、无皮肤改变，加上囊性波动感，明确将乳汁潴留囊肿与感染性病变区分开来。

---
