## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A postpartum, lactating woman with a smooth, mobile, cystic, mildly tender breast mass and no fever should be evaluated with fine-needle aspiration, which confirms galactocele by yielding milky fluid and provides immediate therapeutic relief.**

**产后哺乳期女性出现光滑、可移动、囊性、轻压痛乳腺包块且无发热，应行细针穿刺抽吸评估，抽出乳白色液体即可确诊乳汁潴留囊肿并立即缓解症状。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "CALM" Galactocele Features / 记忆钩 — "CALM" 乳汁潴留囊肿四要素:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>C</strong>ystic, fluctuant mass — smooth and mobile, NOT rock-hard / 囊性波动包块——光滑可移动，非石硬<br />
• <strong>A</strong>febrile — normal vitals, NO fever distinguishes from mastitis/abscess / 无发热——生命体征正常，区别于乳腺炎/脓肿<br />
• <strong>L</strong>actating woman — postpartum or recently stopped breast-feeding / 哺乳女性——产后或近期停止哺乳<br />
• <strong>M</strong>ilky aspirate on FNA — confirms diagnosis AND treats simultaneously / FNA抽出乳白色液体——同时确诊并治疗</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Galactocele & Postpartum Breast Masses / 高频知识表 — 乳汁潴留囊肿与产后乳腺包块

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Definition of galactocele<br />
乳汁潴留囊肿定义</td>
<td>Benign milk-filled cyst from lactiferous duct obstruction; contains milk (triglycerides, proteins) rather than serous fluid<br />
因输乳管阻塞形成的良性乳汁充盈囊肿；内含乳汁（甘油三酯、蛋白质）而非浆液</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Ultrasound appearance<br />
超声表现</td>
<td>Cystic mass with variable internal echogenicity depending on milk fat content; no internal vascularity on Doppler<br />
囊性包块，内部回声因乳汁脂肪含量不同而变化；多普勒无内部血流信号</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>FNA findings<br />
细针穿刺结果</td>
<td>Milky white or creamy fluid; cytology shows fat globules, foamy macrophages, and benign ductal cells<br />
乳白色或奶油状液体；细胞学见脂肪球、泡沫状巨噬细胞和良性导管细胞</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Complications<br />
并发症</td>
<td>Superimposed bacterial infection → abscess; rupture → granulomatous inflammation; rarely persist as chronic mass<br />
继发细菌感染→脓肿；破裂→肉芽肿性炎症；少数持续存在成为慢性包块</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Management algorithm<br />
处理流程</td>
<td>FNA first (diagnosis + treatment) → if recurrent or non-resolving: repeat aspiration or surgical excision → if bloody aspirate or solid component: biopsy to rule out malignancy<br />
首选FNA（诊断+治疗）→若复发或未消退：重复抽吸或手术切除→若血性抽吸物或实性成分：活检排除恶性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Bromocriptine indications<br />
溴隐亭适应证</td>
<td>Hyperprolactinemia, prolactinoma, Parkinson's disease, acromegaly — NOT galactocele<br />
高泌乳素血症、催乳素瘤、帕金森病、肢端肥大症——不适用于乳汁潴留囊肿</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Family history risk stratification<br />
家族史风险分层</td>
<td>First-degree relative with breast cancer &lt;50 years = high risk (warrants genetic counseling, BRCA testing); ≥50 years = lower but not negligible risk<br />
一级亲属乳腺癌发病年龄&lt;50岁=高风险（需遗传咨询、BRCA检测）；≥50岁=较低但不可忽视的风险</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

---

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of postpartum breast mass:** Galactocele (cystic, afebrile), mastitis (diffuse, febrile), abscess (fluctuant, febrile, purulent), fibroadenoma (firm, rubbery, non-tender, not lactation-related), pregnancy-associated breast cancer (rare but present in young women — bloody nipple discharge, hard irregular mass, lymphadenopathy)\
  **产后乳腺包块鉴别:** 乳汁潴留囊肿（囊性、无发热）、乳腺炎（弥漫、发热）、脓肿（波动感、发热、脓性）、纤维腺瘤（质韧、无压痛、与哺乳无关）、妊娠相关乳腺癌（罕见但见于年轻女性——血性乳头溢液、质硬不规则包块、淋巴结肿大）

- **Key complication to know:** Secondary infection of a galactocele transforms it into a breast abscess requiring incision and drainage plus antistaphylococcal antibiotics; early FNA prevents this progression\
  **重要并发症:** 乳汁潴留囊肿继发感染转变为乳腺脓肿，需切开引流加抗葡萄球菌抗生素；早期FNA可预防此进展

- **Variant — non-lactating galactocele:** Can occur in women who recently stopped breast-feeding within weeks to months; same cystic presentation, same FNA management\
  **题目变式——非哺乳期乳汁潴留囊肿:** 可见于近期（数周至数月内）停止哺乳的女性；同样的囊性表现，同样的FNA处理

- **Step 2 CK test-taking tip:** Any postpartum cystic breast mass without fever → galactocele → FNA; any postpartum breast tenderness with fever → mastitis → dicloxacillin; fluctuant + fever + failure of antibiotics → abscess → I&D; remembering this three-step triage covers \>90% of postpartum breast question variants\
  **Step 2 CK答题技巧:** 产后囊性乳腺包块无发热→乳汁潴留囊肿→FNA；产后乳腺压痛伴发热→乳腺炎→双氯西林；波动感+发热+抗生素无效→脓肿→切开引流；记住这三步分诊可覆盖\>90%的产后乳腺题目变式

# Question 45 — Innocent (Benign) Heart Murmur / 良性（功能性）心脏杂音

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>An <strong>18-year-old man</strong> is brought to the physician 1 hour after he felt <strong>light-headed while playing basketball</strong>. He has <strong>not had chest pain, palpitations, or shortness of breath</strong>. He has no history of serious illness and takes no medications. His <strong>father died in a motor vehicle collision at the age of 35 years</strong>. There is <strong>no family history of serious illness</strong>. The patient's <strong>pulse is 80/min</strong>, and <strong>blood pressure is 115/85 mm Hg</strong>. There is no jugular venous distension. Pulmonary examination shows no abnormalities. A diagram of cardiac auscultation is shown. <strong>The murmur does not change with inspiration, position, or Valsalva maneuver.</strong> An <strong>ECG shows no abnormalities.</strong> Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Aortic valve repair<br />
B) Implantation of a cardiac defibrillator<br />
C) Recommendation not to play competitive sports<br />
D) Warfarin therapy<br />
E) No management is indicated at this time</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>18-year-old male athlete, light-headed during basketball<br />
18岁男性，打篮球时头晕</td>
<td>Young athletes commonly have innocent flow murmurs; exertional presyncope without syncope is less alarming than true syncope<br />
年轻运动员常有功能性血流杂音；运动性头晕但无晕厥，危险性远低于真正晕厥</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Father died in MVA at age 35 — NOT sudden cardiac death<br />
父亲35岁死于车祸，非心源性猝死</td>
<td>Only inherited cardiac conditions (HCM, long QT) raise familial risk; MVA death is unrelated to cardiac genetics<br />
只有遗传性心脏病（HCM、长QT）才提高家族风险；车祸死亡与心脏遗传无关</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No family history of serious illness<br />
无严重疾病家族史</td>
<td>Eliminates heritable arrhythmia syndromes and cardiomyopathies as background risk<br />
排除遗传性心律失常综合征和心肌病的背景风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Murmur unchanged with Valsalva, position, or inspiration<br />
杂音对Valsalva手法、体位、呼吸均无变化</td>
<td>HCM murmur intensifies with Valsalva (↓ preload); right-sided murmurs increase with inspiration; absence of dynamic change argues against obstructive pathology<br />
HCM杂音随Valsalva增强（前负荷↓）；右心杂音随吸气增强；无动态变化反对梗阻性病理</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ECG shows no abnormalities<br />
心电图无异常</td>
<td>Excludes long QT (QTc prolongation), delta waves (WPW), LVH (HCM), and conduction defects<br />
排除长QT（QTc延长）、δ波（WPW）、左室肥厚（HCM）及传导异常</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No chest pain, syncope, or palpitations<br />
无胸痛、晕厥或心悸</td>
<td>Absence of high-risk cardiac symptoms strongly argues against dangerous structural or electrical etiology<br />
无高危心脏症状，强烈反对危险性结构或电生理病因</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Innocent murmurs** arise from **turbulent blood flow** through normal cardiac structures — not from valvular disease, septal defects, or outflow tract obstruction：

**功能性杂音**由正常心脏结构内的**湍流血液**产生——并非来自瓣膜病、间隔缺损或流出道梗阻：

- High-output states (exercise, anemia, fever, pregnancy) amplify physiologic turbulence and can unmask or intensify innocent murmurs\
  高心输出量状态（运动、贫血、发热、妊娠）放大生理性湍流，可显现或加重功能性杂音

- Still's murmur (most common in children 3–7 years): vibratory/musical quality, grade 1–3/6, midsystolic, heard best at left lower sternal border\
  Still杂音（3–7岁儿童最常见）：振动感/音乐感，1–3/6级，收缩中期，左下胸骨旁最清晰

- Pulmonary flow murmur: soft ejection murmur at left upper sternal border, common in adolescents and thin-chested individuals\
  肺动脉血流杂音：左上胸骨旁柔和喷射性杂音，青少年和胸壁薄者常见

- Unlike pathologic murmurs, innocent murmurs produce no thrill, no fixed S2 split, and no added heart sounds (S3/S4)\
  与病理性杂音不同，功能性杂音无震颤、无固定S2分裂、无额外心音（S3/S4）

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Diastolic murmurs and holosystolic murmurs are NEVER innocent — they always require echocardiographic evaluation.

**解剖小窍门:** 舒张期杂音和全收缩期杂音从来不是良性的——始终需要超声心动图评估。

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Observation Only / 正确答案 (E) — 仅观察随访

**No management** is appropriate for this healthy adolescent with a benign flow murmur and no risk factors for serious cardiac disease：

**无需干预**适用于该健康青少年——有良性血流杂音但无严重心脏病危险因素：

- No high-risk cardiac symptoms: no syncope (only mild presyncope), no chest pain, no palpitations\
  无高危心脏症状：无晕厥（仅轻微晕厥前兆）、无胸痛、无心悸

- No family history of sudden cardiac death or heritable cardiac conditions\
  无心源性猝死或遗传性心脏病家族史

- Normal ECG excludes conduction abnormalities and arrhythmogenic substrates\
  心电图正常，排除传导异常及致心律失常基质

- Murmur without dynamic change rules out HCM (which amplifies with Valsalva due to reduced preload)\
  杂音无动态变化，排除HCM（HCM因前负荷减少而在Valsalva时增强）

**Diagnosis:** Benign/innocent heart murmur — a grade 1–3 midsystolic murmur from turbulent normal blood flow through a structurally normal heart.

**诊断:** 良性/功能性心脏杂音——湍流正常血液经过结构正常的心脏所产生的1–3级收缩中期杂音。

**Treatment:** Reassurance and observation; return for evaluation if symptoms develop (syncope, chest pain, palpitations, exercise intolerance).

**治疗:** 安慰和观察随访；如出现症状（晕厥、胸痛、心悸、运动不耐受）则返诊评估。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Aortic valve repair<br />
A — 主动脉瓣修复</td>
<td>Requires structural valve pathology; bicuspid/stenotic aortic valve would show absent or diminished S2, paradoxical S2 splitting, and murmur radiating to carotids; none present here<br />
需要结构性瓣膜病变；主动脉瓣二叶畸形/狭窄会出现S2消失或减弱、S2矛盾分裂、杂音向颈动脉放射；本例均无</td>
<td>Aortic stenosis: soft/absent S2, carotid radiation, ECG LVH, delayed carotid upstroke / 主动脉瓣狭窄：S2减弱/消失、颈动脉放射、心电图左室肥厚、颈动脉搏动延迟</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Implantation of a cardiac defibrillator<br />
B — 植入心脏除颤器</td>
<td>ICD indicated for HCM with high sudden-death risk or congenital long QT syndrome (torsades de pointes risk); patient has no family history, normal ECG, and no syncope<br />
ICD适用于猝死高风险HCM或先天性长QT综合征（尖端扭转风险）；本例无家族史、心电图正常、无晕厥</td>
<td>HCM: Valsalva amplifies murmur, ECG shows LVH + septal Q waves; long QT: QTc &gt; 440 ms (men) / HCM：Valsalva增强杂音，心电图左室肥厚+间隔Q波；长QT：QTc&gt;440ms（男）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Recommendation not to play competitive sports<br />
C — 建议不参加竞技运动</td>
<td>Sports restriction reserved for HCM, severe aortic stenosis, long QT, Marfan syndrome — none suggested here; an innocent murmur is NOT a contraindication to athletics<br />
运动限制仅适用于HCM、重度主动脉瓣狭窄、长QT、马凡综合征——本例均无；良性杂音不是体育运动的禁忌证</td>
<td>Sports restriction triggers: HCM + syncope or family SCD, or documented dangerous arrhythmia / 运动限制触发条件：HCM+晕厥或家族猝死，或记录在案的危险性心律失常</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Warfarin therapy<br />
D — 华法林治疗</td>
<td>Warfarin for ASD/VSD complicated by paradoxical thromboembolism; ASD presents with fixed split S2; VSD has a harsh holosystolic murmur — neither auscultatory finding is present<br />
华法林用于ASD/VSD并发矛盾栓塞；ASD有固定分裂S2；VSD有粗糙全收缩期杂音——本例均无上述听诊特征</td>
<td>ASD: fixed split S2; VSD: holosystolic, loudest at left lower sternal border, often with thrill / ASD：固定分裂S2；VSD：全收缩期，左下胸骨旁最响，常伴震颤</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — No management is indicated at this time ✓<br />
E — 目前无需处理 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — benign flow murmur in an asymptomatic adolescent with normal ECG, no family history of cardiac disease, and no dynamic murmur changes; observation is appropriate<br />
正确——无症状青少年的良性血流杂音，心电图正常，无心脏病家族史，杂音无动态变化；观察随访即可</td>
<td>No risk factors + no symptoms + normal ECG = innocent murmur, no intervention needed / 无危险因素+无症状+心电图正常=功能性杂音，无需干预</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Choice C (no competitive sports) — it feels intuitively protective for a young athlete, but sports restriction requires documented high-risk cardiac pathology, not a benign murmur with a normal workup.*

选项C（不参加竞技运动）是最具迷惑性的干扰项——对年轻运动员的保护本能让人倾向于选它，但运动限制必须有记录在案的高危心脏病理，而非检查正常的良性杂音。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Innocent vs. Pathological Heart Murmur / 功能性杂音 vs. 病理性杂音鉴别

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Feature</strong><br />
<strong>特征</strong></th>
<th><strong>Innocent Murmur</strong><br />
<strong>功能性杂音</strong></th>
<th><strong>Pathological Murmur</strong><br />
<strong>病理性杂音</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Timing<br />
时相</td>
<td>Midsystolic only<br />
仅收缩中期</td>
<td>Holosystolic, diastolic, or continuous<br />
全收缩期、舒张期或连续性</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Grade &amp; thrill<br />
级别与震颤</td>
<td>≤ 3/6, no thrill<br />
≤3/6级，无震颤</td>
<td>Often ≥ 3/6; thrill may be present<br />
常≥3/6级；可有震颤</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>S1/S2 quality<br />
心音质量</td>
<td>Normal S1 and S2<br />
S1和S2正常</td>
<td>Absent/diminished S2 (AS); fixed split S2 (ASD); added S3/S4<br />
S2消失/减弱（主动脉瓣狭窄）；固定分裂S2（ASD）；附加S3/S4</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Dynamic maneuver response<br />
动态手法反应</td>
<td>May soften with Valsalva/standing (↓ preload)<br />
Valsalva/站立时可减弱（前负荷↓）</td>
<td>HCM louder with Valsalva; fixed intensity in structural valvular disease<br />
HCM随Valsalva增强；结构性瓣膜病强度固定不变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ECG<br />
心电图</td>
<td>Normal<br />
正常</td>
<td>LVH, delta waves (WPW), QTc prolongation, RBBB (ASD)<br />
左室肥厚、δ波（WPW）、QTc延长、右束支传导阻滞（ASD）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Symptoms<br />
症状</td>
<td>Asymptomatic<br />
无症状</td>
<td>Syncope, chest pain, dyspnea, exercise intolerance, palpitations<br />
晕厥、胸痛、呼吸困难、运动不耐受、心悸</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Management<br />
处理</td>
<td>Reassurance and observation<br />
安慰和观察随访</td>
<td>Echocardiography ± cardiology referral ± intervention<br />
超声心动图±心脏科转诊±干预</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**An asymptomatic young athlete with a midsystolic murmur unchanged by dynamic maneuvers, a normal ECG, and no family history of sudden cardiac death has an innocent murmur requiring only observation.**

**无症状年轻运动员出现收缩中期杂音，动态手法无变化，心电图正常，无猝死家族史，为功能性杂音，仅需观察随访。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — SILENT (Innocent Murmur Checklist) / 记忆钩 — SILENT（良性杂音核查清单）:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>S</strong>ystolic only (midsystolic, never holosystolic or diastolic) — diastolic = always pathologic / 仅收缩期（收缩中期，绝非全收缩期或舒张期）——舒张期杂音=始终病理性<br />
• <strong>I</strong>solated finding — no added heart sounds, no thrill, no abnormal S2 / 孤立发现——无额外心音、无震颤、无异常S2<br />
• <strong>L</strong>ow grade (≤ 3/6) — louder murmurs demand echocardiographic evaluation / 低级别（≤3/6）——更响的杂音需超声心动图评估<br />
• <strong>E</strong>CG normal — any ECG abnormality triggers echo immediately / 心电图正常——任何心电图异常立即触发超声心动图检查<br />
• <strong>N</strong>o family history of SCD or heritable cardiac disease / 无猝死或遗传性心脏病家族史<br />
• <strong>T</strong>hrill absent — presence of thrill = structural heart disease, never innocent / 无震颤——震颤存在=结构性心脏病，绝非良性</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Innocent Murmur & Dangerous Mimics / 高频知识表 — 功能性杂音与危险鉴别诊断

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Still's murmur<br />
Still杂音</td>
<td>Most common innocent murmur in children age 3–7; vibratory/musical quality, grade 1–3/6, midsystolic, left lower sternal border; softens or disappears with standing<br />
3–7岁儿童最常见功能性杂音；振动感/音乐感，1–3/6级，收缩中期，左下胸骨旁；站立时减弱或消失</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pulmonary flow murmur<br />
肺动脉血流杂音</td>
<td>Soft midsystolic ejection murmur at left upper sternal border; common in adolescents, pregnant women, and high-output states (anemia, fever)<br />
左上胸骨旁柔和收缩中期喷射性杂音；青少年、孕妇及高心输出量状态（贫血、发热）常见</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>HCM murmur features<br />
HCM杂音特点</td>
<td>Harsh systolic murmur at LLSB; increases with Valsalva and standing (↓ preload); decreases with squatting and hand-grip (↑ preload/afterload); ECG shows LVH + septal Q waves<br />
左下胸骨旁粗糙收缩期杂音；Valsalva和站立时增强（前负荷↓）；下蹲和握拳时减弱（前负荷/后负荷↑）；心电图左室肥厚+间隔Q波</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ASD murmur features<br />
房间隔缺损杂音特点</td>
<td>Fixed split S2 (pathognomonic); soft pulmonary ejection murmur from increased pulmonary flow; associated with RBBB on ECG; risk of paradoxical embolism<br />
固定分裂S2（特征性）；因肺血流增多产生柔和肺动脉喷射性杂音；心电图常有右束支传导阻滞；有矛盾栓塞风险</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Red flags mandating echocardiography<br />
需超声心动图的危险信号</td>
<td>Diastolic murmur; holosystolic murmur; murmur intensifying with Valsalva; grade ≥ 4 murmur; abnormal ECG; syncope; family history of SCD or cardiomyopathy<br />
舒张期杂音；全收缩期杂音；Valsalva增强的杂音；≥4级杂音；心电图异常；晕厥；猝死或心肌病家族史</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Long QT syndrome<br />
长QT综合征</td>
<td>No murmur; exertional syncope or sudden death, especially with auditory triggers (congenital Romano-Ward); QTc &gt; 460 ms (women) / &gt; 440 ms (men); treated with beta-blockers ± ICD<br />
无杂音；运动性晕厥或猝死，先天性Romano-Ward型可由声音触发；QTc&gt;460ms（女）/&gt;440ms（男）；β受体阻滞剂±ICD治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Sports participation guidelines<br />
运动参与指南</td>
<td>AHA/ACC: innocent murmur is NOT a contraindication to competitive sports; restrict only with HCM, severe aortic stenosis, long QT, Marfan with aortic dilation<br />
AHA/ACC：功能性杂音不是竞技运动禁忌证；仅限制HCM、重度主动脉瓣狭窄、长QT、主动脉扩张的马凡综合征</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of exertional presyncope in young athletes:** HCM, long QT syndrome, WPW, vasovagal syncope, aortic stenosis, anomalous coronary artery origin — an innocent murmur itself does NOT cause presyncope or syncope\
  **年轻运动员运动性晕厥前兆鉴别:** HCM、长QT综合征、WPW、血管迷走性晕厥、主动脉瓣狭窄、冠状动脉异常起源——良性杂音本身不引起晕厥前兆或晕厥

- **Variant — when echo is warranted despite benign appearance:** If the examiner is uncertain, the patient or family is highly anxious, or any single red flag exists, echocardiography is safe, non-invasive, and definitively excludes structural disease\
  **题目变式——即使外观良性何时仍需超声:** 若检查者不确定、患者或家属高度焦虑、或存在任何单一危险信号，超声心动图安全无创，可明确排除结构性心脏病

- **Key complication of missed HCM:** Sudden cardiac death during competitive athletics — HCM is the leading cause of sudden death in young athletes in the United States, accounting for ~36% of cases\
  **漏诊HCM的关键并发症:** 竞技运动时猝死——HCM是美国年轻运动员猝死的首要原因，约占36%

- **Cause of death distinction — clinical trap:** Father dying in a motor vehicle accident at age 35 is a deliberate distractor; only unexplained sudden death, cardiac arrest, or known heritable cardiac disease in a first-degree relative constitutes a true cardiac risk flag\
  **死因区分——临床陷阱:** 父亲35岁死于车祸是刻意设置的干扰项；只有一级亲属的不明原因猝死、心脏骤停或已知遗传性心脏病才构成真正的心脏危险信号

# Question 46 — Acute Pulmonary Embolism / 急性肺栓塞

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>37-year-old woman</strong> is brought to the emergency department 30 minutes after an <strong>episode of syncope</strong> at a shopping mall. She says she had <strong>shortness of breath</strong> and was <strong>sweating</strong> before she passed out. She has a childhood history of asthma. She currently has panic disorder and gastroesophageal reflux disease. Current medications include sertraline, omeprazole, and an <strong>oral contraceptive</strong>. On arrival, she is alert and oriented to person, place, and time. Her temperature is 37.4°C (99.3°F), <strong>pulse is 110/min</strong>, and <strong>blood pressure is 90/60 mm Hg</strong>. <strong>Pulse oximetry on room air shows an oxygen saturation of 90%.</strong> Examination, including neurologic examination, shows no abnormalities. Laboratory studies show: Hemoglobin 12 g/dL, Hematocrit 36%, Leukocyte count 9000/mm³. Arterial blood gas analysis on room air: <strong>pH 7.46</strong>, <strong>PCO₂ 30 mm Hg</strong>, <strong>PO₂ 62 mm Hg</strong>.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most likely explanation for these findings?</strong></p>
<p>A) Asthma<br />
B) Congestive heart failure<br />
C) Panic episode<br />
D) Pneumonia<br />
E) Pulmonary embolism</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Oral contraceptive use<br />
口服避孕药使用</td>
<td>Estrogen-containing OCPs increase VTE risk 3–5× by promoting a hypercoagulable state<br />
含雌激素的避孕药通过促进高凝状态使静脉血栓栓塞风险升高 3–5 倍</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Unexplained syncope<br />
不明原因晕厥</td>
<td>PE can present as syncope due to acute right heart strain and decreased cardiac output; must trigger PE workup<br />
肺栓塞可因急性右心室负荷增加和心输出量下降导致晕厥，应立即触发肺栓塞排查</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Tachycardia 110/min + Hypotension 90/60 mm Hg<br />
心动过速 + 低血压</td>
<td>Hemodynamic compromise suggests massive PE with right ventricular strain and impending cardiovascular collapse<br />
血流动力学损害提示大面积肺栓塞伴右心室受累和即将发生的心血管崩溃</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>SpO₂ 90% / PO₂ 62 mm Hg on room air<br />
室内空气下血氧饱和度 90% / 氧分压 62 mmHg</td>
<td>Significant hypoxemia indicates true V/Q mismatch — hallmark of PE; cannot be explained by panic alone<br />
明显低氧血症提示真正的通气/血流比例失调——肺栓塞标志性表现；单纯惊恐发作不能解释</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>pH 7.46 / PCO₂ 30 mm Hg (respiratory alkalosis)<br />
pH 7.46 / PCO₂ 30 mmHg（呼吸性碱中毒）</td>
<td>Hyperventilation driven by hypoxemia; combined with elevated A-a gradient (~50 mmHg) distinguishes PE from panic disorder<br />
低氧血症驱动的过度换气；联合升高的A-a梯度（约50 mmHg）将肺栓塞与惊恐障碍区分开来</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>WBC 9000/mm³ (normal), temperature 37.4°C (afebrile)<br />
白细胞正常、体温 37.4°C（无发热）</td>
<td>Argues strongly against pneumonia or sepsis as the etiology<br />
有力反对肺炎或败血症作为病因</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Neurologic examination: no abnormalities<br />
神经系统查体：无异常</td>
<td>Excludes seizure, stroke, or other neurologic causes of syncope<br />
排除癫痫、卒中或其他神经系统晕厥病因</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Pulmonary embolism** obstructs pulmonary arterial blood flow, creating **ventilation-perfusion (V/Q) mismatch** — alveoli are ventilated but not perfused — resulting in **hypoxemia**, reflex **tachypnea**, and acute right heart strain:

**肺栓塞**阻塞肺动脉血流，产生**通气/血流（V/Q）比例失调**——肺泡有通气但无灌注——导致**低氧血症**、反射性**呼吸急促**和急性右心室负荷增加：

- Thrombus (usually from DVT) lodges in pulmonary artery → dead space ventilation → V/Q mismatch → hypoxemia\
  血栓（通常来自深静脉血栓）嵌顿于肺动脉 → 死腔通气 → V/Q比例失调 → 低氧血症

- Hypoxemia triggers hyperventilation → PCO₂ ↓ → respiratory alkalosis (pH ↑)\
  低氧血症触发过度换气 → PCO₂↓ → 呼吸性碱中毒（pH↑）

- A-a gradient = PAO₂ − PaO₂ ≈ 112 − 62 = 50 mm Hg (normal for age 37 ≈ 13 mm Hg) — markedly elevated\
  A-a梯度 = PAO₂ − PaO₂ ≈ 112 − 62 = 50 mmHg（37岁正常值≈13 mmHg）——明显升高

- Acute right ventricular strain → ↓ cardiac output → syncope + hypotension\
  急性右心室负荷增加 → 心输出量↓ → 晕厥 + 低血压

- Reflex tachycardia attempts to compensate for reduced stroke volume\
  反射性心动过速试图补偿每搏输出量降低

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Most PEs originate from proximal lower extremity DVT; thrombus travels via the inferior vena cava → right atrium → right ventricle → pulmonary arteries.

**解剖小窍门:** 大多数肺栓塞起源于下肢近端深静脉血栓；血栓经下腔静脉 → 右心房 → 右心室 → 肺动脉迁移。

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Pulmonary Embolism / 正确答案 (E) — 肺栓塞

**Pulmonary embolism** is obstruction of the pulmonary vasculature (most commonly by thrombus from DVT) causing V/Q mismatch, hypoxemia, and acute right heart strain, classically presenting with dyspnea, chest pain, and hypoxemia:

**肺栓塞**是肺血管阻塞（最常见为深静脉血栓），导致V/Q失调、低氧血症和急性右心室负荷增加，经典表现为呼吸困难、胸痛和低氧血症：

- Classic triad: dyspnea + pleuritic chest pain + hemoptysis (only ~30% have all three; atypical presentations are common)\
  经典三联征：呼吸困难 + 胸膜炎性胸痛 + 咯血（仅约30%同时具备三项；不典型表现常见）

- ABG signature: PO₂ ↓ + pH ↑ + PCO₂ ↓ + elevated A-a gradient (V/Q mismatch, not present in panic disorder)\
  ABG特征：PO₂↓ + pH↑ + PCO₂↓ + 肺泡-动脉氧梯度升高（V/Q失调，惊恐障碍中不出现）

- This patient: OCP use + syncope + tachycardia + hypotension + SpO₂ 90% → consistent with massive PE\
  本例：避孕药 + 晕厥 + 心动过速 + 低血压 + SpO₂ 90% → 符合大面积肺栓塞

**Diagnosis:** Clinical scoring (Wells criteria) → CT pulmonary angiography (gold standard); D-dimer if low pretest probability; V/Q scan if CT contraindicated

**诊断:** 临床评分（Wells标准）→ CT肺动脉造影（金标准）；低预测概率可查D-二聚体；CT禁忌时行V/Q显像

**Treatment:** Anticoagulation (IV unfractionated heparin as initial therapy); systemic thrombolytics (alteplase) for massive PE with hemodynamic instability; surgical or catheter-directed embolectomy if thrombolytics contraindicated

**治疗:** 抗凝（初始治疗首选静脉普通肝素）；血流动力学不稳定的大面积肺栓塞用全身溶栓（阿替普酶）；溶栓禁忌时考虑外科手术或导管取栓

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Asthma<br />
A — 哮喘</td>
<td>Asthma exacerbation causes wheezing, prolonged expiration, and obstructive pattern; syncope is rare; no wheeze on exam; childhood history alone does not explain current acute presentation<br />
哮喘急性发作引起喘息、呼气延长和阻塞性模式；晕厥罕见；体格检查无喘鸣音；仅有儿童期病史不能解释当前急性表现</td>
<td>Asthma → wheezing + obstructive ABG pattern; this patient has hypoxemia + elevated A-a gradient with no wheezing<br />
哮喘 → 喘息 + 阻塞性ABG改变；本例无喘息但有低氧血症和升高的A-a梯度</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Congestive heart failure<br />
B — 充血性心力衰竭</td>
<td>No JVD, peripheral edema, bilateral crackles, S3/S4 gallop, or ascites; age 37 makes de novo CHF very unlikely without underlying structural disease<br />
无颈静脉怒张、周围性水肿、双侧湿啰音、奔马律或腹水；37岁无基础结构性心脏病者新发心衰极不可能</td>
<td>CHF → bilateral crackles + S3 + edema + elevated BNP; physical exam here is entirely normal<br />
心衰 → 双侧湿啰音 + S3 + 水肿 + BNP升高；本例查体完全正常</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Panic episode<br />
C — 惊恐发作</td>
<td>Panic causes respiratory alkalosis but PO₂ and A-a gradient should be NORMAL (no true V/Q mismatch); prior panic disorder does not exclude PE; PE must be ruled out first<br />
惊恐发作引起呼吸性碱中毒，但PO₂和A-a梯度应正常（无真正V/Q失调）；既往惊恐障碍不排除肺栓塞；必须先排除肺栓塞</td>
<td>Panic → respiratory alkalosis + normal PO₂ + normal A-a gradient; this patient has PO₂ 62 + A-a ≈ 50 mmHg<br />
惊恐 → 呼吸性碱中毒 + PO₂正常 + A-a梯度正常；本例PO₂ 62 + A-a约50 mmHg</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Pneumonia<br />
D — 肺炎</td>
<td>No fever, no productive cough, no leukocytosis (WBC 9000 normal); acute-onset syncope is not typical of pneumonia<br />
无发热、无咳痰、白细胞不高（WBC 9000正常）；急性起病晕厥不是肺炎的典型表现</td>
<td>Pneumonia → fever + productive cough + leukocytosis + infiltrate on CXR<br />
肺炎 → 发热 + 咳痰 + 白细胞增多 + 胸片浸润影</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Pulmonary embolism ✓<br />
E — 肺栓塞 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — OCP use (hypercoagulable) + syncope + tachycardia + hypotension + SpO₂ 90% + elevated A-a gradient all converge on massive PE<br />
正确——避孕药（高凝状态）+ 晕厥 + 心动过速 + 低血压 + SpO₂ 90% + 升高的A-a梯度均指向大面积肺栓塞</td>
<td>All clinical and ABG features fit V/Q mismatch from pulmonary arterial obstruction<br />
所有临床及ABG特征均符合肺动脉阻塞所致V/Q失调</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most dangerous trap is panic episode (C): this patient has a known panic disorder, and both panic and PE produce hyperventilation with respiratory alkalosis — the critical separator is the A-a gradient, which is elevated in PE (V/Q mismatch) but normal in panic (no intrinsic lung pathology).*

最危险的陷阱是惊恐发作（C）：本患者有已知惊恐障碍，且惊恐发作与肺栓塞均产生伴呼吸性碱中毒的过度换气——关键鉴别点是肺泡-动脉氧梯度，肺栓塞时升高（V/Q失调），惊恐发作时正常（无内在肺部病变）。

晕厥</td>

<td>Rare; usually presyncope only<br />
罕见；通常仅有晕厥前兆</td>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A woman on oral contraceptives presenting with unexplained syncope, hemodynamic instability, hypoxemia, and elevated A-a gradient has pulmonary embolism until proven otherwise — do not anchor on her panic disorder history.**

**口服避孕药的女性出现不明原因晕厥、血流动力学不稳定、低氧血症及升高的肺泡-动脉氧梯度，在排除前应视为肺栓塞——不要锚定于其惊恐障碍病史。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — PE Risk Factors "CLOTS" / 记忆钩 — 肺栓塞危险因素 "CLOTS（凝块）":</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>C</strong>ancer / Coagulopathy — malignancy activates coagulation; inherited thrombophilia (Factor V Leiden, Protein C/S deficiency) / 癌症/凝血病——恶性肿瘤激活凝血；遗传性血栓形成倾向（Factor V Leiden、蛋白C/S缺乏）<br />
• <strong>L</strong>ong immobility — prolonged bed rest, long flights, post-operative state / 长期制动——长期卧床、长途飞行、术后状态<br />
• <strong>O</strong>ral contraceptives / Obesity — estrogen raises VTE risk 3–5×; obesity promotes venous stasis / 口服避孕药/肥胖——雌激素使VTE风险升高3–5倍；肥胖促进静脉淤血<br />
• <strong>T</strong>rauma / surgery — vessel wall injury combined with immobility / 外伤/手术——血管壁损伤联合制动<br />
• <strong>S</strong>tasis / prior DVT — venous insufficiency; prior clot confers high recurrence risk / 血液淤滞/既往深静脉血栓——静脉功能不全；既往血栓复发风险高</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Pulmonary Embolism Diagnosis and Management / 高频知识表 — 肺栓塞诊断与处理

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Wells Criteria for PE<br />
Wells肺栓塞评分标准</td>
<td>DVT signs (+3), alternative Dx less likely (+3), HR &gt;100 (+1.5), immobility/surgery (+1.5), prior DVT/PE (+1.5), hemoptysis (+1), malignancy (+1); score ≤4 = low/moderate probability; &gt;4 = high probability → proceed to CTPA<br />
DVT体征(+3)、其他诊断不太可能(+3)、HR&gt;100(+1.5)、制动/手术(+1.5)、既往DVT/PE(+1.5)、咯血(+1)、恶性肿瘤(+1)；≤4=低/中概率；&gt;4=高概率→直接行CT肺动脉造影</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ABG Pattern in PE<br />
肺栓塞动脉血气模式</td>
<td>Hypoxemia (PO₂ ↓) + respiratory alkalosis (pH ↑, PCO₂ ↓) + elevated A-a gradient; A-a gradient = PAO₂ − PaO₂; normal &lt; 10–15 mmHg; markedly elevated in PE due to V/Q mismatch<br />
低氧血症(PO₂↓)+呼吸性碱中毒(pH↑,PCO₂↓)+肺泡-动脉氧梯度升高；A-a梯度=PAO₂−PaO₂；正常&lt;10–15 mmHg；V/Q失调时显著升高</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>ECG Findings in PE<br />
肺栓塞心电图表现</td>
<td>Most common: sinus tachycardia; classic (but rare) S1Q3T3 = deep S wave in lead I, Q wave + T-wave inversion in lead III; right bundle branch block; new right heart strain pattern<br />
最常见：窦性心动过速；经典（但罕见）S1Q3T3 = I导联深S波，III导联Q波+T波倒置；右束支传导阻滞；新发右心室负荷增加表现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>CT Pulmonary Angiography<br />
CT肺动脉造影</td>
<td>Gold standard for PE diagnosis; demonstrates filling defects in pulmonary arteries; preferred over V/Q scan when CXR is abnormal or patient is unstable<br />
肺栓塞诊断金标准；显示肺动脉充盈缺损；胸片异常或患者不稳定时优先于V/Q显像</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Massive vs. Submassive PE Classification<br />
大面积与次大面积肺栓塞分类</td>
<td>Massive PE: SBP &lt;90 mm Hg or hemodynamic instability → thrombolytics (alteplase) ± embolectomy; Submassive: RV dysfunction without hypotension → consider thrombolytics; Stable: anticoagulation alone<br />
大面积：SBP &lt;90 mmHg或血流动力学不稳定 → 溶栓（阿替普酶）± 取栓；次大面积：RV功能障碍但无低血压 → 考虑溶栓；稳定型：单独抗凝</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>OCP and VTE Risk<br />
口服避孕药与VTE风险</td>
<td>Estrogen raises VTE risk 3–5×; risk amplified with additional thrombophilia, obesity, or smoking; progestin-only pills (mini-pill) carry significantly lower VTE risk and are preferred in high-risk patients<br />
雌激素使VTE风险增加3–5倍；合并血栓形成倾向、肥胖或吸烟时风险更高；单孕激素避孕药VTE风险显著较低，高风险患者优先考虑</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of unexplained syncope:** consider PE, vasovagal, arrhythmia (SVT, VT), aortic stenosis, hypertrophic cardiomyopathy, and orthostatic hypotension — PE must be actively excluded given its lethality\
  **不明原因晕厥的鉴别诊断:** 需考虑肺栓塞、血管迷走性晕厥、心律失常（SVT、VT）、主动脉瓣狭窄、肥厚型心肌病和体位性低血压——肺栓塞因其致死性必须主动排除

- **Key complication of massive PE:** acute cor pulmonale (acute right heart failure) with risk of cardiovascular collapse; RV dilation on echo is a poor prognostic sign; treat with IV heparin + systemic thrombolysis (alteplase 100 mg over 2 hours)\
  **大面积肺栓塞的关键并发症:** 急性肺心病（急性右心衰竭）伴心血管崩溃风险；超声心动图显示右室扩张是预后不良征象；静脉肝素联合全身溶栓（阿替普酶2小时内100 mg）

- **Variant — PE mimicking panic disorder:** coexistence of panic disorder should never delay PE workup; the A-a gradient is the decisive test — panic produces no V/Q mismatch and therefore a normal A-a gradient despite respiratory alkalosis\
  **题目变式——肺栓塞模拟惊恐障碍:** 惊恐障碍共存不应延误肺栓塞排查；A-a梯度是决定性检查——惊恐发作不产生V/Q失调，因此尽管有呼吸性碱中毒A-a梯度仍正常

- **Risk factor counseling:** women on combined OCPs with additional VTE risk factors (obesity, thrombophilia, smoking, immobility) should switch to progestin-only contraception (mini-pill, levonorgestrel IUD) or non-hormonal methods; after a PE, OCPs are permanently contraindicated\
  **危险因素咨询:** 使用复方避孕药且有额外VTE风险因素（肥胖、血栓形成倾向、吸烟、制动）的女性应改用单孕激素避孕（纯孕激素片、左炔诺孕酮宫内节育器）或非激素方法；发生肺栓塞后口服避孕药永久禁用

# Question 47 — Multiple Myeloma / 多发性骨髓瘤

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>62-year-old woman</strong> comes to the physician because of a <strong>2-month history of generalized fatigue</strong> and <strong>mild low back pain</strong>. She has not had any other symptoms. She has no history of serious illness and takes no medications. Her last health maintenance examination was 10 months ago, and a complete blood count at that time was within the reference range. Examination today shows no abnormalities. Laboratory studies show: <strong>Hematocrit 30%</strong>, <strong>Mean corpuscular volume 103 μm³</strong>, Leukocyte count 8200/mm³ (Segmented neutrophils 67%, Bands 4%, Lymphocytes 29%), Platelet count 165,000/mm³, <strong>Serum Ca²⁺ 10.9 mg/dL</strong>, <strong>Creatinine 1.8 mg/dL</strong>. A blood smear is shown.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate next step to confirm the diagnosis?</strong></p>
<p>A) Liver function tests<br />
B) Measurement of serum vitamin B12 (cobalamin) concentration<br />
C) Serum iron studies<br />
D) Colonoscopy<br />
E) Bone marrow biopsy</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />

<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>

<tbody>
<tr>
<td>62-year-old woman<br />
62岁女性</td>
<td>Multiple myeloma peaks after age 60; age is the strongest demographic risk factor<br />
多发性骨髓瘤好发于60岁以上，年龄是最重要的人口学危险因素</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Generalized fatigue + mild low back pain<br />
全身乏力 + 轻度腰背痛</td>

MM典型表现：贫血引起全身乏力+溶骨性病变引起骨痛</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>MCV 103 μm³ (macrocytic anemia)<br />
MCV 103（大细胞性贫血）</td>
<td>Rules out iron deficiency (microcytic); in MM, macrocytosis from rapid plasma cell proliferation consuming folate<br />
排除缺铁性贫血（小细胞）；MM中浆细胞快速增殖消耗叶酸导致大细胞性改变</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Serum Ca²⁺ 10.9 mg/dL (hypercalcemia)<br />
血钙10.9 mg/dL（高钙血症）</td>
<td>Osteoclast activation by myeloma cells releases calcium from bone; "C" in CRAB criteria<br />
骨髓瘤细胞激活破骨细胞，导致骨钙释放；属于CRAB标准中的"C"</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Creatinine 1.8 mg/dL (renal dysfunction)<br />
肌酐1.8 mg/dL（肾功能损害）</td>
<td>Light chain (Bence Jones protein) cast nephropathy plus hypercalcemia-induced renal vasoconstriction; "R" in CRAB<br />
轻链（Bence Jones蛋白）管型肾病+高钙血症致肾血管收缩；属于CRAB中的"R"</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>CBC normal 10 months ago → now anemic<br />
10个月前血常规正常→现在贫血</td>
<td>Documents rapid disease progression consistent with an acquired neoplastic process<br />
记录疾病快速进展，符合获得性肿瘤性疾病特征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Rouleaux formation on blood smear (implied by image)<br />
血涂片缗钱状排列（图片所示）</td>
<td>Hallmark of MM; paraprotein coats RBCs, reduces zeta potential, causing RBCs to stack like coins<br />
MM的标志性血涂片表现；副蛋白包被红细胞，降低静电斥力，红细胞叠放如硬币</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Multiple myeloma** arises from **neoplastic clonal proliferation of plasma cells** in the bone marrow, overproducing **monoclonal immunoglobulin (M protein)**. The downstream pathology follows directly from mass effect, protein deposition, and paracrine signaling:

**多发性骨髓瘤**源于骨髓中**浆细胞的肿瘤性克隆增殖**，过量产生**单克隆免疫球蛋白（M蛋白）**，后续病理改变直接来源于占位效应、蛋白沉积和旁分泌信号：

- Marrow infiltration by plasma cells → displaces normal hematopoiesis → **anemia**, leukopenia, thrombocytopenia\
  浆细胞浸润骨髓 → 挤压正常造血 → **贫血**、白细胞减少、血小板减少

- Myeloma cells secrete osteoclast-activating factors (IL-1, IL-6, RANKL) → **lytic bone lesions** → back pain + hypercalcemia\
  骨髓瘤细胞分泌破骨细胞活化因子（IL-1、IL-6、RANKL） → **溶骨性病变** → 骨痛+高钙血症

- Free light chains (Bence Jones proteins) deposit in renal tubules → **cast nephropathy** → renal dysfunction\
  游离轻链（Bence Jones蛋白）沉积于肾小管 → **管型肾病** → 肾功能损害

- Excess paraprotein coats RBCs → reduces electrostatic repulsion (zeta potential) → **rouleaux formation**\
  大量副蛋白包被红细胞 → 降低静电斥力（zeta电位） → **缗钱状排列**

- Rapid plasma cell division consumes folate → functional folate deficiency → **macrocytic anemia** (MCV \>100)\
  浆细胞快速分裂消耗叶酸 → 功能性叶酸缺乏 → **大细胞性贫血**（MCV \>100）

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Lytic myeloma lesions are "cold" on bone scan (no osteoblast activity) — a negative bone scan does NOT rule out MM; skeletal survey X-ray or MRI is required.

**解剖小窍门:** 骨髓瘤溶骨灶在骨扫描上为"冷区"（无成骨细胞活性）——骨扫描阴性不能排除MM，需行骨骼X线平片或MRI。

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Bone Marrow Biopsy / 正确答案 (E) — 骨髓活检

**Bone marrow biopsy** is the gold-standard confirmatory test for multiple myeloma, demonstrating clonal plasma cell infiltration exceeding 10% of marrow cellularity:

**骨髓活检**是确诊多发性骨髓瘤的金标准，可显示克隆性浆细胞超过骨髓细胞总量的10%：

- Clonal plasma cells \>10% on biopsy is the diagnostic threshold distinguishing MM from MGUS\
  活检示克隆性浆细胞\>10%是区分MM与意义未明单克隆丙球病（MGUS）的诊断界值

- Plasma cells appear large with eccentric nuclei and "clock-face/cartwheel" chromatin pattern\
  浆细胞体积大，核偏位，染色质呈"时钟面/车轮状"排列

- Immunohistochemistry confirms monoclonal kappa or lambda light chain restriction\
  免疫组化确认单克隆κ或λ轻链限制性表达

- Biopsy combined with SPEP, UPEP, and imaging establishes definitive diagnosis and guides staging\
  活检联合血清蛋白电泳、尿蛋白电泳及影像学，确立诊断并指导分期

**Diagnosis:** MM is confirmed when bone marrow biopsy shows \>10% clonal plasma cells plus at least one CRAB criterion or a myeloma-defining biomarker (free light chain ratio \>100, or \>1 focal lesion on MRI).

**诊断:** 骨髓活检示克隆性浆细胞\>10%，且伴至少1项CRAB标准或骨髓瘤定义性生物标志物（游离轻链比值\>100，或MRI\>1个局灶病变）时，确诊MM。

**Treatment:** Induction with VRd (bortezomib + lenalidomide + dexamethasone); transplant-eligible patients proceed to autologous stem cell transplant after induction.

**治疗:** VRd方案诱导（硼替佐米+来那度胺+地塞米松）；适合移植者诱导后行自体干细胞移植。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Liver function tests<br />
A — 肝功能检查</td>
<td>LFTs may be abnormal due to plasma cell infiltration of the liver, but are nonspecific and cannot confirm MM<br />
肝功能可因浆细胞浸润肝脏而异常，但无特异性，不能确诊MM</td>
<td>Nonspecific finding; biopsy is required for definitive diagnosis<br />
无特异性；确诊需骨髓活检</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Serum vitamin B12 (cobalamin) concentration<br />
B — 血清维生素B12浓度</td>
<td>B12 deficiency causes macrocytic anemia but cannot explain hypercalcemia or renal dysfunction; MM depletes folate, not B12<br />
B12缺乏可致大细胞贫血，但不能解释高钙血症或肾功能损害；MM消耗叶酸而非B12</td>
<td>B12 deficiency cannot produce hypercalcemia + renal failure; full CRAB picture points to MM<br />
B12缺乏不会引起高钙血症+肾衰竭；完整CRAB表现指向MM</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Serum iron studies<br />
C — 血清铁检查</td>
<td>Iron studies evaluate microcytic/hypochromic anemia from iron deficiency; MCV 103 (macrocytic) directly contradicts iron deficiency<br />
铁检查用于评估缺铁性小细胞低色素贫血；MCV 103（大细胞）直接排除缺铁</td>
<td>MCV 103 = macrocytic; iron deficiency = microcytic (MCV &lt;80)<br />
MCV 103=大细胞；缺铁=小细胞（MCV &lt;80）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Colonoscopy<br />
D — 结肠镜</td>
<td>Colonoscopy evaluates GI bleeding causing iron-deficiency anemia; inappropriate given macrocytosis and systemic CRAB findings<br />
结肠镜评估消化道出血引起的缺铁性贫血；本例大细胞贫血+系统性CRAB表现不适用</td>
<td>GI bleeding → microcytic anemia, not macrocytic + hypercalcemia + renal failure<br />
消化道出血→小细胞贫血，非大细胞贫血+高钙+肾损害</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Bone marrow biopsy ✓<br />
E — 骨髓活检 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Gold standard confirming MM by demonstrating &gt;10% clonal plasma cells<br />
正确——通过显示骨髓克隆性浆细胞&gt;10%确诊MM的金标准</td>
<td>Anemia + hypercalcemia + renal dysfunction = CRAB → confirm with biopsy<br />
贫血+高钙+肾功能损害=CRAB三联征→活检确诊</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The strongest distractor is (B) Vitamin B12 — MCV 103 naturally suggests megaloblastic anemia, but B12 deficiency cannot account for hypercalcemia (Ca 10.9) or renal impairment (Cr 1.8); when these three findings cluster together, always think CRAB/multiple myeloma first.*

最强干扰项是B（维生素B12）——MCV 103自然让人联想到巨幼细胞性贫血，但B12缺乏无法解释高钙血症（Ca 10.9）或肾功能损害（Cr 1.8）；当三者同时出现时，首先想到CRAB/多发性骨髓瘤。

通常无</td>

溶骨性"穿凿样"病变</td>

无</td>

无（可有骨量减少）</td>

标志性并发症</td>
<td>Renal failure, pathologic fractures, infections<br />
肾衰竭、病理性骨折、感染</td>
<td>~1%/year risk of progression to MM<br />
每年约1%进展为MM</td>
<td>Hyperviscosity syndrome, Raynaud's, cold agglutinins<br />
高黏滞血症综合征、雷诺现象、冷凝集素</td>
</tr>

确诊方式</td>
<td>Bone marrow biopsy &gt;10% plasma cells<br />
骨髓活检浆细胞&gt;10%</td>

观察随访；无症状者无需活检</td>
<td>Bone marrow biopsy (lymphoplasmacytic infiltration)<br />
骨髓活检（淋巴浆细胞浸润）</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A 62-year-old woman with macrocytic anemia, hypercalcemia, renal dysfunction, and rouleaux formation on smear has multiple myeloma — confirmed by bone marrow biopsy showing \>10% clonal plasma cells.**

**62岁女性，表现为大细胞性贫血、高钙血症、肾功能损害及血涂片缗钱状排列，诊断为多发性骨髓瘤——骨髓活检示克隆性浆细胞\>10%可确诊。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — CRAB Criteria for Multiple Myeloma / 记忆钩 — 多发性骨髓瘤CRAB诊断标准:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>C</strong>alcium elevated (&gt;10.5 mg/dL) — osteoclast activation releases calcium from lytic bone lesions / 高钙血症（&gt;10.5 mg/dL）——破骨细胞激活从溶骨灶释放钙<br />
• <strong>R</strong>enal dysfunction (Cr &gt;2 mg/dL or GFR &lt;40) — Bence Jones protein cast nephropathy + hypercalcemia / 肾功能损害（Cr&gt;2或GFR&lt;40）——Bence Jones蛋白管型肾病+高钙血症<br />
• <strong>A</strong>nemia (Hgb &lt;10 g/dL) — marrow infiltration displaces normal hematopoiesis / 贫血（Hgb&lt;10）——浆细胞浸润挤压正常造血<br />
• <strong>B</strong>one lesions (lytic, "punched-out" on X-ray, cold on bone scan) — osteoclast-activating paracrine factors / 骨质病变（X线"穿凿样"溶骨，骨扫描冷区）——旁分泌破骨细胞活化因子</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Multiple Myeloma Workup & Management / 高频知识表 — 多发性骨髓瘤诊断与处理

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Diagnostic criteria (IMWG 2014)<br />
诊断标准（IMWG 2014）</td>
<td>&gt;10% clonal plasma cells on biopsy + ≥1 CRAB criterion OR myeloma-defining biomarker (FLC ratio &gt;100, BM plasma cells &gt;60%, &gt;1 focal MRI lesion)<br />
活检克隆性浆细胞&gt;10%+≥1项CRAB，或骨髓瘤定义性生物标志物（FLC比值&gt;100，浆细胞&gt;60%，MRI&gt;1个局灶病变）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Blood smear finding<br />
血涂片表现</td>
<td>Rouleaux formation (RBCs stacked like coins) from excess paraprotein coating reducing zeta potential; highly suggestive of MM<br />
缗钱状排列（红细胞叠放如硬币），副蛋白包被降低zeta电位所致；高度提示MM</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Protein electrophoresis<br />
蛋白电泳</td>
<td>Serum SPEP: M-spike in gamma region; 24-hr urine UPEP detects Bence Jones protein (free kappa or lambda light chains)<br />
血清SPEP：γ区M蛋白峰；24小时尿UPEP检出Bence Jones蛋白（游离κ或λ轻链）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Imaging strategy<br />
影像学策略</td>
<td>Skeletal survey X-ray: punched-out lytic lesions; whole-body low-dose CT or PET-CT preferred; bone scan NOT useful (no osteoblast activity in lytic lesions)<br />
骨骼X线平片：穿凿样溶骨灶；首选全身低剂量CT或PET-CT；骨扫描无用（溶骨灶无成骨活性）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Why macrocytic anemia in MM<br />
MM中大细胞贫血机制</td>
<td>Rapidly proliferating plasma cells consume large amounts of folate → functional folate deficiency → megaloblastic changes; NOT due to B12 deficiency<br />
快速增殖的浆细胞大量消耗叶酸 → 功能性叶酸缺乏 → 巨幼细胞样改变；非B12缺乏所致</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>First-line treatment<br />
一线治疗</td>
<td>VRd induction (bortezomib + lenalidomide + dexamethasone); transplant-eligible patients: autologous SCT; maintenance with lenalidomide<br />
VRd诱导（硼替佐米+来那度胺+地塞米松）；适合移植者行自体干细胞移植；来那度胺维持治疗</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hypercalcemia management<br />
高钙血症处理</td>
<td>IV normal saline hydration (mainstay), bisphosphonates (zoledronic acid), calcitonin for rapid effect; treat underlying MM<br />
静脉生理盐水水化（主要措施）、双膦酸盐（唑来膦酸）、降钙素快速降钙；同时治疗基础MM</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of macrocytic anemia with systemic features:** Vitamin B12 deficiency (neurologic sx, no CRAB), folate deficiency (dietary, no bone lesions), liver disease (transaminase elevation), hypothyroidism (TSH elevated), and MM (CRAB criteria)\
  **伴系统性表现的大细胞贫血鉴别:** 维生素B12缺乏（神经系统症状，无CRAB）、叶酸缺乏（饮食相关，无骨质病变）、肝病（转氨酶升高）、甲减（TSH升高），以及MM（CRAB标准）

- **Smoldering myeloma variant:** Clonal plasma cells 10–60% in marrow OR M protein ≥3 g/dL, but NO CRAB criteria — managed with observation only; 10% annual risk of progression to symptomatic MM\
  **冒烟型骨髓瘤变式:** 骨髓克隆性浆细胞10–60%或M蛋白≥3 g/dL，但无CRAB标准——仅观察随访；每年约10%进展为有症状MM

- **Three mechanisms of renal failure in MM:** (1) Light chain cast nephropathy — most common; (2) Hypercalcemia → renal vasoconstriction + nephrocalcinosis; (3) AL amyloidosis — free light chains deposit as amyloid fibrils in glomeruli\
  **MM肾衰竭三种机制:** （1）轻链管型肾病——最常见；（2）高钙血症→肾血管收缩+肾钙质沉着；（3）AL型淀粉样变——游离轻链以淀粉样纤维形式沉积于肾小球

- **Immunodeficiency in MM:** Neoplastic plasma cells suppress normal polyclonal immunoglobulin production → secondary hypogammaglobulinemia → susceptibility to encapsulated bacteria (S. pneumoniae, H. influenzae); vaccinate and consider IVIG for recurrent infections\
  **MM免疫缺陷:** 肿瘤性浆细胞抑制正常多克隆免疫球蛋白产生→继发性低丙球蛋白血症→易感荚膜菌（肺炎链球菌、流感嗜血杆菌）；需接种疫苗，反复感染者考虑静注免疫球蛋白

# Question 48 — Hepatitis A Vaccination for MSM / 甲肝疫苗接种（男男性行为者）

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>37-year-old man</strong> comes to the physician for a routine health maintenance examination. He feels well. He has no history of serious illness and takes no medications. He received the <strong>hepatitis B vaccine</strong> at the age of 28 years. He does not smoke or drink alcohol. During the past 6 months, he has been sexually active with <strong>one male partner</strong>, and they <strong>do not use condoms</strong>. The patient works as an accountant and <strong>has not traveled outside the USA</strong>. Examination shows no abnormalities. A blood sample is obtained for serum lipid studies and an HIV antibody test. In addition to counseling this patient about risk factors for sexually transmitted diseases, which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) PPD skin test<br />
B) Haemophilus influenzae type b vaccine<br />
C) Hepatitis A vaccine<br />
D) Meningococcal vaccine<br />
E) Pneumococcal polysaccharide vaccine, 23-valent</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: C</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>37-year-old man, routine health maintenance<br />
37岁男性，常规健康维护</td>
<td>Preventive care visit — focus on immunization gaps and appropriate screening<br />
预防保健就诊——重点关注接种空缺和适当筛查</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Sexually active with one male partner (MSM)<br />
与一名男性伴侣有性行为（MSM）</td>
<td>CDC ACIP explicitly lists MSM as a priority group for Hepatitis A vaccination<br />
CDC ACIP明确将MSM列为甲肝疫苗优先接种群体</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Does not use condoms<br />
不使用安全套</td>
<td>Increases fecal-oral exposure risk through oral-anal sexual contact, a HAV transmission route<br />
增加通过口肛性接触的粪口暴露风险，这是HAV传播途径之一</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Received hepatitis B vaccine at age 28<br />
28岁时已接种乙肝疫苗</td>
<td>HBV is already covered — directs attention to the Hepatitis A immunization gap<br />
乙肝已覆盖——提示关注甲肝接种空缺</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Has not traveled outside the USA<br />
未出境旅行</td>
<td>Eliminates travel as the sole indication, but MSM status alone is sufficient for Hep A vaccination<br />
排除旅行为唯一指征，但MSM身份本身即已足够</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>No history of serious illness<br />
无严重疾病史</td>
<td>Excludes chronic liver disease and immunosuppression as additional indications<br />
排除慢性肝病和免疫抑制作为额外指征</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Hepatitis A virus (HAV)** is a **nonenveloped, single-stranded RNA virus** transmitted via the **fecal-oral route**, causing self-limited but sometimes severe acute hepatitis:

**甲型肝炎病毒（HAV）**是一种经**粪口途径**传播的**无包膜单链RNA病毒**，可引起自限性但有时较重的急性肝炎：

- HAV replicates in hepatocytes → immune-mediated lysis → transaminitis, hyperbilirubinemia, jaundice\
  HAV在肝细胞中复制 → 免疫介导细胞溶解 → 转氨酶升高、高胆红素血症、黄疸

- Sexual transmission occurs via oral-anal contact (rimming), making MSM a recognized **high-risk group** for HAV outbreaks\
  性传播通过口肛接触发生，使MSM成为公认的HAV暴发**高危群体**

- HAV does **not** cause chronic hepatitis — no carrier state, no cirrhosis; but fulminant failure can occur in those with underlying liver disease\
  HAV**不**导致慢性肝炎——无携带状态，无肝硬化；但在基础肝病患者中可发生暴发性肝衰竭

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** HAV lives in the gut, spreads fecal-orally, and never integrates into the host genome — hence no chronic carrier state unlike HBV or HCV.

**解剖小窍门:** HAV定居于肠道，经粪口途径传播，从不整合至宿主基因组——因此与HBV或HCV不同，不存在慢性携带状态。

## 3. Correct Answer (C) — Hepatitis A Vaccine / 正确答案 (C) — 甲肝疫苗

**Hepatitis A vaccine** is a CDC ACIP-recommended inactivated vaccine specifically indicated for MSM patients regardless of other risk factors:

**甲肝疫苗**是CDC ACIP推荐的灭活疫苗，明确适用于MSM患者，无论其他危险因素如何：

- Inactivated (killed virus) vaccine — safe in immunocompromised; given as a **2-dose IM series** at 0 and 6–12 months\
  灭活（灭活病毒）疫苗——免疫低下者可安全使用；以**2次肌注系列**给予，0和6-12个月各一次

- Seroconversion \>94% after dose 1; approaches 100% after dose 2; protection lasts ≥25 years\
  第1剂后血清转化率\>94%；第2剂后接近100%；保护持续≥25年

- ACIP-listed indications: MSM, international travelers (endemic areas), HIV-positive patients, homeless individuals, injection drug users, chronic liver disease\
  ACIP列出的适应证：MSM、前往流行地区的国际旅行者、HIV阳性患者、无家可归者、注射毒品者、慢性肝病

**Diagnosis:** This patient is MSM with no documented Hepatitis A immunity — this preventive visit is the appropriate time to initiate vaccination.

**诊断:** 该患者为MSM且无甲肝免疫记录——此预防性就诊是启动接种的恰当时机。

**Treatment:** Administer Hepatitis A vaccine first dose today; schedule second dose at 6–12 months.

**治疗:** 今日接种甲肝疫苗第一剂；6-12个月后安排第二剂。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />

<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — PPD skin test<br />
A — PPD皮试</td>
<td>Not routinely indicated for MSM; reserved for healthcare workers, HIV-positive patients, injection drug users, or documented TB exposure<br />
MSM不常规推荐；保留用于医护人员、HIV阳性患者、注射毒品者或有记录的TB暴露者</td>

儿科疫苗，从2月龄起4剂系列；免疫功能正常的成人无指征</td>
<td>Age 37, immunocompetent — Hib vaccine has no role in adult preventive care<br />
37岁、免疫功能正常——Hib疫苗在成人预防保健中无作用</td>

<tr>
<td>C — Hepatitis A vaccine ✓<br />
C — 甲肝疫苗 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — MSM is an explicit CDC ACIP indication; no documented HAV immunity on record<br />
正确——MSM是CDC ACIP明确指征；无甲肝免疫记录</td>

<tr>

D — 脑膜炎球菌疫苗</td>
<td>Indicated for asplenia, complement deficiency, college freshmen in dormitories, military recruits, and travelers to endemic areas — none of which apply here<br />
适用于无脾、补体缺陷、住宿大学新生、军队新兵及前往流行地区旅行者——均不适用于此患者</td>
<td>No high-risk meningococcal exposure identified; MSM is not a meningococcal vaccine indication<br />
未识别脑膜炎球菌高风险暴露；MSM不是脑膜炎球菌疫苗指征</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Pneumococcal polysaccharide vaccine, 23-valent<br />
E — 23价肺炎球菌多糖疫苗</td>
<td>Indicated for adults ≥65 years or those with chronic heart, renal, or liver disease, asplenia, or who are current smokers — patient is 37 and healthy<br />
适用于≥65岁成人或慢性心/肾/肝病、无脾或当前吸烟者——患者37岁且健康</td>
<td>Age alone (37) and absence of comorbidities disqualify PPSV23<br />
仅年龄（37岁）及无合并症即排除PPSV23</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The strongest distractor is Choice A (PPD): test-takers may conflate HIV risk in MSM with TB screening, but MSM status alone does not warrant PPD testing — only confirmed HIV-positive status, healthcare work, or TB exposure would.*

最常见的干扰项是选项A（PPD）：考生容易将MSM人群的HIV风险与结核筛查混淆，但仅MSM身份本身不需要PPD检测——只有确认HIV阳性、医疗工作或TB暴露才需要。

## 5. High-Yield Summary Table — Hepatitis A vs. Hepatitis B: Virology & Vaccine Comparison / 甲型肝炎 vs 乙型肝炎：病毒学与疫苗对比

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**A 37-year-old MSM man with no documented Hepatitis A immunity should receive the Hepatitis A vaccine per CDC ACIP guidelines, which explicitly list MSM as a priority vaccination group due to fecal-oral sexual transmission risk.**

**一名37岁无甲肝免疫记录的MSM男性应按CDC ACIP指南接种甲肝疫苗，该指南因粪口性传播风险明确将MSM列为优先接种群体。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "HITH" for HAV Vaccine High-Risk Groups / 记忆钩 — "HITH" 记忆甲肝疫苗高危人群:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>H</strong>omeless / HIV-positive — impaired immunity and crowded conditions amplify HAV risk / 无家可归者/HIV阳性——免疫受损和拥挤环境放大HAV风险<br />
• <strong>I</strong>njection drug users — shared needles + fecal-oral overlap in high-risk settings / 注射毒品者——共用针具 + 高风险环境中粪口传播叠加<br />
• <strong>T</strong>ravelers to endemic areas — fecal-oral exposure via contaminated food and water / 前往流行地区的旅行者——经污染食物和水的粪口暴露<br />
• <strong>H</strong>omosexual men (MSM) — oral-anal sexual contact is a direct fecal-oral route / 男同性恋者（MSM）——口肛性接触是直接的粪口途径</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — HAV Vaccine Indications & Clinical Pearls / 高频知识表 — 甲肝疫苗适应证与临床要点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>HAV vaccine type<br />
HAV疫苗类型</td>
<td>Inactivated (killed) virus — NOT live; safe in immunocompromised patients; combination Hep A+B (Twinrix) available as 3-dose series<br />
灭活（灭活）病毒——非活疫苗；免疫功能低下患者可安全使用；甲乙肝联合疫苗（Twinrix）以3剂系列提供</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>CDC ACIP indications for HAV vaccine<br />
CDC ACIP甲肝疫苗指征</td>
<td>MSM, injection drug users, homeless, international travelers to endemic areas, HIV+, chronic liver disease (including HCV), close contacts of international adoptees<br />
MSM、注射毒品者、无家可归者、前往流行地区国际旅行者、HIV阳性、慢性肝病（含HCV）、国际收养儿童密切接触者</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>HAV serology interpretation<br />
HAV血清学解读</td>
<td>Anti-HAV IgM = acute infection; anti-HAV IgG = past infection or successful vaccination; total anti-HAV = immunity<br />
抗HAV IgM = 急性感染；抗HAV IgG = 既往感染或成功接种；总抗HAV = 免疫力</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>HAV clinical features<br />
HAV临床特征</td>
<td>Fever, nausea, vomiting, RUQ pain, jaundice, hepatomegaly; labs: elevated ALT/AST, alkaline phosphatase, total bilirubin; many cases subclinical in children<br />
发热、恶心、呕吐、右上腹痛、黄疸、肝肿大；化验：ALT/AST、碱性磷酸酶、总胆红素升高；儿童中许多病例无症状</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Post-exposure prophylaxis (PEP) for HAV<br />
HAV暴露后预防</td>
<td>Within 2 weeks of exposure: Hep A vaccine (healthy individuals &lt;40 yo) OR immunoglobulin (IG) (&gt;40 yo, immunocompromised, chronic liver disease)<br />
暴露后2周内：甲肝疫苗（健康、&lt;40岁）或免疫球蛋白（IG）（&gt;40岁、免疫低下、慢性肝病）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>HAV vs. chronic liver disease<br />
HAV与慢性肝病</td>
<td>HAV never causes chronic hepatitis or cirrhosis; however, patients with underlying liver disease (HBV, HCV, alcoholic) have markedly increased risk of fulminant hepatic failure<br />
HAV从不引起慢性肝炎或肝硬化；但基础肝病患者（HBV、HCV、酒精性）发生暴发性肝衰竭的风险显著增加</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Comprehensive MSM preventive care at this visit:** Beyond Hep A vaccine, this patient needs HIV result follow-up, STI screening (gonorrhea, chlamydia, syphilis), and assessment for HIV PrEP eligibility given condomless sex\
  **此次就诊的全面MSM预防保健:** 除甲肝疫苗外，该患者还需要HIV结果随访、STI筛查（淋病、衣原体、梅毒），以及鉴于无套性行为评估HIV PrEP资格

- **HAV outbreak epidemiology:** Recent large US outbreaks have affected MSM communities and homeless populations; older outbreaks typically linked to contaminated shellfish or produce (fecal-oral via food handlers)\
  **HAV暴发流行病学:** 近期美国大型暴发影响MSM社区和无家可归人群；早期暴发通常与污染贝类或农产品相关（经食品处理者粪口传播）

- **Hep B vaccine already given — don't repeat:** Patient received HBV vaccine series at age 28; post-vaccination serology (anti-HBs) is not routinely checked except in healthcare workers or immunocompromised patients\
  **乙肝疫苗已接种——勿重复:** 患者28岁时已完成HBV疫苗系列；接种后血清学检测（抗HBs）除医护人员或免疫低下患者外不常规检查

- **Variant scenario — if patient were HIV-positive:** HIV+ status would add indications for PPD testing, PPSV23 (regardless of age), and more frequent STI screening — changing management substantially from this baseline case\
  **题目变式——若患者HIV阳性:** HIV阳性状态将增加PPD检测、PPSV23接种（不论年龄）和更频繁STI筛查的指征——与此基线病例相比管理有实质性改变

# Question 49 — Panic Disorder / 惊恐障碍

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>27-year-old man</strong> comes to the physician because of a <strong>1-month history of sudden episodes</strong> of a "scary choking feeling." He has had three episodes during this period; the episodes are accompanied by <strong>nausea, sweating, and "heart pounding" sensations</strong>. The symptoms <strong>peak within 5 to 10 minutes</strong> and disappear about 15 minutes later. The first two episodes "came out of the blue" while he was at work; the last episode occurred when he was stuck in traffic. He is <strong>fearful that he will have another episode</strong> and that "someone will notice and think I'm going crazy." He has no history of serious medical illness and takes no medications. He is a veteran of the U.S. Marine Corps and experienced some intense fighting 5 years ago. He has <strong>occasional nightmares involving combat</strong> and intermittent sadness when he thinks about military comrades who were killed. He has occasional difficulty falling asleep. He has had <strong>no changes in energy level or appetite</strong>. He is 175 cm (5 ft 9 in) tall and weighs 82 kg (180 lb); BMI is 27 kg/m². Vital signs are within normal limits. Physical examination shows no abnormalities. On mental status examination, he is anxious but relates well with the physician. His serum <strong>thyroid-stimulating hormone concentration is within the reference range</strong>. A 12-lead <strong>ECG shows a normal sinus rhythm</strong>.</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate pharmacotherapy?</strong></p>
<p>A) Bupropion<br />
B) Buspirone<br />
C) Haloperidol<br />
D) Lithium carbonate<br />
E) Paroxetine<br />
F) Risperdal</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: E</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Sudden episodes peaking within 5–10 minutes<br />
突发发作，5-10分钟内达高峰</td>
<td>Classic temporal profile of a panic attack; DSM-5 requires symptoms to peak within minutes<br />
符合惊恐发作的典型时间特征；DSM-5要求症状在数分钟内达峰</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>"Came out of the blue" — attacks at work and in traffic<br />
发作"毫无原因"——在工作和堵车时均可发生</td>
<td>Unexpected/uncued attacks are the hallmark of panic disorder vs. PTSD (which requires trauma-triggered attacks)<br />
非预期/无诱因发作是惊恐障碍的核心特征，区别于需由创伤线索触发的PTSD</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Fearful of future episodes; worry about others noticing<br />
害怕再次发作；担心他人察觉</td>
<td>Anticipatory anxiety is a DSM-5 diagnostic criterion for panic disorder<br />
预期性焦虑是惊恐障碍的DSM-5诊断标准之一</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Nausea, sweating, "heart pounding"<br />
恶心、出汗、"心跳加速"</td>
<td>≥4 somatic symptoms required for panic attack diagnosis; these represent classic sympathetic surge<br />
诊断惊恐发作需≥4项躯体症状；这些是交感神经激活的典型表现</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Combat veteran with occasional nightmares and sadness<br />
退伍军人，偶有战斗噩梦和悲伤</td>
<td>Subthreshold PTSD features — high-yield distractor! Attacks are NOT triggered by combat reminders, ruling out PTSD<br />
亚阈值PTSD特征——高频干扰项！发作并非由创伤线索触发，可排除PTSD</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Normal TSH and normal ECG<br />
TSH正常，ECG正常</td>
<td>Rules out hyperthyroidism and arrhythmia as organic causes of episodic palpitations and anxiety<br />
排除甲状腺功能亢进及心律失常等发作性心悸和焦虑的器质性病因</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

**Panic disorder** arises from dysregulation of the **fear circuit**, particularly the **amygdala**, which generates false-alarm fear responses in the absence of real threat:

**惊恐障碍**源于**恐惧回路**的失调，尤其是**杏仁核**在没有真实威胁的情况下发出假警报信号：

- Amygdala hyperactivation triggers the hypothalamic-pituitary-adrenal axis and sympathetic nervous system, producing the classic somatic symptoms\
  杏仁核过度激活触发下丘脑-垂体-肾上腺轴及交感神经系统，产生经典躯体症状

- The "choking" sensation reflects CO₂ hypersensitivity — panic disorder patients have a lower suffocation-alarm threshold than the general population\
  "窒息感"反映了CO₂高敏感性——惊恐障碍患者的窒息警报阈值低于普通人群

- After an initial spontaneous attack, interoceptive conditioning occurs: internal body sensations (slight tachycardia, mild dyspnea) become conditioned stimuli triggering subsequent attacks\
  初次自发发作后，内感受性条件化形成：轻微心动过速等体内感觉成为触发后续发作的条件刺激

- SSRIs desensitize this hyperactive fear circuit over 2–4 weeks by increasing serotonin availability at limbic synapses\
  SSRIs通过增加边缘系统突触处5-羟色胺浓度，在2-4周内使过度激活的恐惧回路脱敏

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** The amygdala is the brain's "smoke detector" — panic disorder is a false-alarm state where the detector is set dangerously sensitive.

**解剖小窍门:** 杏仁核是大脑的"烟雾探测器"——惊恐障碍是探测器灵敏度设定过高导致的持续假警报状态。

## 3. Correct Answer (E) — Paroxetine (SSRI) / 正确答案 (E) — 帕罗西汀（选择性5-羟色胺再摄取抑制剂）

**Paroxetine** is an SSRI with FDA approval specifically for panic disorder and is the prototypical first-line pharmacotherapy:

**帕罗西汀**是一种获FDA批准用于惊恐障碍的SSRI，是标准一线药物治疗代表药物：

- SSRIs (paroxetine, sertraline, fluoxetine, escitalopram) are first-line pharmacotherapy for panic disorder — superior long-term efficacy with favorable side-effect profile vs. TCAs or MAOIs\
  SSRIs（帕罗西汀、舍曲林、氟西汀、艾司西酞普兰）是惊恐障碍的一线药物——与TCAs或MAOIs相比，长期疗效优越且副作用可控

- Onset of anxiolytic effect is 2–4 weeks; patients should be counseled that SSRIs may transiently worsen anxiety at initiation (start low, go slow)\
  抗焦虑起效需2-4周；需告知患者SSRI起始阶段可能短暂加重焦虑（小剂量起始，缓慢加量）

- Short-term benzodiazepines may be co-prescribed for acute symptom relief during SSRI titration phase\
  SSRI滴定期间可短期联用苯二氮䓬类药物以缓解急性症状

- CBT with interoceptive exposure is equally effective and preferred as psychotherapy when available\
  含内感受性暴露的CBT疗效相当，有条件时作为首选心理治疗方案

**Diagnosis:** Panic disorder requires recurrent unexpected panic attacks plus ≥1 month of anticipatory anxiety or maladaptive behavioral change. This patient's attacks are spontaneous and uncued by trauma reminders, distinguishing it from PTSD.

**诊断:** 惊恐障碍需反复出现的非预期惊恐发作，加上≥1个月的预期性焦虑或适应不良行为改变。本患者发作自发出现，非由创伤线索触发，与PTSD相区别。

**Treatment:** SSRIs (paroxetine or sertraline) first-line; short-term benzodiazepines for acute bridging; CBT as psychotherapy of choice.

**治疗:** 一线用药为SSRIs（帕罗西汀或舍曲林）；急性期桥接可短期使用苯二氮䓬类；心理治疗首选CBT。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Bupropion<br />
A — 安非他酮</td>
<td>Dopamine/norepinephrine reuptake inhibitor used for depression and smoking cessation; no evidence for panic disorder and may worsen anxiety/agitation<br />
多巴胺/去甲肾上腺素再摄取抑制剂，用于抑郁症和戒烟；对惊恐障碍无循证依据，且可能加重焦虑/激越</td>
<td>No anxiety/panic indication; can paradoxically worsen panic symptoms via norepinephrine surge<br />
无焦虑/惊恐适应症；可通过去甲肾上腺素激增反常加重惊恐症状</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Buspirone<br />
B — 丁螺环酮</td>
<td>5-HT1A partial agonist effective for generalized anxiety disorder (GAD); NOT effective for panic disorder per evidence<br />
5-HT1A部分激动剂，对广泛性焦虑障碍有效；循证证据显示对惊恐障碍无效</td>
<td>Treat GAD, not panic disorder; also provides no acute relief, making it doubly inappropriate here<br />
针对GAD，非惊恐障碍；亦无急性缓解效果，因此双重不适用</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Haloperidol<br />
C — 氟哌啶醇</td>
<td>Typical antipsychotic (D2 antagonist); indicated for schizophrenia and acute psychosis; no role in any anxiety disorder<br />
典型抗精神病药（D2拮抗剂）；适用于精神分裂症和急性精神病；在任何焦虑障碍中均无治疗地位</td>
<td>No psychotic features present; antipsychotics are not anxiolytics<br />
患者无精神病性症状；抗精神病药不具有抗焦虑作用</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Lithium carbonate<br />
D — 碳酸锂</td>
<td>Mood stabilizer for bipolar disorder and augmentation of refractory depression; no role in panic or anxiety treatment<br />
双相障碍及难治性抑郁症的情绪稳定剂；在惊恐或焦虑治疗中无地位</td>
<td>No mood cycling, no mania, no bipolar features; choosing lithium implies a diagnostic error<br />
无情绪循环、躁狂或双相特征；选择锂盐意味着根本性诊断错误</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Paroxetine ✓<br />
E — 帕罗西汀 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — FDA-approved SSRI specifically for panic disorder; first-line long-term pharmacotherapy<br />
正确——帕罗西汀是FDA批准专门用于惊恐障碍的SSRI；一线长期药物治疗方案</td>
<td>Recurrent unexpected panic attacks + anticipatory anxiety = panic disorder → SSRI<br />
反复非预期惊恐发作+预期性焦虑=惊恐障碍→SSRI</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>F — Risperdal (Risperidone)<br />
F — 利培酮（Risperdal）</td>
<td>Atypical antipsychotic (D2/5-HT2A antagonist); indicated for schizophrenia and bipolar disorder; no role in panic disorder<br />
非典型抗精神病药（D2/5-HT2A拮抗剂）；适用于精神分裂症和双相障碍；在惊恐障碍中无治疗地位</td>
<td>No psychosis or bipolar features; using an antipsychotic here reflects a complete misdiagnosis<br />
患者无精神病或双相特征；在此使用抗精神病药反映诊断根本性错误</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The highest-yield distractor is Buspirone (B): both GAD and panic disorder involve anxiety, but buspirone is specifically NOT effective for panic disorder — USMLE frequently tests this distinction.*

最高频干扰项是丁螺环酮（B）：GAD和惊恐障碍都涉及焦虑，但丁螺环酮对惊恐障碍特异性无效——USMLE频繁考查这一鉴别点。
