## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**Panic disorder = recurrent UNEXPECTED panic attacks (peaking in minutes) + anticipatory anxiety → first-line pharmacotherapy is an SSRI such as paroxetine.**

**惊恐障碍=反复非预期惊恐发作（数分钟内达峰）+预期性焦虑→一线药物治疗为SSRI，如帕罗西汀。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — PANIC Criteria for Panic Disorder / 记忆钩 — "PANIC"记忆惊恐障碍诊断要点:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>P</strong>eak within minutes — symptoms must reach maximum intensity in under 10 min / 症状须在10分钟内达高峰<br />
• <strong>A</strong>nticipatory anxiety — ≥1 month of worry about future attacks is a DSM-5 criterion / ≥1个月的对再次发作的担忧是DSM-5标准<br />
• <strong>N</strong>o cue required — attacks are unexpected and spontaneous, NOT trauma-triggered / 无需诱因——发作自发且非创伤触发<br />
• <strong>I</strong>nvolves ≥4 somatic symptoms (palpitations, sweating, choking, chest pain, nausea, dizziness…) / 涉及≥4项躯体症状（心悸、出汗、窒息感、胸痛、恶心、头晕…）<br />
• <strong>C</strong>BT + SSRI = treatment combo of choice / CBT联合SSRI是首选治疗组合</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Panic Disorder: Diagnosis & Pharmacology / 高频知识表 — 惊恐障碍：诊断与药理

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>DSM-5 panic attack symptom list<br />
DSM-5惊恐发作症状列表</td>
<td>≥4 of 13: palpitations, sweating, trembling, shortness of breath, choking sensation, chest pain, nausea, dizziness, derealization/depersonalization, fear of losing control, fear of dying, paresthesias, chills/hot flashes<br />
13项中≥4项：心悸、出汗、颤抖、气短、窒息感、胸痛、恶心、头晕、现实解体/人格解体、失控感、濒死感、感觉异常、寒颤/潮热</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Panic disorder DSM-5 criteria<br />
惊恐障碍DSM-5诊断标准</td>
<td>Recurrent unexpected panic attacks + ≥1 month of (1) persistent worry/concern about attacks OR (2) significant maladaptive behavioral change (e.g., avoidance)<br />
反复非预期惊恐发作+≥1个月：(1)持续担忧发作，或(2)明显的适应不良行为改变（如回避）</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>First-line pharmacotherapy<br />
一线药物治疗</td>
<td>SSRIs: paroxetine and sertraline are FDA-approved for panic disorder specifically; fluoxetine and escitalopram also commonly used; onset 2–4 weeks<br />
SSRIs：帕罗西汀和舍曲林获FDA专项批准用于惊恐障碍；氟西汀和艾司西酞普兰也常用；起效2-4周</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Acute bridging agents<br />
急性期桥接药物</td>
<td>Benzodiazepines (clonazepam, lorazepam) for rapid symptom control during SSRI initiation; limit to weeks due to dependence risk; avoid in veterans with substance use history<br />
苯二氮䓬类（氯硝西泮、劳拉西泮）在SSRI起效前用于快速控制症状；因依赖风险限于数周；有物质滥用史的退伍军人慎用</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Psychotherapy<br />
心理治疗</td>
<td>CBT with interoceptive exposure is gold standard; teaches patients to tolerate physical sensations without catastrophizing; equally effective as SSRIs long-term<br />
含内感受性暴露的CBT是金标准；教导患者耐受躯体感觉而不进行灾难化认知；长期疗效与SSRI相当</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Medical rule-out workup<br />
需排除的器质性疾病</td>
<td>ECG (arrhythmia/SVT), TSH (hyperthyroidism), urine/plasma metanephrines (pheochromocytoma), fasting glucose (hypoglycemia), Holter if attacks correlate with exertion<br />
心电图（心律失常/室上速）、TSH（甲亢）、尿/血浆甲氧基肾上腺素（嗜铬细胞瘤）、空腹血糖（低血糖）、如发作与活动相关则行Holter监测</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Why NOT buspirone for panic<br />
丁螺环酮为何不用于惊恐障碍</td>
<td>Buspirone is effective for GAD (chronic diffuse worry) via 5-HT1A partial agonism but has NO demonstrated efficacy for panic disorder; mechanism too slow and targets wrong circuit<br />
丁螺环酮通过5-HT1A部分激动对GAD（慢性弥漫性担忧）有效，但对惊恐障碍无循证疗效；机制过慢且靶向回路不匹配</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Subthreshold PTSD as distractor:** This patient has combat exposure, nightmares, and intermittent sadness — but lacks sufficient re-experiencing, hyperarousal (exaggerated startle), and avoidance of trauma reminders to meet PTSD criteria; critically, his attacks are not trauma-cued\
  **亚阈值PTSD作为干扰项:** 患者有战斗暴露、噩梦和间歇性悲伤——但缺乏充分的再体验、过度唤起（惊跳反应增强）和对创伤线索的回避，未达PTSD标准；关键是其发作非创伤线索触发

- **Paroxetine discontinuation syndrome:** Among SSRIs, paroxetine has the shortest half-life and highest risk of discontinuation syndrome (dizziness, electric-shock sensations, flu-like symptoms) — always taper slowly; this is a USMLE favorite side effect comparison point\
  **帕罗西汀停药综合征:** 帕罗西汀在SSRIs中半衰期最短，停药综合征风险最高（头晕、电击感、流感样症状）——务必缓慢减量；这是USMLE热门副作用对比考点

- **Pheochromocytoma mimicry:** Episodic hypertension, diaphoresis, and palpitations can perfectly mimic panic attacks — rule out with urine/plasma metanephrines, especially if attacks are associated with headache, severe hypertension, or pallor\
  **嗜铬细胞瘤的鉴别:** 发作性高血压、大汗和心悸可完美模拟惊恐发作——尤其伴头痛、严重高血压或皮肤苍白时，需检测尿/血浆甲氧基肾上腺素排除

- **Variant — situational panic disorder:** When attacks consistently occur in specific situations (bridges, crowds, traffic) rather than being truly unexpected, consider specific phobia or agoraphobia — the last attack in traffic for this patient is still classified as panic disorder, not agoraphobia, because most attacks were spontaneous\
  **题目变式——情境性惊恐:** 当发作始终在特定情境（桥梁、人群、堵车）出现而非真正随机时，考虑特定恐怖症或广场恐怖症——本患者最后一次在堵车时发作仍归类为惊恐障碍，因为大多数发作是自发的

# Question 50 — Posterior Urethral Injury from Pelvic Fracture / 骨盆骨折致后尿道损伤

## Question Stem / 题干

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p>A <strong>previously healthy 25-year-old man</strong> is brought to the emergency department <strong>2 hours</strong> after being involved in a <strong>motor vehicle collision</strong>. He was the restrained driver. On arrival, he is alert and oriented to person, place, and time. He says he has <strong>severe lower abdominal pain</strong>. His temperature is 37.5°C (99.5°F), <strong>pulse is 105/min</strong>, respirations are 18/min, and blood pressure is 120/70 mm Hg. Abdominal examination shows <strong>ecchymoses over the lower quadrants</strong> and an abrasion where the seat belt was fastened. There is <strong>suprapubic tenderness</strong>. Palpation of the iliac crests produces pain. There is <strong>blood at the urethral meatus</strong>. His <strong>hematocrit is 30%</strong>. X-rays of the pelvis show a <strong>fracture of the superior and inferior right pubic rami and the right sacroiliac joint</strong>. Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</p>
<p><strong>Q: Which of the following is the most appropriate next step in management?</strong></p>
<p>A) Cystography<br />
B) Retrograde urethrography<br />
C) Placement of a suprapubic catheter<br />
D) Intravenous pyelography<br />
E) Bladder irrigation</p>
<p><strong>Correct Answer: B</strong></p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 1. Key Stem Clues / 题干关键词抓考点

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Key Stem Clue</strong><br />
<strong>关键词</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why It Matters</strong><br />
<strong>为什么重要</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Blood at urethral meatus<br />
尿道口出血</td>
<td>Cardinal sign of urethral injury — mandates retrograde urethrography before any catheterization attempt<br />
尿道损伤的主要体征——任何导尿操作前必须先行逆行尿道造影</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pelvic fracture (pubic rami + sacroiliac joint)<br />
骨盆骨折（耻骨支 + 骶髂关节）</td>
<td>Pelvic ring disruption is the primary mechanism for posterior urethral injury via shear forces<br />
骨盆环断裂通过剪切力是后尿道损伤的主要机制</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Suprapubic tenderness<br />
耻骨上压痛</td>
<td>Suggests lower urinary tract involvement — bladder or posterior urethra<br />
提示下尿路受累——膀胱或后尿道</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Motor vehicle collision, restrained driver<br />
机动车碰撞，系安全带驾驶员</td>
<td>High-energy deceleration trauma; seatbelt generates shear forces across the pelvic ring<br />
高能量减速创伤；安全带在骨盆环处产生剪切力</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Hematocrit 30%<br />
红细胞压积 30%</td>
<td>Significant hemorrhage from pelvic fracture — pelvic veins and arteries may be disrupted<br />
骨盆骨折致大量出血——骨盆静脉和动脉可能断裂</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Pulse 105/min (tachycardia)<br />
脉搏 105 次/分（心动过速）</td>
<td>Compensatory response to hypovolemia from pelvic hemorrhage despite relatively preserved BP<br />
尽管血压相对保留，仍为骨盆出血致低血容量的代偿性反应</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 2. Mechanism / 机制理解

The **posterior urethra** (membranous and prostatic portions) traverses the **urogenital diaphragm** and is anchored by the puboprostatic ligaments. When the **pelvic ring** is disrupted by fracture, shear forces avulse the urethra at the **prostatomembranous junction** — the most vulnerable point:

**后尿道**（膜部和前列腺部）穿过**泌尿生殖膈**，由耻骨前列腺韧带固定。当骨折导致**骨盆环**断裂时，剪切力在**前列腺膜部交界处**撕脱尿道——这是最脆弱的部位：

- Pubic rami fractures displace anteriorly, stretching the prostatic urethra beyond its elastic limit\
  耻骨支骨折向前移位，将前列腺尿道拉伸超出其弹性极限

- The membranous urethra (least mobile segment) tears first because it is tethered to the urogenital diaphragm\
  膜部尿道（活动度最小段）因固定于泌尿生殖膈而最先撕裂

- Extravasated urine collects in the retropubic space (space of Retzius), causing chemical inflammation and risk of sepsis\
  外渗尿液聚集于耻骨后间隙（Retzius 间隙），引起化学性炎症并有败血症风险

**Anatomic rule of thumb:** Anterior urethra (bulbar/penile) is injured by straddle injuries to the perineum; posterior urethra (membranous/prostatic) is injured by pelvic ring fractures.

**解剖小窍门:** 前尿道（球部/阴茎部）因会阴骑跨伤受损；后尿道（膜部/前列腺部）因骨盆环骨折受损。

## 3. Correct Answer (B) — Retrograde Urethrography / 正确答案 (B) — 逆行尿道造影

**Retrograde urethrography (RUG)** is the gold-standard first test whenever urethral injury is suspected following trauma:

**逆行尿道造影 (RUG)** 是创伤后疑似尿道损伤时的金标准首选检查：

- Water-soluble contrast is injected retrograde into the fossa navicularis under fluoroscopy\
  在透视下将水溶性造影剂逆行注射入舟状窝

- Extravasation of contrast outside the urethral lumen confirms tear location and degree (partial vs. complete)\
  造影剂溢出尿道腔外证实撕裂部位和程度（不完全 vs. 完全）

- Must be performed BEFORE urethral catheterization to avoid converting a partial tear into complete disruption\
  必须在导尿管插入之前进行，以防将不完全撕裂转变为完全断裂

**Diagnosis:** RUG showing contrast extravasation at the prostatomembranous junction confirms posterior urethral injury. Degree of injury guides immediate management decisions.

**诊断:** RUG 显示前列腺膜部交界处造影剂外溢证实后尿道损伤。损伤程度指导即时处理决策。

**Treatment:** Partial tears: gentle urethral catheterization or suprapubic diversion; complete disruptions: suprapubic catheter now, delayed urethroplasty at 3–6 months to allow hematoma resolution.

**治疗:** 不完全撕裂：轻柔导尿或耻骨上造瘘引流；完全断裂：立即耻骨上膀胱造瘘，待血肿吸收后 3-6 个月延期行尿道成形术。

## 4. Options Elimination / 错误选项排除逻辑

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
<col style="width: 33%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Option</strong><br />
<strong>选项</strong></th>
<th><strong>Why Wrong</strong><br />
<strong>为什么错</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Discriminator</strong><br />
<strong>鉴别要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>A — Cystography<br />
A — 膀胱造影</td>
<td>Evaluates bladder rupture (intraperitoneal vs. extraperitoneal), not the urethra; requires retrograde catheter placement which is contraindicated before RUG<br />
评估膀胱破裂（腹腔内 vs. 腹腔外），而非尿道；需要逆行插管，在 RUG 之前属禁忌</td>
<td>Blood at meatus = urethra first; cystography comes after RUG confirms urethral integrity<br />
尿道口出血 = 尿道优先；膀胱造影在 RUG 确认尿道完整后进行</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>B — Retrograde urethrography ✓<br />
B — 逆行尿道造影 ✓</td>
<td>CORRECT — Identifies urethral injury site and degree before any instrumentation; prevents converting partial to complete tear<br />
正确——在任何器械操作前确定尿道损伤部位和程度；防止不完全撕裂转变为完全断裂</td>
<td>Blood at meatus + pelvic fracture = RUG is always the first step<br />
尿道口出血 + 骨盆骨折 = RUG 永远是第一步</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>C — Placement of a suprapubic catheter<br />
C — 放置耻骨上导尿管</td>
<td>Appropriate management after injury is confirmed and characterized, but not the diagnostic first step<br />
损伤确认并明确后的适当处理，但不是首要诊断步骤</td>
<td>Suprapubic catheter is a treatment, not a diagnostic tool; injury pattern must be defined by RUG first<br />
耻骨上导尿管是治疗措施而非诊断工具；损伤类型必须先由 RUG 确定</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>D — Intravenous pyelography<br />
D — 静脉肾盂造影</td>
<td>Evaluates upper urinary tract (kidneys, ureters) — no clinical findings here point to upper tract injury<br />
评估上尿路（肾脏、输尿管）——此处无临床表现指向上尿路损伤</td>
<td>No flank pain, no costovertebral angle tenderness, no mechanism for renal trauma — IVP is misdirected<br />
无腰痛、无肋脊角压痛、无肾损伤机制——IVP 方向错误</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>E — Bladder irrigation<br />
E — 膀胱冲洗</td>
<td>Used to manage intravesical clot burden in bladder hematuria; requires urethral catheter placement, which is contraindicated until RUG is done<br />
用于处理膀胱内血凝块；需要插入尿道导管，在 RUG 完成前属禁忌</td>
<td>Inserting a catheter blindly with urethral injury risks false passage creation and complete disruption<br />
尿道损伤时盲目插管有形成假道和完全断裂的风险</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

*The most tempting distractor is Choice A (cystography) — bladder injury co-exists in up to 15% of pelvic fractures, but blood at the urethral meatus mandates RUG first; cystography requires retrograde catheterization, which is absolutely contraindicated before urethral integrity is confirmed.*

最容易误选的干扰项是 A（膀胱造影）——骨盆骨折中膀胱损伤共发率高达 15%，但尿道口出血要求先行 RUG；膀胱造影需逆行插管，在尿道完整性确认前绝对禁忌。

尿道狭窄（球部最常见）</td>

狭窄 + 勃起功能障碍 + 尿失禁</td>

## 6. One-Sentence Summary & Memory Hook / 一句话总结 & 记忆钩

**In any trauma patient with blood at the urethral meatus — especially with a pelvic fracture — retrograde urethrography must be performed before any urethral catheterization.**

**任何创伤患者出现尿道口出血——尤其合并骨盆骨折——必须在任何导尿操作前先行逆行尿道造影。**

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 100%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><p><strong>Memory Hook — "BUMP" Rule for Urethral Injury / 记忆钩 — 尿道损伤 "BUMP" 法则:</strong></p>
<p>• <strong>B</strong>lood at meatus — the single sign that stops you from placing a catheter / 尿道口出血——阻止插管的唯一体征<br />
• <strong>U</strong>rethrography retrograde — always the first test, no exceptions / 逆行尿道造影——永远是第一步检查，无例外<br />
• <strong>M</strong>embranous urethra tears at urogenital diaphragm in pelvic fracture / 骨盆骨折时膜部尿道在泌尿生殖膈处撕裂<br />
• <strong>P</strong>rostate high-riding on DRE = complete posterior disruption / 直肠检查前列腺上移 = 完全性后尿道断裂</p></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
</tbody>
</table>

## 7. High-Yield Topic Knowledge — Urethral Injury in Trauma / 高频知识表 — 创伤性尿道损伤

<table>
<colgroup>
<col style="width: 50%" />
<col style="width: 50%" />
</colgroup>
<thead>
<tr>
<th><strong>Topic</strong><br />
<strong>考点</strong></th>
<th><strong>Key Points</strong><br />
<strong>要点</strong></th>
</tr>
</thead>
<tbody>
<tr>
<td>Classic triad of posterior urethral injury<br />
后尿道损伤经典三联征</td>
<td>Blood at urethral meatus + inability to void + high-riding/boggy prostate on rectal exam; associated with pelvic fracture<br />
尿道口出血 + 无法排尿 + 直肠检查前列腺上移/松软；与骨盆骨折相关</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Retrograde urethrography technique<br />
逆行尿道造影技术</td>
<td>20–30 mL water-soluble contrast injected into fossa navicularis under fluoroscopy; contrast extravasation = urethral tear confirmed<br />
在透视下将 20-30 mL 水溶性造影剂注入舟状窝；造影剂外溢 = 确认尿道撕裂</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Why not catheterize first<br />
为何不先插尿管</td>
<td>Blind catheterization in partial tear converts to complete disruption; false passage formation leads to infection, stricture, fistula<br />
不完全撕裂时盲目插管转变为完全断裂；假道形成导致感染、狭窄、瘘管</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Sequence after RUG confirms injury<br />
RUG 确认损伤后的处理顺序</td>
<td>Partial tear → attempt gentle catheterization OR suprapubic diversion; complete tear → suprapubic catheter now, urethroplasty at 3–6 months<br />
不完全撕裂→尝试轻柔导尿或耻骨上造瘘；完全撕裂→立即耻骨上膀胱造瘘，3-6 个月后行尿道成形术</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Complications of missed diagnosis<br />
漏诊的并发症</td>
<td>Urethral stricture (up to 50%), urethrocutaneous fistula, erectile dysfunction, urinary incontinence, urosepsis<br />
尿道狭窄（高达 50%），尿道皮肤瘘，勃起功能障碍，尿失禁，尿源性败血症</td>
</tr>
<tr>
<td>Bladder co-injury with pelvic fracture<br />
骨盆骨折合并膀胱损伤</td>
<td>Occurs in ~15% of cases; evaluate with cystography only AFTER RUG confirms intact urethra; extraperitoneal rupture &gt; intraperitoneal<br />
约 15% 病例发生；仅在 RUG 确认尿道完整后行膀胱造影评估；腹腔外破裂 &gt; 腹腔内破裂</td>
</tr>
</tbody>
</table>

## 8. Extensions / 延伸扩展

- **Differential of traumatic hematuria by imaging modality:** Renal injury → CT urogram (flank pain, CVA tenderness); bladder rupture → cystography (suprapubic pain, perivesical fluid on CT); urethral injury → RUG (meatal blood) — each organ has its own dedicated study\
  **创伤性血尿按影像检查的鉴别:** 肾损伤→CT 尿路造影（腰痛、肋脊角压痛）；膀胱破裂→膀胱造影（耻骨上疼痛、CT 示膀胱周积液）；尿道损伤→RUG（尿道口出血）——每个器官有其专用检查

- **Key complication:** Urethral stricture is the most feared long-term sequela, occurring in up to 50% of posterior injuries; presents years later as progressive voiding difficulty and requires urethroplasty\
  **关键并发症:** 尿道狭窄是最令人担忧的远期后遗症，后尿道损伤发生率高达 50%；多年后以进行性排尿困难出现，需行尿道成形术

- **Variant — female urethral injury:** Female urethra is short (~4 cm) and mobile, making injury rare; when it occurs it is associated with major anterior pelvic ring disruption and vaginal laceration\
  **题目变式——女性尿道损伤:** 女性尿道短（约 4 cm）且活动度大，损伤罕见；发生时与严重前骨盆环断裂和阴道撕裂相关

- **ATLS principle:** Urethral injury is flagged during "E" (Exposure) of the primary survey; Foley catheter insertion is deferred until RUG clears the urethra — this prevents a catastrophic iatrogenic complication in the trauma bay\
  **ATLS 原则:** 尿道损伤在初级评估"E"（暴露）阶段标记；Foley 导尿管插入推迟至 RUG 明确尿道通畅——防止创伤急救室发生灾难性医源性并发症
